yasyānandabhavena maṅgalakalāsaṃbhāvitena sphuradhāmnā siddharasāmṛtena karuṇāvīkṣāsudhāsindhunā । bhaktānāṃ prabhavaprasaṃhṛtijarārāgādirogāḥ kṣaṇācchāntiṃ yānti jagatpradhānabhiṣaje tasmai parasmai namaḥ ।। ādimaścandrasenaśca laṅkeśaśca viśāradaḥ । kapālī mattamāṇḍavyau bhāskaraḥ śūrasenakaḥ ।।
ratnakośaśca śambhuśca sāttviko naravāhanaḥ । indrado gomukhaścaiva kambalir vyāḍireva ca ।। nāgārjunaḥ surānando nāgabodhir yaśodhanaḥ । khaṇḍaḥ kāpāliko brahmā govindo lampako hariḥ ।।
saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyākā rasasiddhipradāyakāḥ । rasāṅkuśo bhairavaśca nandī svacchandabhairavaḥ ।। manthānabhairavaścaiva kākacaṇḍīśvarastathā । vāsudeva ṛṣiḥ śṛṅgaḥ kriyātantrasamuccayī ।।
rasendratilako yogī bhālukī maithilāhvayaḥ । mahādevo narendraśca vāsudevo harīśvaraḥ ।। eteṣāṃ kriyate anyeṣāṃ tantrāṇyālokya saṃgrahaḥ । rasānāmatha siddhānāṃ cikitsārthopayoginām ।।
sūnunā siṃhaguptasya rasaratnasamuccayaḥ । rasoparasalohāni yantrādikaraṇāni ca ।। śuddhyarthamapi lohānāṃ tantrādikaraṇāni ca । śuddhiḥ sattvaṃ drutirbhasmakaraṇaṃ ca pravakṣyate ।।
asti nīhāranilayo mahānuttaradiṅmukhe । uttuṅgaśṛṅgasaṃghātalaṅghitābhro mahīdharaḥ ।। viśrāmāya viyanmārgavilaṅghanaghanaśramaḥ । avatīrṇa iva kṣoṇīṃ śaradambumucāṃ gaṇaḥ ।।
rāśirāśīviṣādhīśaphaṇāphalakarociṣām । bhittvā bhuvamivottīrṇo yo vibhāti bhṛśonnataḥ ।। jvaladauṣadhayo yasya nitambamaṇibhūmayaḥ । naktamuddāmataḍitāmanukurvanti vārmucām ।।
kaṭake saṃcarantīnāṃ yasya kiṃnarayoṣitām । pādeṣu dhāturāgeṇa lākṣākṛtyamanuṣṭhitam ।। avataṃsitaśītāṃśurācchāditadigambaraḥ । yo guhādhigato lokairgirīśa iti gīyate ।।
nimīlitadṛśo nityaṃ munayo yasya sānuṣu । pratyakṣayanti giriśamavāṅmanasagocaram ।। śilātalapratihatairyasya nirjharaśīkaraiḥ । ahanyapi nirīkṣante yakṣāstārāṅkitaṃ nabhaḥ ।।
nīhārapavanodrekaniḥsahā yatra puruṣāḥ । nijastrīṇāṃ niṣevante kucoṣmāṇaṃ nirantaram ।। saṃcaran kaṭake yasya nidāghe api divākaraḥ । uddāmahimaruddhoṣmā na śītāṃśorvibhidyate ।।
guhāgṛheṣu kastūrīmṛganābhisugandhiṣu । gāyanti yatra kiṃnaryo gaurīpariṇayotsavam ।। cakāsti tatra jagatāmādidevo maheśvaraḥ । rasātmanā jagattrātuṃ jāto yasmānmahārasaḥ ।।
śatāśvamedhena kṛtena puṇyaṃ gokoṭibhiḥ svarṇasahasradānāt । nṛṇāṃ bhavetsūtakadarśanena yatsarvatīrtheṣu kṛtābhiṣekāt ।। vidhāya rasaliṅgaṃ yo bhaktiyuktaḥ samarcayet । jagattritayaliṅgānāṃ pūjāphalamavāpnuyāt ।।
bhakṣaṇaṃ sparśanaṃ dānaṃ dhyānaṃ ca paripūjanam । pañcadhā rasapūjoktā mahāpātakanāśinī ।। hanti bhakṣaṇamātreṇa pūrvajanmāghasambhavam । rogasaṃghamaśeṣāṇāṃ narāṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
pūrvajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ sadyo naśyati dehinām । sugandhapiṣṭasūtena yadi śambhurvilepitaḥ ।। abhrakaṃ truṭimātraṃ yo rasasya parijārayet । śatakratuphalaṃ tasya bhavedityabravīcchivaḥ ।।
yaśca nindati sūtendraṃ śambhostejaḥ parātparam । sa patennarake ghore yāvatkalpavikalpanā ।। rogibhyo yo rasaṃ datte śuddhipākasamanvitam । tulādānāśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti śāśvatam ।।
siddhe rase kariṣyāmi nirdāridryagadaṃ jagat । rasadhyānamidaṃ proktaṃ brahmahatyādipāpanut ।। abhragrāso hi sūtasya naivedyaṃ parikīrtitam । rasasyetyarcanaṃ kṛtvā prāpnuyātkratujaṃ phalam ।।
udare saṃsthite sūte yasyotkrāmati jīvitam । sa mukto duṣkṛtādghorātprayāti paramaṃ padam ।। mūrchitvā harati rujaṃ bandhanamanubhūya muktido bhavati । amarīkaroti hi mṛtaḥ ko anyaḥ karuṇākaraḥ sūtāt ।।
suragurugodvijahiṃsāpāpakalāpodbhavaṃ kilāsādhyam । śvitraṃ tadapi ca śamayati yastasmātkaḥ pavitrataraḥ sūtāt ।। rasabandha eva dhanyaḥ prārambhe yasya satatamitikaraṇā । setsyati rase kariṣye mahīmahaṃ nirjarāmaraṇām ।।
sukṛtaphalaṃ tāvadidaṃ sukule yajjanma dhīśca tatrāpi । sāpi ca sakalamahītalatulanaphalā bhūtalaṃ ca suvidheyam ।। bhūtalavidheyatāyāḥ phalamarthāste ca vividhabhogaphalāḥ । bhogāśca santi śarīre tadanityamato vṛthā sakalam ।।
iti dhanaśarīrabhogānmatvānityānsadaiva yatanīyam । muktau sā ca jñānāt taccābhyāsāt sa ca sthire dehe ।। tatsthairye na samarthaṃ rasāyanaṃ kimapi mūlalohādi । svayamasthirasvabhāvaṃ dāhyaṃ kledyaṃ ca śoṣyaṃ ca ।।
kāṣṭhauṣadhyo nāge nāgo vaṅge atha vaṅgamapi śulbe । śulbaṃ tāre tāraṃ kanake kanakaṃ ca līyate sūte ।। amṛtatvaṃ hi bhajante haramūrtau yogino yathā līnāḥ । tadvatkavalitagagane rasarāje hemalohādyāḥ ।।
paramātmanīva satataṃ bhavati layo yatra sarvasattvānām । eko asau rasarājaḥ śarīramajarāmaraṃ kurute ।। sthiradehe abhyāsavaśāt prāpya jñānaṃ guṇāṣṭakopetam । prāpnoti brahmapadaṃ na punarbhavavāsajanmaduḥkhāni ।।
ekāṃśena jagadyugapadavaṣṭabhyāvasthitaṃ paraṃ jyotiḥ । pādaistribhistadamṛtaṃ sulabhaṃ na viraktimātreṇa ।। na hi dehena kathaṃcidvyādhijarāmaraṇaduḥkhavidhureṇa । kṣaṇabhaṅgureṇa sūkṣmaṃ tadbrahmopāsituṃ śakyam ।।
nāmāpi dehasiddhe ko gṛhṇīyādvinā śarīreṇa । yadyogagamyamamalaṃ manaso api na gocaraṃ tattvam ।। yajñāddānāttapaso vedādhyayanāddamātsadācārāt । atyantabhūyasī kila yogavaśādātmasaṃvittiḥ ।।
bhrūyugamadhyagataṃ yacchikhividyutsūryavajjagadbhāsi । keṣāṃcitpuṇyadṛśāmunmīlati cinmayaṃ paraṃ jyotiḥ ।। paramānandaikarasaṃ paramaṃ jyotiḥsvabhāvamavikalpam । vigalitasakalakleśaṃ jñeyaṃ śāntaṃ svasaṃvedyam ।।
tasminnādhāya manaḥ sphuradakhilaṃ cinmayaṃ jagatpaśyan । utsannakarmabandho brahmatvamihaiva cāpnoti ।। rāgadveṣavimuktāḥ satyācārā mṛṣārahitāḥ । sarvatra nirviśeṣā bhavanti cidbrahmasaṃsparśāt ।।
tiṣṭhantyaṇimādiyutā vilasaddehāḥ sadoditānandāḥ । brahmasvabhāvamamṛtaṃ samprāptāś caiva kṛtakṛtyāḥ ।। āyatanaṃ vidyānāṃ mūlaṃ dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇām । śreyaḥ paraṃ kimanyaccharīramajarāmaraṃ vihāyaikam ।।
pratyakṣeṇa pramāṇena yo na jānāti sūtakam । adṛṣṭavigrahaṃ devaṃ kathaṃ jñāsyati cinmayam ।। yajjarayā jarjaritaṃ kāsaśvāsādiduḥkhavivaśaṃ ca । yogyaṃ tanna samādhau pratihatabuddhīndriyaprasaram ।।
bālaḥ ṣoḍaśavarṣo viṣayarasāsvādalampaṭaḥ parataḥ । yātaviveko vṛddho martyaḥ kathamāpnuyānmuktim ।। asminn eva śarīre yeṣāṃ paramātmano na saṃvedaḥ । dehatyāgādūrdhvaṃ teṣāṃ tadbrahma dūrataram ।।
brahmādayo yatante tasmindivyāṃ tanuṃ samāśritya । jīvanmuktāścānye kalpāntasthāyino munayaḥ ।। tasmājjīvanmuktiṃ samīhamānena yoginā prathamam । divyā tanurvidheyā haragaurīsṛṣṭisaṃyogāt ।।
śaile asmiñ śivayoḥ prītyā parasparajigīṣayā । sampravṛtte ca sambhoge trilokīkṣobhakāriṇi ।। vinivārayituṃ vahniḥ sambhogaṃ preṣitaḥ suraiḥ । kāṅkṣamāṇais tayoḥ putraṃ tārakāsuramārakam ।।
kapotarūpiṇaṃ prāptaṃ himavatkandare analam । apakṣibhāvasaṃkṣubdhaṃ smaralīlāvilokinam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā lajjitaḥ śambhurvirataḥ suratāttadā । pracyutaścaramo dhāturgṛhītaḥ śūlapāṇinā ।।
prakṣipto vadane vahnergaṅgāyāmapi so apatat । bahiḥ kṣiptastayā so api paridahyamānayā ।। saṃjātāstanmalādhānāddhātavaḥ siddhihetavaḥ । yāvadagnimukhādreto nyapatadbhūrisārataḥ ।।
śatayojananimnāṃstānkṛtvā kūpāṃstu pañca ca । tadāprabhṛti kūpasthaṃ tadretaḥ pañcadhābhavat ।। raso rasendraḥ sūtaśca pārado miśrakastathā । iti pañcavidho jātaḥ kṣetrabhedena śambhujaḥ ।।
raso rakto vinirmuktaḥ sarvadoṣai rasāyanaḥ । saṃjātāstridaśāstena nīrujā nirjarāmarāḥ ।। rasendro doṣanirmuktaḥ śyāvo rūkṣo aticañcalaḥ । rasāyino abhavaṃstena nāgā mṛtyujarojjhitāḥ ।।
devairnāgaiś ca tau kūpau pūritau mṛdbhir aśmabhiḥ । tadāprabhṛti lokānāṃ tau jātāv atidurlabhau ।। īṣatpītaśca rūkṣāṅgo doṣayuktaśca sūtakaḥ । daśāṣṭasaṃskṛtaiḥ siddho dehaṃ lohaṃ karoti saḥ ।।
athānyakūpajaḥ ko api sa calaḥ śvetavarṇavān । pārado vividhairyogaiḥ sarvarogaharaḥ sa hi ।। mayūracandrikāchāyaḥ sa raso miśrako mataḥ । so apyaṣṭādaśasaṃskārayuktaścātīva siddhidaḥ ।।
trayaḥ sūtādayaḥ sūtāḥ sarvasiddhikarā api । nijakarmavinirmāṇaiḥ śaktimanto atimātrayā ।। etāṃ rasasamutpattiṃ yo jānāti sa dhārmikaḥ । āyur ārogyasaṃtānaṃ rasasiddhiṃ ca vindati ।।
rasanātsarvadhātūnāṃ rasa ityabhidhīyate । jarāruṅmṛtyunāśāya rasyate vā raso mataḥ ।। rasoparasarājatvādrasendra iti kīrtitaḥ । dehalohamayīṃ siddhiṃ sūte sūtastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
rogapaṅkābdhimagnānāṃ pāradānāc ca pāradaḥ । sarvadhātugataṃ tejomiśritaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati ।। tasmātsa miśrakaḥ prokto nānārūpaphalapradaḥ । evaṃbhūtasya sūtasya martyamṛtyugadacchidaḥ ।
prabhāvān mānuṣā jātā devatulyabalāyuṣaḥ ।। tān dṛṣṭvābhyarthito rudraḥ śakreṇa tadanantaram । doṣaiśca kañcukābhiśca rasarājo niyojitaḥ ।। tadāprabhṛti sūto asau naiva sidhyatyasaṃskṛtaḥ ।
jalago jalarūpeṇa tvarito haṃsago bhavet ।। malago malarūpeṇa sadhūmo dhūmago bhavet । anyā jīvagatirdaivī jīvo aṇḍādiva niṣkramet ।। sa tāṃś ca jīvayejjīvāṃstena jīvo rasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
rasasya pañcavidhagatimāha jalaga iti ।। jalarūpeṇa dravatvena jalagaḥ jalena saha gamanaśīlaḥ bhavet rasasya cūrṇaprāyo atisūkṣmāṃśa iti bhāvaḥ tvaritaḥ cañcalaḥ cāñcalyādityarthaḥ haṃsagaḥ haṃsavad gamanaśīlaḥ bhavet malarūpeṇa malavattvāt malagaḥ malena saha miśritaḥ doṣasaṃśliṣṭaḥ bhavet sadhūmaḥ vahnidṛṣṭatvāt dhūmagaḥ dhūmena saha gamanaśīlaḥ uḍḍayanasvabhāvaḥ bhavet anyā aparā pañcamītyarthaḥ daivī adṛśyarūpā jīvasya rasasya gatiḥ gamanam astīti śeṣaḥ tayā gatyā aṇḍāt deharūpakośāt jīvaḥ ātmā iva niṣkramet rasa iti bhāvaḥ kena pathā dehāt jīvo nirgacchati tat yathā na dṛśyate tathā pāradasya pañcamī gatirapi na jñātum śakyate ityarthaḥ ।। pūrvaśloke jīvagatiśabdena rasagatiriti pradarśitaṃ jīvaśabdasya rasārthatve hetumāha sa iti ।। saḥ rasaḥ tān jīvān jīvayet jarāmaraṇādivināśanadvārā dīrghajīvanaṃ pradāpayet tena hetunā rasaḥ jīvaḥ jīvayatīti vyutpattyā jīvanadāyakaḥ smṛtaḥ kathitaḥ ।।
catasro gatayo dṛśyā adṛśyā pañcamī gatiḥ ।। mantradhyānādinā tasya rudhyate pañcamī gatiḥ ।। saṃprati pañcabhūtātmakasya tasya gatibhedena nāmabhedamāha jalaga iti ।। yaḥ pārado jalarūpeṇa jalasvabhāvena gacchati sa jalago jalagativiśiṣṭa ityucyate ।।
tanmayāstu suvarṇādilohāḥ ।। sthirasattvā rasādayo'pi tanmayāḥ ।। bhūmimalakiṭṭayogenaiva teṣāṃ ghanatvaṃ sthiratvaṃ ca ।। ata eva drutirūpeṇaiva teṣāṃ sthitiḥ sambhavati ।।
jalasvabhāvo'dhogamanarūpaḥ ।। nirmaladrutirūpalohānām apyadhogamanaṃ dṛśyata eva ।। yaḥ pāradastvaritastvarayā vegena yukto nātyucchritam ākāśe gacchati kiṃtu bhūmisaṃnihitākāśe bhuvi ca sa haṃsaga ityucyate ।। haṃsa ivākāśe gacchatīti haṃsagaḥ ।।
sa tu mayūragaṇḍūpadādiṣu vyavasthitaḥ ।। yastu malarūpeṇa kṛṣṇavarṇenāṃśena viśiṣṭo gacchati sa malaga ityucyate ।। yaśca sadhūmo dhūmena dhūmasamānavarṇordhvarekhāsahitākāśagatyā saha vartata iti sadhūmaḥ sa dhūmaga ityucyate ।। sa tu haritālahiṅgulamanaḥśilārasakagaurīpāṣāṇādiṣu vyavasthitaḥ ।।
te hi dhūmarodhāt sphoṭaṃ kṛtvodgacchantītyanubhūyate ।। nābhiyantrabhūdharalohamūṣādiyantrādinā nirdhūmajāraṇāyāmapi mahatā prayatnenāpi teṣāṃ sthiratvaṃ mīmāṃsyaṃ bhavati bhavennanveti ।। anyā caturthī gatiḥ pāradasyāsti ।। sā tu jīvagatirityucyate ।।
jīvasyevādṛśyā gatirjīvagatiḥ ।। ata eva sā daivītyapyucyate ।। tasyā devagaterivādṛśyatvāttayā yuktaḥ sa pārado'ṇḍājjīva ivādṛśyagatyā yuktaḥ svasthānānniṣkramennirgacchati ।। aṇḍāddehasya nirgamanaṃ dṛśyate dehasahitasya jīvasya tu bahirnirgamanaṃ na dṛśyate ।।
bālasya cālanaśvāsocchvāsādikriyayā cānumīyate tadvad asyāpīti bhāvaḥ ।। tayā gatyā yukta evāyaṃ jīvānprāṇino jīvayettena sa raso jīvanāmnā smṛtaḥ ।। kārayettaṃ saṃskāranipuṇavaidyahastena rājā tatsamo vasumānvātmanaḥ prajānāṃ ca rakṣaṇārtham iti bhāvaḥ ।। iti bhinnagatitvācca sūtarājyasya durlabhaḥ ।
saṃskārastasya bhiṣajā nipuṇena tu rakṣayet ।। prathame rajasi snātāṃ hayārūḍhāṃ svalaṃkṛtām । vīkṣamāṇāṃ vadhūṃ dṛṣṭvā jighṛkṣuḥ kūpago rasaḥ ।। udgacchati javātsāpi taṃ dṛṣṭvā yāti vegataḥ ।
anugacchati tāṃ sūtaḥ sīmānaṃ yojanonmitam ।। pratyāyāti tataḥ kūpaṃ vegataḥ śivasambhavaḥ । mārganirmitagarteṣu sthitaṃ gṛhṇanti pāradam । patito darade deśe gauravādvahnivaktrataḥ ।।
sa raso bhūtale līnas tattaddeśanivāsinaḥ । tāṃ mṛdaṃ pātanayantre kṣiptvā sūtaṃ haranti ca ।। abhravaikrāntamākṣīkavimalādrijasasyakam । capalo rasakaśceti jñātvāṣṭau saṃgrahed rasān ।।
devyā rajo bhavedgandho dhātuḥ śukraṃ tathābhrakam iti kṣepakaḥ । gaurītejaḥ paramamamṛtaṃ vātapittakṣayaghnam prajñābodhi praśamitarujaṃ vṛṣyamāyuṣyamagryam । balyaṃ snigdhaṃ rucidam akaphaṃ dīpanaṃ śītavīryaṃ tattadyogaiḥ sakalagadahṛd vyoma sūtendrabandhi ।। rājahastād adhastād yatsamānītaṃ ghanaṃ khaneḥ ।
bhavettaduktaphaladaṃ niḥsattvaṃ niṣphalaṃ param ।। tadevābhrakaṃ bhūmimadhye rājahastāt sapādahastād adhastād adhobhāgasthaṃ yat khanijaṃ ghanam abhrakaṃ vajrākhyaṃ tad eva pūrvoktaguṇam ।। itaraṃ tu vāyujalamūtramalatāpakṛmisaṃbandhānniḥsāraṃ jñeyam ।। idam upalakṣaṇaṃ sarveṣāṃ khanijadravyāṇām ।।
prāyasteṣāṃ hi bhūmigarbhasthānām eva pūrṇātmaguṇatvāt ।। atra ghanaśabdo abhrakamātravācako'pi vajrābhrake paryavasyati ।। tasyaiva yathoktaguṇatvāt ।। pinākaṃ nāgamaṇḍūkaṃ vajramityabhrakaṃ matam ।
śvetādivarṇabhedena pratyekaṃ taccaturvidham ।। pinākaṃ pāvakottaptaṃ vimuñcati daloccayam । tatsevitaṃ malaṃ baddhvā mārayatyeva mānavam ।। nāgābhraṃ nāgavatkuryāddhvaniṃ pāvakasaṃsthitam ।
tadbhuktaṃ kurute kuṣṭhaṃ maṇḍalākhyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। utplutyotplutya maṇḍūkaṃ dhmātaṃ patati cābhrakam । tatkuryādaśmarīrogamasādhyaṃ śastrato anyathā ।। vajrābhraṃ vahnisaṃtaptaṃ nirmuktāśeṣavaikṛtam ।
dehalohakaraṃ tacca sarvarogaharaṃ param ।। śvetaṃ raktaṃ ca pītaṃ ca kṛṣṇamevaṃ caturvidham । śvetaṃ śvetakriyāsūktaṃ raktābhaṃ raktakarmaṇi । pītābhamabhrakaṃ yattu śreṣṭhaṃ tatpītakarmaṇi ।।
caturvidhaṃ varaṃ vyoma yadyapyuktaṃ rasāyane । tathāpi kṛṣṇavarṇābhraṃ koṭikoṭiguṇādhikam ।। snigdhaṃ pṛthudalaṃ varṇasaṃyuktaṃ bhārato adhikam । sukhanirmocyapattraṃ ca tadabhraṃ śastamīritam ।।
sacandrikaṃ ca kiṭṭābhaṃ vyoma na grāsayedrasaḥ । grasitaśca niyojyo asau lohe caiva rasāyane ।। grāsābhāve hyupoṣita iva rasaḥ kāryakaro na bhavedityāha sacandrikamiti ।। sacandrikaṃ cākacikyasahitam ।।
kiṭṭābhaṃ prabhūtakiṭṭam ।। grasitaśca grasitābhrasattva eva lohe svarṇādyutpādane lohamāraṇe rogavāraṇārthaṃ lohaprayoge ca niyojyaḥ ।। tathā rasāyane jvarāṅkuśādi tattadrase rasāyane ca lakṣmīvilāsavajrapañjarādirūpe vakṣyamāṇa ityarthaḥ ।। rasa īyate prāpyate'neneti vyutpattyātra rasaśabdena rasarasāyanayoḥ saṃgrahāt ।।
niścandrikaṃ mṛtaṃ vyoma sevyaṃ sarvagadeṣu ca । sevitaṃ candrasaṃyuktaṃ mehaṃ mandānalaṃ caret ।। yair uktaṃ yuktinirmuktaiḥ pattrābhrakarasāyanam । tair dṛṣṭaṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ viṣaṃ jīvanahetave ।।
sattvārthaṃ sevanārthaṃ ca yojayecchodhitābhrakam । anyathā tv aguṇaṃ kṛtvā vikarotyeva niścitam ।। prataptaṃ saptavārāṇi nikṣiptaṃ kāñjike abhrakam । nirdoṣaṃ jāyate nūnaṃ prakṣiptaṃ vāpi gojale ।।
triphalākvathite cāpi gavāṃ dugdhe viśeṣataḥ । tato dhānyābhrakaṃ kṛtvā piṣṭvā matsyākṣikārasaiḥ ।। matsyākṣikā hilamocikā gaṇḍadūrvā vā ।। cakrīṃ kṛtvā viśoṣyātha puṭed ardhebhake puṭe ।
tatastadabhrakaṃ dhānyābhrakaṃ kṛtvā matsyākṣikārasenaikadinaparyantaṃ saṃmardya cakrīṃ vartulasthūlavaṭikāṃ vidhāyāvaśoṣya śarāvasaṃpuṭitaṃ kṛtvārdhe'bhrake puṭe puṭed ardhe'bhrake puṭam ardhagajapuṭaṃ tacca gajapuṭagatārdhabhāgaṃ vanopalaiḥ pūrayitvā bhavati ।। puṭet paced ityarthaḥ ।। pratipuṭam abhrakasya mardanaṃ tataścakrīṃ kṛtvā viśoṣya śarāvasaṃpuṭitaṃ kāryam ।। puṭedevaṃ hi ṣaḍvāraṃ paunarnavarasaiḥ saha ।।
kalāṃśaṭaṅkaṇenāpi saṃmardya kṛtacakrikam । ardhebhākhyapuṭais tadvat saptavāraṃ puṭet khalu ।। evaṃ vāsārasenāpi taṇḍulīyarasena ca । prapuṭet saptavārāṇi pūrvaproktavidhānataḥ ।
evaṃ siddhaṃ ghanaṃ sarvayogeṣu viniyojayet ।। cūrṇābhraṃ śālisaṃyuktaṃ vastrabaddhaṃ hi kāñjike । niryātaṃ mardanādvastrāddhānyābhramiti kathyate ।। dhānyābhravidhimāha cūrṇābhramiti ।।
cūrṇābhra abhracūrṇaṃ śālisaṃyuktam adyāpyatra śāliparimāṇaṃ noktaṃ tathāpi tantrāntarānusaraṇāt pādamitaśālidhānyasahitaṃ boddhavyaṃ tathā ca rasendrasārasaṃgrahe । pādāṃśaṃ śālisaṃyuktamabhrakaṃ kambalodare । trirātraṃ sthāpayennīre tat klinnaṃ mardayeddṛḍham । kambalādgalitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vālukārahitaṃ yat ।
taddhānyābhramiti proktamabhramāraṇasiddhaye । iti ।। niryātaṃ nirgatam ।। abhraṃ cūrṇitaṃ kṛtvā pādāṃśaśālidhānyena saha sthūlavastre baddhvā kāñjike tāvanmardanīyaṃ yāvad vastracchidrāt ślakṣṇaṃ vālukārahitaṃ sat niryāti taddhānyābhraṃ smṛtam ।।
dhānyābhraṃ kāsamardasya rasena parimarditam । puṭitaṃ daśavāreṇa mriyate nātra saṃśayaḥ । tadvanmustārasenāpi taṇḍulīyarasena ca ।। pītāmalakasaubhāgyapiṣṭaṃ cakrīkṛtābhrakam ।
puṭitaṃ ṣaṣṭivārāṇi sindūrābhaṃ prajāyate । kṣayādyakhilarogaghnaṃ bhavedrogānupānataḥ ।। vaṭamūlatvacaḥ kvāthais tāmbūlīpattrasārataḥ । vāsāmatsyākṣikābhyāṃ vā mīnākṣyā sakaṭhillayā ।।
payasā vaṭavṛkṣasya marditaṃ puṭitaṃ ghanam । bhavedviṃśativāreṇa sindūrasadṛśaprabham ।। pādāṃśaṭaṅkaṇopetaṃ musalīrasamarditam । rundhyātkoṣṭhyāṃ dṛḍhaṃ dhmātaṃ sattvarūpaṃ bhaved ghanam ।।
kāsamardaghanādhānyavāsānāṃ ca punarbhuvaḥ । matsyākṣyāḥ kāṇḍavallyāśca haṃsapādyā rasaiḥ pṛthak ।। piṣṭvā piṣṭvā prayatnena śoṣayed gharmayogataḥ । palaṃ godhūmacūrṇasya kṣudramatsyāśca ṭaṅkaṇam ।।
pratyekamaṣṭamāṃśena dattvā dattvā vimardayet । mardane mardane samyakśoṣayedraviraśmibhiḥ ।। pañcājaṃ pañcagavyaṃ vā pañcamāhiṣameva ca । kṣiptvā golānprakurvīta kiṃcittindukato adhikān ।।
payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ mūtraṃ saviṭkaṃ cājam ucyate । adhaḥpātanakoṣṭhyāṃ hi dhmātvā sattvaṃ nipātayet ।। koṣṭhyāṃ kiṭṭaṃ samāhṛtya vicūrṇya ravakān haret । koṣṭhyām avaśiṣṭasattvaṃ kācakiṭṭasaṃśliṣṭaṃ kaṇarūpaṃ durgrāhyaṃ tattu agnau śānte sati samāhṛtyaikīkṛtya bahir niṣkāsya saṃkuṭya vicūrṇya tatsaṃśliṣṭaṃ kaṇasattvaṃ haret ।।
kiṭṭāt pṛthakkṛtya gṛhṇīyāt ।। tatkiṭṭaṃ svalpaṭaṅkena gomayena vimardya ca ।। golānvidhāya saṃśoṣya gharme bhūyo api pūrvavat । bhūyaḥ kiṭṭaṃ samāhṛtya mṛditvā sattvamāharet ।।
atha sattvakaṇāṃstāṃstu kvāthayitvāmlakāñjikaiḥ । śodhanīyagaṇopetaṃ mūṣāmadhye nirudhya ca ।। samyagdrutaṃ samāhṛtya dvivāraṃ pradhamed ghanam । iti śuddhaṃ bhavetsattvaṃ yojyaṃ rasarasāyane ।।
madhutailavasājyeṣu drāvitaṃ parivāpitam । parivāpitaṃ prakṣiptam ।। mṛdu syāddaśavāreṇa sattvaṃ lohādikaṃ kharam ।। paṭṭacūrṇaṃ vidhāyātha goghṛtena pariplutam ।
bharjayetsaptavārāṇi cullīsaṃsthitakharpare ।। agnivarṇaṃ bhavedyāvadvāraṃ vāraṃ vicūrṇayet । tṛṇaṃ kṣiptvā dahedyāvattāvadvā bharjanaṃ caret ।। tataḥ sagandhakaṃ piṣṭvā vaṭamūlakaṣāyataḥ ।
puṭedviṃśativāreṇa vārāheṇa puṭena hi ।। punarviṃśativārāṇi triphalotthakaṣāyataḥ । triphalāmuṇḍikābhṛṅgapatrapathyākṣamūlakaiḥ ।। bhāvayitvā prayoktavyaṃ sarvarogeṣu mātrayā ।
sattvābhrātkiṃcidaparaṃ nirvikāraṃ guṇādhikam ।। evaṃ cecchatavārāṇi puṭapākena sādhitam । guṇavajjāyate atyarthaṃ paraṃ pācanadīpanam ।। gandharvapattratoyena guḍena saha bhāvitam ।
adhordhvaṃ vaṭapatrāṇi niścandraṃ tripuṭaiḥ khagam ।। kṣudhaṃ karoti cātyarthaṃ guñjārdhamitisevayā । tattadrogaharairyogaiḥ sarvarogaharaṃ param ।। sattvasya golakaṃ dhmātaṃ sasyasaṃyuktakāñjike ।
nirvāpya tatkṣaṇenaiva kuṭṭayellohapārayā ।। lohapārayā lohamusalena ।। sampratāpya ghanasthūlakaṇān kṣiptvātha kāñjike । tatkṣaṇena samāhṛtya kuṭṭayitvā rajaścaret ।।
goghṛtena ca taccūrṇaṃ bharjayet pūrvavat tridhā । dhātrīphalarasaistadvaddhātrīpatrarasena vā ।। bharjane bharjane kāryaṃ śilāpaṭṭena peṣaṇam । tataḥ punarnavāvāsārasaiḥ kāñjikamiśritaiḥ ।।
prapuṭeddaśavārāṇi daśavārāṇi gandhakaiḥ । evaṃ saṃśodhitaṃ vyomasattvaṃ sarvaguṇottaram । yatheṣṭaṃ viniyoktavyaṃ jāraṇe ca rasāyane ।। drutayo naiva nirdiṣṭāḥ śāstre dṛṣṭā api dṛḍham ।
vinā śaṃbhoḥ prasādena na sidhyanti kadācana ।। vallaḥ dviguñjā guñjātrayam iti līlāvatī sārdhaguñjeti rājanighaṇṭuḥ ।। vellavyoṣasamanvitaṃ ghṛtayutaṃ vallonmitaṃ sevitaṃ divyābhraṃ kṣayapāṇḍuruggrahaṇikāśūlāmakuṣṭhāmayam । jūrtiṃ śvāsagadaṃ pramehamaruciṃ kāsāmayaṃ durdharaṃ mandāgniṃ jaṭharavyathāṃ vijayate yogairaśeṣāmayān ।।
aṣṭāsraś cāṣṭaphalakaḥ ṣaṭkoṇo masṛṇo guruḥ । śuddhamiśritavarṇaiśca yukto vaikrānta ucyate ।। śveto raktaśca pītaśca nīlaḥ pārāpatacchaviḥ । śyāmalaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇaśca karburaścāṣṭadhā hi saḥ ।।
āyuḥpradaśca balavarṇakaro ativṛṣyaḥ prajñāpradaḥ sakaladoṣagadāpahārī । dīptāgnikṛt pavisamānaguṇastarasvī vaikrāntakaḥ khalu vapurbalalohakārī ।। rasāyaneṣu sarveṣu pūrvagaṇyaḥ pratāpavān । vajrasthāne niyoktavyo vaikrāntaḥ sarvadoṣahā ।।
daityendro māhiṣaḥ siddhaḥ sahadevasamudbhavaḥ । durgā bhagavatī devī taṃ śūlena vyamardayat ।। tasya raktaṃ tu patitaṃ yatra yatra sthitaṃ bhuvi । tatra tatra tu vaikrāntaṃ vajrākāraṃ mahārasam ।।
vindhyasya dakṣiṇe vāsti hy uttare vāsti sarvataḥ । vikṛntayati lohāni tena vaikrāntakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। śvetaḥ pītastathā rakto nīlaḥ pārāvataprabhaḥ । mayūrakaṇṭhasadṛśaścānyo marakataprabhaḥ ।।
dehasiddhikaraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ pīte pītaṃ site sitam । sarvārthasiddhidaṃ raktaṃ tathā marakataprabham । śeṣe dve niṣphale varjye vaikrāntamiti saptadhā ।। yatra kṣetre sthitaṃ caiva vaikrāntaṃ tatra bhairavam ।
vināyakaṃ ca sampūjya gṛhṇīyācchuddhamānasaḥ ।। vaikrānto vajrasadṛśo dehalohakaro mataḥ । viṣaghno rasarājaśca jvarakuṣṭhakṣayapraṇut ।। vaikrāntakāḥ syustridinaṃ viśuddhāḥ saṃsveditāḥ kṣārapaṭūni dattvā ।
amleṣu mūtreṣu kulattharambhānīre athavā kodravavāripakvāḥ ।। kulatthakvāthasaṃsvinno vaikrāntaḥ pariśudhyati । mriyate aṣṭapuṭair gandhanimbukadravasaṃyutaḥ ।। vaikrānteṣu ca tapteṣu hayamūtraṃ vinikṣipet ।
paunaḥpunyena vā kuryāddravaṃ dattvā puṭaṃ tvanu । bhasmībhūtaṃ tu vaikrāntaṃ vajrasthāne niyojayet ।। mocamoraṭapālāśakṣāragomūtrabhāvitam । vajrakandaniśākalkaphalacūrṇasamanvitam ।।
tatkalkaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ lākṣācūrṇaṃ vaikrāntasaṃbhavam । navasārasamāyuktaṃ meṣaśṛṅgīdravānvitaṃ ।। piṇḍitaṃ mūkamūṣasthaṃ dhmāpitaṃ ca haṭhāgninā । tatraiva patate sattvaṃ vaikrāntasya na saṃśayaḥ ।।
sattvapātanayogena marditaśca vaṭīkṛtaḥ । mūṣāstho ghaṭikādhmāto vaikrāntaḥ sattvamutsṛjet ।। bhasmatvaṃ samupāgato vikṛtako hemnā mṛtenānvitaḥ pādāṃśena kaṇājyavellasahito guñjāmitaḥ sevitaḥ । yakṣmāṇaṃ jaraṇaṃ ca pāṇḍugudajaṃ śvāsaṃ ca kāsāmayaṃ duṣṭāṃ ca grahaṇīm uraḥkṣatamukhān rogāñjayed dehakṛt ।।
sūtabhasmārdhasaṃyuktaṃ nīlavaikrāntabhasmakaṃ । mṛtābhrasattvamubhayostulitaṃ parimarditam ।। kṣaudrājyasaṃyutaṃ prātarguñjāmātraṃ niṣevitam । nihanti sakalānrogāndurjayānanyabheṣajaiḥ ।
triḥsaptadivasair nṝṇāṃ gaṅgāmbha iva pātakam ।। suvarṇaśailaprabhavo viṣṇunā kāñcano rasaḥ । tāpyāṃ kirātacīneṣu yavaneṣu ca nirmitaḥ । tāpyaḥ sūryāṃśusaṃtapto mādhave māsi dṛśyate ।।
madhuraḥ kāñcanābhāsaḥ sāmlo rajatasaṃnibhaḥ । kiṃcitkaṣāyamadhuraḥ śītaḥ pāke kaṭurlaghuḥ । tatsevanājjarāvyādhiviṣairna paribhūyate ।। mākṣiko dvividho hemamākṣikastāramākṣikaḥ ।
tatrādyaṃ mākṣikaṃ kānyakubjotthaṃ svarṇasaṃnibham ।। tapatītīrasambhūtaṃ pañcavarṇasuvarṇavat । pāṣāṇabahalaḥ proktastārākhyo alpaguṇātmakaḥ ।। mākṣīkadhātuḥ sakalāmayaghnaḥ prāṇo rasendrasya paraṃ hi vṛṣyaḥ ।
durmelalohadvayamelanaś ca guṇottaraḥ sarvarasāyanāgryaḥ ।। eraṇḍatailaluṅgāmbusiddhaṃ śudhyati mākṣikam । siddhaṃ vā kadalīkandatoyena ghaṭikādvayam । taptaṃ kṣiptaṃ varākvāthe śuddhimāyāti mākṣikam ।।
mātuluṅgāmbugandhābhyāṃ piṣṭaṃ mūṣodare sthitam । pañcakroḍapuṭair dagdhaṃ mriyate mākṣikaṃ khalu ।। eraṇḍasnehagavyājair mātuluṅgarasena vā । kharparasthaṃ dṛḍhaṃ pakvaṃ jāyate dhātusaṃnibham ।
evaṃ mṛtaṃ rase yojyaṃ rasāyanavidhāv api ।। triṃśāṃśanāgasaṃyuktaṃ kṣārair amlaiśca vartitam । dhmātaṃ prakaṭamūṣāyāṃ sattvaṃ muñcati mākṣikam ।। saptavāraṃ paridrāvya kṣiptaṃ nirguṇḍikārase ।
mākṣīkasattvasaṃmiśraṃ nāgaṃ naśyati niścitam ।। kṣaudragandharvatailābhyāṃ gomūtreṇa ghṛtena ca । kadalīkandasāreṇa bhāvitaṃ mākṣikaṃ muhuḥ । mūṣāyāṃ muñcati dhmātaṃ sattvaṃ śulbanibhaṃ mṛdu ।।
guñjābījasamacchāyaṃ drutadrāvaṃ ca śītalam । tāpyasattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ taddehalohakaraṃ param ।। mākṣīkasattvena rasendrapiṣṭaṃ kṛtvā vilīne ca baliṃ nidhāya । saṃmiśrya saṃmardya ca khalvamadhye nikṣipya sattvaṃ drutimabhrakasya ।।
vidhāya golaṃ lavaṇākhyayantre paceddinārdhaṃ mṛduvahninā ca । svataḥ suśītaṃ paricūrṇya samyagvallonmitaṃ vyoṣaviḍaṅgayuktam ।। saṃsevitaṃ kṣaudrayutaṃ nihanti jarāṃ sarogāṃ tvapamṛtyumeva । duḥsādhyarogānapi saptavāsarairnaitena tulyo asti sudhāraso api ।।
eraṇḍotthena tailena guñjākṣaudraṃ ca ṭaṅkaṇam । marditaṃ tasya vāpena sattvaṃ mākṣīkajaṃ dravet ।। vimalastrividhaḥ prokto hemādyastārapūrvakaḥ । tṛtīyaḥ kāṃsyavimalastattatkāntyā sa lakṣyate ।।
vimalasya bhedamāha vimala iti ।। vimalaḥ mākṣikaviśeṣaḥ ।। tattatkāntyā hemādīnāṃ prabhayā ।। paryāyamuktāvalīkṛtā vimalaśabdena raupyamākṣikaṃ gṛhītam ।।
vartulaḥ koṇasaṃyuktaḥ snigdhaśca phalakānvitaḥ । marutpittaharo vṛṣyo vimalo atirasāyanaḥ ।। pūrvo hemakriyāsūkto dvitīyo rūpyakṛnmataḥ । tṛtīyo bheṣaje teṣu pūrvapūrvo guṇottaraḥ ।।
āṭarūṣajale svinno vimalo vimalo bhavet । jambīrasvarase svinno meṣaśṛṅgīrase athavā । āyāti śuddhiṃ vimalo dhātavaśca yathā pare ।। gandhāśmalakucāmlaiśca mriyate daśabhiḥ puṭaiḥ ।।
saṭaṅkalakucadrāvairmeṣaśṛṅgyāśca bhasmanā । piṣṭo mūṣodare liptaḥ saṃśoṣya ca nirudhya ca ।। ṣaṭprasthakokilairdhmāto vimalaḥ sīsasaṃnibhaḥ । sattvaṃ muñcati tadyukto rasaḥ syātsa rasāyanaḥ ।।
vimalaṃ śigrutoyena kāṅkṣīkāsīsaṭaṅkaṇam । kāṅkṣī saurāṣṭramṛttikā ।। vajrakandasamāyuktaṃ bhāvitaṃ kadalīrasaiḥ ।। mokṣakakṣārasaṃyuktaṃ dhmāpitaṃ mūkamūṣagam ।
sattvaṃ candrārkasaṃkāśaṃ patate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। tatsattvaṃ sūtasaṃyuktaṃ piṣṭaṃ kṛtvā sumarditam । vilīne gandhake kṣiptvā jārayettriguṇālakaṃ ।। śilāṃ pañcaguṇāṃ cāpi vālukāyantrake khalu ।
tārabhasmadaśāṃśena tāvadvaikrāntakaṃ mṛtaṃ ।। sarvamekatra saṃcūrṇya paṭena parigālya ca । nikṣipya kūpikāmadhye paripūrya prayatnataḥ ।। līḍho vyoṣavarānvito vimalako yukto ghṛtaiḥ sevito hanyāddurbhagakṛjjvarāñśvayathukaṃ pāṇḍupramehārucīḥ ।
mūlārtiṃ grahaṇīṃ ca śūlamatulaṃ yakṣmāmayaṃ kāmalāṃ sarvānpittamarudgadānkimaparairyogairaśeṣāmayān ।। śilādhātur dvidhā prokto gomūtrādyo rasāyanaḥ । karpūrapūrvakaścānyastatrādyo dvividhaḥ punaḥ । sasattvaścaiva niḥsattvastayoḥ pūrvo guṇādhikaḥ ।।
grīṣme tīvrārkataptebhyaḥ pādebhyo himabhūbhṛtaḥ । svarṇarūpyārkagarbhebhyaḥ śilādhāturviniḥsaret ।। svarṇagarbhagirerjāto japāpuṣpanibho guruḥ । sasvalpatiktaḥ susvāduḥ paramaṃ tadrasāyanam ।।
tatrādau svarṇādibhya utpattibhedena trividhasya gomūtragandhinaḥ tasya lakṣaṇādikamāha svarṇeti ।। tantrāntare tu utpattibhedena bhinnasya tasya cāturvidhyamuktaṃ yathā carake । nātyuṣṇaśītaṃ dhātubhyaścaturbhyastasya saṃbhavaḥ । hemno'tha rajatāttāmrāt varaṃ kālāyasādapi ।।
iti ।। atra tu āyasaṃ noktaṃ tallakṣaṇamapi tatraiva draṣṭavyaṃ yathā । yattu guggulusaṃkāśaṃ tiktakaṃ lavaṇānvitam । vipāke kaṭu śītaṃ ca sarvaśreṣṭhaṃ tadāyasaṃ ।।
gomūtragandhi sarveṣāṃ sarvakarmasu yaugikam । rasāyanaprayogeṣu paścimaṃ tu viśiṣyate ।। iti ।। atra haimaśilājatuno paramarasāyanatvenoktatvād āyasasyāpi mukhyataḥ rasāyanaguṇatvena ekakāryakatvād āyasaṃ pṛthaṅnoktamiti mantavyam ।।
rūpyagarbhagirerjātaṃ madhuraṃ pāṇḍuraṃ guru । śilājaṃ pittarogaghnaṃ viśeṣātpāṇḍurogahṛt ।। tāmragarbhaṃ girerjātaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ ghanaṃ guru । śilājaṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ tiktoṣṇaṃ kṣayarogahṛt ।।
vahnau kṣiptaṃ bhavedyattalliṅgākāramadhūmakam । salile atha vilīnaṃ ca tacchuddhaṃ hi śilājatu ।। nūnaṃ sajvarapāṇḍuśophaśamanaṃ mehāgnimāndyāpahaṃ medaśchedakaraṃ ca yakṣmaśamanaṃ śūlāmayonmūlanam । gulmaplīhavināśanaṃ jaṭharahṛcchūlaghnamāmāpahaṃ sarvatvaggadanāśanaṃ kimaparaṃ dehe ca lohe hitam ।।
rasoparasasūtendraratnaloheṣu ye guṇāḥ । vasanti te śilādhātau jarāmṛtyujigīṣayā ।। kṣārāmlagojalair dhautaṃ śudhyatyeva śilājatu ।। śilādhātuṃ ca dugdhena triphalāmārkavadravaiḥ ।
lohapātre vinikṣipya śodhayedatiyatnataḥ ।। kṣārāmlaguggulopetaiḥ svedanīyantramadhyagaiḥ । sveditaṃ ghaṭikāmānācchilādhātu viśudhyati ।। śilayā gandhatālābhyāṃ mātuluṅgarasena ca ।
puṭitaṃ hi śilādhātu mriyate aṣṭagiriṇḍakaiḥ ।। bhasmībhūtaśilodbhavaṃ samatulaṃ kāntaṃ ca vaikrāntakaṃ yuktaṃ ca triphalākaṭutrikaghṛtairvallena tulyaṃ bhajet । pāṇḍau yakṣmagade tathāgnisadane meheṣu mūlāmaye gulmaplīhamahodare bahuvidhe śūle ca yonyāmaye ।। seveta yadi ṣaṇmāsaṃ rasāyanavidhānataḥ ।
valīpalitanirmukto jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sukhī ।। piṣṭaṃ drāvaṇavargeṇa sāmlena girisaṃbhavam । kṣiptvā mūṣodare ruddhvā gāḍhairdhmātaṃ hi kokilaiḥ । sattvaṃ muñcecchilādhātuḥ śvasanairlohasaṃnibham ।।
pāṇḍuraṃ sikatākāraṃ karpūrādyaṃ śilājatu । mūtrakṛcchrāśmarīmehakāmalāpāṇḍunāśanam ।। elātoyena saṃbhinnaṃ siddhaṃ śuddhimupaiti tat । naitasya māraṇaṃ sattvapātanaṃ vihitaṃ budhaiḥ ।।
pītvā hālāhalaṃ vāntaṃ pītāmṛtagarutmatā । viṣeṇāmṛtayuktena girau marakatāhvaye । tadvāntaṃ hi ghanībhūtaṃ saṃjātaṃ sasyakaṃ khalu ।। mayūrakaṇṭhasacchāyaṃ bhārāḍhyamatiśasyate ।।
dravyaṃ viṣayutaṃ yattaddravyādhikaguṇaṃ bhavet । hālāhalaṃ sudhāyuktaṃ sudhādhikaguṇaṃ tathā ।। niḥśeṣadoṣaviṣahṛdgadaśūlamūlakuṣṭhāmlapaittikavibandhaharaṃ paraṃ ca । rasāyanaṃ vamanarekakaraṃ garaghnaṃ śvitrāpahaṃ gaditamatra mayūratuttham ।।
sasyakaṃ śuddhimāpnoti raktavargeṇa bhāvitam ।। snehavargeṇa saṃsiktaṃ saptavāramadūṣitam । dolāyantreṇa susvinnaṃ sasyakaṃ praharatrayam । gomahiṣyājamūtreṣu śudhyate pañcakharparam ।।
lakucadrāvagandhāśmaṭaṅkaṇena samanvitam । nirudhya mūṣikāmadhye mriyate kaukkuṭaiḥ puṭaiḥ ।। sasyakasya tu cūrṇaṃ tu pādasaubhāgyasaṃyutam । karañjatailamadhyasthaṃ dinamekaṃ nidhāpayet ।।
andhamūṣāsyamadhyasthaṃ dhmāpayetkokilatrayam । indragopākṛti caiva sattvaṃ bhavati śobhanam ।। nimbudravālpaṭaṅkābhyāṃ mūṣāmadhye nirudhya ca । tāmrarūpaṃ paridhmātaṃ sattvaṃ muñcati sasyakam ।।
śuddhaṃ sasyaṃ śilākrāntaṃ pūrvabheṣajasaṃyutam । nānāvidhānayogena sattvaṃ muñcati niścitam ।। sattvametatsamādāya kharabhūnāgasattvabhuk । tanmudrikā kṛtasparśā śūlaghnī tatkṣaṇād bhavet ।।
carācaraṃ viṣaṃ bhūtaḍākinīdṛggataṃ jayet । mudrikeyaṃ vidhātavyā dṛṣṭapratyayakārikā ।। rāmavat somasenānīr mudrite api tathākṣaram । himālayottare pārśve aśvakarṇo mahādrumaḥ ।
tatra śūlaṃ samutpannaṃ tatraiva vilayaṃ gatam ।। mantreṇānena mudrāmbho nipītaṃ saptamantritam । sadyaḥ śūlaharaṃ proktamiti bhālukibhāṣitam ।। anayā mudrayā taptaṃ tailamagnau suniścitam ।
lepitaṃ hanti vegena śūlaṃ yatra kvacidbhavet । sadyaḥ sūtikaraṃ nāryāḥ sadyo netrarujāpaham ।। capalaḥ yaśadaḥ dasteti loke ।। gauraḥ śveto aruṇaḥ kṛṣṇaścapalastu caturvidhaḥ ।
hemābhaścaiva tārābho viśeṣādrasabandhanaḥ ।। śeṣau tu madhyau lākṣāvacchīghradrāvau tu niṣphalau । athoddeśakramānurodhena tutthavarṇanāntaraṃ capalaṃ varṇayati gaura iti ।। ayaṃ padārtho vyāvahārikanāmnāsmin deśe loke na prasiddhaḥ ।।
pāṣāṇaviśeṣo'yaṃ jasadakhanisaṃnihitabhūgarbha upalabhyata ityanumīyate ।। āṅglabhāṣāyāṃ reḍiyam iti nāmnopalabdhaḥ padārtho ayam eveti kecit ।। kṛtrimastu paribhāṣādhyāye vakṣyamāṇaḥ ।। vaṅgavaddravate vahnau capalastena kīrtitaḥ ।।
capalo lekhanaḥ snigdho dehalohakaro mataḥ । rasarājasahāyaḥ syāttiktoṣṇamadhuro mataḥ ।। capalaḥ sphaṭikacchāyaḥ ṣaḍasrī snigdhako guruḥ । tridoṣaghno ativṛṣyaśca rasabandhavidhāyakaḥ ।।
mahāraseṣu kaiściddhi capalaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। jambīrakarkoṭakaśṛṅgaverair vibhāvanābhiścapalasya śuddhiḥ ।। śailaṃ tu cūrṇayitvā tu dhānyāmlopaviṣair viṣaiḥ । piṇḍaṃ baddhvā tu vidhivatpātayeccapalaṃ tathā ।।
rasako dvividhaḥ prokto durduraḥ kāravellakaḥ । sadalo durduraḥ prokto nirdalaḥ kāravellakaḥ ।। rasakasya dvaividhyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ cāha rasaka iti ।। rasakaḥ kharparītutthakaviśeṣaḥ yad uktaṃ bhāvaprakāśe ।
kharparītutthakaṃ tutthād anyat tad rasakaṃ smṛtam । ye guṇāstutthake proktāste guṇāḥ rasake smṛtāḥ ।। iti ।। sadalaḥ sapattraḥ vaṃśapattraharitālavad iti bhāvaḥ ।।
athoddeśakramaprāptaṃ rasakaṃ varṇayati rasaka iti ।। rasako jasadopādānakhanijamṛttikā ।। tatsattvaṃ jasadatulyam evotpadyate ।। sattvapāte śubhaḥ pūrvo dvitīyaścauṣadhādiṣu ।
rasakaḥ sarvamehaghnaḥ kaphapittavināśanaḥ । netrarogakṣayaghnaśca lohapāradarañjanaḥ ।। nāgārjunena saṃdiṣṭau rasaśca rasakāvubhau । śreṣṭhau siddharasau khyātau dehalohakarau param ।।
rasaśca rasakaścobhau yenāgnisahanau kṛtau । dehalohamayī siddhirdāsī tasya na saṃśayaḥ ।। kaṭukālābuniryāsa āloḍya rasakaṃ pacet । śuddhaṃ doṣavinirmuktaṃ pītavarṇaṃ tu jāyate ।।
kharparaḥ parisaṃtaptaḥ saptavāraṃ nimajjitaḥ । bījapūrarasasyāntarnirmalatvaṃ samaśnute ।। nṛmūtre vāśvamūtre vā takre vā kāñjike athavā । pratāpya majjitaṃ samyakkharparaṃ pariśudhyati ।।
naramūtre sthito māsaṃ rasako rañjayeddhruvam । śuddhatāmraṃ rasaṃ tāraṃ śuddhasvarṇaprabhaṃ yathā ।। haridrātriphalārālāsindhudhūmaiḥ saṭaṅkaṇaiḥ । sāruṣkaraiśca pādāṃśaiḥ sāmlaiḥ saṃmardya kharparam ।।
liptaṃ vṛntākamūṣāyāṃ śoṣayitvā nirudhya ca । mūṣāmukhopari nyasya kharparaṃ pradhamettataḥ ।। kharpare prahṛte jvālā bhavennīlā sitā yadi । tadā saṃdaṃśato mūṣāṃ dhṛtvā kṛtvā tvadhomukhīm ।।
śanairāsphālayedbhūmau yathā nālaṃ na bhajyate । vaṅgābhaṃ patitaṃ sattvaṃ samādāya niyojayet । evaṃ tricaturairvāraiḥ sarvaṃ sattvaṃ viniḥsaret ।। sābhayājatubhūnāganiśādhūmajaṭaṅkaṇam ।
mūkamūṣāgataṃ dhmātaṃ śuddhaṃ sattvaṃ vimuñcati ।। lākṣāguḍāsurīpathyāharidrāsarjaṭaṅkaṇaiḥ । samyaksaṃcūrṇya tatpakvaṃ godugdhena ghṛtena ca ।। vṛntākamūṣikāmadhye nirudhya guṭikākṛtim ।
dhmātvā dhmātvā samākṛṣya ḍhālayitvā śilātale । sattvaṃ vaṅgākṛtiṃ grāhyaṃ rasakasya manoharam ।। yadvā jalayutāṃ sthālīṃ nikhanetkoṣṭhikodare । sacchidraṃ tanmukhe mallaṃ tanmukhe adhomukhīṃ kṣipet ।।
mūṣopari śikhitrāṃśca prakṣipya pradhameddṛḍham । patitaṃ sthālikānīre sattvamādāya yojayet ।। tatsattvaṃ tālakopetaṃ prakṣipya khalu kharpare । kharpare mṛtkaṭāhe ityarthaḥ ।।
mardayellohadaṇḍena bhasmībhavati niścitam ।। tadbhasma mṛtakāntena samena saha yojayet । aṣṭaguñjāmitaṃ cūrṇaṃ triphalākvāthasaṃyutam ।। kāntapātrasthitaṃ rātrau tilajaprativāpakam ।
niṣevitaṃ nihantyāśu madhumehamapi dhruvam ।। pittaṃ kṣayaṃ ca pāṇḍuṃ ca śvayathuṃ gulmameva ca । raktagulmaṃ ca nārīṇāṃ pradaraṃ somarogakam ।। yonirogānaśeṣāṃśca viṣamāṃśca jvarānapi ।
rajaḥśūlaṃ ca nārīṇāṃ kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ ca hidhmikām ।। gandhāśmagairikāsīsakāṅkṣītālaśilāñjanam । kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ cetyuparasāścāṣṭau pāradakarmaṇi ।। pārvatyuvāca ।
gandhakasya tu māhātmyaṃ tadguhyaṃ vada me prabho ।। īśvara uvāca । śvetadvīpe purā devi sarvaratnavibhūṣite । sarvakāmamaye ramye tīre kṣīrapayonidheḥ ।।
vidyādharādimukhyābhiraṅganābhiśca yoginām । siddhāṅganābhiḥ śreṣṭhābhistathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।। devāṅganābhī ramyābhiḥ krīḍitābhirmanoharaiḥ । gītairnṛtyairvicitraiśca vādyairnānāvidhaistathā ।।
evaṃ saṃkrīḍamānāyāḥ prābhavat prasṛtaṃ rajaḥ । tadrajo atīva suśroṇi sugandhi sumanoharam ।। rajasaścātibāhulyādvāsaste raktatāṃ yayau । tatra tyaktvā tu tadvastraṃ susnātā kṣīrasāgare ।।
vṛtā devāṅganābhistvaṃ kailāsaṃ punarāgatā । ūrmibhistadrajovastraṃ nītaṃ madhye payonidheḥ ।। evaṃ te śoṇitaṃ bhadre praviṣṭaṃ kṣīrasāgare । kṣīrābdhimathane caitadamṛtena sahotthitam ।।
nijagandhena tānsarvānharṣayansarvadānavān । tato devagaṇairuktaṃ gandhakākhyo bhavatvayam ।। rasasya bandhanārthāya jāraṇāya bhavatvayam । ye guṇāḥ pārade proktāste caivātra bhavantviti ।।
iti devagaṇaiḥ prītaiḥ purā proktaṃ sureśvari । tenāyaṃ gandhako nāma vikhyātaḥ kṣitimaṇḍale ।। sa cāpi trividho devi śukacañcunibho varaḥ । madhyamaḥ pītavarṇaḥ syācchuklavarṇo adhamaḥ priye ।।
caturdhā gandhako jñeyo varṇaiḥ śvetādibhiḥ khalu । śveto atra khaṭikāprokto lepane lohamāraṇe ।। khaṭhikā khaḍu cās iti nāmnā loke prasiddhā ।। tathā cāmalasāraḥ syādyo bhavetpītavarṇavān ।
śukapicchaḥ sa eva syācchreṣṭho rasarasāyane ।। raktaśca śukatuṇḍākhyo dhātuvādavidhau varaḥ । durlabhaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇaśca sa jarāmṛtyunāśanaḥ ।। gandhāśmātirasāyanaḥ sumadhuraḥ pāke kaṭūṣṇo mataḥ kaṇḍūkuṣṭhavisarpadadrudalano dīptānalaḥ pācanaḥ ।
āmonmocanaśoṣaṇo viṣaharaḥ sūtendravīryaprado gaurīpuṣpabhavastathā kṛmiharaḥ satyātmakaḥ sūtajit ।। balinā sevitaḥ pūrvaṃ prabhūtabalahetave ।। vāsukiṃ karṣatastasya tanmukhajvālayā drutā । vasā gandhakagandhāḍhyā sarvato niḥsṛtā tanoḥ ।।
gandhakatvaṃ ca samprāptā gandho abhūtsaviṣaḥ smṛtaḥ । tasmād balivasetyukto gandhako atimanoharaḥ ।। payaḥsvinno ghaṭīmātraṃ vāridhauto hi gandhakaḥ । gavyājyavidruto vastrādgālitaḥ śuddhimṛcchati ।।
evaṃ saṃśodhitaḥ so ayaṃ pāṣāṇān ambare tyajet । ghṛte viṣaṃ tuṣākāraṃ svayaṃ piṇḍatvameva ca ।। iti śuddho hi gandhāśmā nāpathyairvikṛtiṃ vrajet । apathyādanyathā hanyātpītaṃ hālāhalaṃ yathā ।।
gandhako drāvito bhṛṅgarase kṣipto viśudhyati । tadrasaiḥ saptadhā bhinno gandhakaḥ pariśudhyati ।। sthālyāṃ dugdhaṃ vinikṣipya mukhe vastraṃ nibadhya ca । gandhakaṃ tatra nikṣipya cūrṇitaṃ sikatākṛti ।।
chādayetpṛthudīrgheṇa kharpareṇaiva gandhakam । jvālayetkharparasyordhvaṃ vanachāṇais tathopalaiḥ ।। dugdhe nipatito gandho galitaḥ pariśudhyati । śatavāraṃ kṛtaṃ caiva nirgandho jāyate dhruvam ।।
matāntaramāha sthālyāmiti ।। jvālayedityatra vahnimiti śeṣaḥ ।। vanacchāṇaiḥ vanopalaiḥ ।। upalaiḥ gṛhajātaśuṣkagomayapiṇḍaiḥ ।।
itthaṃ viśuddhastriphalājyabhṛṅgamadhvanvitaḥ śāṇamito hi līḍhaḥ । gṛdhrākṣitulyaṃ kurute akṣiyugmaṃ karoti rogojjhitadīrghamāyuḥ ।। kalāṃśavyoṣasaṃyuktaṃ gandhakaṃ ślakṣṇacūrṇitam । aratnimātre vastre tad viprakīrya viveṣṭya tat ।।
sūtreṇa veṣṭayitvātha yāmaṃ taile nimajjayet । dhṛtvā saṃdaṃśato vartimadhyaṃ prajvālayecca tam । druto nipatito gandho binduśaḥ kācabhājane ।। tāṃ drutiṃ prakṣipet pattre nāgavallyās tribindukām ।
vallena pramitaṃ svacchaṃ sūtendraṃ ca vimardayet ।। aṅgulyātha sapattrāṃ tāṃ drutiṃ sūtaṃ ca bhakṣayet । karoti dīpanaṃ tīvraṃ kṣayaṃ pāṇḍuṃ ca nāśayet ।। kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ ca śūlārtigrahaṇīm atidurdharām ।
āmaṃ vināśayatyāśu laghutvaṃ prakaroti ca ।। ghṛtākte lohapātre tu vidrutaṃ śuddhagandhakam । ghṛtāktadarvikākṣiptaṃ dviniṣkapramitaṃ bhajet । hanti kṣayamukhān rogān kuṣṭharogaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
kṣārāmlatailasauvīravidāhi dvidalaṃ tathā । śuddhagandhakasevāyāṃ tyajedyogayutena hi ।। gandhakastulyamaricaḥ ṣaḍguṇatriphalānvitaḥ । ghṛṣṭaḥ śamyākamūlena pītaścākhilakuṣṭhahā ।।
tanmūlaṃ salile piṣṭaṃ lepayetpratyaham tanau । dṛṣṭapratyayayogo ayaṃ sarvatra prativīryavān । śrīmatā somadevena samyagatra prakīrtitaḥ ।। dviniṣkapramitaṃ gandhaṃ piṣṭvā tailena saṃyutam ।
athāpāmārgatoyena satailamaricena hi ।। vilipya sakalaṃ dehaṃ tiṣṭhedgharme tataḥ param । takrabhaktaṃ ca bhuñjīta tṛtīye prahare khalu ।। bhajedrātrau tathā vahniṃ samutthāya tathā prage ।
mahiṣīchagaṇam liptvā snāyācchītena vāriṇā ।। tato abhyajya ghṛtairdehaṃ snāyādiṣṭoṣṇavāriṇā । amunā kramayogena vinaśyatyativegataḥ । durjayā bahukālīnā pāmā kaṇḍuḥ suniścitam ।।
gandhakasya prayogāṇāṃ śataṃ tanna prakīrtitam । granthavistārabhītena somadevena bhūbhujā ।। athavārkasnuhīkṣīrair vastraṃ lepyaṃ tu saptadhā । gandhakaṃ navanītena piṣṭvā vastraṃ lipedghanam ।।
tadvartiṃ jvalitāṃ daṃśe dhṛtāṃ kuryād adhomukhīm । tailaṃ patedadhobhāṇḍe grāhyaṃ yogeṣu yojayet ।। śuddhagandho haredrogānkuṣṭhamṛtyujarādikān । agnikārī mahānuṣṇo vīryavṛddhiṃ karoti ca ।।
pāṣāṇagairikaṃ caikaṃ dvitīyaṃ svarṇagairikam ।। pāṣāṇagairikaṃ proktaṃ kaṭhinam tāmravarṇakam । atyantaśoṇitaṃ snigdhaṃ masṛṇaṃ svarṇagairikam ।। svādu snigdhaṃ himaṃ netryaṃ kaṣāyaṃ raktapittanut ।
hidhmāvamiviṣaghnaṃ ca raktaghnaṃ svarṇagairikam । pāṣāṇagairikaṃ cānyatpūrvasmādalpakaṃ guṇaiḥ ।। gairikaṃ tu gavāṃ dugdhairbhāvitaṃ śuddhim ṛcchati ।। gairikaṃ sattvarūpaṃ hi nandinā parikīrtitam ।।
kair apyuktaṃ patetsattvaṃ kṣārāmlaklinnagairikāt । upatiṣṭhati sūtendramekatvaṃ guṇavattaram ।। kāsīsaṃ vālukādyekaṃ puṣpapūrvam athāparam ।। kṣārāmlāgarudhūmābhaṃ soṣṇavīryaṃ viṣāpaham ।
vālukāpuṣpakāsīsaṃ śvitraghnaṃ keśarañjanam ।। puṣpādikāsīsamatipraśastaṃ soṣṇaṃ kaṣāyāmlam atīva netryam । viṣānilaśleṣmagadavraṇaghnaṃ śvitrakṣayaghnaṃ kacarañjanaṃ ca ।। sakṛdbhṛṅgāmbunā klinnaṃ kāsīsaṃ nirmalaṃ bhavet ।।
tuvarīsattvavatsattvametasyāpi samāharet ।। kāsīsaṃ śuddhimāpnoti pittaiśca rajasā striyāḥ ।। balinā hatakāsīsaṃ krāntaṃ kāsīsamāritam । ubhayaṃ samabhāgaṃ hi triphalāvellasaṃyutam ।।
viṣamāṃśaghṛtakṣaudraplutaṃ śāṇamitaṃ prage । sevitaṃ hanti vegena śvitraṃ pāṇḍukṣayāmayam ।। gulmaplīhagadaṃ śūlaṃ mūlarogaṃ viśeṣataḥ । rasāyanavidhānena sevitaṃ vatsarāvadhi ।।
āmasaṃśoṣaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mandāgniparidīpanam । palitaṃ valibhiḥ sārdhaṃ vināśayati niścitam ।। saurāṣṭrāśmani sambhūtā sā tuvarī matā । vastreṣu lipyate yāsau mañjiṣṭhārāgabandhinī ।।
phaṭakī phullikā ceti dvitīyā parikīrtitā ।। īṣatpītā guruḥ snigdhā pītikā viṣanāśanī । vraṇakuṣṭhaharā sarvakuṣṭhaghnī ca viśeṣataḥ ।। nirbhārā śubhravarṇā ca snigdhā sāmlāparā matā ।
sā phullatuvarī proktā lepāttāmraṃ caredayaḥ ।। tadbhedāvāha sphaṭikī pītiketi ।। sphaṭikīlepācchatavāraṃ tāmrapatraṃ lohapatraṃ prati vā liptā satī tatpaścāt caret pāradena prayojyakartrā cārayed bhakṣitāṃ kārayed ityarthaḥ ।। yato jāraṇāyām asyā viḍadravyatvenopayogāt ।।
antarbhāvitaṇyartho atra caradhātuḥ ।। lepād iti ।। phullatuvarīlepena tāmraṃ lauhāṃśam ujhati tāmre yaḥ lauhāṃśaḥ vidyate sa nirgacchatītyarthaḥ tāmraṃ lauhavat kāṭhinyaṃ gacchatītyartho vā ।। kāṅkṣī kaṣāyā kaṭukāmlakaṇṭhyā keśyā vraṇaghnī viṣanāśanī ca ।
śvitrāpahā netrahitā tridoṣaśāntipradā pāradajāraṇī ca ।। tuvarī kāñjike kṣiptvā tridinācchuddhimṛcchati ।। kṣārāmlair marditā dhmātā sattvaṃ muñcati niścitam ।। gopittena śataṃ vārān saurāṣṭrāṃ bhāvayettataḥ ।
dhamitvā pātayetsattvaṃ krāmaṇaṃ cātiguhyakam ।। haritālaṃ dvidhā proktaṃ pattrādyaṃ piṇḍasaṃjñakam ।। svarṇavarṇaṃ guru snigdhaṃ tanupattraṃ ca bhāsuram । tat pattratālakaṃ proktaṃ bahupattraṃ rasāyanam ।।
niṣpattraṃ piṇḍasadṛśam svalpasattvaṃ tathāguru । strīpuṣpaharaṇaṃ tattu guṇālpaṃ piṇḍatālakam ।। śleṣmaraktaviṣavātabhūtanutkevalaṃ ca khalu puṣpahṛtstriyaḥ । snigdhamuṣṇakaṭukaṃ ca dīpanaṃ kuṣṭhahāri haritālamucyate ।।
snigdhaṃ kūṣmāṇḍatoye vā tilakṣārajale api vā । toye vā cūrṇasaṃyukte dolāyantreṇa śudhyati ।। aśuddhaṃ tālamāyughnaṃ kaphamārutamehakṛt । tāpasphoṭāṅgasaṃkocaṃ kurute tena śodhayet ।।
tālakaṃ kaṇaśaḥ kṛtvā daśāṃśena ca ṭaṅkaṇam । jambīrotthadravaiḥ kṣālyaṃ kāñjikaiḥ kṣālayettataḥ ।। vastre caturguṇe baddhvā dolāyantre dinaṃ pacet । sacūrṇenāranālena dinaṃ kūṣmāṇḍaje rase ।
svedyaṃ vā śālmalītoyaistālakaṃ śuddhimāpnuyāt ।। madhutulye ghanībhūte kaṣāye brahmamūlaje । trivāraṃ tālakaṃ bhāvyaṃ piṣṭvā mūtre atha māhiṣe ।। upalairdaśabhirdeyaṃ puṭaṃ ruddhvātha peṣayet ।
evaṃ dvādaśadhā pācyaṃ śuddhaṃ yogeṣu yojayet ।। kulitthakvāthasaubhāgyamahiṣyājyamadhuplutam । sthālyāṃ kṣiptvā vidadhyācca tv amlena chidrayoginā ।। samyaṅnirudhya śikhinaṃ jvālayetkramavardhitam ।
ekapraharamātraṃ hi randhramācchādya gomayaiḥ ।। yāmānte chidramudghāṭya dṛṣṭe dhūme ca pāṇḍure । śītāṃ sthālīṃ samuttārya sattvamutkṛṣya cāharet ।। sarvapāṣāṇasattvānāṃ prakārāḥ santi koṭiśaḥ ।
granthavistārabhītyāto likhitā na mayā khalu ।। palālakaṃ raverdugdhairdinamekaṃ vimardayet । kṣiptvā ṣoḍaśikātaile miśrayitvā tataḥ pacet ।। anāvṛtapradeśe ca saptayāmāvadhi dhruvam ।
svāṅgaśītamadhasthaṃ ca sattvaṃ śvetaṃ samāharet ।। chāgalasyātha bālasya balinā ca samanvitam । tālakaṃ divasadvaṃdvaṃ mardayitvātiyatnataḥ ।। yuktaṃ drāvaṇavargeṇa kācakupyāṃ vinikṣipet ।
tridhā tāṃ ca mṛdā liptvā pariśoṣya kharātape ।। tataḥ kharparakacchidre tāmardhāṃ caiva kūpikām । praveśya jvālayedagniṃ dvādaśapraharāvadhi । kūpikaṇṭhasthitaṃ śītaṃ śuddhaṃ sattvaṃ samāharet ।।
palārdhapramitaṃ tālaṃ baddhvā vastre site dṛḍhe । balinālipya yatnena trivāraṃ pariśoṣya ca ।। drāvite triphale tāmre kṣipettālakapoṭalīm । bhasmanā chādayecchīghraṃ tāmreṇāveṣṭitaṃ sitam ।
mṛdulaṃ sattvamādadyātproktaṃ rasarasāyane ।। manaḥśilā tridhā proktā śyāmāṅgī kaṇavīrakā । khaṇḍākhyā ceti tadrūpaṃ vivicya parikathyate ।। śyāmā raktā sagaurā ca bhārāḍhyā śyāmikā matā ।
tejasvinī ca nirgaurā tāmrābhā kaṇavīrakā ।। cūrṇībhūtātiraktāṅgī sabhārā khaṇḍapūrvikā । uttaroktaguṇaiḥ śreṣṭhā bhūrisattvā prakīrtitā ।। manaḥśilā sarvarasāyanāgryā tiktā kaṭūṣṇā kaphavātahantrī ।
sattvātmikā bhūtaviṣāgnimāndyakaṇḍūtikāsakṣayahāriṇī ca ।। aśmarīṃ mūtrakṛcchraṃ ca aśuddhā kurute śilā । mandāgniṃ malabandhaṃ ca śuddhā sarvarujāpahā ।। agastyapattratoyena bhāvitā saptavārakam ।
śṛṅgaverarasair vāpi viśudhyati manaḥśilā ।। jayantībhṛṅgarājottharaktāgastyarasaiḥ śilām । dolāyantre pacedyāmaṃ yāmaṃ chāgotthamūtrakaiḥ । kṣālayedāranālena sarvarogeṣu yojayet ।।
aṣṭamāṃśena kiṭṭena guḍaguggulusarpiṣā । koṣṭhyāṃ ruddhvā dṛḍhaṃ dhmātā sattvaṃ muñcenmanaḥśilā ।। bhūnāgadhautasaubhāgyamadanaiśca vimarditaiḥ । kāravallīdalāmbhobhirmūṣāṃ kṛtvātra nikṣipet ।।
śilāṃ kṣārāmlaniṣpiṣṭāṃ pradhamettadanantaram । kokilādvayamātraṃ hi dhmānātsattvaṃ tyajatyasau ।। sauvīramañjanaṃ proktaṃ rasāñjanamataḥ param । srotoñjanaṃ tadanyacca puṣpāñjanakameva ca ।
nīlāñjanaṃ ca teṣāṃ hi svarūpamiha varṇyate ।। sauvīramañjanaṃ dhūmraṃ raktapittaharaṃ himam । viṣahidhmākṣirogaghnaṃ vraṇaśodhanaropaṇam ।। sauvīraṃ kṛṣṇavarṇasurmā iti lokabhāṣāyām ।।
rasāñjanaṃ ca pītābhaṃ viṣavaktragadāpaham । śvāsahidhmāpahaṃ varṇyaṃ vātapittāsranāśanam ।। rasāñjanamiti ।। etad rasod iti brijabhāṣāyām uttaradeśe prasiddham ।।
etad rītikiṭṭajanyaṃ dāruharidrākaṣāyājadugdhapākajanyaṃ tu rasāñjanam ityapi vadanti ।। srotoñjanaṃ himaṃ snigdhaṃ kaṣāyaṃ svādu lekhanam । netryaṃ hidhmāviṣachardikaphapittāsraroganut ।। srotoñjanamiti ।।
śvetavarṇasurmā iti loke prasiddham ।। puṣpāñjanaṃ sitaṃ snigdhaṃ himaṃ sarvākṣiroganut । atidurdharahidhmāghnaṃ viṣajvaragadāpaham ।। puṣpāñjanamiti ।।
etad rītipuṣpajanyam ।। jastaphūl iti mahārāṣṭrabhāṣāyāṃ prasiddham ।। nīlāñjanaṃ guru snigdhaṃ netryaṃ doṣatrayāpaham । rasāyanaṃ suvarṇaghnaṃ lohamārdavakārakam ।।
nīlāñjanamiti ।। nīlavarṇasurmā iti loke prasiddhaḥ ।। añjanāni viśudhyanti bhṛṅgarājanijadravaiḥ ।। manohvāsattvavat sattvam añjanānāṃ samāharet ।।
valmīkaśikharākāraṃ bhaṅge nīlotpaladyuti । ghṛṣṭaṃ tu gairikacchāyaṃ srotojaṃ lakṣayedbudhaḥ ।। valmīkaśikharākāraṃ valmīkavat unnatāvanatabahuśikharaviśiṣṭam ।। gośakṛdrasamūtreṣu ghṛtakṣaudravasāsu ca ।
bhāvitaṃ bahuśastacca śīghraṃ badhnāti sūtakam ।। sūryāvartādiyogena śuddhimeti rasāñjanam ।। rājāvartakavatsattvaṃ grāhyaṃ srotoñjanādapi ।। himavatpādaśikhare kaṅkuṣṭhamupajāyate ।
tatraikaṃ nālikākhyaṃ hi tadanyadreṇukaṃ matam ।। pītaprabhaṃ guru snigdhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhamādimam । śyāmapītaṃ laghu tyaktasattvaṃ neṣṭaṃ hi reṇukam ।। kecidvadanti kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ sadyojātasya dantinaḥ ।
varcaśca śyāmapītābhaṃ recanaṃ parikathyate ।। katicit tejivāhānāṃ nālaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhasaṃjñakam । matāntaramāha katiciditi ।। katicidvadanti kiṃ tejivāhānāṃ prabalavegasāmarthyaviśiṣṭāśvānāṃ nālaṃ sadyojātānāṃ teṣāṃ nābhinālaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhamiti ।।
vadanti śvetapītābhaṃ tadatīva virecanam ।। atha kramaprāptaṃ kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ varṇayati himavaditi ।। sa ca pītavarṇaḥ ।। ślakṣṇānekasacākacikyaphalakaviśiṣṭaḥ khanijaḥ kṣudrapāṣāṇaḥ prāṇijaśca ।।
ubhayamapi dvividhaṃ nalikā reṇukaśceti khanijabhedau ।। rase rasāyanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ niḥsattvaṃ bahuvaikṛtam ।। kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ tiktakaṭukaṃ vīryoṣṇaṃ cātirecanam । vraṇodāvartaśūlārtigulmaplīhagudārtinut ।।
sūryāvartakakadalī vandhyā kośātakī ca suradālī । śigruśca vajrakando niraṅkaṇā kākamācī ca ।। āsāmekarasena tu lavaṇakṣārāmlabhāvitaṃ bahuśaḥ । śudhyanti rasoparasā dhmātā muñcanti sattvāni ।।
kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ śuddhimāyāti tridhā śuṇṭhyambubhāvitam ।। sattvākarṣo asya na prokto yasmātsattvamayaṃ hi tat ।। bhajedenaṃ virekārthaṃ grāhibhiryavamātrayā । nāśayedāmapūrtiṃ ca virecya kṣaṇamātrataḥ ।।
bhakṣitaḥ saha tāmbūlairviricyāsūnvināśayet ।। barburīmūlikākvāthajīrasaubhāgyakaṃ samam । kaṅkuṣṭhaṃ viṣanāśāya bhūyo bhūyaḥ pibennaraḥ ।। gaurīpāṣāṇaḥ śuklapāṣāṇaḥ phulkhaḍi iti loke ।।
kampillaḥ kṣudrapāṣāṇaviśeṣaḥ kapileti nāmnā loke prasiddho gaurīpāṣāṇo dāruṇaviṣarūpo'yaṃ pāṣāṇaviśeṣaḥ somala iti mahārāṣṭrabhāṣāyāṃ prasiddhaḥ ।। kampillaścapalo gaurīpāṣāṇo navasārakaḥ । vahnijāraḥ svanāmakhyātaḥ paścimasāgarasambhūta auṣadhiviśeṣaḥ ।। agnijāro bahir arṇavojjhito viśiṣṭanakrajarāyuḥ ।।
kapardo vahnijāraśca girisindūrahiṅgulau ।। girisindūraḥ parvatapāṣāṇodare raktavarṇaḥ padārthaviśeṣaḥ ।। hiṅgulaścūrṇapāradaḥ svanāmnaiva loke prasiddhaḥ ।। mṛddāraśṛṅgaṃ sīsakasamutpannaḥ pārvatīyadhātuviśeṣaḥ ।।
moddāraśṛṅgaṃ murdāíśiṃgeti loke prasiddham ।। modāraśṛṅgam ityaṣṭau sādhāraṇarasāḥ smṛtāḥ । rasasiddhakarāḥ proktā nāgārjunapuraḥsaraiḥ ।। candrikāḍhyaḥ cākacakyaviśiṣṭaḥ sacandrābhravad ujjvalakaṇābahulaḥ ityarthaḥ ।।
iṣṭikācūrṇasaṃkāśaścandrikāḍhyo atirecanaḥ । saurāṣṭradeśe cotpannaḥ sa hi kampillakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pittavraṇādhmānavibandhanighnaḥ śleṣmodarārtikṛmigulmavairī । mūlāmaśophajvaraśūlahārī kampillako recyagadāpahārī ।।
gaurīpāṣāṇakaḥ pīto vikaṭo hatacūrṇakaḥ । sphaṭikābhaśca śaṅkhābho haridrābhas trayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। gaurīpāṣāṇasya paryāyān varṇabhedena traividhyaṃ cāha gaurīti ।। pītavikaṭahatacūrṇakāḥ iti ime trayaḥ paryāyāḥ ।।
pūrva iti ।। pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ haridrābhagaurīpāṣāṇāt śaṅkhābhaḥ śaṅkhābhapāṣāṇāt sphaṭikābhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ ।। trividhasya tasya svarūpamāha yaḥ kiṃcit pītavarṇo vikaṭakarāla āhataḥ saṃcūrṇarūpo bhavati sa gaurīpāṣāṇa ityucyate ।। ayam eva sphaṭikasamānacākacikyaviśiṣṭaḥ ।।
etad viśeṣaṇaṃ dvitīyabhedasyāpi sambhavati ।। dvitīyaḥ śaṅkhābhaḥ so'pi cākacikyaviśiṣṭaḥ ।। tṛtīyabhedāpanno yaḥ sa tu haridrābho haridrāsamānaḥ pūrṇapītavarṇaḥ ।। trividhamadhya uttarottarāt pūrvapūrvaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ ।।
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ guṇaiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kāravallīphale kṣipet । svedayeddhaṇḍikāmadhye śuddho bhavati mūṣakaḥ ।। tālavadgrāhayetsattvaṃ śuddhaṃ śubhraṃ prayojayet ।। rasabandhakaraḥ snigdho doṣaghno rasavīryakṛt ।।
karīrapīlukāṣṭheṣu pacyamāneṣu codbhavaḥ । kṣāro asau navasāraḥ syāccūlikālavaṇābhidhaḥ ।। iṣṭikādahane jātaṃ pāṇḍuraṃ lavaṇaṃ laghu । taduktaṃ navasārākhyaṃ cūlikālavaṇaṃ ca tat ।।
rasendrajāraṇaṃ lohadrāvaṇaṃ jaṭharāgnikṛt । gulmaplīhāsyaśoṣaghnaṃ bhuktamāṃsādijāraṇam । viḍākhyaṃ ca tridoṣaghnaṃ cūlikālavaṇam matam ।। pītābhā granthikā pṛṣṭhe dīrghavṛttā varāṭikā ।
rasavaidyairvinirdiṣṭā sā carācarasaṃjñikā ।। sārdhaniṣkabharā śreṣṭhā niṣkabhārā ca madhyamā । pādonaniṣkabhārā ca kaniṣṭhā parikīrtitā ।। pariṇāmādiśūlaghnī grahaṇīkṣayanāśinī ।
kaṭūṣṇā dīpanī vṛṣyā netryā vātakaphāpahā । rasendrajāraṇe proktā viḍadravyeṣu śasyate ।। tadanye tu varāṭāḥ syur guravaḥ śleṣmapittalāḥ ।। varāṭāḥ kāñjike svinnā yāmācchuddhimavāpnuyuḥ ।।
samudreṇāgninakrasya jarāyur bahirujjhitaḥ । saṃśuṣko bhānutāpena so agnijāra iti smṛtaḥ ।। agnijārastridoṣaghno dhanurvātādivātanut । vardhano rasavīryasya dīpano jāraṇastathā ।।
tad abdhikṣārasaṃśuddhaṃ tasmācchuddhirna hīṣyate ।। mahāgiriṣu cālpīyaḥpāṣāṇāntaḥsthito rasaḥ । śuṣkaśoṇaḥ sa nirdiṣṭo girisindūrasaṃjñayā ।। girisindūrasya svarūpalakṣaṇam āha maheti ।।
himālayādibṛhatparvatāntarvartikṣudrapāṣāṇadvayamadhyanisṛtaḥ raktavarṇarasaviśeṣaḥ śuṣkībhūtaḥ girisindūra iti khyātaḥ ।। atha girisindūram āha mahāgiriṣviti ।। alpīyo'tyalpaḥ ।। ayaṃ loke prāyo nopalabhyate ।।
kecittu kāmiyāṃ sindūra iti nāmnā prasiddho'yaṃ padārtho'tiraktavarṇa iti vadanti ।। loke'tiprasiddhastu nāgasaṃbhava eva ।। sa eva cātra grāhya iti rāvaṇamatam ।। sindūro nāgasaṃbhava iti tadvacanāditi ।।
tridoṣaśamanam bhedi rasabandhanamagrimam । dehalohakaraṃ netryaṃ girisindūramīritam ।। hiṅgulaḥ śukatuṇḍākhyo haṃsapākastathāparaḥ ।। prathamo alpaguṇastatra carmāraḥ sa nigadyate ।।
śvetarekhaḥ pravālābho haṃsapākaḥ sa īritaḥ ।। athoddeśakramaprāptaṃ hiṅgulaṃ varṇayati hiṅgula iti ।। ayaṃ rasaḥ pāradakhanijamṛdviśeṣaḥ ।। ata eva prathamādhyāya uktam ।
tāṃ mṛdaṃ pātanāyantre pātayanti rasaṃ tataḥ । iti ।। kṛtrimo'pi loke dṛśyate pāradagandhakanavasāgarapākajanyaḥ ।। khanijo'yaṃ dvividhaḥ ।।
tasya cottamasya lakṣaṇamāha śvetareṣa iti ।। sa ca haṃsapāka iti nāmnā kathitaḥ pākena vyavasthitaḥ ।। śvetaraktavarṇaviśiṣṭatvāt ।। ayaṃ uttamaḥ ।।
prathamastu hīnaśvetareṣo'lpaguṇaḥ ।। sa tu carmāra iti nigadyate ।। hiṅgulaḥ sarvadoṣaghno dīpano atirasāyanaḥ । sarvarogaharo vṛṣyo jāraṇāyātiśasyate ।।
etasmādāhṛtaḥ sūto jīrṇagandhasamo guṇaiḥ ।। saptakṛtvārdrakadrāvairlakucasyāmbunāpi vā । śoṣito bhāvayitvā ca nirdoṣo jāyate khalu ।। kimatra citraṃ daradaḥ subhāvitaḥ kṣīreṇa meṣyā bahuśo amlavargaiḥ ।
evaṃ suvarṇaṃ bahugharmatāpitaṃ karoti sākṣādvarakuṅkumaprabham ।। daradaḥ pātanāyantre pātitaśca jalāśraye । tatsattvaṃ sūtasaṃkāśaṃ pātayennātra saṃśayaḥ ।। sadalaṃ pītavarṇaṃ ca bhavedgurjaramaṇḍale ।
arbudasya gireḥ pārśve jātaṃ mṛddāraśṛṅgakam ।। mṛddāraśṛṅgasya lakṣaṇam utpattisthānaṃ cāha sadalamiti ।। vaṃśapattraharitālavat paṭalaviśiṣṭam ।। mṛddāraśṛṅgasya paryāyādikaṃ nighaṇṭvādau anyatra vā kutrāpi granthe na paridṛśyate paraṃ tu asmaddeśe yanmudrāśaṅkha iti nāmnā prasiddhaṃ paścimadeśe tat murdārśiṅ iti nāmnā tatratyairabhidhīyate ato manye mṛddāraśṛṅgakaṃ mudrāśaṅkha eva iti ।।
gurjaramaṇḍale gurjaradeśe ।। arbudagireḥ pārśve nāgakhanisthānabhūte ca jātam utpannaṃ yad viśiṣṭaṃ kṣudrapāṣāṇātmakaṃ dravyaṃ sadalapītavarṇātmakaṃ tanmṛddāraśṛṅganāmnā prathitaṃ bhavet ।। tadguṇānāha sīsasattvamiti ।। sīsasattvasyopādānaṃ kāraṇam ।।
sīsasattvaṃ guru śleṣmaśamanaṃ puṃgadāpaham । rasabandhanamutkṛṣṭaṃ keśarañjanamuttamam ।। sādhāraṇarasāḥ sarve mātuluṅgārdrakāmbunā । trirātraṃ bhāvitāḥ śuṣkā bhaveyurdoṣavarjitāḥ ।।
yāni kāni ca sattvāni tāni śudhyantyaśeṣataḥ । dhmātāni śuddhivargeṇa milanti ca parasparam ।। iti karavālabhairavaḥ । rājāvarto alparaktorunīlikāmiśritaprabhaḥ ।
gurutvamasṛṇaḥ śreṣṭhastadanyo madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pramehakṣayadurnāmapāṇḍuśleṣmānilāpahaḥ । dīpanaḥ pācano vṛṣyo rājāvarto rasāyanaḥ ।। nimbudravaiḥ sagomūtraiḥ sakṣāraiḥ sveditāḥ khalu ।
dvitrivāreṇa śudhyanti rājāvartādidhātavaḥ ।। śirīṣapuṣpārdrarasai rājāvartaṃ viśodhayet ।। luṅgāmbugandhakopeto rājāvarto vicūrṇitaḥ । puṭanātsaptavāreṇa rājāvarto mṛto bhavet ।।
rājāvartasya cūrṇaṃ tu kunaṭīghṛtamiśritam । vipacedāyase pātre mahiṣīkṣīrasaṃyutam ।। saubhāgyapañcagavyena piṇḍībaddhaṃ tu jārayet । dhmāpitaṃ khadirāṅgāraiḥ sattvaṃ muñcati śobhanam ।।
anena kramayogena gairikaṃ vimalaṃ bhavet । kramāt pītaṃ ca raktaṃ ca sattvaṃ patati śobhanam ।। maṇayo api ca vijñeyāḥ sūtabandhasya kārakāḥ ।। vaikrāntaḥ sūryakāntaśca hīrakaṃ mauktikaṃ maṇiḥ ।।
rājāvarto rāuṭī iti brijabhāṣāyām ।। candrakāntastathā caiva rājāvartaśca saptamaḥ । garuḍodgārakaṃ tārkṣyaṃ marakata ityaparaparyāyadvayam ।। pannā iti loke prasiddham ।।
garuḍodgārakaścaiva jñātavyā maṇayastvamī ।। puṣparāgaṃ pukhrāj iti loke prasiddham ।। mahānīlamindranīlam ।। padmarāgaṃ māṇikyam ।।
puṣparāgaṃ mahānīlaṃ padmarāgaṃ pravālakam । vaiḍūryaṃ tad yadākāśe sajalameghaśabdād aṅkuraviśiṣṭaṃ bhavati ।। ata evāsyābhraloham iti paryāyāntaram ।। etat pirojā iti loke prasiddham ।।
vaiḍūryaṃ ca tathā nīlamete ca maṇayo matāḥ । yatnataḥ saṃgrahītavyā rasabandhasya kāraṇāt ।। padmarāgendranīlākhyau tathā marakatottamaḥ । puṣparāgaḥ savajrākhyaḥ pañca ratnavarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
māṇikyamuktāphalavidrumāṇi tārkṣyaṃ ca puṣpaṃ bhiduraṃ ca nīlam । gomedakaṃ cātha vidūrakaṃ ca krameṇa ratnāni navagrahāṇām ।। grahānumaitryā kuruvindapuṣpapravālamuktāphalatārkṣyavajram । nīlākhyagomedavidūrakaṃ ca krameṇa mudrādhṛtamiṣṭasiddhyai ।।
rase rasāyane dāne dhāraṇe devatārcane । surakṣyāṇi sujātīni ratnānyuktāni siddhaye ।। māṇikyaṃ padmarāgākhyaṃ dvitīyaṃ nīlagandhi ca ।। kuśeśayadalacchāyaṃ svacchaṃ snigdhaṃ mahatsphuṭam ।
vṛttāyataṃ samaṃ gātraṃ māṇikyaṃ śreṣṭhamucyate ।। nīlaṃ gaṅgāmbusambhūtaṃ nīlagarbhāruṇacchavi । pūrvamāṇikyavacchreṣṭhamāṇikyaṃ nīlagandhi tat ।। randhrakārkaśyamālinyaraukṣyāvaiśadyasaṃyutam ।
cipiṭaṃ laghu vakraṃ ca māṇikyaṃ duṣṭamaṣṭadhā ।। māṇikyaṃ dīpanaṃ vṛṣyaṃ kaphavātakṣayārtinut । bhūtavetālapāpaghnaṃ karmajavyādhināśanam ।। hlādi śvetaṃ laghu snigdhaṃ raśmivannirmalaṃ mahat ।
khyātaṃ toyaprabhaṃ vṛttaṃ mauktikaṃ navadhā śubham ।। toyaprabhaṃ jalābhaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati tatra dūrato jalabhramotpādakam ityarthaḥ yadvā jalavat taralacchāyaṃ lāvaṇyaviśiṣṭam iti yāvat ।। muktāphalaṃ laghu himaṃ madhuraṃ ca kāntidṛṣṭyagnipuṣṭikaraṇaṃ viṣahāri bhedi । vīryapradaṃ jalanidherjanitā ca śuktirdīptā ca paktirujamāśu haredavaśyam ।।
nirjalaṃ nirjaḍaṃ ḍalayor aikyāt aśiśiramityarthaḥ uṣṇamiti yāvad yadvā vicchāyaṃ dṛśyate ca lāvaṇye jalaśabdopacāraḥ muktāphalasya taralacchāyā eva lāvaṇyaśabdabodhikā yaduktaṃ । muktāphaleṣu chāyāyāstaralatvam ivāntarā । pratibhāti yadaṅgeṣu tallāvaṇyam ihocyate ।। iti ।।
atra jalaśabdena muktāphalagatataralacchāyā bodhyā ।। rūkṣāṅgaṃ nirjalaṃ śyāvaṃ tāmrābhaṃ lavaṇopamam । vikaṭaṃ viṣamagātram ।। ardhaśubhraṃ ca vikaṭaṃ granthilaṃ mauktikaṃ tyajet ।।
kaphapittakṣayadhvaṃsi kāsaśvāsāgnimāndyanut । puṣṭidaṃ vṛṣyamāyuṣyaṃ dāhaghnaṃ mauktikaṃ matam ।। pakvabimbaphalacchāyaṃ vṛttāyatamavakrakam । snigdhamavraṇakaṃ sthūlaṃ pravālaṃ saptadhā śubham ।।
pāṇḍuraṃ śvetapītamiśravarṇam ।। dhūsaraṃ śvetakṛṣṇamiśravarṇam ।। pāṇḍuraṃ dhūsaraṃ sūkṣmaṃ savraṇaṃ kaṇḍarānvitam । kaṇḍarānvitaṃ sirāvṛtam ।।
nirbhāraṃ śulbavarṇaṃ ca pravālaṃ neṣyate aṣṭadhā ।। kṣayapittāsrakāsaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ pācanaṃ laghu । viṣabhūtādiśamanaṃ vidrumaṃ netraroganut ।। haridvarṇaṃ guru snigdhaṃ sphuradraśmicayaṃ śubham ।
masṛṇaṃ bhāsuraṃ tārkṣyaṃ gātraṃ saptaguṇaṃ matam ।। kapilaṃ karkaśaṃ nīlaṃ pāṇḍu kṛṣṇaṃ ca lāghavam । cipiṭaṃ vikaṭaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ tārkṣyaṃ na śasyate ।। jvaracchardiviṣaśvāsasaṃnipātāgnimāndyanut ।
durnāmapāṇḍuśophaghnaṃ tārkṣyamojovivardhanam ।। puṣparāgaṃ guru svacchaṃ snigdhaṃ sthūlaṃ samaṃ mṛdu । karṇikāraprasūnābhaṃ masṛṇaṃ śubhamaṣṭadhā ।। niṣprabhaṃ karkaśaṃ rūkṣaṃ pītaṃ śyāmaṃ natonnatam ।
kapiśaṃ kapilaṃ pāṇḍu puṣparāgaṃ parityajet ।। puṣparāgaṃ viṣacchardikaphavātāgnimāndyanut । dāhakuṣṭhāsraśamanaṃ dīpanaṃ pācanaṃ laghu ।। vajraṃ ca trividhaṃ proktaṃ naro nārī napuṃsakam ।
pūrvaṃ pūrvamiha śreṣṭhaṃ rasavīryavipākataḥ ।। aṣṭaphalakam aṣṭadhāram astrādīnām agrabhāgavat sūkṣmāgram ityarthaḥ ।। aṣṭāsraṃ vāṣṭaphalakaṃ ṣaṭkoṇamatibhāsuram । ambudendradhanurvāritaraṃ puṃvajramucyate ।।
tadeva cipiṭākāraṃ strīvajraṃ vartulāyatam । vartulaṃ kuṇṭhakoṇāgraṃ kiṃcidguru napuṃsakam ।। strīpuṃnapuṃsakaṃ vajraṃ yojyaṃ strīpuṃnapuṃsake । vyatyāsānnaiva phaladaṃ puṃvajreṇa vinā kvacit ।।
śvetādivarṇabhedena tadekaikaṃ caturvidham । brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdraṃ svasvavarṇaphalapradam ।। uttamottamavarṇaṃ hi nīcavarṇaphalapradam । nyāyo ayaṃ bhairaveṇoktaḥ padārtheṣvakhileṣvapi ।।
āyuḥpradaṃ jhaṭiti sadguṇadaṃ ca vṛṣyaṃ doṣatrayapraśamanam sakalāmayaghnam । sūtendrabandhavadhasadguṇakṛtpradīpanaṃ mṛtyuṃjayaṃ tadamṛtopamameva vajram ।। gauratrāsaśca binduśca rekhā ca jalagarbhatā । sarvaratneṣvamī pañca doṣāḥ sādhāraṇā matāḥ ।
atha sādhāraṇān sarvaratnadoṣān āha grāsastrāsaśceti ।। -d grāso grasitaikadeśatvam ।। -d trāsaḥ sabāhyābhyantaramalaviśiṣṭatvam ।। -d binduḥ prasiddhaḥ ।। -d
sa cānekavidhaḥ ।। -d rekhā prasiddhā ।। -d jalagarbhatā ।। -d yatrāntaḥ koṭara ivāntaḥ śuṣiraviśiṣṭajalābhāso bhavati tādṛśatvam ।। -d
kṣetratoyabhavā doṣā ratneṣu na laganti te ।। kulatthakvāthake svinnaṃ kodravakvathitena vā । ekayāmāvadhi svinnaṃ vajraṃ śudhyati niścitam ।। vajraṃ matkuṇaraktena caturvāraṃ vibhāvitam ।
sugandhimūṣikāmāṃsairvartitairmardya veṣṭayet ।। puṭetpuṭairvarāhākhyaistriṃśadvāraṃ tataḥ param । dhmātvā dhmātvā śataṃ vārānkulatthakvāthake kṣipet । anyairuktaḥ śataṃ vārānkartavyo ayaṃ vidhikramaḥ ।।
kulatthakvāthasaṃyuktalakucadravapiṣṭayā । śilayā liptamūṣāyāṃ vajraṃ kṣiptvā nirudhya ca ।। aṣṭavāraṃ puṭetsamyagviśuṣkaiśca vanotpalaiḥ । śatavāraṃ tato dhmātvā nikṣiptaṃ śuddhapārade ।
niścitaṃ mriyate vajraṃ bhasma vāritaraṃ bhavet ।। satyavāk somasenānīr etadvajrasya māraṇam । dṛṣṭapratyayasaṃyuktamuktavānrasakautukī ।। viliptaṃ matkuṇasyāsre saptavāraṃ viśoṣitam ।
kāsamardarasāpūrṇe lohapātre niveśitam ।। saptavāraṃ paridhmātaṃ vajrabhasma bhavetkhalu । brahmajyotirmunīndreṇa kramo ayaṃ parikīrtitaḥ ।। nīlajyotirlatākande ghṛṣṭaṃ gharme viśoṣitam ।
vajraṃ bhasmatvamāyāti karmavajjñānavahninā ।। madanasya phalodbhūtarasena kṣoṇināgakaiḥ । kṛtakalkena saṃlipya puṭedviṃśativārakam । vajracūrṇaṃ bhavedvaryaṃ yojayecca rasādiṣu ।।
tadvajraṃ cūrṇayitvātha kiṃciṭ ṭaṅkaṇasaṃyutam । kharabhūnāgasattvena viṃśenāvartate dhruvam । tulyasvarṇena taddhmātaṃ yojanīyaṃ rasādiṣu ।। triguṇena rasenaiva saṃmardya guṭikīkṛtam ।
mukhe dhṛtaṃ karotyāśu caladdantavibandhanam ।। triṃśadbhāgamitaṃ hi vajrabhasitaṃ svarṇaṃ kalābhāgikaṃ tāraṃ cāṣṭaguṇaṃ sitāmṛtavaraṃ rudrāṃśakaṃ cābhrakam । pādāṃśaṃ khalu tāpyakaṃ vasuguṇaṃ vaikrāntakaṃ ṣaḍguṇaṃ bhāgo apyuktarasai raso ayamuditaḥ ṣāḍguṇyasaṃsiddhaye ।। jalanīlendranīlaṃ ca śakranīlaṃ tayorvaram ।।
śvaityagarbhitanīlābhaṃ laghu tajjalanīlakam । kārṣṇyagarbhitanīlābhaṃ sabhāraṃ śakranīlakam ।। ekacchāyaṃ guru snigdhaṃ svacchaṃ piṇḍitavigraham । mṛdu madhye lasajjyotiḥ saptadhā nīlamuttamam ।।
komalaṃ vihitaṃ rūkṣaṃ nirbhāraṃ raktagandhi ca । cipiṭābhaṃ sasūkṣmaṃ ca jalanīlaṃ ca saptadhā ।। śvāsakāsaharaṃ vṛṣyaṃ tridoṣaghnaṃ sudīpanam । viṣamajvaradurnāmapāpaghnaṃ nīlamīritam ।।
gomedaḥsamarāgatvādgomedaṃ ratnamucyate ।। susvacchagojalacchāyaṃ svacchaṃ snigdhaṃ samaṃ guru । nirdalaṃ niṣpattram aśubhagomedasya sapaṭalatvād atra śubhagomedasya nirdalatvāvatāraṇam ।। nirdalaṃ masṛṇaṃ dīptaṃ gomedaṃ śubhamaṣṭadhā ।।
vicchāyaṃ laghu rūkṣāṅgaṃ cipiṭaṃ paṭalānvitam । niṣprabhaṃ pītakācābhaṃ gomedaṃ na śubhāvaham ।। gomedaṃ kaphapittaghnaṃ kṣayapāṇḍukṣayaṃkaram । dīpanaṃ pācanaṃ rucyaṃ tvacyaṃ buddhiprabodhanam ।।
vaidūryaṃ śyāmaśubhrābhaṃ samaṃ svacchaṃ guru sphuṭam । bhramacchubhrottarīyeṇa garbhitaṃ śubhamīritam ।। śyāmaṃ toyasamacchāyaṃ cipiṭaṃ laghu karkaśam । raktagarbhottarīyaṃ ca vaidūryaṃ naiva śasyate ।।
vaidūryaṃ raktapittaghnaṃ prajñāyurbalavardhanam । pittapradhānarogaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ malamocanam ।। śudhyatyamlena māṇikyaṃ jayantyā mauktikaṃ tathā । vidrumaṃ kṣāravargeṇa tārkṣyaṃ godugdhakaistathā ।।
puṣparāgaṃ ca saṃdhānaiḥ kulatthakvāthasaṃpuṭaiḥ । taṇḍulīyajalair vajraṃ nīlaṃ nīlīrasena ca । rocanābhiśca gomedaṃ vaidūryaṃ triphalājalaiḥ ।। lakucaḥ ḍahukaḥ ।।
lakucadrāvasampiṣṭaiḥ śilāgandhakatālakaiḥ । vajraṃ vinānyaratnāni mriyante aṣṭapuṭaiḥ khalu ।। rāmaṭhaṃ pañcalavaṇaṃ kṣārāṇāṃ tritayaṃ tathā । māṃsadravo amlavetaśca cūlikālavaṇaṃ tathā ।।
sthūlaṃ kumbhīphalaṃ pakvaṃ tathā jvālāmukhī śubhā । dravantī ca rudantī ca payasyā citramūlakam ।। dugdhaṃ snuhyāstathārkasya sarvaṃ saṃmardya yatnataḥ । golaṃ vidhāya tanmadhye prakṣipettadanantaram ।।
guṇavannavaratnāni jātimanti śubhāni ca । bhūrje taṃ golakaṃ kṛtvā sūtreṇāveṣṭya yatnataḥ ।। punarvastreṇa saṃveṣṭya dolāyantre nidhāya ca । sarvāmlayuktasaṃdhānaparipūrṇaghaṭodare ।।
ahorātratrayaṃ yāvat svedayet tīvravahninā । tasmādāhṛtya saṃkṣālya ratnajāṃ drutimāharet । ratnatulyaprabhā laghvī dehalohakarī śubhā ।। muktācūrṇaṃ tu saptāhaṃ vetasāmlena marditam ।
jambīrodaramadhye tu dhānyarāśau vinikṣipet । saptāhāduddhṛtaṃ caiva puṭe dhṛtvā drutirbhavet ।। vajravallyantarasthaṃ ca kṛtvā vajraṃ nirodhayet । amlabhāṇḍagataṃ svedyaṃ saptāhād dravatām vrajet ।।
śvetavarṇaṃ tu vaikrāntamamlavetasabhāvitam । saptāhānnātra saṃdehaḥ kharagharme dravatyasau ।। ketakīsvarasaṃ grāhyaṃ saindhavaṃ svarṇapuṣpikā । indragopakasaṃyuktaṃ sarvaṃ bhāṇḍe vinikṣipet ।
saptāhaṃ svedayettasminvaikrāntaṃ dravatāṃ vrajet ।। lohāṣṭake tathā vajravāpanāt svedanād drutiḥ । jāyate nātra saṃdeho yogasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।। kurute yogarājo ayaṃ ratnānāṃ drāvaṇaṃ param ।।
kusumbhatailamadhye tu saṃsthāpyā drutayaḥ pṛthak । tiṣṭhanti cirakālaṃ tu prāpte kārye niyojayet ।। sūryādigrahanigrahāpaharaṇaṃ dīrghāyurārogyadaṃ । saubhāgyodayabhāgyavaśyavibhavotsāhapradaṃ dhairyakṛt ।।
duśchāyācaladhūlisaṃgatibhavālakṣmīharaṃ sarvadā । ratnānāṃ paridhāraṇaṃ nigaditaṃ bhūtādinirnāśanam ।। śuddhaṃ lohaṃ kanakarajataṃ bhānulohāśmasāraṃ pūtīlohaṃ dvitayamuditaṃ nāgavaṃgābhidhānam । miśraṃ lohaṃ tritayamuditaṃ pittalaṃ kāṃsyavartaṃ dhātur lohe luha iti mataḥ so'pyanekārthavācī ।।
prākṛtaṃ sahajaṃ vahnisambhūtaṃ khanisaṃbhavam । raseṃdravedhasaṃjātaṃ svarṇaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam ।। āyurlakṣmīprabhādhīsmṛtikaramakhilavyādhividhvaṃsi puṇyaṃ bhūtāveśapraśāntismarabharasukhadaṃ saukhyapuṣṭiprakāśi । gāṅgeyaṃ cātha rūpyaṃ gadaharamajarākāri mehāpahāri kṣīṇānāṃ puṣṭikāri sphuṭamatikaraṇaṃ vīryavṛddhiprakāri ।।
brahmāṇḍaṃ saṃvṛtaṃ yena rajoguṇabhuvā khalu । tatprākṛtamiti proktaṃ devānāmapi durlabham ।। brahmā yenāvṛto jātaḥ suvarṇena jarāyuṇā । tanmerurūpatāṃ yātaṃ suvarṇaṃ sahajaṃ hi tat ।।
visṛṣṭamagninā śaivaṃ tejaḥ pītaṃ suduḥsaham । abhūtsarvaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ suvarṇaṃ vahnisaṃbhavam ।। etatsvarṇatrayaṃ divyaṃ varṇaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiryutam । dhāraṇādeva tatkuryāccharīramajarāmaram ।।
tatra tatra girīṇāṃ hi jātaṃ khaniṣu yadbhavet । taccaturdaśavarṇāḍhyaṃ bhakṣitaṃ sarvarogahṛt ।। tattrividhaṃ ṣoḍaśavarṇayuktam ।। te ca varṇā granthāntare viśiṣṭadravyasāmyam udāhṛtya pṛthakpradarśitāḥ ।।
śvetaḥ śvetajapāpuṣpe balakṣaḥ kadalīsume । syādarjunastu kumude vidvadbhiḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। pāṇḍuvarṇo bhavedreṇau ketakīpuṣpaje tathā । hariṇaḥ pītaśabalaśukladravye sunirdiśet ।।
dhūsaro bakule puṣpe kṛṣṇaḥ syād atasīsume । haricchirīṣaje pattre rakto raktotpale smṛtaḥ ।। kṛṣṇamiśre lohite syād aruṇaḥ śvetaraktake । pāṭalo'tho markaṭe tu kapiśaḥ kṛṣṇalohite ।।
bhaved dhūmro rocanābhaḥ piṅgo'tho syātpiśaṅgakaḥ । padmadhūlau karburaśca smṛtaścendradhanuḥsamaḥ ।। iti ।। raseṃdravedhasambhūtaṃ tadvedhajamudāhṛtam ।
rasāyanaṃ mahāśreṣṭhaṃ pavitraṃ vedhajaṃ hi tat ।। prasiddhasvarṇaṃ khanisaṃbhavam āha tatra tatreti ।। girīṇām ।। ete ca girayo himālayavindhyasahyakarṇāṭakasthanīlagiriprabhṛtayaḥ svarṇakhanisthānatvena prasiddhāḥ santi ।।
kāṣṭhāṃ prāptau pītaraktavarṇau paripūrṇau vihāya caturdaśavarṇapūrṇaṃ khanijaṃ bhavati ।। ratnaparīkṣakaisteṣāmeva varṇānām utkarṣavibhājakā yāvacchataṃ vikalpitāḥ kakṣā loke prasiddhāḥ ।। snigdhaṃ medhyaṃ viṣagadaharaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ vṛṣyamagryaṃ yakṣmonmādapraśamanaparaṃ deharogapramāthi । medhābuddhismṛtisukhakaraṃ sarvadoṣāmayaghnaṃ rucyaṃ dīpi praśamitarujaṃ svādupākaṃ suvarṇam ।।
saukhyaṃ vīryaṃ balaṃ hanti rogavargaṃ karoti ca । aśuddhamamṛtaṃ svarṇaṃ tasmācchuddhaṃ ca mārayet ।। karṣapramāṇaṃ tu suvarṇapatraṃ śarāvaruddhaṃ paṭudhātuyuktam । aṅgārasaṃsthaṃ praharārdhamānaṃ dhmānena tatsyānnanu pūrṇavarṇam ।।
lohānāṃ māraṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarveṣāṃ rasabhasmanā । mūlībhirmadhyamaṃ prāhuḥ kaniṣṭhaṃ gandhakādibhiḥ । arilohena lohāriṇā haritāleneti yāvat ।। -d arilohena lohasya māraṇaṃ durguṇapradam ।।
kṛtvā kaṇṭakavedhyāni svarṇapatrāṇi lepayet । luṃgāṃbubhasmasūtena mriyate daśabhiḥ puṭaiḥ ।। drute vinikṣipetsvarṇe lohamānaṃ mṛtaṃ rasam । vicūrṇya luṅgatoyena daradena samanvitam ।
jāyate kuṃkumacchāyaṃ svarṇaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ puṭaiḥ ।। hemnaḥ pādaṃ mṛtaṃ sūtaṃ piṣṭamamlena kenacit । patre liptvā puṭaiḥ pacyādaṣṭabhirmriyate dhruvam ।। maṃḍūkāsthivasāṭaṃkahayalālendragopakaiḥ ।
prativāpaḥ galitasya dhātoḥ dravyāntareṇa avacūrṇanam ।। prativāpena kanakaṃ suciraṃ tiṣṭhati drutam ।। cūrṇaṃ surendragopānāṃ devadālīphaladravaiḥ । devadālī hastighoṣakaḥ ।।
bhāvitaṃ sadṛśaṃ hema karoti jalavaddrutam ।। etadbhasma suvarṇajaṃ kaṭughṛtopetaṃ dviguṃjonmitaṃ līḍhaṃ hanti nṛṇāṃ kṣayāgnisadanaṃ śvāsaṃ ca kāsārucim । ojodhātuvivardhanaṃ balakaraṃ pāṇḍvāmayadhvaṃsanaṃ pathyaṃ sarvaviṣāpahaṃ garaharaṃ duṣṭagrahaṇyādinut ।। balaṃ ca vīryaṃ harate narāṇāṃ rogavrajaṃ kopayatīva kāye ।
asaukhyakāraṃ ca sadaiva hemāpakvaṃ sadoṣaṃ maraṇaṃ karoti ।। sahajaṃ khanisaṃjātaṃ kṛtrimaṃ trividhaṃ matam । rajataṃ pūrvapūrvaṃ hi svaguṇairuttarottaram ।। kailāsādyadrisambhūtaṃ sahajaṃ rajataṃ bhavet ।
tatspṛṣṭaṃ hi sakṛdvyādhināśanaṃ dehināṃ bhavet ।। himālayādikūṭeṣu yadrūpaṃ jāyate hi tat । khanijaṃ kathyate tajjñaiḥ paramaṃ hi rasāyanam ।। śrīrāmapādukānyastaṃ vaṃgaṃ yadrūpyatāṃ gatam ।
tatpādarūpyamityuktaṃ kṛtrimaṃ sarvaroganut ।। ghanaṃ svacchaṃ guru snigdhaṃ dāhe chede sitaṃ mṛdu । sphoṭarahitaṃ vraṇavat gaṇḍarahitam ।। śaṃkhābhaṃ masṛṇaṃ sphoṭarahitaṃ rajataṃ śubham ।।
dāhe raktaṃ ca pītaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ sphuṭaṃ laghu । sthūlāṅgaṃ karkaśāṅgaṃ ca rajataṃ tyājyamaṣṭadhā ।। rūpyaṃ vipākamadhuraṃ tuvarāmlasāraṃ śītaṃ saraṃ paramalekhanakaṃ ca rūpyam । snigdhaṃ ca vātakaphajijjaṭharāgnidīpi balyaṃ paraṃ sthiravayaskaraṇaṃ ca medhyam ।।
raupyaṃ śītaṃ kaṣāyāmlaṃ snigdhaṃ vātaharaṃ guru । rasāyanavidhānena sarvarogāpahārakam ।। taile takre gavāṃ mūtre hyāranāle kulatthaje । kramānniṣecayettaptaṃ drāve drāve tu saptadhā ।
svarṇādilohapatrāṇāṃ śuddhireṣā praśasyate ।। āyuḥ śukraṃ balaṃ hanti tāpaviḍbandharogakṛt । aśuddhaṃ na mṛtaṃ tāraṃ śuddhaṃ māryamato budhaiḥ ।। vāpitaṃ kalkīkṛtaṃ piṣṭamityarthaḥ ।।
nāgena ṭaṃkaṇenaiva vāpitaṃ śuddhimṛcchati । tāraṃ trivāraṃ nikṣiptaṃ taile jyotiṣmatībhave ।। kharpare bhasmacūrṇābhyāṃ paritaḥ pālikāṃ caret । tatra rūpyaṃ vinikṣipya samasīsasamanvitam ।।
jātasīsakṣayaṃ yāvaddhamettāvatpunaḥ punaḥ । itthaṃ saṃśodhitaṃ rūpyaṃ yojanīyaṃ rasādiṣu ।। matāntaramāha kharpare iti ।। bhasmacūrṇābhyāṃ sīsakabhasmaṭaṅkaṇacūrṇābhyāṃ pālikām ālavālam ।।
atrāyaṃ vidhiḥ nāgabhasmaṭaṅkaṇacūrṇe jalena piṣṭvā tatpiṇḍena mṛtkharparaṃ paritaḥ ālavālaṃ racayitvā tanmadhye samasīsacūrṇapiṣṭaraupyaṃ nikṣipya tāvat bhastrayā dhamet yāvat sīsakṣayo na bhavediti ।। lakucadravasūtābhyāṃ tārapatraṃ pralepayet । ūrdhvādho gandhakaṃ dattvā mūṣāmadhye nirudhya ca ।। svedayedvālukāyantre dinamekaṃ dṛḍhāgninā ।
svāṃgaśītāṃ ca tāṃ piṣṭiṃ sāmlatālena marditām । puṭeddvādaśavārāṇi bhasmībhavati rūpyakam ।। mākṣīkacūrṇaluṃgāmlamarditaṃ puṭitaṃ śanaiḥ । triṃśadvāreṇa tattāraṃ bhasmasājjāyatetarām ।।
bhāvyaṃ tāpyaṃ snuhīkṣīraistārapatrāṇi lepayet । mārayetpuṭayogena nirutthaṃ jāyate dhruvam ।। tārapatraṃ caturbhāgaṃ bhāgaikaṃ śuddhatālakam । mardyaṃ jambīrajadrāvaistārapatrāṇi lepayet ।।
śodhayed andhayantre ca triṃśadutpalakaiḥ pacet । caturdaśapuṭairevaṃ nirutthaṃ jāyate dhruvam ।। saptadhā naramūtreṇa bhāvayeddevadālikām । taccūrṇāvāpamātreṇa drutiḥ syātsvarṇatārayoḥ ।।
bhasmībhūtaṃ rajatamamalaṃ tatsamau vyomabhānū sarvaistulyaṃ trikaṭu savaraṃ sāraghājyena yuktam । līḍhaṃ prātaḥ kṣapayatitarāṃ yakṣmapāṇḍūdarārśaḥ śvāsaṃ kāsaṃ nayanajarujaḥ pittarogānaśeṣān ।। mlecchaṃ nepālakaṃ ceti tayornepālakaṃ varam । nepālādanyakhanyutthaṃ mlecchamityabhidhīyate ।।
tāmrasya khanidvayaṃ vartate ।। tatraikakhanisthaṃ nepālam iti khyātam ।। nepālī kunaṭī ।। tatsamaraktavarṇatvāt ।।
khaner nepāladeśasaṃnihitatvād vā nepāleti saṃjñā ।। athavā rūḍhasaṃjñeyam ।। tato'nyakhanisthaṃ tu mleccham ityabhidhīyate ।। yathā mlecchadhātur aspaṣṭaśabde tathā spaṣṭaśabdaraktavarṇatvānmleccham iti saṃjñā ।।
sitakṛṣṇāruṇacchāyam ativāmi kaṭhorakam । kṣālitaṃ ca punaḥ kṛṣṇam etanmlecchakatāmrakam ।। susnigdhaṃ mṛdulaṃ śoṇaṃ ghanāghātakṣamaṃ guru । nirvikāraṃ guṇaśreṣṭhaṃ tāmraṃ nepālamucyate ।।
pāṇḍuraṃ kṛṣṇaśoṇaṃ ca laghusphuṭanasaṃyutam । sadalaṃ sapattraṃ paṭalasaṃyutam iti yāvat dalaṃ jor iti loke iti bhāvamiśraḥ ।। rūkṣāṅgaṃ sadalaṃ tāmraṃ neṣyate rasakarmaṇi ।। tāmraṃ tiktakaṣāyakaṃ ca madhuraṃ pāke'tha vīryoṣṇakaṃ sāmlaṃ pittakaphāpahaṃ jaṭhararukkuṣṭhāmajantvantakṛt ।
ūrdhvādhaḥ pariśodhanaṃ viṣayakṛt sthaulyāpahaṃ kṣutkaraṃ durnāmakṣayapāṇḍurogaśamanaṃ netryaṃ paraṃ lekhanam ।। aśuddhaṃ tāmramāyurghnaṃ kāntivīryabalāpaham । vāntimūrcchābhramotkledaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ śūlaṃ karoti tat ।। utkledabhedabhramadāhamohāstāmrasya doṣāḥ khalu durdharāste ।
viśodhanāttadvigatasvadoṣaṃ sudhāsamaṃ syād rasavīryapāke ।। tāmraṃ kṣārāmlasaṃyuktaṃ drāvitaṃ dattagairikam । nikṣiptaṃ mahiṣītakre chagaṇe saptavārakam । pañcadoṣavinirmuktaṃ bhasmayogyaṃ hi jāyate ।।
tāmranirmalapatrāṇi liptvā nimbvambusindhunā । dhmātvā sauvīrakakṣepādviśudhyatyaṣṭavārataḥ ।। nimbvambupaṭuliptāni tāpitānyaṣṭavārakam । viśudhyantyarkapatrāṇi nirguṃḍyārasamajjanāt ।।
gomūtreṇa pacedyāmaṃ tāmrapatraṃ dṛḍhāgninā । śudhyate nātra saṃdeho māraṇaṃ cāpyathocyate ।। jambīrarasasampiṣṭarasagandhakalepitam । śulbapatraṃ śarāvasthaṃ tripuṭairyāti pañcatām ।।
athavā māritaṃ tāmramamlenaikena marditam । tadgolaṃ sūraṇasyāntā ruddhvā sarvatra lepayet ।। śuṣkaṃ gajapuṭe pacyātsarvadoṣaharaṃ bhavet । vāntiṃ bhrāntiṃ virekaṃ ca na karoti kadācana ।।
tāmrapatrāṇi sūkṣmāṇi gomūtre pañcayāmakam । kṣiptvā rasena bhāṇḍe taddviguṇaṃ dehi gandhakam ।। amlaparṇī cāṅgerī ।। amlaparṇīṃ prapiṣyātha hyabhito dehi tāmrakam ।
samyaṅ nirudhya bhāṇḍe tamagniṃ jvālaya yāmakam । bhasmībhavati tāmraṃ tadyatheṣṭaṃ viniyojayet ।। sūtād dviguṇitaṃ tāmrapatraṃ kanyārasaiḥ plutam । piṣṭvā tulyena balinā bhāṇḍamadhye vinikṣipet ।।
channaṃ śarāvakeṇaitattadūrdhvaṃ lavaṇaṃ tyajet । mukhe śarāvakaṃ dattvā vahniṃ yāmacatuṣṭayam ।। avacūrṇyaiva tacchulbaṃ vallamātraṃ prayojayet । pippalīmadhunā sārdhaṃ sarvarogeṣu yojayet ।।
śvāsaṃ kāsaṃ kṣayaṃ pāṇḍumagnimāṃdyamarocakam । gulmaplīhayakṛnmūrcchāśūlapaktyartham uttamam ।। doṣatrayasamudbhūtānāmayāñjayati dhruvam । rogānupānasahitaṃ jayeddhātugataṃ jvaram ।
rase rasāyane tāmraṃ yojayedyuktamātrayā ।। śulbatulyena sūtena balinā tatsamena ca । tadardhāṃśena tālena śilayā ca tadardhayā ।। vidhāya kajjalīṃ ślakṣṇāṃ bhinnakajjalasannibhām ।
yantrādhyāyavinirdiṣṭagarbhayantrodarāntare ।। kajjalīṃ tāmrapatrāṇi paryāyeṇa vinikṣipet । prapacedyāmaparyantaṃ svāṃgaśītaṃ vicūrṇayet ।। tattadrogaharānupānasahitatāmraṃ dvivallonmitaṃ saṃlīḍhaṃ pariṇāmaśūlamudaraṃ śūlaṃ ca pāṇḍujvaram ।
gulmaplīhayakṛtkṣayāgnisadanaṃ mehaṃ ca mūlāmayaṃ duṣṭāṃ ca grahaṇīṃ hared dhruvam idaṃ śrīsomanāthābhidham ।। muṃḍaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca kāṃtaṃ ca triprakāramayaḥ smṛtam ।। mṛdu kuṇṭhaṃ kaḍāraṃ ca trividhaṃ muṇḍamucyate ।। drutadrāvamavisphoṭaṃ cikkaṇaṃ mṛdu tacchubham ।।
hataṃ yatprasared duḥkhāttatkuṇṭhaṃ madhyamaṃ smṛtam ।। yaddhataṃ bhajyate bhaṃge kṛṣṇaṃ syāttatkaḍārakam ।। muṇḍaṃ paraṃ mṛdulakaṃ kaphavātaśūlamūlāmamehagadakāmalapāṇḍuhāri । gulmāmavātajaṭharārtiharaṃ pradīpi śophāpahaṃ rudhirakṛtkhalu koṣṭhaśodhi ।।
aśuddhalohaṃ na hitaṃ niṣevaṇād āyurbalaṃ kāntivināśi niścitam । hṛdi prapīḍāṃ tanute hyapāṭavaṃ rujaṃ karotyeva viśodhya mārayet ।। kharaṃ sāraṃ ca hṛnnālaṃ tārāvaṭṭaṃ ca vājiram । kālalohābhidhānaṃ ca ṣaḍvidhaṃ tīkṣṇamucyate ।।
paruṣaṃ pogaronmuktaṃ bhaṃge pāradavacchavi । namane bhaṅguraṃ yattatkharalohamudāhṛtam ।। pogaraṃ kuñcitālakavat taraṅgāyitaṃ tena unmuktaṃ tadrahitam ityarthaḥ ।। yat paruṣaṃ kaṭhoraṃ pogaronmuktaṃ pogaram alakavat kuṭilarekhās tābhir muktaṃ tadrahitam ityarthaḥ ।।
vegabhaṅguradhāraṃ yatsāralohaṃ tadīritam । pogarābhāsakaṃ pāṇḍubhūmijaṃ sāramucyate ।। kṛṣṇapāṇḍuvapuścañcubījatulyorupogaram । chedane cātiparuṣaṃ hṛnnālamiti kathyate ।।
aṅgakṣayā ca vaṅgaṃ ca pogarasyābhidhātrayam । cikuraṃ bhaṅguraṃ lohāt pogaraṃ tatparaṃ matam ।। kharalakṣaṇe pogaronmuktam ityuktam ataḥ pogarasya paryāyādikam āha aṅgakṣayeti ।। tritvaṃ cātra pogaram apekṣya bodhyaṃ tena aṅgakṣayā vaṅgaṃ pogaraṃ ca ityekārtham ।।
pogarasya svarūpalakṣaṇamāha cikuram iti ।। lohāt lauhagātre ityarthaḥ ।। atra saptamyarthe pañcamīti boddhavyam yat cikuraṃ bhaṅguraṃ kuñcitakuntalavadbhaṅgīviśeṣaḥ ityarthaḥ ।। pogaraśabdo'trāgataḥ ।।
sa cāpratisiddhārthaḥ ।। ato bodhārthaṃ tatparyāyān āha aṅgachāyā ca vaṅgaṃ cikuraṃ ca iti pogarasyābhidhātrayaṃ nāmatrayam asti ।। evaṃ ca nāmānyetāni viśiṣṭākāratejasa ityarthaḥ ।। vaṅgasyeva rekhānāṃ śvetacchāyātvād vaṅgamiti saṃjñā ।।
kāntīnāṃ cikurākāratvāt keśākāratvāccikuram ityapi nāma ।। yad uktam eva kharalohaṃ tadyadi lohādbhaṅguraṃ lohamayaghanaghātena bhaṅguraṃ bhavati paraṃtu pogaraṃ pogaraviśiṣṭaṃ dṛśyeta tarhi tat kharaloham api paramuttamaṃ matam ।। pogarairvajrasaṃkāśaiḥ sūkṣmarekhaiśca sāndrakaiḥ । nicitaṃ śyāmalāṅgaṃ ca vājīraṃ tatprakīrtyate ।।
nīlakṛṣṇaprabhaṃ sāndraṃ masṛṇaṃ guru bhāsuram । lohāghāte apyabhaṅgātmadhāraṃ kālāyasaṃ matam ।। rūkṣaṃ syāt kharalohakaṃ samadhuraṃ pāke'tha vīrye himaṃ tiktoṣṇaṃ kaphapittakuṣṭhajaṭharaplīhāmapāṃḍvartinut । sadyaḥ śūlayakṛdgadakṣayajarāmehāmavātāpahaṃ dīptaṃ cātirasāyanaṃ balakaraṃ durnāmadāhāpaham ।।
kharalohātparaṃ sarvamekaikasmācchatottaram ।। bhrāmakaṃ cumbakaṃ caiva karṣakaṃ drāvakaṃ tathā । evaṃ caturvidhaṃ kāntaṃ romakāntaṃ ca pañcamam ।। ekadvitricatuṣpañcasarvatomukham eva tat ।
tasya cokto vyastaḥ samasto vā bhedo'yaṃ jāraṇāyāṃ sakaladhātubhakṣaṇārthaṃ pāradasya mukharūpo bhavatītyāha ekadvitrīti ।। kevalabhrāmakasattvasya prathamaṃ yathāvidhijāraṇenāpi pāradasya mukhaṃ bhavati ।। tataḥ pāradaḥ sarvāṃllohādīn grasati ।। ata ekabhedo'pi kaścitpāradamukhaṃ bhavati ।।
yasya tad ekamukham ।। bhrāmakacumbakayoḥ sattvadvayasyaikīkṛtasya yathāvidhijāraṇena pāradamukhaṃ kṛtaṃ cet saṃyuktabhedadvayaviśiṣṭaṃ tat kāntaṃ dvimukham ucyate ।। b evam evārthastrimukhādau bodhyaḥ ।। vijātīyadravyagrāsāntarasahitam apyetat prathamaṃ jāritaṃ cenmukhaṃ bhavatītyataḥ sarvatomukham ityuktam ।।
sajātīyavijātīyavyastasamastaṃ bhedaviśiṣṭam etanmukhaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ ।। pītaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ tathā raktaṃ trivarṇaṃ syātpṛthak pṛthak । krameṇa devatāstatra brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।। sparśavedhi sparśamātreṇaiva vedhakārakaṃ rasendrasya vedhākhyasaṃskārasaṃpādakaṃ vā ityarthaḥ ।।
sparśavedhi bhavetpītaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rasāyane । raktavarṇaṃ tathā cāpi rasabandhe praśasyate ।। bhrāmakaṃ tu kaniṣṭhaṃ syāccumbakaṃ madhyamaṃ tathā । uttamaṃ karṣakaṃ caiva drāvakaṃ cottamottamam ।।
bhrāmayellohajātaṃ yattatkāntaṃ bhrāmakaṃ matam ।। cumbayeccumbakaṃ kāntaṃ karṣayetkarṣakaṃ tathā ।। sākṣād yaddrāvayellohaṃ tatkāntaṃ drāvakaṃ bhavet ।। tadromakāntaṃ sphuṭitād yato romodgamo bhavet ।।
kaniṣṭhaṃ syādekamukhaṃ madhyaṃ dvitrimukhaṃ bhavet । catuṣpañcamukhaṃ śreṣṭhamuttamaṃ sarvatomukham ।। bhrāmakaṃ cumbakaṃ caiva vyādhināśe praśasyate । rase rasāyane caiva karṣakaṃ drāvakaṃ hitam ।।
madonmattagajaḥ sūtaḥ kāntam aṅkuśamucyate ।। kṣetraṃ jñātvā grahītavyaṃ tatprayatnena dhīmatā । mārutātapavikṣiptaṃ varjayennātra saṃśayaḥ ।। pātre yasya prasarati jale tailabindurna lipto gandhaṃ hiṅgustyajati ca tathā tiktatāṃ nimbakalkaḥ ।
pāke dugdhaṃ bhavati śikharākārakaṃ naiti bhūmau kāntaṃ lauhaṃ tadidamuditaṃ lakṣaṇoktaṃ ca nānyat ।। kāntāyo atirasāyanottarataraṃ svasthe cirāyuḥpradaṃ snigdhaṃ mehaharaṃ tridoṣaśamanaṃ śūlāmamūlāpaham । gulmaplīhayakṛtkṣayāmayaharaṃ pāṇḍūdaravyādhinut tiktoṣṇaṃ himavīryakaṃ kimaparaṃ yogena sarvārtinut ।। samyagauṣadhakalpānāṃ lohakalpaḥ praśasyate ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena śuddhaṃ lohaṃ ca mārayet ।। nāyaḥ pacetpañcapalād arvāg ūrdhvaṃ trayodaśāt ।। ādau mantrastataḥ karma kartavyaṃ mantra ucyate ।। oṃ amṛtodbhavāya svāhā anena mantreṇa lohamāraṇam ।
lakṣottaraguṇaṃ sarvaṃ lohaṃ syāduttarottaram । kāntaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ tatra tadapyevaṃ guṇottaram ।। śaśakṣatajasaṃliptaṃ trivāraṃ paritāpitam । muṇḍādisakalaṃ lohaṃ sarvadoṣān vimuñcati ।।
kvāthyamaṣṭaguṇe toye triphalāṣoḍaśaṃ palam । tatkvāthe pādaśeṣe tu lohasya palapañcakam ।। kṛtvā patrāṇi taptāni saptavāraṃ niṣecayet । evaṃ pralīyate doṣo girijo lohasambhavaḥ ।।
sāmudralavaṇopetaṃ taptaṃ nirvāpitaṃ khalu । triphalākvathite nūnaṃ giridoṣam ayastyajet ।। ciñcāphalajalakvāthādayo doṣam udasyati ।। yadvā phalatrayopetaṃ gomūtre kvathitaṃ kṣaṇam ।
recitaṃ srāvitam ।। recitaṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ kṣiptvāyaḥ kharpare pacet ।। cālayellohadaṇḍena yāvatkṣiptaṃ tṛṇaṃ dahet । piṣṭvā piṣṭvā pacedevaṃ pañcavāramataḥ param ।।
dhātrīphalarasair yadvā triphalākvathitodakaiḥ । puṭellohaṃ caturvāraṃ bhavedvāritaraṃ khalu ।। snehāktaṃ loharajo mūtre svarase'pi rātridhātrīṇām । pṛthagevaṃ saptakṛtvo bharjitamakhilāmaye yojyam ।।
tīkṣṇalohasya patrāṇi nirdalāni dṛḍhe'nale । dhmātvā kṣipejjale sadyaḥ pāṣāṇolūkhalodare ।। kaṇḍayedgāḍhanirghātaiḥ sthūlayā lohapārayā । tanmadhyātsthūlakhaṇḍāni ruddhvā malladvayāntare ।।
dhmātvā kṣiptvā jale samyak pūrvavatkaṇḍayetkhalu । taccūrṇaṃ sūtagandhābhyāṃ puṭedviṃśativārakam ।। puṭe puṭe vidhātavyaṃ peṣaṇaṃ dṛḍhavattaram । evaṃ bhasmīkṛtaṃ lohaṃ tattadrogeṣu yojayet ।।
kāntāyaḥ kamanīyakāntijananaṃ pāṇḍvāmayonmūlanam । yakṣmavyādhinibarhaṇaṃ garaharaṃ doṣatrayonmūlanam । nānākuṣṭhanibarhaṇaṃ balakaraṃ vṛṣyaṃ vayaḥstambhanam । sarvavyādhiharaṃ rasāyanavaraṃ bhaumāmṛtaṃ nāparam ।।
hiṅgulasya palānpañca nārīstanyena peṣayet । tena lohasya patrāṇi lepayetpalapañcakam ।। ruddhvā gajapuṭe pacyātkaṣāyaistraiphalaiḥ punaḥ । jambīrairāranālairvā viṃśatyaṃśena hiṅgulam ।।
piṣṭvā ruddhvā pacellohaṃ taddravaiḥ pācayetpunaḥ । catvāriṃśatpuṭairevaṃ kāntaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca muṇḍakam । mriyate nātra saṃdeho dattvā dattvaiva hiṅgulam ।। atha pūrvoditaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vasubhallakavāsayoḥ ।
puṭitaṃ patratoyena triṃśadvārāṇi yatnataḥ । śoṇitaṃ jāyate bhasma kṛtasindūravibhramam ।। yadvā tīkṣṇadalodbhūtaṃ rajaśca triphalājalaiḥ । piṣṭvā dattvaudanaṃ kiṃciccakrikāṃ pravidhāya ca ।।
śoṣayitvātiyatnena prapacetpañcabhiḥ puṭaiḥ । raktavarṇaṃ hi tadbhasma yojanīyaṃ yathāyatham ।। matsyākṣīgandhabāhlīkairlakucadravapeṣitaiḥ । vilipya sakalaṃ lohaṃ matsyākṣīkalkalepitam ।।
bhastrābhyāṃ sudṛḍhaṃ dhmātvā triśūlīnirgamāvadhi । triśūlī triśūlavaccaṭikātrayam ityarthaḥ ।। athoddhṛtya kṣipetkvāthe triphalāgojalātmake ।। tasmādāhṛtya saṃtāḍya mṛtamādāya lohakam ।
punaśca pūrvavad dhmātvā mārayedakhilāyasam ।। khaṇḍayitvā tato gandhaguḍatriphalayā saha । puṭettriṃśativārāṇi nirutthaṃ bhasma jāyate ।। samagandham ayaścūrṇaṃ kumārīvāribhāvitam ।
puṭīkṛtaṃ kiyatkālamavaśyaṃ mriyate hyayaḥ ।। jambīrarasasaṃyukte darade taptamāyasam । bahuvāraṃ vinikṣiptaṃ mriyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। gomūtraistriphalā kvāthyā tatkaṣāyeṇa bhāvayet ।
triḥsaptāhaṃ prayatnena dinaikaṃ mardayetpunaḥ ।। ruddhvā gajapuṭe pacyāddinaṃ kvāthena mardayet । divā mardyaṃ puṭedrātrāvekaviṃśaddināvadhi । ekaviṃśatpuṭairevaṃ mriyate trividhaṃ hyayaḥ ।।
yatpātrādhyuṣite toye tailabindurna sarpati । tāreṇāvartate yattatkāntalohaṃ tanūkṛtam ।। ayasāmuttamaṃ siñcettaptaṃ taptaṃ varārase । evaṃ śuddhāni lohāni piṣṭānyamlena kenacit ।।
mṛtasūtasya pādena praliptāni puṭānale । pacettulyena vā tāpyagandhāśmaharatejasā ।। taptaṃ kṣārāmlasaṃliptaṃ śaśarakte nidhāpitam । kāntalohaṃ bhavedbhasma sarvadoṣavivarjitam ।।
śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ dvidhā gandhaṃ khallena kṛtakajjalam । dvayoḥ samaṃ lohacūrṇaṃ mardayetkanyakādravaiḥ ।। yāmadvayātsamuddhṛtya yadgolaṃ tāmrapātrake । ācchādyairaṃḍapatraiśca yāmārdhe'tyuṣṇatāṃ vrajet ।।
dhānyarāśau nyasetpaścāttridinānte samuddharet । saṃpeṣya gālayedvastre satyaṃ vāritaraṃ bhavet । kāntaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca muṃḍaṃ ca nirutthaṃ jāyate mṛtam ।। svarṇādīnmārayedevaṃ cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā ca lohavat ।
siddhayogo hyayaṃ khyātaḥ siddhānāṃ sumukhāgataḥ ।। anubhūtaṃ mayā satyaṃ sarvarogajarāpaham । triphalāmadhusaṃyuktaṃ sarvarogeṣu yojayet ।। etasmād apunarbhavaṃ hi bhasitaṃ lohasya divyāmṛtaṃ samyak siddharasāyanaṃ trikaṭukīvellājyamadhvanvitam ।
