hanyānniṣkamitaṃ jarāmaraṇajavyādhīṃśca satputradaṃ diṣṭe śrīgiriśena kālayavanodbhūtyai purā tatpituḥ ।। lohaṃ jantuvikārapāṇḍupavanakṣīṇatvapittāmayasthaulyārśograhaṇījvarārtikaphajicchophapramehapraṇut । gulmaplīhaviṣāpahaṃ balakaraṃ kuṣṭhāgnimāndyapraṇut saukhyālambirasāyanaṃ mṛtiharaṃ kiṭṭaṃ ca kāntādivat ।। mṛtāni lohāni rasībhavanti nighnanti yuktāni mahāmayāṃśca ।
abhyāsayogād dṛḍhadehasiddhiṃ kurvanti rugjanmajarāvināśam ।। pakvajambūphalacchāyaṃ kāntalohaṃ taduttamam ।। triḥsaptakṛtvo gomūtre jālinībhasmabhāvitam । śoṣayettasya vāpena tīkṣṇaṃ mūṣāgataṃ dravet ।।
suradālibhasma galitaṃ triḥsaptakṛtvo'tha gojale śuṣkam । vāpena salilasadṛśaṃ karoti mūṣāgataṃ tīkṣṇam ।। suradālibhavaṃ bhasma naramūtreṇa gālitam । triḥsaptavāraṃ tatkṣāravāpāt kāntadrutir bhavet ।।
gaṃdhakaṃ kāṃtapāṣāṇaṃ cūrṇayitvā samaṃ samam । drute lohe pratīvāpo deyo lohāṣṭakaṃ dravet ।। devadālyā dravairbhāvyaṃ gaṃdhakaṃ dinasaptakam । tena pravāpamātreṇa lauhaṃ tiṣṭhati sūtavat ।।
aśuddhalohaṃ na hitaṃ niṣevaṇād āyurbalaṃ kāntivināśi niścitam । hṛdi prapīḍāṃ tanute hyapāṭavaṃ rujaṃ karotyeva viśodhya mārayet ।। kiṭṭāddaśaguṇaṃ muṇḍaṃ muṇḍāttīkṣṇaṃ śatonmitam । tīkṣṇāllakṣaguṇaṃ kāntaṃ bhakṣaṇātkurute guṇān ।
tasmāt kāntaṃ sadā sevyaṃ jarāmṛtyuharaṃ nṛṇām ।। āyuṣpradātā balavīryakartā rogaprahartā madanasya kartā । ayaḥsamānaṃ na hi kiṃcid anyadrasāyanaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ hi jantoḥ ।। akṣāṅgārairdhametkiṭṭaṃ lohajaṃ tadgavāṃ jalaiḥ ।
secayedakṣapātrāntaḥ saptavāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ । maṇḍūro'yaṃ samākhyātaścūrṇaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ prayojayet ।। gomūtraistriphalā kvāthyā tatkvāthe secayecchanaiḥ । lohakiṭṭaṃ susaṃtaptaṃ yāvajjīryati tatsvayam ।
taccūrṇaṃ jāyate peṣyaṃ maṇḍūro'yaṃ prayojayet ।। ye guṇā mārite muṇḍe te guṇā muṇḍakiṭṭake । tasmātsarvatra maṇḍūraṃ rogaśāntyai prayojayet ।। khurakaṃ miśrakaṃ ceti dvividhaṃ vaṃgamucyate ।
khuraṃ tatra guṇaiḥ śreṣṭhaṃ miśrakaṃ na hitaṃ matam ।। na hitam iti ।। tatra nāgamiśraṇenāśuddhatvāt ।। dhavalaṃ mṛtaṃ snigdhaṃ drutadrāvaṃ sagauravam ।
niḥśabdaṃ pattrībhūtamapi śabdarahitaṃ pattrībhūtaṃ raṅgāntaraṃ yathā saśabdaṃ bhavati tathā na ityarthaḥ ।। niḥśabdaṃ khuravaṃgaṃ syāt miśrakaṃ śyāmaśubhrakam ।। vaṅgaṃ tiktoṣṇakaṃ rūkṣamīṣad vātaprakopanam । mehaśleṣmāmayaghnaṃ ca medoghnaṃ kṛmināśanam ।।
drāvayitvā niśāyukte kṣiptaṃ nirguṇḍikārase । viśudhyati trivāreṇa khuravaṃgaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। amlatakravinikṣiptaṃ varṣābhūviṣatindubhiḥ । kaṭphalāṃbugataṃ vaṃgaṃ dvitīyaṃ pariśudhyati ।।
śudhyati nāgo vaṃgo ghoṣo ravirātape'pi munisaṃkhyaiḥ । nirguṇḍīrasasekaistanmūlarajaḥpravāpaiśca ।। satālenārkadugdhena liptvā vaṃgadalāni ca । bodhiciṃcātvacaḥ kṣārairdadyāllaghupuṭāni ca ।
mardayitvā caredbhasma tadrasādiṣu śasyate ।। pradrāvya kharpare vaṃgaṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ rasaṃ kṣipet । bhāradvājasya vanakārpāsyāḥ ।। svalpasvalpālakaṃ dattvā bhāradvājasya kāṣṭhataḥ ।
mardayitvā caredbhasma tadrasādiṣu śasyate ।। palāśadravayuktena vaṃgapatraṃ pralepayet । tālena puṭitaṃ paścānmriyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। bhallātatailasaṃliptaṃ vaṃgaṃ vastreṇa veṣṭitam ।
ciṃcāpippalapālāśakāṣṭhāgnau yāti pañcatām ।। vaṃgabhasmasamaṃ kāntaṃ vyomabhasma ca tatsamam । mardayetkanakāmbhobhirnimbapatrarasairapi ।। dāḍimasya mayūrasya rasena ca pṛthak pṛthak ।
bhūpālāvartabhasmātha vinikṣipya samāṃśakam ।। gomūlakaśilādhātujalaiḥ samyagvimardayet । tato guggulatoyena mardayitvā dināṣṭakam ।। viśoṣya paricūrṇyātha samabhāgena yojayet ।
ghṛṣṭaṃ bandhūkaniryāsair nākulībījacūrṇakaiḥ ।। nākulībījaṃ rāsnābījaṃ śālmalībījaṃ vā ।। tataḥ kṣipetkaraṇḍāntarvidhāya paṭagālitam । gotakrapiṣṭarajanīsāreṇa saha pāyayet ।।
caturbhir vallakaistulyaṃ ramyaṃ vaṃgarasāyanam । niścitaṃ tena naśyanti mehā viṃśatibhedakāḥ ।। śālayo mudgasūpaṃ ca navanītaṃ tilodbhavam । paṭolaṃ tiktatuṇḍīraṃ takraṃ pathyāya śasyate ।।
drutadrāvaṃ mahābhāraṃ chede kṛṣṇaṃ samujjvalam । pūtigandhaṃ bahiḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śuddhaṃ sīsamato'nyathā ।। atyuṣṇaṃ sīsakaṃ snigdhaṃ tiktaṃ vātakaphāpaham । pramehatoyadoṣaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ cāmavātanut ।।
sinduvārajaṭākauntīharidrācūrṇakaṃ kṣipet । drute nāge'tha nirguṇḍyās trivāraṃ nikṣipedrase । nāgaḥ śuddho bhavedevaṃ mūrchāsphoṭādi nācaret ।। tiryagākāracullyāṃ tu tiryagvaktraṃ ghaṭaṃ nyaset ।
taṃ ca vaktraṃ vinā sarvaṃ gopayedyatnato mṛdā ।। bhṛṣṭayantrābhidhe tasmin pātre sīsaṃ vinikṣipet । palaviṃśatikaṃ śuddhamadhastīvrānalaṃ kṣipet ।। drute nāge kṣipetsūtaṃ śuddhaṃ karṣamitaṃ śubham ।
gharṣayitvā kṣipetkṣāramekaikaṃ hi palaṃ palam ।। arjunasyākṣavṛkṣasya mahārājagirerapi । mahārājagiriḥ śākaviśeṣaḥ rājaśākam itiyāvat sa tu laghusthūlabhedena dvividhaḥ atra ca sthūlo grāhyaḥ ।। dāḍimasya mayūrasya kṣiptvā kṣāraṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।
evaṃ viṃśatirātrāṇi pacettīvreṇa vahninā । vighaṭṭayandṛḍhaṃ dorbhyāṃ lohadarvyā prayatnataḥ ।। raktaṃ tajjāyate bhasma kapotacchāyameva vā । nāgaṃ doṣavinirmuktaṃ jāyate'tirasāyanam ।।
atredaṃ kāryaṃ vakrākārāṃ cullīṃ kṛtvā tadupari ghaṭamekaṃ vakramukhaṃ kṛtvā sthāpayet tato vaktramātraṃ vihāya kṛtsnaṃ ghaṭāvayavaṃ mṛllepenācchādayet bhṛṣṭayantrākhye'smin yantre viṃśatipalamānaṃ śuddhaṃ sīsakaṃ dattvā tīvrottāpena dravīkuryāt tataḥ tasmin karṣapramāṇaṃ śodhitapāradaṃ prakṣipya darvyā ghaṭṭayet miśrībhūte ca tasmin pratyekaṃ palamānaṃ arjunādīnāṃ kṣāraṃ pṛthak pṛthak dattvā lauhadarvyā dṛḍhaṃ ghaṭṭayan tīvrāgninā viṃśatirātraṃ pacet ।। tiryagākārā tiraścīnā yā dīrghā cullī āhāḷa iti mahārāṣṭrabhāsāyāṃ prasiddhā tasyāṃ ghaṭaṃ tiryagvaktram etādṛśaṃ ghaṭaṃ nyased adhiśrayet ।। taṃ ghaṭaṃ ca vaktraṃ vinā bāhye samaṃ tato'ṅgulasthūlaṃ mṛdā gopayellepayet ।। bhṛṣṭayantrākhye tasmin viṃśatipalamitaṃ sīsaṃ vinikṣipet ।।
tasmin drute sati ekakarṣaṃ śuddhasūtaṃ tatra kṣiptvā tato darvyā vighaṭṭya itastataḥ saṃcālyaikībhūte satyarjunādīnāṃ pratyekaṃ kṣāraṃ palamitaṃ kṣipet ।। tato dorbhyāṃ lohadarvyā vighaṭṭayaṃścālayan viṃśatirātraparyantaṃ tīvrāgninā pacet ।। tena vidhinā nāgabhasma raktavarṇaṃ kapotacchāyaṃ kṛṣṇamiśraraktavarṇaṃ vā bhavet ।। tāpasphoṭādikaratvarūpadoṣarahitaṃ bhasmībhūtaṃ nāgaṃ rasāyanaṃ bhavati ।।
hatamutthāpitaṃ sīsaṃ daśavāreṇa sidhyati । tanmṛtaṃ sīsakaṃ sarvadoṣamuktaṃ rasāyanam ।। aśvatthaciṃcātvagbhasma nāgasya caturaṃśataḥ । kṣipennāgaṃ pacetpātre cālayellohacāṭunā ।।
lohacāṭunā lohadarvyā ।। yāmādbhasma taduddhṛtya bhasmatulyā manaḥśilā । jambīrair āranālairvā piṣṭvā ruddhvā puṭe pacet ।। svāṃgaśītaṃ punaḥ piṣṭvā viṃśatyaṃśaśilāyutam ।
amlenaiva tu yāmaikaṃ pūrvavatpācayetpuṭe । evaṃ ṣaṣṭipuṭaiḥ pakvo nāgaḥ syātsunirutthitaḥ ।। śilayā ravidugdhena nāgapatrāṇi lepayet । mārayetpuṭayogena nirutthaṃ jāyate tathā ।।
evaṃ nāgodbhavaṃ bhasma tāpyabhasmārdhabhāgikam । pādaṃ pādaṃ kṣipedbhasma śulbasya vimalasya ca ।। kāntābhrasattvayoś cāpi sphaṭikasya pṛthak pṛthak । sarvamekatra saṃcūrṇya puṭettriphalavāriṇā ।।
triṃśadvanagiriṇḍaiśca triṃśadvāraṃ vicūrṇya tat । vyoṣavellakacūrṇaiśca samāṃśaiḥ saha melayet ।। madhvājyasahitaṃ hanti pralīḍhaṃ vallamātrayā । aśītivātajānrogāndhanurvātaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
kapharogānaśeṣāṃśca mūtrarogāṃśca sarvaśaḥ । śvāsaṃ kāsaṃ kṣayaṃ pāṇḍuṃ śvayathuṃ śītakajvaram ।। grahaṇīmāmadoṣaṃ ca vahnimāndyaṃ sudurjaram । sarvānudakadoṣāṃśca tattadrogānupānataḥ ।।
rītikā kākatuṇḍī ca dvividhaṃ pittalaṃ bhavet ।। tat pittalaṃ dvividham ।। rītikā kākatuṇḍī ceti bhedāt ।। tatra rītikāyā dvau bhedau ।।
kiṃcittāmrābhā svarṇavarṇā ca ।। saṃtāpya kāṃjike kṣiptā tāmrābhā rītikā matā ।। evaṃ yā jāyate kṛṣṇā kākatuṇḍīti sā matā ।। rītistiktarasā rūkṣā jantughnī sāsrapittanut ।
pāṇḍukuṣṭhaharā yogātsoṣṇavīryā ca śītalā ।। kākatuṇḍī gatasnehā tiktoṣṇā kaphapittanut । yakṛtplīhaharā śītavīryā ca parikīrtitā ।। gurvī mṛdvī ca pītābhā sārāṅgī tāḍanakṣamā ।
susnigdhā masṛṇāṅgī ca rītiretādṛśī śubhā ।। barbarā adhamā ityarthaḥ ।। pāṇḍupītā kharā rūkṣā barbarā tāḍanākṣamā । pūtigandhā tathā laghvī rītirneṣṭā rasādiṣu ।।
taptvā kṣiptvā ca nirguṇḍīrase śyāmārajo'nvite । śyāmārajo'nvite haridrācūrṇasaṃyute ।। pañcavāreṇa saṃśuddhiṃ rītirāyāti niścitam ।। nimbūrasaśilāgandhaveṣṭitā puṭitāṣṭadhā ।
rītirāyāti bhasmatvaṃ tato yojyā yathāyatham ।। tāmravanmāraṇaṃ tasyāḥ kṛtvā sarvatra yojayet ।। mṛtārakūṭakaṃ kāntaṃ vyomasattvaṃ ca māritam । trayaṃ samāṃśakaṃ tulyaṃ vyoṣaṃ jantughnasaṃyutam ।।
brahmabījājamodāgnibhallātatilasaṃyutam । ajamodā yamānī antaḥparimārjanakatvāt ।। sevitaṃ niṣkamātraṃ hi jantughnaṃ kuṣṭhanāśanam । viśeṣācchvetakuṣṭhaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ pācanaṃ hitam ।।
suvarṇarītikācūrṇaṃ bhakṣitaṃ veṣṭitaṃ punaḥ । chāgena kṛṣṇavarṇena mattena taruṇena ca ।। talliptaṃ kharpare dagdhaṃ drutiṃ muñcati śobhanām । caturdaśalasadvarṇasuvarṇasadṛśachaviḥ ।
dehalohakarī proktā yuktā rasarasāyane ।। aṣṭabhāgena tāmreṇa dvibhāgakhurakeṇa ca । vidrutena bhavetkāṃsyaṃ tatsaurāṣṭrabhavaṃ śubham ।। tīkṣṇaśabdaṃ mṛdu snigdhamīṣacchyāmalaśubhrakam ।
nirmalaṃ dāharaktaṃ ca ṣoḍhā kāṃsyaṃ praśasyate ।। tatpītaṃ dahane tāmraṃ kharaṃ rūkṣaṃ ghanāsaham । mandanādaṃ gatajyotiḥ saptadhā kāṃsyamutsṛjet ।। kāṃsyaṃ laghu ca tiktoṣṇaṃ lekhanaṃ dṛkprasādanam ।
kṛmikuṣṭhaharaṃ vātapittaghnaṃ dīpanaṃ hitam ।। ghṛtamekaṃ vinā cānyatsarvaṃ kāṃsyagataṃ nṛṇām । bhuktamārogyasukhadaṃ hitaṃ sātmyakaraṃ tathā ।। taptaṃ kāṃsyaṃ gavāṃ mūtre vāpitaṃ pariśudhyati ।।
mriyate gandhatālābhyāṃ nirutthaṃ pañcabhiḥ puṭaiḥ ।। trikṣāraṃ pañcalavaṇaṃ saptadhāmlena bhāvayet । ārakūṭaṃ pittalam ।। kāṃsyārakūṭapatrāṇi tena kalkena lepayet ।
ruddhvā gajapuṭe pakvaṃ śuddhabhasmatvamāpnuyāt ।। kāṃsyārkarītilohāhijātaṃ tadvartalohakam । tadeva pañcalohākhyaṃ lohavidbhirudāhṛtam ।। himāmlaṃ kaṭukaṃ rūkṣaṃ kaphapittavināśanam ।
rucyaṃ tvacyaṃ kṛmighnaṃ ca netryaṃ malaviśodhanam ।। tadbhāṇḍe sādhitaṃ sarvam annavyañjanasūpakam । amlena varjitaṃ cātidīpanaṃ pācanaṃ hitam ।। drutamaśvajale kṣiptaṃ vartalohaṃ viśudhyati ।।
mriyate gandhatālābhyāṃ puṭitaṃ vartalohakam । teṣu teṣviha yogeṣu yojanīyaṃ yathāvidhi ।। jātimadbhirviśuddhaiśca vidhinā parisādhitaiḥ । rasoparasalohādyaiḥ sūtaḥ sidhyati nānyathā ।।
ratnāni lohāni varāṭaśuktipāṣāṇajātaṃ khuraśṛṅgaśalyam । mahārasādyeṣu kaṭhoradehaṃ bhasmīkṛtaṃ syāt khalu sūtayogyam ।। vajrāṇāṃ drāvaṇārthāya sattvaṃ bhūnāgajaṃ bruve । tadeva paramaṃ tejaḥ sūtarājendravajrayoḥ ।।
dhautabhūnāgasambhūtaṃ mardayedbhṛṃgajadravaiḥ । nimbūdravaiśca nirguṇḍyāḥ svarasaistridinaṃ pṛthak ।। taddrāvaṇagaṇopetaṃ saṃmardya vaṭakīkṛtam । nirudhya dṛḍhamūṣāyāṃ dvidaṇḍaṃ pradhamed dṛḍham ।।
svataḥśītaṃ samāhṛtya paṭṭake viniveśya tat । ravakān rājikātulyān reṇūn atibharānvitān ।। dvādaśāṃśārkasaṃyuktāndhamitvā ravakānharet । prakṣālya ravakānāśu samādāya prayatnataḥ ।।
vajrādidrāvaṇaṃ tena prakurvīta yathepsitam । kharasattvam idaṃ proktaṃ rasāyanamanuttamam । dvitrimūṣāsu caikasyāṃ sattvaṃ bhavati niścitam ।। bhujaṅgamānupādāya catuṣprasthasamanvitān ।
suvarṇarūpyatāmrāyaskāṃtasaṃbhūtibhūmijān ।। prakṣālya rajanītoyaiḥ śītalaiśca jalairapi । upoṣitaṃ mayūraṃ vā śūraṃ vā caraṇāyudham ।। krameṇa cārayitvātha tadviṣṭhāṃ samupāharet ।
kṣārāmlaiḥ saha saṃpeṣya viśoṣya ca kharātape ।। tataḥ kharparake kṣiptvā bharjayitvā maṣīṃ caret । maṣīṃ drāvaṇavargeṇa saṃyuktāṃ saṃpramarditām ।। nirudhya koṣṭhikāmadhye pradhamed ghaṭikādvayam ।
khoṭaṃ rasajāraṇabandhanadravyaviśeṣaṃ bhūnāgasattvasya rasajārakatvāt atra khoṭaśabdena ravakareṇurūpaṃ bhūnāgasattvaṃ bodhyam ।। śītalībhūtamūṣāyāḥ khoṭamāhṛtya peṣayet ।। prakṣālya ravakānsūkṣmānsamādāya prayatnataḥ । suvarṇamānavad dhmātvā ravaṃ kṛtvā niyojayet ।।
bhūnāgodbhavasattvamuttamamidaṃ śrīsomadevoditaṃ dattaṃ pādamitaṃ dviśāṇakanakenaikaṃ gatenormikām । taddhautāmbuvilepitaṃ sthiracarodbhūtaṃ viṣaṃ netraruk śūlaṃ mūlagadaṃ ca karṇajarujo hanyāt prasūtigraham ।। mūlānyuttaravāruṇyā jarjarīkṛtya kāṃjike । kṣipedaṅkollabījānāṃ peśikāṃ jarjarīkṛtām ।
tattailaṃ ghṛtavatstyānaṃ grāhyaṃ tattu yathāvidhi ।। peṭakārī jyotiṣmatī ।। saṃpeṣyottaravāruṇyāḥ peṭakāryā dalānyatha । kāñjikena tatastena kalkena parimardayet ।।
rajaścāṅkollabījānāṃ tadbaddhvā viralāmbare । tadvilambyātape tīvre tasyādhaścaṣakaṃ nyaset । tasminnipatitaṃ tailamādeyaṃ śvitranāśanam ।। aṅkollabījasambhūtaṃ cūrṇaṃ saṃmardya kāñjikaiḥ ।
ekarātroṣitaṃ tattu piṇḍīkṛtya tataḥ param ।। svedayetkanduke yantre ghaṭikādvitayaṃ tataḥ । tāṃ ca piṇḍīṃ dṛḍhe vastre baddhvā niṣpīḍya kāṣṭhataḥ ।। adhaḥpātrasthitaṃ tailaṃ samāhṛtya niyojayet ।
evaṃ kandukayantreṇa sarvatailānyupāharet ।। kākatuṇḍī śvetaguñjā ।। aṅkolasyāpi tailaṃ syātkākatuṇḍyā samūlayā ।। vākucī somarājī ।।
devadālī hastighoṣakaḥ ।। karkoṭī karkoṭakaṃ kāṃkola iti bhāṣā ।। vākucidevadālyośca karkoṭīmūlato bhavet ।। apāmārgakaṣāyeṇa tailaṃ syādviṣamuṣṭijam ।।
mūlakvāthaiḥ kumāryāśca tailaṃ jaipālajaṃ haret ।। kvāthai raktāpāmārgasya vākucītailamāharet ।। kṛṣṇāyāḥ kākatuṇḍyāśca bījacūrṇāni kārayet । kāntapāṣāṇacūrṇaṃ ca ekīkṛtya nirodhayet ।
dhānyarāśigataṃ paścāduddhṛtya tailamāharet ।। rasaśāstrāṇi sarvāṇi samālocya yathākramam । sādhakānāṃ hitārthāya prakaṭīkriyate adhunā ।। na krameṇa vinā śāstraṃ na śāstreṇa vinā kramaḥ ।
śāstraṃ kramayutaṃ jñātvā yaḥ karoti sa siddhibhāk ।। ācāryo jñānavāndakṣo rasaśāstraviśāradaḥ । mantrasiddho mahāvīro niścalaśivavatsalaḥ ।। devībhaktaḥ sadā dhīro devatāyāgatatparaḥ ।
sarvāmnāyaviśeṣajñaḥ kuśalo rasakarmaṇi । evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyukto rasavidyāgurur bhavet ।। gurubhaktāḥ sadācārāḥ satyavanto dṛḍhavratāḥ । nirālasyāḥ svadharmajñāḥ sadājñāparipālakāḥ ।।
dambhamātsaryanirmuktāḥ kulācāreṣu dīkṣitāḥ । atyantasādhakāḥ śāntā mantrārādhanatatparāḥ । ityevaṃ lakṣaṇairyuktāḥ śiṣyāḥ syuḥ sūtasiddhaye ।। sahāyāḥ sodyamāstatra yathā śiṣyāstato'dhikāḥ ।
kulīnāḥ svāmibhaktāśca kartavyā rasakarmaṇi ।। nāstikā ye durācārāścumbakā guruto'parāt । vidyāṃ grahītumicchati cauryacchadmakhalotsavāt ।। na teṣāṃ sidhyate kiṃcin maṇimantrauṣadhādikam ।
kurvanti yadi mohena nāśayanti svakaṃ dhanam । iha loke sukhaṃ nāsti paraloke tathaiva ca ।। tasmād bhaktibalādeva saṃtuṣyati yadā guruḥ । tadā śiṣyeṇa sā grāhyā rasavidyātmasiddhaye ।
hastamastakayogena varaṃ labdhvā susādhayet ।। ātaṅkarahite deśe dharmarājye manorame । umāmaheśvaropete samṛddhe nagare śubhe ।। kartavyaṃ sādhanaṃ tatra rasarājasya dhīmatā ।
atyantopavane ramye caturdvāropaśobhite ।। tatra śālā prakartavyā suvistīrṇā manoramā । samyagvātāyanopetā divyacitrair vicitritā ।। tatsamīpe same dīpte kartavyaṃ rasamaṇḍapam ।
atiguptaṃ suvistīrṇaṃ kapāṭārgalaśobhitam ।। dhvajachattravitānāḍhyaṃ puṣpamālāvilambitam । bherīkāhalaghaṇṭādiśṛṅgīnādāvanāditam ।। bhūḥ samā tatra kartavyā sudṛḍhā darpaṇopamā ।
tanmadhye vedikā ramyā kartavyā lakṣaṇānvitā ।। niṣkatrayaṃ hemapattraṃ rasendraṃ navaniṣkakam । amlena mardayed yāmaṃ tena liṅgaṃ tu kārayet ।। dolāyantre sāranāle jambīrasthaṃ dinaṃ pacet ।
talliṅgaṃ pūjayettatra suśubhairupacārakaiḥ ।। liṅgakoṭisahasrasya yatphalaṃ samyagarcanāt । tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ rasaliṅgārcanādbhavet ।। brahmahatyāsahasrāṇi gohatyāścāyutāni hi ।
tatkṣaṇādvilayaṃ yānti rasaliṅgasya darśanāt ।। sparśanātprāpyate muktiriti satyaṃ śivoditam । āgneyyāṃ śrīghoreṇa mantrarājena cārcayet ।। aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ śubhraṃ pañcavaktraṃ trilocanam ।
pretārūḍhaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ rasaliṅgaṃ vicintayet ।। tasyotsaṅge mahādevīmekavaktrāṃ caturbhujām । akṣamālāṅkuśaṃ dakṣe vāme pāśābhayaṃ śubham । dadhatīṃ taptahemābhāṃ pītavastrāṃ vibhāvayet ।।
vāṅmayī śrīḥ kāmarājaśaktibījaṃ rasāṅkuśāyai namo dvādaśārṇaiṣā jñeyā vidyā rasāṅkuśā ।। anayā pūjayeddevīṃ gandhapuṣpākṣatādibhiḥ । nandībhṛṅgīmahākālakulīrān pūrvadikkramāt । pūjayen nāmamantraiś ca praṇavādinamo'ntakaiḥ ।।
eva nityārcanaṃ tatra kartavyaṃ rasasiddhaye ।। rasavidyā śivenoktā dātavyā sādhakāya vai । yathoktena vidhānena guruṇā muditātmanā ।। sumuhūrte sunakṣatre candratārābalānvite ।
kalaśaṃ toyasampūrṇaṃ hemaratnaphalairyutam ।। sthāpayed rasaliṅgāgre divyavastreṇa veṣṭitam । gandhapuṣpākṣatair dhūpair naivedyaiśca supūjayet ।। pūjānte havanaṃ kuryādyonikuṇḍe sulakṣaṇe ।
tilājyaiḥ pāyasaiḥ puṣpaiḥ śatapuṣpādikaiḥ pṛthak ।। aghoreṇa rasāṅkuśyā homānte śiṣyamāhvayet । kālinīśaktisaṃyuktaṃ rasasiddhiparāyaṇam ।। yasyāstu kuñcitāḥ keśāḥ śyāmā yā padmalocanā ।
surūpā taruṇī bhinnā vistīrṇajaghanā śubhā ।। saṃkīrṇahṛdayā pīnastanabhāreṇa namritā । cumbanāliṅgasparśakomalā mṛdubhāṣiṇī ।। aśvatthapattrasadṛśayonideśasuśobhitā ।
kṛṣṇapakṣe puṣpavatī sā nārī kālinī smṛtā । rasabandhe prayoge ca uttamā sā rasāyane ।। tadabhāve surūpā tu yā kācit taruṇāṅganā । tasyā deyaṃ trisaptāhaṃ gandhakaṃ ghṛtasaṃyutam ।
karṣaikaikaṃ prabhāte tu sā bhavetkālinīsamā ।। evaṃ śaktiyuto yo asau dīkṣayet taṃ gurūttamaḥ । susnātam abhiṣiñceta mantreṇa kalaśodakaiḥ ।। aghorāmaṅkuśīṃ vidyāṃ dadhyācchiṣyāya sadguruḥ ।
yathāśaktyā suśiṣyeṇa dātavyā gurudakṣiṇā ।। athājñayā gurormantraṃ lakṣaṃ lakṣaṃ pṛthagjapet । oṃ hrāṃ hrīṃ hrūṃ adyoratara prasphuṭa prakaṭa kaha śamaya jāta daha pātaya oṃ hrīṃ hraiṃ hrauṃ hrūṃ aghorāya phaṭ imam aghoramantraṃ tu auṃ kāmarājaśaktibījarasāṅkuśāyai ājñayā vidyāṃ rasāṅkuśām । anayā pūjayeddevīṃ śaktim aṅkuśavidyayā ।।
daśāṃśaṃ juhuyātkuṇḍe trikoṇe hastamātrake । jātipuṣpaṃ trimadhvaktaṃ pūrṇānte kanyakārcanam ।। kṛtvātha praviśecchālāṃ śuddhāṃ liptāṃ savedikām । ṣaṭkoṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tatra sindūreṇa dvihastakam ।।
vedikāyāṃ likhetsamyak tadbahiś cāṣṭapattrakam । kamalaṃ caturasraṃ ca caturdvāraiḥ suśobhitam ।। karṇikāyāṃ nyaset khallaṃ lohajaṃ svarṇalekhitam । tanmadhye rasarājaṃ tu palānāṃ śatamātrakam ।
pañcāśatpañcaviṃśad vā pūjayed rasaliṅgavat ।। vajravaikrāntavajrābhrakāntapāṣāṇaṭaṅkaṇam । bhūnāgaḥ śaktayaścaitāḥ ṣaṭkoṇe pūjayet kramāt ।। gandhatālakakāsīsaśilākaṅkuṣṭhabhūṣaṇam ।
rājāvarto gairikaṃ ca khyātā uparasā amī । pūjyā aṣṭadaleṣvete pūrvādīśānagaṃ kramāt ।। rasakaṃ vimalā tāpyaṃ capalā tuttham añjanam । hiṅgulaṃ sasyakaṃ caiva khyātā ete mahārasāḥ ।
pūrvādīśānaparyantaṃ pattrāgreṣu prapūjayet ।। pūrvadvāre svarṇaraupye dakṣiṇe tāmrasīsake । paścime vaṅgakāntau ca uttare muṇḍatīkṣṇake । sarvametad aghoreṇa pūjayed aṅkuśānvitam ।।
viḍaṃ kāñjikayantrāṇi kṣāramṛllavaṇāni ca । koṣṭhī mūṣā vaṅkanālatuṣāṅgāravanopalāḥ ।। bhastrikā daṇḍikānekā śilā khalvānyulūkhalam । svarṇakāropakaraṇaṃ samastatulanāni ca ।।
mṛtkāṣṭhatāmralohotthapātrāṇi vividhāni ca । divyauṣadhīnāṃ vargāśca rañjakasnehanāni ca । etāni dvārabāhye tu mūlamantreṇa pūjayet ।। vāṅmāyā hrīṃ tataḥ kṣeṃ ca kṣmaśca pañcākṣaro manuḥ ।
anena mantreṇa bhairavaṃ tatra pūjayet । sarveṣāṃ rasasiddhānāṃ nāma saṃkīrtayet tadā ।। vyālācāryaś candrasenaḥ subuddhirnaravāhanaḥ । nāgārjuno ratnaghoṣaḥ surānando yaśodhanaḥ ।।
indraśca māṇḍavyaścarpaṭī śūrasenakaḥ । āgamo nāgabuddhiś ca khaṇḍaḥ kāpāliko mataḥ ।। kāmāris tāntrikaḥ śambhur laṅkālampaṭaśāradau । bāṇāsuro muniśreṣṭho govindaḥ kapilo baliḥ ।।
ete sarve tu sūtendrā rasasiddhā mahābalāḥ । caranti sarvalokeṣu nityā bhogaparāyaṇāḥ ।। saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyākā rasasiddhipradāyakāḥ । vaidyāḥ pūjyāḥ prayatnena tataḥ kuryādrasārcanam ।।
harṣayandvijadevānāṃ tarpayediṣṭadevatāḥ । kumārīyoginīyogīśvarānmelakasādhakān । tarpayet pūjayed bhaktyā yathāśaktyanusārataḥ ।। ityevaṃ sarvasambhārayuktaṃ kuryādrasotsavam ।
sarvavighnapraśāntyarthaṃ sarvepsitaphalapradam ।। anyathā yo vimūḍhātmā mantradīkṣākramādvinā । kartumicchati sūtasya sādhanaṃ guruvarjitaḥ ।। nāsau siddhimavāpnoti yatnakoṭiśatairapi ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena śāstroktāṃ kārayetkriyām ।। samyaksādhanasodyamā guruyutā rājājñayālaṃkṛtā nānākarmaparāṅmukhā rasaparāś cāḍhyā janaiścārthitāḥ । mātrāyantrasupākakarmakuśalāḥ sarvauṣadhe kovidāḥ teṣāṃ sidhyati nānyathā vidhibalācchrīpāradaḥ pāradaḥ ।। rasaśāstraṃ pradātavyaṃ viprāṇāṃ dharmahetave ।
rājñe vaiśyāya vṛddhyarthaṃ dāsyārtham itarasya ca ।। gurau tuṣṭe śivastuṣyecchive tuṣṭe rasastathā । rase tuṣṭe kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sidhyantyeva na saṃśayaḥ ।। rasavidyā dṛḍhaṃ gopyā māturguhyamiva dhruvam ।
bhaved vīryavatī guptā nirvīryā ca prakāśanāt ।। na rogividitaṃ kāryaṃ bahubhirviditaṃ tathā । rogiṇāṃ bahubhirjñātaṃ bhavennirvīryam auṣadham ।। rasaśālāṃ prakurvīta sarvabādhāvivarjite ।
sarvauṣadhimaye deśe ramye kūpasamanvite ।। yakṣatryakṣasahasrākṣadigvibhāge suśobhane । nānopakaraṇopetāṃ prākāreṇa suśobhitām ।। śālāyāḥ pūrvadigbhāge sthāpayed rasabhairavam ।
vahnikarmāṇi cāgneye yāmye pāṣāṇakarma ca ।। nairṛtye śastrakarmāṇi vāruṇe kṣālanādikam । śoṣaṇaṃ vāyukoṇe ca vedhakarmottare tathā । sthāpanaṃ siddhavastūnāṃ prakuryād īśakoṇake ।।
padārthasaṃgrahaḥ kāryo rasasādhanahetukaḥ । sattvapātanakoṣṭhīṃ ca jharatkoṣṭhīṃ suśobhanām ।। bhūmikoṣṭhīṃ calatkoṣṭhīṃ jaladroṇyo apyanekaśaḥ । bhastrikāyugalaṃ tadvannalike vaṃśalohayoḥ ।।
svarṇādimayyaḥ kuṇḍyo vartulapātrāṇi ।। svarṇāyoghoṣaśulvāśmakuṇḍyaś carmakṛtāṃ tathā । karaṇāni vicitrāṇi dravyāṇyapi samāharet ।। kaṇḍaṇī peṣaṇī svalpā droṇīrūpāśca vartulāḥ ।
āyasāstaptakhallāśca mardakāśca tathāvidhāḥ ।। sūkṣmacchidrasahasrāḍhyā dravyagālanahetave । kaṭatrāṇi kaṣāyitacarmakhaṇḍāni ।। cālanī ca kaṭatrāṇi śalākā hi ca kuṇḍalī ।।
cālanī trividhā proktā tatsvarūpaṃ ca kathyate । vaiṇavībhiḥ śalākābhirnirmitā grathitā guṇaiḥ । kīrtitā sā sadā sthūladravyāṇāṃ gālane hitā ।। iyaṃ catuṣkoṇā dīrghacālanī ।।
tatra dīrghāḥ śalākāstiraścīnāśca vaṃśamayyaś catuṣkoṇakāṣṭhapaṭṭikāchidreṣu bahirnirgatāgrāḥ sūtrabaddhāḥ kāryāḥ ।। cūrṇacālanahetośca cālanyanyāpi vaṃśajā ।। karṇikārasya śālmalyā harijātasya kambayā । caturaṅgulavistārayuktayā nirmitā śubhā ।।
kuṇḍalyaratnivistārā chāgacarmābhiveṣṭitā । vājivālāmbarānaddhatalā cālanikā parā । tayā pracālanaṃ kuryāddhartuṃ sūkṣmataraṃ rajaḥ ।। kuṇḍalīṃ kuṇḍalākārāṃ vartulāṃ tṛtīyāṃ cālanīṃ vidadhyāt ।।
vājivālā aśvapucchakeśāḥ ।। ambaraṃ vastram ।। tadanyatareṇānaddhatalā baddhatalā ।। kuṇḍalī cālanyā veṣṭanī ।।
aratnivistārā prasāritakaniṣṭhāṅgulibaddhamuṣṭihastapramāṇāyatā caturaṅgulavistṛtakarṇikārādivalkalanirmitā aratnivistāraveṣṭanī yuktā chāgacarmamaṇḍitā aśvapucchakeśasūkṣmavastraracitataladeśā sūkṣmataradravyacālanārtham aparavidhā cālanītyarthaḥ ।। mūṣāmṛttuṣakārpāsavanopalakapiṣṭakam । trividhaṃ bheṣajaṃ dhātujīvamūlamayaṃ tathā । śarkarā vālukā ।। -d
śarkarā atikṣudrapāṣāṇaravakāḥ ।। -d tadapekṣayā sthūlāḥ śvetāḥ kaṇāḥ sitopalāḥ ।। -d śarkarāśabdena vālukāpi grāhyā ।। -d śikhitrā govaraṃ caiva śarkarā ca sitopalā ।।
sitopalā kaṭhinī phulakaḍī iti bhāṣā ।। śikhitrāḥ pāvakocchiṣṭā aṅgārāḥ kokilā matāḥ ।। dagdhakāṣṭhakaṭhinakhaṇḍānāmeva śikhitrasaṃjñā kokilasaṃjñā ca ।। saṃprati teṣāṃ sāmānyam avāntarabhedaṃ cāha śikhitrā iti ।।
pāvakena vahninā bhuktvā ucchiṣṭāḥ parityaktā aṅgārāḥ śikhitrāḥ kokilāśca matāḥ ।। viśeṣastvittham vahninā bhuktvā svayaṃ tyaktāḥ śikhitrā haṭhāt pratikūlavāyudhūlikṣepamṛttikādinipīḍanādinā yatnena vahnito viyojitā aṅgārāḥ kokilā matā iti ceti ।। te prajvalitā jalena vinā nirvāṇāḥ kṛtā vahnimuktāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। kokilāś cetitāṅgārā nirvāṇāḥ payasā vinā ।।
śikhitralakṣaṇe kokilā uktāḥ ataḥ kokilāśabdasyārtham āha kokilā iti ।। cetitāṅgārāḥ taptāṅgārāḥ payaso vinā svayaṃ nirvāṇāḥ śāntāḥ cet te aṅgārāḥ kokilāḥ matāḥ kokilāḥ kaylā iti bhāṣā ।। piṣṭakaṃ chagaṇaṃ chāṇam upalaṃ cotpalaṃ tathā । giriṇḍopalasāṭhī ca saṃśuṣkacchagaṇābhidhāḥ ।।
caṣakaṃ pānapātraṃ vāṭī glās iti prasiddham ।। kācāyomṛdvarāṭānāṃ kūpikā caṣakāni ca ।। kūpikā kupikā siddhā golā caiva giriṇḍikā ।। caṣakaṃ ca kaṭorī ca vāṭikā khārikā tathā ।
kañcolī grāhikā ceti nāmānyekārthakāni hi ।। kṣudraśiprāḥ kṣudrākārāḥ śuktayaḥ ।। śūrpādiveṇupātrāṇi kṣudraśiprāśca śaṅkhikāḥ । śaṅkhikāḥ kṣudraśaṅkhamayapātrāṇi ।।
kṣurakā nāpitasya śastraviśeṣāḥ ।। pākyo yavakṣāraḥ ।। kṣuraprāśca tathā pākyaḥ yaccānyattatra yujyate । pālikā darvī ।।
karṇikā vilīti mahārāṣṭrabhāṣāyām ।। sā cātra vartulākāradantapaṅktiśikharā grāhyā ।। pālikā karṇikā caiva śākacchedanaśastrakāḥ ।। śālāsammārjanādyaṃ hi rasapākāntakarma yat ।
tatropayogi yaccānyattatsarvaṃ paravidyayā ।। śrīrasāṅkuśayā sarvaṃ mantrayitvā samarcayet । anyathā tadgataṃ tejaḥ parigṛhṇanti bhairavāḥ ।। rasasaṃcintakā vaidyā nighaṇṭujñāśca vārttikāḥ ।
sarvadeśajabhāṣājñāḥ saṃgrāhyāste'pi sādhakaiḥ ।। rasapākāvasānaṃ hi sadāghoraṃ ca jāpayet ।। sodyamāḥ śucayaḥ śūrā baliṣṭhāḥ paricārakāḥ ।। dharmiṣṭhaḥ satyavāgvidvān śivakeśavapūjakaḥ ।
sadayaḥ padmahastaśca saṃyojyo rasavaidyake ।। patākākumbhapāthojamatsyacāpāṅkapāṇikaḥ । anāmādhastharekhāṅkaḥ sa syādamṛtahastavān ।। adeśikaḥ kṛpāmukto lubdho guruvivarjitaḥ ।
kṛṣṇarekhākaro vaidyo dagdhahastaḥ sa ucyate ।। nigrahamantrajñāste yojyā nidhisādhane ।। baliṣṭhāḥ satyavantaśca raktākṣāḥ kṛṣṇavigrahāḥ । bhūtatrāsanavidyāśca te yojyā balisādhane ।।
nirlobhāḥ satyavaktāro devabrāhmaṇapūjakāḥ । yaminaḥ pathyabhoktāro yojanīyā rasāyane ।। dhanavanto vadānyāśca sarvopaskarasaṃyutāḥ । guruvākyaratā nityaṃ dhātuvādeṣu te śubhāḥ ।।
tattadauṣadhanāmajñāḥ śucayo vañcanojjhitāḥ । nānāviṣayabhāṣājñāste matā bheṣajāhṛtau ।। śucīnāṃ satyavākyānāmāstikānāṃ manasvinām । saṃdehojjhitacittānāṃ rasaḥ sidhyati sarvadā ।।
daśāṣṭakriyayā siddho raso'sau sādhakottamaḥ । hā raso naṣṭamityuktvā sevetānyatra taṃ rasam ।। rasasiddho bhavenmartyo dātā bhoktā na yācakaḥ । jarāmukto jagatpūjyo divyakāntiḥ sadā sukhī ।।
kathyate somadevena mugdhavaidyaprabuddhaye । paribhāṣā rasendrasya śāstraiḥ siddhaiśca bhāṣitā ।। ardhaṃ siddharasasya tailaghṛtayorlehasya bhāgo'ṣṭamaḥ saṃsiddhākhilalohacūrṇavaṭakādīnāṃ tathā saptamaḥ । yo dīyeta bhiṣagvarāya gadibhirnirdiśya dhanvantarim sarvārogyasukhāptaye nigadito bhāgaḥ sa dhanvantareḥ ।।
bhaiṣajyakrīṇitadravyabhāgo apy ekādaśo hi yaḥ । vaṇigbhyo gṛhyate vaidyai rudrabhāgaḥ sa ucyate ।। pragṛhyādhikarudrāṃśaṃ yo asamīcīnam auṣadham । dāpayellubdhadhīr vaidyaḥ sa syād viśvāsaghātakaḥ ।।
dhātubhir gandhakādyaiśca nirdravair mardito rasaḥ । suślakṣṇaḥ kajjalābho asau kajjalītyabhidhīyate ।। atha kajjalīlakṣaṇamāha dhātubhiriti ।। dhātavaśca ।
svarṇaṃ rūpyaṃ ca tāmraṃ ca raṅgaṃ jasadameva ca । sīsaṃ lohaṃ ca saptaite dhātavo girisaṃbhavāḥ । iti ।। ādyaśabdena haritālamanaḥśilādisaṃgrahaḥ ।।
cakāreṇopadhātusaṃgrahaḥ ।। teṣāṃ bhāgo rasasamo viṣamo vā yathopadeśaṃ grāhyaḥ ।। saiva kajjalī dravaṃ dattvā marditā cedrasapaṅkasaṃjñāṃ labhate ।। kajjalyupayogaśca rasasindūrādividhānārthaṃ bodhyaḥ ।।
rasapaṅkopayogaṃ trailokyasundararasādividhānārthaṃ vakṣyati ।। sadravā marditā saiva rasapaṅka iti smṛtā ।। arkāṃśatulyād rasato atha gandhān niṣkārdhatulyāt truṭiśo abhi khalle । arkātape tīvratare vimardyāt piṣṭī bhavet sā navanītarūpā ।।
atha piṣṭīlakṣaṇamāha arkāṃśeti ।। niṣkārdhatulyānniṣkārdharūpabhāgamitād ityarthaḥ ।। gandhakād arkāṃśatulyād rasato'rkaśabdo dvādaśasaṃkhyābodhakaḥ ।। tatsaṃkhyākā ye'ṃśā bhāgā niṣkārdhātmakā bhāgāstattulyād rasāt pāradāt ।।
niṣkārdhetyupalakṣaṇaṃ gṛhītakiṃcinmānasya ।। tena gandhakasya yo bhāgastato dvādaśaguṇitaḥ pāradabhāgo'tra grāhya ityarthaḥ ।। yathoktabhāgam ubhayaṃ pṛthaggṛhītvā tīvre'rkātape lohe khalve truṭiśa īṣanmānena punaḥ punardattvā mardanānnavanītarūpā mṛdulā navanītākhyā ca piṣṭī bhavati ।। atra navanītākhyo gandhako bhakṣyaḥ pāradaśca bhakṣakaḥ ।।
sa tu nānārūpapiṣṭīṣu samāna eva ।। ato bhakṣyanāmnā bhedabodhakeneyaṃ navanītākhyetyabhidhīyate ।। asyā nāmāntaraṃ gandhakapiṣṭīti ।। khalle vimardya gandhena dugdhena saha pāradam ।
peṣaṇāt piṣṭatāṃ yāti sā piṣṭīti matā paraiḥ ।। caturthāṃśasuvarṇena rasena ghṛṣṭiṣaṣṭikā । bhavet pātanapiṣṭī sā rasasyottamasiddhidā ।। atha pātanapiṣṭīlakṣaṇamāha caturthāṃśeti ।।
caturthāṃśaṃ śuddhaṃ svarṇacūrṇaṃ pāradamadhye prakṣipya taptalohakhalve amlarasena jambīrādijena yāmaparyantaṃ dviyāmaparyantaṃ vā mardanena saṃjātā cūrṇarūpā sā hemapiṣṭikāpi pātanopayogena siddhikaratvāt pātanapiṣṭir ityabhidhīyate ।। tādṛśīṃ piṣṭiṃ kṛtvā pātanāyantre adhasthapātrāntastala ūrdhvabhājane vā liptvā praharacatuṣṭayaparyantam agniyogenordhvaṃ pāradaṃ pātayet ।। tadanantaraṃ pāradāt pṛthagbhūtvādhobhāgasthatatsvarṇacūrṇam ūrdhvalagnapāradaṃ ca yantrād bahirniṣkāsyaikīkṛtya punastaptalohakhalve'mlena rasena pūrvavanmardayitvā pūrvavat pātayet ।। evaṃ śatadhā pātanena kṣīṇo gatirahito nirdoṣaḥ pāradaḥ sthiro'gnisaho bhavati ।।
tataśca bījādijāraṇakrameṇālpāyāsenaiva dehalohakaratvarūpottamasiddhipradaśca bhavatītyarthaḥ ।। rūpyaṃ vā jātarūpaṃ vā rasagandhādibhirhatam । samutthitaṃ ca bahuśaḥ sā kṛṣṭī hematārayoḥ ।। jātarūpaṃ suvarṇam ।।
samutthitam iti antarbhūtaṇyarthaprayogas tena samutthāpitaṃ śoṣitamityartha ūrdhvapātanāyantre sādhitamityartho vā ।। sā utthāpanakriyā ।। kṛṣṭīti ।। svarṇaraupyayoḥ sā kriyā kṛṣṭīti bodhyam ।।
rasādibhiḥ saha svarṇaṃ vā raupyaṃ vā kenacinmārakadravyeṇa saṃmardya bahuśaḥ ātape śoṣayed athavā rasagandhādibhirmāritaṃ svarṇaṃ raupyaṃ vā bahuvāram ūrdhvapātanayantreṇa samutthāpayet sā kriyā kṛṣṭī bodhyā ।। piṣṭīṃ kṣipet suvarṇāntar na varṇo hīyate tayā ।। pūrvarītyā kṛtayā suvarṇaraupyayor anyatarakṛṣṭyā saha suvarṇaṃ saṃmardya puṭanena svarṇasya varṇānyatā na jāyate ।। svarṇakṛṣṭyā kṛtaṃ bījaṃ rasasya parirañjanam ।।
bījaṃ nirvāpaṇaviśeṣeṇa ityādinā vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇo dhātuviśeṣāṇāṃ vicitrasaṃskāraviśeṣaḥ ।। uktaprakāreṇaiva kṛtasvarṇakṛṣṭīnirmitaṃ bījaṃ pāradaṃ rañjayet ।। atha kṛṣṭīlakṣaṇamāha rūpyamiti ।। jātarūpyaṃ suvarṇam ।।
ādiśabdena mākṣikahiṅgulādiparigrahaḥ ।। tairmāritaṃ punaḥ punaḥ pañcamitrasaṃskāreṇa prakṛtyavasthāpannaṃ kṛtam ।। evaṃ saptavāraṃ daśavāraṃ votthāpitasvarṇatāraṃ ca krameṇa hemakṛṣṭī tārakṛṣṭī cābhidhīyate ।। rasagandhādiyogena malavyapohanād ujjvalam utkṛṣṭaṃ sārūpyaṃ svarṇaṃ tāraṃ cetyarthaḥ ।।
tāṃ svarṇakṛṣṭīṃ drute hīnavarṇasvarṇe kṣipet ।। tena kṣepeṇa varṇo na hīyate tatsvarṇaṃ hīnavarṇaṃ na dṛśyate ।। pūrṇavarṇaṃ dṛśyata ityarthaḥ ।। evameva hīnavarṇatāre tārakṛṣṭyāḥ kṣepeṇāpi tāraṃ pūrṇavarṇaṃ bhavatītyartho'pi bodhyaḥ ।।
kṛtaṃ kalpitaṃ saṃskṛtam ityarthaḥ ।। bījaṃ śuddhaṃ svarṇotpādakaṃ lohadhātvādipāradasya pītavarṇatvakaraṃ bhavet ।। rasahṛdaye'ṣṭamāvabodhe pāradasya kṛṣṭimapi pūjyapādā udājahruḥ ।। tāmraṃ tīkṣṇasamāyuktaṃ drutaṃ nikṣipya bhūriśaḥ ।
sagandhalakucadrāve nirgataṃ varalohakam ।। varalohaprastutaprakāramāha tāmramiti ।। tīkṣṇasamāyuktaṃ tīkṣṇalauhasaṃyuktam ।। bhūriśaḥ saptavārān ityarthaḥ ।।
tīkṣṇalauhaṃ tāmraṃ ca agnisaṃtāpena dravīkṛtya gandhakacūrṇamiśritalakucarase nikṣiped ghanībhūtaṃ taddvayamuttolya punaḥ drāvayitvā pūrvarase nikṣiped evaṃ saptavārān ।। drutamityatra mṛtam iti pāṭho mṛtaṃ bhasmībhūtam ।। evaṃ prakriyayā tasmād utkṛṣṭalauhaṃ nirgamiṣyatīti ।। tena raktīkṛtaṃ svarṇaṃ hemaraktītyudāhṛtam ।।
nikṣiptā sā drute svarṇe varṇotkarṣavidhāyinī । tārasya rañjanī cāpi bījarāgavidhāyinī ।। evameva prakartavyā tāraraktī manoharā । rañjanī khalu rūpyasya bījānāmapi rañjanī ।।
atha hemaraktītāraraktyor lakṣaṇaṃ phalaṃ cāha tāmramiti ।। tīkṣṇalohena samabhāgena saṃyuktam ekīkṛtaṃ tāmraṃ bahuvāraṃ drutaṃ kṛtvā gandhakasahite lakucarase nirvāpayet ।। tadvallohamiti khyātaṃ tārasya rañjanī drute tasminnikṣepeṇetyarthaḥ ।। tāraraktīkaraṇārthaṃ tu varalohena tāram eva dhamanenaikīkṛtya raktīkṛtaṃ kāryaṃ sāpi rūpyasya bījānāṃ ca rañjanī raktavarṇotpādikā ।।
mṛtena vā baddharasena vānyallohena vā sādhitamanyaloham । sitaṃ ca pītatvamupāgataṃ taddalaṃ hi candrānalayoḥ prasiddham ।। māsakṛtabaddhena rasena saha yojitam । sādhitaṃ vānyalohena sitaṃ pītaṃ ca taddalam ।।
saṃprati tāradalasya svarṇadalasya ca lakṣaṇamāha mṛteneti ।। mṛtena bhasmībhūtena pāradena yena kenaciddravyeṇa baddho yaḥ pāradastena baddhapāradena mṛtena lohena vā sādhitaṃ saṃskṛtam anyalohaṃ vijātīyaṃ lohaṃ sitatvam upāgataṃ prāptaṃ śvetavarṇaviśiṣṭam athavā pītatvam upāgataṃ prāptaṃ pītavarṇaviśiṣṭaṃ bhavet ।। tatkrameṇa candradalam analadalaṃ svarṇadalaṃ śāstre prasiddham ।। analaḥ svarṇam ।।
kṛtrimarajataṃ kṛtrimasvarṇaṃ cetyarthaḥ ।। ravā iti nāmnā loke prasiddham ।। mākṣikeṇa hataṃ tāmraṃ daśavāraṃ samutthitam । tadvadviśuddhanāgaṃ hi dvitayaṃ taccatuṣpalam ।।
nīlāñjanahataṃ bhūyaḥ saptavāraṃ samutthitam । iti saṃsiddhametaddhi śulvanāgaṃ prakīrtyate ।। śulvanāgamāha mākṣikeṇeti ।। svarṇamākṣikeṇa saha māritaṃ tāmraṃ tathā sīsakaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak daśavāraṃ samutthāpitaṃ kṛtvā tayoḥ pratyekaṃ catuṣpalaṃ ādāya ekīkuryāttataḥ tadubhayaṃ bhūyaḥ nīlāñjanena saha bhasmīkṛtya saptavāraṃ samutthāpayed evaṃ ca tayoḥ śulvanāga iti saṃjñā jāyate iti ।।
saṃprati śulbanāgalakṣaṇamāha mākṣikeṇeti ।। samabhāgamākṣikeṇa māritaṃ tāmraṃ pañcamitrasaṃskāreṇa samutthitaṃ kuryāt ।। evaṃ daśavāraṃ kṛtvā tadvattāmravanmākṣikeṇaiva māritaṃ viśuddhaṃ nāgaṃ tadubhayaṃ mithaḥ samaṃ catuṣpalamitaṃ gṛhītvā punar nīlāñjanena samabhāgena māritaṃ pañcamitrasaṃskāreṇa punarutthāpitaṃ kuryāt ।। evaṃ saptavāraṃ māraṇapūrvakotthāpanena saṃśuddham etaddravyadvaṃdvaṃ rasaśāstre śulbanāgamiti kīrtitam ।।
sādhitastena sūtendro vadane vidhṛto nṛṇām । nihanti māsamātreṇa mehavyūhaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। tadupayogamāha sādhita iti ।। taccūrṇaṃ pāradena samabhāgena śuddhena sahājamūtreṇa saṃmardya vajramūṣāyāṃ dhmānena jātaṃ khoṭaṃ śodhanagaṇena saha dhmānācchuddhaṃ kṛtvā taṃ khoṭabaddhaṃ pāradaṃ mukhamadhye yo dhārayettasya mehasamūhanāśo bhavet ।।
pathyāśanasya varṣeṇa palitavalibhiḥ saha । gṛdhradṛṣṭirlasatpuṣṭiḥ sarvārogyasamanvitaḥ ।। lohaṃ lohāntare kṣiptaṃ dhmātaṃ nirvāpitaṃ drave । pāṇḍupītaprabhaṃ jātaṃ piñjarītyabhidhīyate ।।
piñjarīlakṣaṇamāha lohamiti ।। yathā jasadaṃ mūṣāyāṃ tāmre nikṣipya dhmānenaikībhūtaṃ patrajādyauṣadhīrase pītavargajarase vā nikṣepātpittalaṃ bhavati tadvadanyadapi tādṛgvarṇaṃ saṃkīrṇalohaṃ piñjarīvācyaṃ bhavati ।। sā oṣadhīpatrajā śabdavācyā ।। yasyā utpattau kāraṇaṃ bījasthāne patrameva bhavati ।।
cīritapattrā hrasvakṣupaviśeṣarūpā ceyamupavana utpadyate ।। bhāgāḥ ṣoḍaśa tārasya tathā dvādaśa bhāsvataḥ । ekatrāvartitāstena candrārkamiti kathyate ।। candrārkasaṃjñāmāha bhāgā iti ।।
bhāsvataḥ tāmrasya ।। ekatrāvartitāḥ ekasminneva pātre yugapad dravīkṛtya āloḍitāḥ ।। tena tathā āloḍanena ।। candrārkaṃ lakṣayati bhāgā iti ।।
āvartitā dhmānenaikībhūtarasarūpā ityarthaḥ ।। bhāsvatastāmrasya ।। candrārkasya khoṭabaddharasena vedhātkanakotpattiśca rasasāre'bhihitā ।। sādhyalohe anyalohaṃ cetprakṣiptaṃ vaṅkanālataḥ ।
nirvāpaṇaṃ tu tatproktaṃ vaidyairnirvāhaṇaṃ khalu ।। kṣipennirvāpaṇaṃ dravyaṃ nirvāhye samabhāgikam । āvāhyaṃ vāpanīye ca bhāge dṛṣṭe ca dṛṣṭavat ।। atha nirvāhalakṣaṇamāha sādhyaloha iti ।।
yasyāṃ kriyāyāṃ sādhyalohe nirvāhye lohe drute sati tasmiṃstatrānyalohaṃ vaṅkanālataḥ prakṣiptaṃ vaṅkanālajadhmānenaiva drutaṃ kṛtvā prakṣiptaṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ ।। vaṅkanāletyuktyā bhastrādijadhmānavyāvṛttiḥ ।। nirvāhaṇam ekīkaraṇamiti yāvat ।। nirvāpaṇaṃ nirvāhaṇaṃ cetyanarthāntaram ।।
ekīkaraṇārthakanirvāpaṇaśabdaprayogastu saṃprati nopalabhyate ।। kiṃtu sarvatra tadarthaṃ nirvāhaṇaśabda eva prayukto dṛśyate ।। etacca nirvāhaṇaṃ prāyo bījādisaṃskārārthaṃ kriyate ।। yathā pāradodare bījānāṃ garbhadrāvaṇayogyatāsaṃpādanārthaṃ nirvāhaṇasaṃskāraṃ vyājahāra rasahṛdaye ।
mṛtanāgaṃ mṛtavaṅgaṃ mṛtavaraśulbaṃ mṛtaṃ tathā tīkṣṇam । ekaikaṃ hemavare śatanirvyūḍhaṃ dravati garbhe ca ।। iti ।। ekaguṇasvarṇe nāgādyanyatamaṃ śataguṇanirvāhitaṃ kāryam ityarthaḥ ।।
evaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ svarṇaṃ varabījaṃ bhavati ।। atha nirvāpaṇadravyabhāgānuktisthāne taddravyasya kiyadbhāgaprakṣepaḥ kāryastadāha kṣipediti ।। kṣipennirvāhayedityarthaḥ ।। kṣepasāmānyād anuktāvāvāpadravyamānam apyāha āvāpyamiti ।।
āvāpalakṣaṇam asminnevādhyāye vakṣyati ।। vāpanīye lohādye drute dravye ।। tatra bhāge dṛṣṭa ukte tu dṛṣṭavaduktabhāgamitameva tannirvāhaṇadravyam āvāpadravyaṃ ca kṣipet ।। mṛtaṃ tarati yattoye lohaṃ vāritaraṃ hi tat ।।
mṛtalohasya bodhakānāṃ vividhapāribhāṣikaśabdānāṃ lakṣaṇānyāha mṛtamiti ।। tallohaṃ vāritaram ucyate yanmṛtaṃ sattoye prakṣiptaṃ taratīti ।। aṅguṣṭhatarjanīghṛṣṭaṃ yat tad rekhāntare viśet । mṛtalohaṃ taduddiṣṭaṃ rekhāpūrṇābhidhānataḥ ।।
rekhāpūrṇalauhalakṣaṇamāha aṅguṣṭheti ।। tadrekhāntare tayoḥ tarjanyaṅguṣṭhayoḥ rekhāntare rekhāvakāśe aṅguṣṭhatarjanībhyāṃ gharṣaṇe kṛte yatra lauhe tayoraṅgulyoḥ rekhāsamūhaḥ aṅkito bhavedityarthaḥ ।। tallohaṃ rekhāpūrṇamucyate yanmṛtam aṅguṣṭhatarjanīmadhye saṃmarditaṃ tayoḥ sūkṣmarekhāntaraṃ praviśediti ।। guḍaguñjāsukhasparśamadhvājyaiḥ saha yojitam ।
nāyāti prakṛtiṃ dhmānād apunarbhavam ucyate ।। nirutthalauhalakṣaṇamāha guḍeti ।। sukhasparśaḥ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ nirutthīkārakamitrapañcakavarge ṭaṅkaṇaśabdagrahaṇāt yaduktaṃ rasendrasāre । madhusarpistathā guñjā ṭaṅkaṇaṃ guggulustathā ।
mitrapañcakametattu gaṇitaṃ dhātumelane ।। iti ।। mitrapañcakoktagugguloḥ kāryamatra guḍena saṃpādanīyamiti ।। prakṛtiṃ svarūpam ।।
apunarbhavam apunarutthānaṃ nirutthamiti yāvat ।। atha pūrṇamṛtaṃ talloham apunarbhavam ucyate ।। yat pratyekaṃ samabhāgair guḍādibhiḥ samastaiḥ saha miśritaṃ piṇḍīkṛtaṃ mūṣāmadhye prakṣipya dhmānena prakṛtiṃ pūrvāvasthām āmalohabhāvaṃ na prāpnuyāditi ।। tasyopari guru dravyaṃ dhānyaṃ copanayeddhruvam ।
haṃsavat tīryate vāriṇyuttamaṃ parikīrtitam ।। athottamākhyamṛtalohalakṣaṇamāha yadvā pūrṇamṛtaṃ yallohaṃ vāritaraṃ svapṛṣṭha upanītaṃ dhānyaṃ dhārayati ।। dhānyabhāraṃ sahata ityarthaḥ ।। tatra lohe taddhānyaṃ kathaṃ tarati tadupamayāha yathā jale haṃsaviśeṣāstaranti tadvat tathā dhānyabhārasahaṃ tanmṛtaloham uttamam iti nāmnā śāstre kīrtitam ।।
atra bahuṣu pustakeṣu ūnamaṃ parikīrtitam ityapi pāṭhaḥ ।। tasya svayam ūnam ūnabhāraṃ laghvapi yallohaṃ svāpekṣayā gurudravyaṃ gurudhānyaṃ vā māti sahata iti vyutpattyā kliṣṭārthabodhakaḥ sa pāṭho nātipriyaḥ ।। raupyeṇa saha saṃyuktaṃ dhmātaṃ raupyeṇa cel laget । tadā nirutthamityuktaṃ lohaṃ tad apunarbhavam ।।
nirutthasya lakṣaṇāntaramāha raupyeṇeti ।। raupyaṃ lauhaṃ ca ekatra saṃsthāpya bhastrayā dhmāpanena yadi parasparaṃ miśrībhavet tadāpi nirutthaṃ jñeyam ।। athāpunarbhavākhyamṛtalohasyaiva nirutthasaṃjñāprāpakaṃ lakṣaṇamāha raupyeṇeti ।। saṃyuktaṃ melāpakamadhvājyaṃ dattvā mūṣāyāṃ saṃyojitaṃ na laget na sajjetaikībhāvaṃ na prāpnuyād ityarthaḥ ।।
ekībhāvaśca raupyamānavṛddhyā bodhyaḥ ।। spaṣṭīkṛtaṃ caitad rasasaṃketakalikāyām । lohamadhvājyagaṃ tāraṃ svapramāṇaṃ bhavedyadā । tadā lohaṃ nirutthaṃ syādanyathā sādhayetpunaḥ ।।
iti ।। tāraṃ śuddhatāram ।। nirvāpaṇaviśeṣeṇa tattadvarṇaṃ bhavedyadā । mṛdulaṃ citrasaṃskāraṃ tadbījamiti kathyate ।।
bījamāha nirvāpaṇeti ।। pūrvanirdiṣṭasādhyalohe tattallohamārakānyalohanikṣeparūpanirvāhaṇākhyasaṃskāraviśeṣeṇa yadā sādhyalohaṃ prakṣiptalauhavarṇaṃ bhavet tadā mṛdulaṃ sukhasparśaṃ citrasaṃskāram āhitāpūrvaguṇāntaraṃ tat bījamiti jñeyam ।। atha jāraṇāsaṃskāre prakṣepārhasya bījasya lakṣaṇamāha nirvāhaṇeti ।। nirvāhyate prakṣepeṇaikīkriyate aneneti vyutpattyā nirvāhaṇaśabdena nirvāhakaṃ dravyaṃ grāhyam ।।
prakṣepeṇa guṇaviśeṣotpādanapūrvakaikībhāvasāmānyācca tena śabdena vāpanadravyasyāpi saṃgrahaḥ kāryaḥ ।। etadabhiprāyeṇaiva nirvāpaṇaviśeṣeṇetyapi pāṭho dṛśyate ।। tena nirvāhaṇena nirvyūḍhaṃ yadbījopādānarasalohādi tattadvarṇaṃ nirvāhaṇadravyasya samānavarṇaṃ śāstranirdiṣṭavarṇaṃ ca bhavati ।। vāpanadravyeṇa mṛdu ca bhavettathā sattvabhasmotpādakavidhibhyāṃ ca prāptamārdavam ।।
tathā kṛto vicitrasaṃskāro garbhadrāvako raktavargakaṣāye niṣecanarūpo melāpakadravyasaṃyogādiśca yasyetyevaṃguṇaviśiṣṭaṃ rasaśāstre siddhabījamityabhidhīyate ।। bījaṃ dvividhaṃ pītaṃ sitaṃ ceti bhedāt ।। tadapi pratyekaṃ dvividham ।। akṛtrimaṃ kṛtrimaṃ ca ।।
yaddhi khanisambhūtaṃ śuddhaṃ svarṇaṃ rajataṃ vā tad akṛtrimam ।। yattu dhāturasoparasasaṃyogakriyāviśeṣajanitasvarṇarajatotpādanayogyatāsaṃpannaṃ pītaṃ svarṇarītyādi śvetaṃ vaṅgādi tatkṛtrimam ityācakṣate ।। tadapi pratyekaṃ dvividham ।। śuddhaṃ miśraṃ ca ।।
śuddhamekaikaṃ miśraṃ mithaḥ saṃkīrṇam ।। punarapi sarvam etattridhā bhavati ।। kalpitaṃ rañjitaṃ pakvaṃ ca ।। tatra tatkalpitaśabdavācyaṃ yacchuddharasoparasaśuddhamāritaṃ mithaḥ saṃyuktaṃ miśraṃ vā lohādidvaṃdvīkṛtam ekaikaṃ sattvakaraṇavidhinā nirvāhaṇena dvaṃdvamelāpakavidhinā ca militaṃ śuddhaṃ jātamārdavaṃ tad evaikībhāvaṃ vrajati ca raktādivargeṣu secanena prāptavarṇaṃ rañjitasaṃjñakaṃ bhavati ।।
nirvāhaṇena hemaśeṣakṛtaṃ tāraśeṣakṛtaṃ vā yadbījaṃ bhūdharayantrādiṣu puṭitaṃ tatpakvabījaṃ vadanti ।। evaṃ cedamuktalakṣaṇaṃ sarvabījānāṃ saṃgrāhakaṃ bodhyam ।। atra rasoparasānāṃ śodhanaṃ tu sūryāvartādigaṇena kuryāt ।। śaśaraktabhāvanayā kāntaṃ śudhyati ।।
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ patraṃ ca lavaṇakṣārāmlaravisnuhīkṣīrair liptaṃ dhmātaṃ paścānnirguṇḍīrase bahuvāraṃ niṣecitaṃ sacchudhyati ।। nāgavaṅgaghoṣatāmrāṇi tu prataptāni nirguṇḍīrasasekais tanmūlarajaḥpravāpaiśca śudhyanti ।। sarvo'pi lohaḥ pratapto mākṣīkadaradavāpena bahuvāraṃ kṛtena śudhyati ।। rasoparasānāṃ sattvāni mūloktavidhinā pātayet ।।
saṃprati bījanirvāhaṇavidhiṃ rasahṛdayoktaṃ vakṣyāmi ।। idameva vinirdiṣṭaṃ vaidyairuttaraṇaṃ khalu । saṃspṛṣṭalohayorekalohasya parināśanam ।। uttaraṇamāha idamiti ।।
idaṃ saṃsṛṣṭalohayor ityādinā vakṣyamāṇarūpam ityarthaḥ ।। uttaraṇamiti saṃjñāviśeṣaḥ ।। saṃsṛṣṭeti miśritalauhayoḥ ekalohasya parināśanaṃ dhmāpanādikriyāviśeṣeṇa ekasmāt anyat pṛthakkṛtya bhasmīkaraṇam ekasmād anyasya bahirniṣkāśanaṃ vā ।। pradhmātaṃ vaṅkanālena tattāḍanamudāhṛtam ।।
tāḍanamāha pradhmātamiti ।। tat uttaraṇakriyāniṣpannaṃ saṃsṛṣṭalauhayorekaloham ।। atha tāḍanasaṃjñāmāha saṃsṛṣṭeti ।। parisādhanaṃ dhmānenāvaśeṣakārakaṃ yadvaṅkanālena pradhmātaṃ prakarṣeṇa dhmānaṃ kriyate tadrasaśāstre tāḍanaśabdena kathitam ।।
yathā ghoṣādvaṅgaṃ vināśya tāmrasyāvaśeṣārthaṃ dhmānaṃ tacca gārākoṣṭhyāṃ kāryam ।। cūrṇābhraṃ śālisaṃyuktaṃ vastrabaddhaṃ hi kāñjike । niryātaṃ mardanādvastrāddhānyābhramiti kathyate ।। kṣārāmladrāvakairyuktaṃ dhmātamākarakoṣṭhake ।
yastato nirgataḥ sāraḥ sattvamityabhidhīyate ।। sattvamāha kṣāreti ।। kṣāraḥ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ lauhaśodhakatvāt amlaḥ kāñjikādikaṃ drāvakaḥ guñjāṭaṅkaṇamadhvājyaguḍāḥ drāvakapañcakāḥ ityuktasvarūpaḥ taiḥ ।। ākarakoṣṭhike koṣṭhikāyantre ।।
sāraḥ sthirāṃśaḥ prasādabhāga iti yāvat ।। sattvalakṣaṇamāha kṣārāmleti ।। kṣāro yavakṣārādiḥ ।। amlaṃ jambīrarasādi ।।
drāvakaṃ guḍagugguluguñjādi ।। drāvako gaṇo vakṣyamāṇaḥ ।। pañcājaṃ pañcagavyādi ।। matsyādipiṇḍīdravyaṃ ca tadyuktaṃ tena piṇḍīkṛtaṃ rasoparasādi dravyam ।।
ākarakoṣṭhaka ākaro vakṣyamāṇaḥ ।। koṣṭhikā varṇanasthānagranthaḥ ।। tatrokte yogye koṣṭhe koṣṭhayantre aṅgārakoṣṭhyādau ca mūṣāyāṃ prakṣipya yadā bhastrāvaṅkanālādinā dhmātaṃ syāttadā tato dravyād dravarūpo yaḥ sāro nirgacchati pṛthagākāreṇa nipatati tatsattvamucyate ।। koṣṭhikāśikharāpūrṇaiḥ kokilair dhmānayogataḥ ।
ākaṇṭhamanuprāptair ekakolīsako mataḥ ।। ekakolīsakamāha koṣṭhiketi ।। koṣṭhikāyantrāgrabhāgaparyantam aṅgārairāpūrya dhmāpanavaśāt māraṇīyadravyaiḥ mūṣākaṇṭhaparyantamāgataiḥ upalakṣito yat karma ekakolīsakākhyaḥ kriyāviśeṣo mataḥ ।। atha dhmānakriyāyā mānaviśeṣajñānārthaṃ kṛtāyāḥ kolīsakasaṃjñāyā lakṣaṇamāha koṣṭhikāśikhareti ।।
śikharaparyantaṃ paripūrṇakokilānāṃ dhmānena mūṣākaṇṭhaparyantaṃ yadāpacayo bhavati tāvaddhmānasyaikakolīsaka iti saṃjñā ।। asyā eva nāliśaketi paryāyāntaram ।। drāvaṇe sattvapāte ca mādhukāḥ khādirāḥ śubhāḥ । durdrāve vaṃśajāste tu svedane bādarāḥ śubhāḥ ।।
vidyādharākhyayantrasthād ārdrakadrāvamarditāt । samākṛṣṭo raso yo asau hiṅgulākṛṣṭa ucyate ।। atha hiṅgulākṛṣṭarasamāha vidyādhareti ।। vidyādharayantraṃ dvividhaṃ nirjalaṃ sajalaṃ ca ।।
tatra prathamaṃ kanakasundaraprabhṛtirasānām ūrdhvabhāge puṭanārtham upayujyate ।। tacca nyubjordhvapātreṇa saṃpuṭitam ।। yattu dvitīyam uttānapātraghaṭitaṃ tadatra vidyādharaśabdena grāhyam ।। ārdrakamarditād ityasyāgre hiṅgulāditi śeṣaḥ ।।
svalpatālayutaṃ kāṃsyaṃ vaṅkanālena tāḍitam । muktaraṅgaṃ hi tattāmraṃ ghoṣākṛṣṭam udāhṛtam ।। ghoṣākṛṣṭasya lakṣaṇamāha svalpeti ।। tāḍitaṃ paridhmātam ।।
atra tālaḥ svalpaśabdena kāṃsyasya caturthāṃśena grāhyaḥ ।। raṅgasya tāmrātpṛthagbhūtvā vināśārthaṃ tadupayogo bodhyaḥ ।। tīkṣṇanīlāñjanopetaṃ dhmātaṃ hi bahuśo dṛḍham । kṛṣṇaṃ drutadrāvaṃ varanāgaṃ taducyate ।।
varanāgalakṣaṇamāha tīkṣṇeti ।। atra viśeṣyapadollekhābhāve api varanāga iti saṃjñābalādeva tīkṣṇanīlāñjanopetamityatra nāgamiti viśeṣyapadaṃ śeṣaḥ bodhyaḥ ।। tīkṣṇalauhanīlāñjanasaṃyuktaṃ yat sīsakaṃ bahuvāraṃ dṛḍham ādhmātaṃ sat sukomalaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ drutadrāvaṃ ca syāt tat sīsakaṃ varanāgaṃ bodhyam ।। tīkṣṇamiti pṛthak pāṭhe nīlāñjanaṃ tīkṣṇalauhaṃ ca ityarthaḥ ।।
varanāgasya lakṣaṇamāha tīkṣṇamiti ।। samabhāganīlāñjanasaṃyutaṃ tīkṣṇalohaṃ samabhāgena ṭaṅkaṇaṃ dattvāndhamūṣāyāṃ dṛḍhaṃ dhmātaṃ sadyadā nāgāpekṣayāpyatimṛdu kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ śīghradrāvaṃ ca bhavettadaitad varanāgam ucyate ।। arkāpāmārgakadalībhasmatoyena lolayet ।। tadvastragālitaṃ grāhyaṃ svacchatoyaṃ tadātape ।।
mṛdukṛṣṭaṃ drutadrāvamiti pāṭhe dhmātvā mūṣātaḥ kṛṣṭaṃ bahirākṛṣṭaṃ śītaṃ sadapi saṃjātamārdavam agniyogena śīghradrāvaṃ ca bhavedityarthaḥ ।। nāgādvaraṃ śreṣṭham etad varanāgam iti ।। uttarapadasya pūrvanipātena siddho'yaṃ śabdaḥ ।। asyopayogaṃ tvasthirāṇāṃ kharparādisattvānāṃ sthirīkaraṇārthaṃ pūjyapādā udājahrū rasasāre ।।
tatprakārastu dvitīyādhyāye'tra rasakasattvavidhivyākhyāyāṃ prakāśita eva ।। nāgaṃ nīlāñjanopetamiti pāṭhastu prāmādika eva ।। sattvānāṃ hi sthirīkaraṇe nāgasyānupayogāditi bodhyam ।। mṛtasya punarudbhūtiḥ samproktotthāpanākhyayā ।।
utthāpanaśabdārthamāha mṛtasyeti ।। pāradarasoparasalohādīnām atimūrchitānāṃ prākṛtaguṇakriyāsahitānāṃ vā punarudbhūtiḥ punaḥ pūrvavat sthānāpannatvam utthāpanam ityabhidhīyate ।। utthāpanāmāha mṛtasyeti ।। punarudbhūtiḥ yantrādiyogena svarūpāpādanam ityarthaḥ ।।
drutadravyasya nikṣepo drave taḍḍhālanaṃ matam ।। ḍhālanasaṃjñāṃ lakṣayati drutadravyasyeti ।। yathā varalohakavidhau satīkṣṇatāmrasya dhmānena drutasya lakucadrāve nikṣepo'trādhyāye prāguktaḥ sa ḍhālanaśabdena paribhāṣyate ।। atha capalo dvividhaḥ ।।
pāṣāṇaviśeṣaḥ kṛtrimo dhāturūpaśca ।। tatra pāṣāṇaviśeṣo dvitīyādhyāya uktaḥ ।। triṃśatpalamitaṃ nāgaṃ bhānudugdhena marditam । vimardya puṭayettāvadyāvatkarṣāvaśeṣitam ।।
na tatpuṭasahasreṇa kṣayamāyāti sarvathā । capalo'yaṃ samādiṣṭo vārttikair nāgasambhavaḥ ।। itthaṃ hi capalaḥ kāryo vaṅgasyāpi na saṃśayaḥ ।। tatspṛṣṭahastasaṃspṛṣṭaḥ kevalo badhyate rasaḥ ।।
sa raso dhātuvādeṣu śasyate na rasāyane । ayaṃ hi kharvaṇākhyena lokanāthena kīrtitaḥ ।। bhūbhujaṃgaśakṛttoyaiḥ prakṣālyāpahṛtaṃ rajaḥ । kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ hi tatproktaṃ dhautākhyaṃ rasavādibhiḥ ।।
dhautamāha bhūbhujaṃgeti ।। apahṛtam apacitaṃ niḥsāritamityarthaḥ ।। rajaḥ puṭanādikāle tatsaṃlagnāṅgārādicūrṇam ।। tat capalībhūtaṃ nāgaṃ vaṅgaṃ ca ।।
bhūnāgamalarasaiḥ tanmalamiśrajalairvā pariśodhitamalādikaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ capalībhūtaṃ nāgaṃ vaṅgaṃ ca dhautanāgaṃ dhautavaṅgaṃ ca proktam iti niṣkarṣaḥ ।। dhautasya lakṣaṇamāha bhūbhujaṅgeti ।। bhūbhujaṅgā bhūnāgāḥ ।। teṣāṃ śakṛnmṛdviśeṣarūpameva tatsaṃnidhāvupalabhyate ।।
etasyopayogastu kharasattvotpādanārthaṃ pañcamādhyāye prāgabhihita eva ।। dravyayor mardanādhmānād dvaṃdvānaṃ parikīrtitam ।। dvandvānam āha dravyayor iti ।। saṃsṛṣṭadravyadvayaṃ mardayitvā dhmāpanena dvandvānasaṃjñā jāyate ।।
dvandvānam ityatra bandhanam iti pāṭhāntaram ।। bhāgād dravyādhikakṣepam anu varṇasuvarṇake । dravairvā vahnikāgrāso bhañjanī vādibhir matā ।। bhañjanīmāha bhāgāditi ।।
varṇena suvarṇa iva tasmin varṇasuvarṇake rājapittale bhāgāt māraṇārthanirdiṣṭaprakṣepyabhāgam apekṣya dravyādhikakṣepaṃ dravyāṇāṃ prakṣepyadravyāṇām adhikakṣepam adhikaprakṣepam anu paścād adhikaprakṣepānantaram ityarthaḥ yaḥ vahnikāgrāsaḥ māraṇīyadravyagatavahninirvāpaṇaṃ vāthavā dravair jalādibhiḥ yaḥ vahnikāgrāsaḥ sa bhañjanīti saṃjñayā vādibhiḥ rasavādibhiḥ matā kathitā ।। bhajanīlakṣaṇamāha bhāgādrūpyādhiketi ।। anuvarṇasuvarṇake hīnavarṇasuvarṇe hemakṛṣṭiṃ dattvā śatāṃśavidhinā raktapītavarṇotkarṣārthaṃ yatamānena sādhakena pramādātkāraṇāntareṇa vā yadā rūpyasya yo bhāgaḥ śāstra uktastaṃ vihāya pramāṇāpekṣayādhikaḥ kṣipyate tādṛśakṣepaṃ kṛtvā yadā varṇikāhrāse prāgavasthitapītavarṇasyāpi hrāsaḥ kṣayo bhavati ।। athavā dravyair vedhādāvanupadiṣṭadravyair vaṅganīlāñjanādibhiḥ saṃmīlanenāpi yo varṇikāhrāsaḥ sā rasaśāstre bhañjanīti kathyate ।।
hemakṛṣṭerlakṣaṇaṃ tu ।। rūpyaṃ vā jātarūpaṃ vā rasagandhādibhirhatam । samutthitaṃ ca bahuśaḥ sā kṛṣṭī hematārayoḥ ।। iti prāguktameva ।।
atra vidhau hemakṛṣṭiḥ ।। rasadaradatāpyagandhakamanaḥśilārājavartakaṃ vimalam । puṭamṛtaśulbaṃ tāre nirvyūḍhaṃ hemakṛṣṭiriyam ।। iti ।।
rasadaradādīnāṃ puṭena mṛtaṃ yacchulbaṃ tattāre nirvāhitaṃ kuryāt ।। śatāṃśavidhiśca । aṣṭānavatir bhāgāstārastveko'pi kanakabhāgaḥ syāt । sūtasyaiko bhāgaḥ śatāṃśavidhireṣa vikhyātaḥ ।।
iti rasahṛdaye ।। tatra nirvyūḍhatārabhāgasyādhikakṣepeṇānu varṇasuvarṇe varṇanāśaḥ spaṣṭa eva ।। pataṅgīkalkato jātā lohe tāre ca hematā । dināni katicitsthitvā yātyasau cullakā matā ।।
cullakāmāha pataṅgīti ।। pataṅgīkalkataḥ pataṅgīkalkāntar ityarthaḥ katiciddināni sthitvā lauhaṃ tāraṃ ceti śeṣaḥ tatra lauhe viśeṣataḥ tāre ca yā hematā svarṇasādṛśyaṃ jātā asau hematā cullakā yāti cullakā iti saṃjñāṃ labhate ityarthaḥ iti matā ।। cullakā gilṭī iti loke ।। yadvā lakṣaṇadvayamidaṃ tena pataṅgītyārabhya hematā ityantena ślokārdhena hematālakṣaṇam dinānītyādiślokārdhena ca cullakālavaṇaṃ jñeyam ।।
asmin pakṣe vakṣyamāṇapataṅgīrāgākhyarañjakadravyaviśeṣasya kalkalepanena sarvalauhe viśeṣataḥ raupye hematā iti saṃjñā jāyate ।। hemno bhāvaḥ iti hematā svarṇasādṛśyam ।। tathā asau lauhatārayor hematā katiciddināni sthitvā pataṅgīkalke ityāśayaḥ cullakā yāti cullaketyākhyayā khyātiṃ yātītyarthaḥ ।। atha cullikālakṣaṇamāha pataṅgīkalkata iti ।।
pataṅgī aśuddharasoparasādikṛtabījajīrṇaḥ pāradastadghaṭito yaḥ kalkastena jātaṃ yallohe tāmrādau gauravatejasvitvādiguṇasahitaṃ tāratvaṃ hematā vā kiṃcitkālaparyantaṃ sthitvā naśyati sā kriyā culliketi matā ।। uktaṃ ca rasahṛdaye । yaḥ punaretaiḥ kurute karmāśuddhair bhaved rasastasya । avyāpakaḥ pataṅgī na rase rasāyane yojyaḥ ।।
iti ।। etai rasoparasaiḥ ।। karma jāraṇādikarma ।। pataṅgī pakṣivad ūrdhvagāmī ।।
pāradaghaṭitakalkastu yogataraṅgiṇyādigranthokto bodhyaḥ ।। tathā coktaṃ taraṅgiṇyām । pāradaṣṭaṅka ekasyā dvipalaṃ pītakharparam । mardayetsudṛḍhaṃ tāvad raso yāvad vilīyate ।।
punar jambīranīreṇa guḍena ca samanvitam । śoṣayeccātape piṣṭvā ślakṣṇaṃ kṛtvā ca dhāryate ।। arkadugdhasya dātavyā bhāvanāstā yathā tathā । asya kalkasya siddhasya bhāga ekaśca ṭaṅkaṇaḥ ।।
tāmraṃ bhāgatrayaṃ dattvā dhāmyatām andhamūṣayā । suvarṇaṃ divyatejaḥ syāt kuṅkumād atiricyate ।। iti ।। evaṃ nāgārjunādigranthe tāratvotpādakakalko'pi draṣṭavyaḥ ।।
rañjitāddhi cirāllohāddhmānādvā cirakālataḥ । viniryāsaḥ sa nirdiṣṭaḥ pataṅgīrāgasaṃjñakaḥ ।। saṃprati kriyāviśeṣasiddhasyāciravināśino lohasthasya rāgasya saṃjñāmāha rañjitāditi ।। atrāpi pataṅgikalkata ityanuvartanīyam ।।
tādṛśakalkena rañjitāllohāddhmānādiyatnena vinā kālāntare dhmānena sadyo vā yo rāgo viniryāti viyujya nirgacchati sa pataṅgīrāgasaṃjñako rasaśāstre khyātaḥ ।। pūrvaśloke pataṅgī ityuktam ataḥ tāmeva vivṛṇoti rañjitāditi ।। cirāddīrghakālaṃ vyāpya rañjitād vakṣyamāṇaraktādivargānyatamavargeṇa rāgapariprāptād yasmāt kasmādapi lauhād athavā cirakālataḥ sudīrghakālaṃ dhmānāddhmāpitād yasmāt kasmādapi rañjitalauhād yaḥ viniryāsaḥ niḥsravaḥ sattvamiti yāvat nirgacchatīti śeṣaḥ sa pataṅgīrāgasaṃjñakaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ ।। drute dravyāntarakṣepo lohādye kriyate hi yaḥ ।
sa āvāpaḥ pratīvāpas tadevācchādanaṃ matam ।। druta iti ।। etadudāharaṇaṃ yathā । suradālibhasma galitaṃ triḥsaptakṛtvo'tha gojalaṃ śuṣkam ।
vāpena salilasadṛśaṃ karoti mūṣāgataṃ tīkṣṇam ।। iti ।। tathā । suragopakadeharajaḥ suradāliphalaiḥ samāṃśakair deyaḥ ।
vāpo drute suvarṇe drutamāste tadrasaprakhyam ।। iti ।। rasaprakhyaṃ jalasadṛśam ityarthaḥ ।। drute vahnisthite lohe viramyāṣṭanimeṣakam ।
salilasya parikṣepaḥ so abhiṣeka iti smṛtaḥ ।। abhiṣekamāha drute iti ।। vahnisthite prajvalitacullyupari eva avasthite ।। aṣṭanimeṣakam aṣṭavāram akṣṇor nimīlanonmīlanātmakaṃ kālaṃ viramya dravībhavanānantaram apekṣya ।।
taptasyāpsu vinikṣepo nirvāpaḥ snapanaṃ ca tat ।। pratīvāpādikaṃ kāryaṃ drute lohe sunirmale ।। yadā hutāśo dīptārciḥ śuklotthānasamanvitaḥ । śuddhāvartas tadā jñeyaḥ sa kālaḥ sattvanirgame ।।
drāvyadravyanibhā jvālā dṛśyate dhamane yadā । drāvasyonmukhatā seyaṃ bījāvartaḥ sa ucyate ।। vahnistham eva śītaṃ yattaduktaṃ svāṅgaśītalam ।। agnerākṛṣya śītaṃ yattad bahiḥśītamucyate ।।
kṣārāmlair auṣadhairvāpi dolāyantre sthitasya hi । pacanaṃ svedanākhyaṃ syānmalaśaithilyakārakam ।। svedanamāha kṣārāmlairiti ।। auṣadhaiḥ tattallauhaśodhakadravyāṇāṃ svarasādibhir ityarthaḥ ।।
malaśaithilyakārakaṃ svedanena mārdave jāte antarmalānāṃ pṛthakkaraṇaṃ vīkaraṇaṃ vā ।। idānīm aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāṇāṃ krameṇa lakṣaṇamāha kṣārāmlairiti ।। kṣārā yavakṣārasarjanaṭaṅkaṇāḥ ।। amlaṃ kāñjikādi ।।
auṣadhaistryūṣaṇādibhiḥ sarpākṣyādibhiśca ।। tāstu rasaratnākare parigaṇitā eva svedanādyupayogikāñjikavidhau ।। tathā ca tadgranthaḥ । nānādhānyair yathāprāptaistuṣavarjyair jalānvitaiḥ ।
mṛdbhāṇḍe pūritaṃ rakṣa yāvad amlatvam āpnuyāt ।। tanmadhye bhṛṅgarāṅmuṇḍī viṣṇukrāntā punarnavā । mīnākṣī caiva sarpākṣī sahadevī śatāvarī ।। triphalā girikarṇī ca haṃsapādī ca citrakam ।
samūlaṃ kaṇḍayitvā tu yathālābhaṃ niveśayet ।। pūrvāmlabhāṇḍamadhye tu dhānyāmlakam idaṃ smṛtam । svedanādiṣu sarvatra rasarājasya yojayet ।। iti ।।
sthitasya tryūṣaṇādikalkaliptavastrāvṛtabhūrjapatrapoṭalikāmadhye sthitasya pāradayetyarthaḥ ।। tryūṣaṇādikalko'pi rasaratnākare'bhihitaḥ । tryūṣaṇaṃ lavaṇaṃ rājī rajanī triphalādravam । mahābalā nāgabalā meghanādā punarnavā ।।
meṣaśṛṅgī citrakaṃ ca navasāraṃ samaṃ samam । etat samastaṃ vyastaṃ vā pūrvāmlenaiva peṣayet ।। tatkalkena lipedvastraṃ yāvad aṅgulamātrakam । tanmadhye nikṣipet sūtaṃ baddhvā pacyād dinatrayam ।।
dolāyantre amlasaṃyukte svedito jāyate rasaḥ । prakṣālya kāñjikaiḥ soṣṇaistam ādāya vimardayet ।। iti ।। malaśaithilyakārakaṃ malāśca dvādaśa doṣāḥ ।।
tacchaithilyajanakam ।। śithilānām eva hi teṣām mocayitum śakyatvāt ।। dvādaśa doṣāśca viṣaṃ vahnir malaśceti naisargikāstrayaḥ ।। nāgaja ekaḥ ।।
vaṅgaja ekaḥ ।। tathā bhūmijo girijo vārjaḥ ।। nāgajau dvau ।। vaṅgajau ca dvau ।।
iti sapta kañcukākhyā ityevaṃ dvādaśa doṣā devaiḥ prārthitamaheśvareṇa pārade saṃyojitā bhavanti ।। uditairauṣadhaiḥ sārdhaṃ sarvāmlaiḥ kāñjikairapi । peṣaṇaṃ mardanākhyaṃ syādbahirmalavināśanam ।। mardanamāha uditairiti ।।
uditairauṣadhaiḥ tatra tatroktabheṣajadravyāṇāṃ svarasaiḥ kvāthairvā ityarthaḥ ।। uditairiti ।। vakṣyamāṇamardanavidhyuktair gṛhadhūmādyauṣadhaiḥ sarvāmlairamlavetasapramukhair amlavargoktairdravyaiḥ ।। teṣāṃ rasenetyarthaḥ ।।
tathā kāñjikairapi pāradasya yatpeṣaṇaṃ tridinaparyantaṃ kṛtaṃ tad bahirmalavināśanaṃ bhavati ।। bahirmalaḥ svedenāntarviśliṣṭo bhūtvā pāradadehādbahiḥ saṃśliṣṭo rāgato naisargikadoṣaṃ vihāya navavidho yo malastadvināśako bhavatīti ।। kevalaṃ svedamardanābhyāṃ na sarvathā bhujakañcukadoṣanāśanaṃ bhavati ।। mardanādiṣṭabhaiṣajyair naṣṭapiṣṭatvakārakam ।
tanmūrchanaṃ hi vaṅgāhibhujakañcukanāśanam ।। ato mardanapūrvakam agniyogena nāśaṃ kṛtvā pāradasya yat piṣṭatvotpādanaṃ tanmūrchanasaṃskāranāmnāha mardanādiṣṭeti ।। mardanārthaṃ vakṣyamāṇamūrchanasaṃskāravidhau kathitair gṛhakanyādibhir naṣṭapiṣṭatvakārakaṃ yat karma mardanapūrvakapācanarūpaṃ tanmūrchanam ityabhidhīyate ।। samāsato lakṣaṇaṃ tu dattagrāsasya grāsarahitasya vā gālanapātanavyaktirekeṇa pūrvāvasthāpannatvam ।।
tacca mardanapākābhyāṃ bhavatīti mardanottaraṃ yantrapuṭānyatareṇa pāko'pyaṅgatvena bodhya iti dvau yaugikau ।। bhūjaśabdena bhūjadoṣaprabhṛtītyartho bodhyaḥ ।। te ca kañcukā āvarakāḥ sapta doṣā vaṅgāhidoṣapramukhāḥ ।। te ca mardanāgnibhyāṃ naśyanti ।।
vaṅgaśabdena vaṅgajadoṣo grāhyaḥ ।। ahiśabdena nāgajadoṣaśca ।। doṣāṇāṃ nānātvena vividhadṛḍhaśithilasaṃsargatāratamyena tannāśārthaṃ vividhopāyapradarśanam ucitam eveti na mardanasaṃskāreṇa mūrchanasya gatārthateti śaṅkyamiti bhāvaḥ ।। tanmūrchanaṃ hi vaṅgāhibhūjakañcukanāśanam iti pāṭhaṃ gṛhītveyaṃ vyākhyā ।।
doṣatrayavināśanamiti pāṭhe tu naisargikadoṣanāśe sutarāṃ bahirdoṣanāśa ityabhiprāyaḥ ।। ata evāyaṃ pāṭho rasahṛdayaṭīkāyāṃ caturbhujamiśritair ādṛtaḥ ।। naisargikadoṣetaradoṣāṇāṃ vāraṇāya pūrvoktamardanasaṃskāro naisargikadoṣavāraṇāyāyam iti vyavasthāyāḥ sukaratvāt ।। evaṃ ca vaṅgāhibhūjakañcukanāśanam iti pāṭho na manorama iti bodhyam ।।
mūrchanamāha mardanāditi ।। iṣṭabhaiṣajyaiḥ śodhakāditvena abhimatauṣadhaiḥ ।। naṣṭapiṣṭatvakārakaṃ peṣaṇena svarūpanāśāt yanmūrtibaddhatvam ।। vaṅgeti ।।
nāgavaṅgādidoṣanāśanam ।। etattu rasam uddiśya uktaṃ dhātvantarāṇām api svasvadoṣanāśanam iti ādipadena bodhyam ।। svedātapādiyogena svarūpāpādanaṃ hi yat । tadutthāpanam ityuktaṃ mūrchāvyāpattināśanam ।।
utthāpanamāha svedeti ।। svedaḥ ūrdhvapātanādinā svedanam ātapaḥ raudrasaṃtāpaḥ ādinā mardanādīnām grahaṇam ।। svarūpāpādanaṃ prakṛtyavasthāpanam ।। mūrchāvyāpattināśanaṃ mūrchanakriyājanitasvarūpadhvaṃsarūpavipattivāraṇam ।।
svedeti ।। svedaḥ kāñjikayā kṣārāmlalavaṇaiśca dolāyantre svedanam ।। ātapayogaḥ kāñjikādimarditarasasya kācapātre sūryatāpasthe dhāraṇam ।। ādiśabdena sāgnikacullīsthe kaṭāhe vā pāradasya tasya dhāraṇamityādi ।।
tena pāradasya mūrchitasya yaccāñcalyatejasvitvagauravaviśiṣṭatvarūpam ātmarūpaṃ tatpratiprāpaṇaṃ tadutthāpanam ityucyate ।। svarūpasya vināśena piṣṭatvād bandhanaṃ hi tat । vidvadbhirnirjitaḥ sūto naṣṭapiṣṭiḥ sa ucyate ।। bandhanamāha svarūpasyeti ।।
piṣṭam iṣṭabhaiṣajyaiḥ peṣaṇaṃ piṣṭamiti bhāvoktaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ ।। tattvāt svarūpasya vināśena svakīyaśubhratvacapalatvādirūpāpāyena yad rūpāpādanam iti śeṣastad bandhanaṃ vahninānucchidyamānatvaṃ mūrtibaddhatvam iti vā jñeyam iti śeṣaḥ ।। asyaiva naṣṭapiṣṭir iti saṃjñāntaramāha vidvadbhiriti ।। nirjito bandhanena naṣṭasvarūpaḥ yadvā nirjito mṛtaḥ sa sūtaḥ vidvadbhir naṣṭapiṣṭir ucyate ।।
uktauṣadhairmarditapāradasya yantrasthitasyordhvam adhaś ca tiryak । niryātanaṃ pātanasaṃjñam uktaṃ vaṅgāhisamparkajakañcukaghnam ।। pātanātrayamāha uktauṣadhairiti ।। niryātanaṃ śodhanādyarthaṃ yat kadarthanamityarthaḥ ।।
atha pātanasaṃskārasya lakṣaṇamāha uktauṣadhairiti ।। vakṣyamāṇapātanavidhau nirdiṣṭatriphalādibheṣajaiḥ saha marditapāradasya tata ūrdhvapātanādiyantrasthitasya yanniryāpaṇam ūrdhvādhastiryakprāpaṇaṃ tat pātanam ucyate ।। tena vaṅganāgajā yaugikadoṣā bhūjādisaptakañcukāśca sarvathā naśyanti ।। jalasaindhavayuktasya rasasya divasatrayam ।
sthitir āsthāpanī kumbhe yāsau rodhanamucyate ।। rodhanamāha jaleti ।। jalasaindhavābhyāṃ saha kumbhamadhye divasatrayaṃ rasasya yā āsthāpanī ā samyak sthāpanī ṣaṇḍhadoṣanāśanapūrvakaṃ svavīrye sthāpanakāriṇī kriyeti śeṣaḥ asau sthitiḥ sthāpanaṃ rodhanamityucyate ।। idaṃ hi svedanādikriyājanitakadarthanena ṣaṇḍhabhāvaprāptasya rasasya taddoṣanāśapūrvakavīryaprakarṣādhānārthaṃ jñātavyam ।।
granthāntare asya bodhanam iti saṃjñā nirdiṣṭā ।। rodhanaṃ lakṣayati jaleti ।। kumbhe vakṣyamāṇe ghaṭayantre ।। āpyāyanī puṣṭikarī ।।
atra saindhavamayamūṣāsaṃpuṭitaṃ kṛtvaikaviṃśatidinaparyantaṃ bhūdharapuṭanaṃ sṛṣṭyambujaiḥ saha mardanaṃ ca kṛtvā tataḥ param iti vākyaśeṣo bodhyaḥ ।। rodhanāllabdhavīryasya capalatvanivṛttaye । kriyate pārade svedaḥ proktaṃ niyamanaṃ hi tat ।। niyamanamāha rodhanāditi ।।
svedaḥ svedanam ।। yadyapyatra svedanārthaṃ dravyanirdeśo na kṛtaḥ tathāpi adhyetṝṇāṃ vijñānārthaṃ granthāntaroktaṃ tannirdiśyate tathā ca rasendracintāmaṇau । sarpākṣīciñcikākanyābhṛṅgārakanakāmbubhiḥ । dinaṃ saṃsveditaḥ sūto niyamāt sthiratāṃ vrajet ।।
iti ।। niyamanaṃ capalatvaparihārapūrvakasthiratvasaṃpādanam ।। labdhavīryasya pāradasyeti śeṣaḥ ।। svedaḥ pāradagarbhitamūṣāṃ bhūmimadhye gūḍhāṃ kṛtvā bhūmyupari karīṣāgnir ityarthaḥ ।।
dhātupāṣāṇamūlādyaiḥ saṃyukto ghaṭamadhyagaḥ । grāsārthaṃ tridinaṃ svedo dīpanaṃ tanmataṃ budhaiḥ ।। dīpanamāha dhātviti ।। grāsārthaṃ ghanahemādīnām iti śeṣaḥ ।।
svedaḥ dolāyantre kāñjikādinā rasasya iti śeṣaḥ ।। dīpanaṃ grāsaśaktisaṃjananakriyāviśeṣaḥ ।। rasendracintāmaṇikāreṇa dīpanadravyāṇi anyavidhānyuktāni yathā । kāsīsaṃ pañcalavaṇaṃ rājikā maricāni ca ।
bhūśigrubījam ekatra ṭaṅgaṇena samanvitam ।। āloḍya kāñjike dolāyantre pākād dinaistribhiḥ । dīpanaṃ jāyate samyak sūtarājasya jāraṇe ।। athavā citrakadrāvaiḥ kāñjike tridinaṃ pacet ।।
iti ।। atha dīpanasaṃskāraṃ lakṣayati dhātupāṣāṇeti ।। dhātavastāmrapatrādayaḥ ।। pāṣāṇāḥ sphaṭikā mayūratutthakāsīsādayaḥ ।।
mūlāni sarpākṣyādimūlikāḥ ।। ādyaśabdena kṣāralavaṇodakādi grāhyam ।। ghaṭamadhyago ghaṭayantramadhyagaḥ pāradastridinaparyantaṃ svedyo bhavati yasmin karmaṇi tad dīpanam iti khyātam ।। atha jāraṇāyām ayathābalam ayathākramaṃ ca grāsadānenājīrṇadoṣāt pārade vikriyā syād iti grāsamānavicāro'vaśyaṃ kāryaḥ ।।
iyanmānasya sūtasya bhojyadravyātmikā mitiḥ । iyatītyucyate yāsau grāsamānaṃ samīritam ।। grāsamānamāha iyanmānasyeti ।। iyanmānasya etāvatparimāṇasya sūtasya saṃbandhavivakṣayā ṣaṣṭhī iyanmite sūte ityarthaḥ yā iyatī mitiḥ etāvatparimāṇaṃ bhojyadravyāṇām iti śeṣaḥ iti ucyate bhojyadravyātmikā grasanīyasvarṇādidravyāṇāṃ mānanirdeśarūpā asau uktiḥ grāsamānaṃ samīritam iyanmānaḥ sūtaḥ iyanmānaṃ svarṇādidravyaṃ grasituṃ samarthaḥ evaṃrūpamānanirdeśaḥ grāsamānaṃ jñeyam ।।
ato grāsamānākhyasaṃskārasya lakṣaṇamāha iyanmānasyeti ।। iyacchabdo'tra saṃskāryapāradasya gṛhītamānaviśeṣapalādivācakaḥ ।। tādṛśamānamitapāradasyeyaccatuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśādimitābhrakasattvabījādyātmakaṃ dravyaṃ bhakṣaṇāya dattaṃ cet sukhena cīrṇaṃ jīrṇaṃ ca syāditi niścitā yā bījāder mitis tadgrāsamānaṃ khyātam ।। grāsasya cāraṇaṃ garbhe drāvaṇaṃ jāraṇaṃ tathā ।
iti trirūpā nirdiṣṭā jāraṇā varavārttikaiḥ ।। jāraṇātrayamāha grāsasyeti ।। grāsasya grāsayogyasya svarṇāderityarthaṃ cāraṇaṃ rasāntaḥ kṣepaṇaṃ garbhe drāvaṇaṃ rasāntaḥ taralībhavanaṃ jāraṇaṃ viḍayantrādiyogena dravībhūtagrāsasya pākaḥ ।। atha jāraṇāṃ lilakṣayiṣuḥ prathamaṃ sādhāraṇāṃstadavasthābhedān salakṣaṇān samāsata āha grāsasyeti ।।
śreṣṭhai rasavārttākuśalaiḥ sarvavidhā jāraṇā trirūpā triprakārā kathitā bhavati ।। tatra grāsasya cāraṇaṃ pāradakartṛkagrāsabhakṣaṇakaraṇam ।। garbhadrāvaṇaṃ grastabījādeḥ pāradodare drutikaraṇam ।। jāraṇaṃ ca pārada ekībhāvo anantadṛḍhasaṃbandhena ।।
eṣāṃ lakṣaṇānyanupadaṃ vakṣyati ।। grāsaḥ piṇḍaḥ pariṇāmastisraścākhyāḥ parā punaḥ ।। jāraṇāyā aparaṃ traividhyamāha grāsa iti ।। grāsaḥ kavalīkaraṇarūpajāraṇā piṇḍaḥ kardamavat piṇḍībhavanarūpajāraṇā ।।
parīṇāmaḥ avasthāntaraprāpaṇarūpajāraṇā ।। punarapi jāraṇāyā avasthākṛtanāmāntarāṇi trīṇyāha grāsaḥ piṣṭiḥ parīṇāmaśceti ।। tatra grāso grasanam ।। piṣṭiḥ svedanamardanāgnyādibhiḥ pāradodare drutagrāsasya pāradasahitasya śuṣkaścūrṇaḥ ।।
pariṇāmārthastu prāgukta eva ।। punar jāraṇā dvividhā bhavati ।। samukhā nirmukhā ceti bhedena ।। samukhā nirmukhā ceti jāraṇā dvividhā punaḥ ।।
nirmukhā jāraṇā proktā bījādānena bhāgataḥ ।। tatrādau nirmukhajāraṇāmāha nirmukheti ।। niḥ nāsti mukhaṃ vakṣyamāṇacatuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśaḥ bījaprakṣeparūpamukhalakṣaṇaṃ yatra jāraṇāyāṃ tādṛśī ।। bījeti ।।
bhāgataḥ yathābhāgaṃ tattaddravyajāraṇāyāṃ nirdiṣṭabhāgam anatikramya vakṣyamāṇacatuḥṣaṣṭibhāgāt nyūnatayā adhikatayā vā ityarthaḥ bījādānena śuddhasvarṇaraupyātmakabījagrahaṇam ।। tatrālpavaktavyatvāt prathamaṃ nirmukhāyā eva lakṣaṇamāha nirmukheti ।। catuḥṣaṣṭibhāgamitaṃ bījaṃ prathamaṃ yatra pāradodare na dīyate kiṃtu kevalaṃ śuddhadhātvādigrāsa eva sṛṣṭitrayanīrakaṇāvāsanauṣadhimardanādyupāyair jāryate sā jāraṇā nirmukhetyucyate ।। rasoparasādimṛdudravyajāraṇe tasyā upayogaḥ kāryaḥ ।।
śuddhaṃ svarṇaṃ ca rūpyaṃ ca bījam ityabhidhīyate ।। mukhakaraṇopayogibījaśabdārthamāha śuddhamiti ।। śuddham akṛtrimam uttamaṃ khanijaṃ svarṇaṃ rūpyaṃ vaitacchāstroktaśuddhyā suśuddhaṃ kṛtvātra grāhyam ।। etena kṛtrimanirvyūḍhamahābījādivyāvṛttiḥ kṛtā ।।
catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśato bījaprakṣepo mukhamucyate ।। [samukharasa।-jāraṇā] evaṃ kṛte raso grāsalolupo mukhavān bhavet । kaṭhinānyapi lohāni kṣamo bhavati bhakṣitum ।
iyaṃ hi samukhā proktā jāraṇā mṛgacāriṇā ।। uktabījasya yathākramaṃ svarṇotpādārthaṃ raupyajananārthaṃ ca pāradasya catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśena pāradodare jāraṇārambhe prakṣepaḥ kāryaḥ ।। evaṃ kṛte tasmin bīje pāradodare yathāvidhi cīrṇe jīrṇe ca sati pāradaḥ satvaraṃ grāsabhakṣaṇaṃ karotīti śāstre sa raso mukhavānityucyate ।। tatkṛtaṃ yat kaṭhinalohādibhakṣaṇaṃ sā jāraṇā samukhetyuktā ।।
mṛgacāriṇā mṛgasahitaṃ vane carati saṃsāraṃ vihāya viriktena kenacidvaravārtikena ।। samukhajāraṇām āha evamiti ।। evaṃ kṛte catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśato bījaprakṣepe kṛte ।। mukhavān samukhaḥ ।।
mṛgacāriṇā tadākhyena kenacid rasatantrakṛtā ।। divyauṣadhisamāyogāt sthitaḥ prakaṭakoṣṭhiṣu । bhuñjītākhilalohādyaṃ yo asau rākṣasavaktravān ।। rākṣasamukharasam āha divyauṣadhīti ।।
divyauṣadhiḥ manaḥśilā ।। prakaṭakoṣṭhiṣu vivṛtānanakoṣṭhikāyantreṣu ।। bhuñjīta graset ।। atha mahāmukhapāradasya lakṣaṇamāha divyauṣadhīti ।।
somalatādikāścatuḥṣaṣṭidivyauṣadhyas tatsamāyogas tadrasena kṛtamardanādinā kṛtasaṃskāraḥ ।। tena prakāśamūṣāsvapi sthito'gnisahaḥ pārado dhmānena kaṭhinaṃ mṛdu sarvaṃ lohādi yadā bhunakti asau mahāmukhavān ityucyate ।। rasasya jaṭhare grāsakṣapaṇaṃ cāraṇā matā ।। jāraṇābhedacāraṇālakṣaṇamāha rasasyeti ।।
jaṭhare madhye ityarthaḥ grāsakṣapaṇaṃ grāsasya grāsārhalauhādeḥ kṣapaṇaṃ kṣayamāpādanaṃ rasena saha ekīkaraṇamityarthaḥ ।। pūrvoktacāraṇādīnāṃ lakṣaṇamāha rasasyeti ।। grastasya drāvaṇaṃ garbhe garbhadrutir udāhṛtā ।। bahireva drutiṃ kṛtvā ghanasattvādikaṃ khalu ।
jāraṇāya rasendrasya sā bāhyadrutir ucyate ।। garbhadrutiprasaṅgena bāhyadrutim āha bahir iti ।। bahir eva cullyuparisthakaṭāhādau na tu rasagarbhe ityarthaḥ ।। ghanasattvādikam abhrasattvādikam atrādipadena svarṇasattvādīnāṃ grahaṇaṃ bodhyam ।।
bahireva drutīkṛtyeti ।। abhrakasattvadrutiḥ prāguktaiva dvitīyādhyāye ।। jāraṇāya taptakhalvamadhye dīyata iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।। nirlepatvaṃ drutatvaṃ ca tejastvaṃ laghutā tathā ।
asaṃyogaśca sūtena pañcadhā drutilakṣaṇam ।। druteḥ pañcadhābhedānāha nirlepatvamiti ।। nirlepatvaṃ niḥ niścayena niḥśeṣeṇa vā lepatvaṃ liptatvaṃ drāvāntareṇa saha niḥśeṣeṇa ekībhavanamityarthaḥ yadvā niḥ nirgataḥ lepaḥ liptapadārthaḥ malādiryasmāt tattvaṃ pṛthagbhūtamalādikam ityarthaḥ ।। drutatvaṃ viśeṣeṇa dravībhavanam ।।
tejastvaṃ svarūpāpekṣayā tejobhūyastvam ।। laghutā svābhāvikagurutvamapekṣya lāghavam ।। asaṃyogaśca sūtena pāradena saha pṛthaktayā avasthānam ।। auṣadhādhmānayogena lohadhātvādikaṃ tathā ।
saṃtiṣṭhate dravākāraṃ sā drutiḥ parikīrtitā ।। drutagrāsaparīṇāmo viḍayantrādiyogataḥ । jāraṇetyucyate tasyāḥ prakārāḥ santi koṭiśaḥ ।। jāraṇābhedajāraṇāmāha druteti ।।
viḍaḥ vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇalakṣitaḥ yantraṃ koṣṭhikādikaṃ tadādiyogataḥ atrādipadena mūṣāpuṭādīnāṃ grahaṇaṃ drutasya garbhe taralitasya grāsasya svarṇādeḥ parīṇāmaḥ paripākaḥ svātmani abhedarūpeṇa pariṇamanam ।। rasendracintāmaṇau tu jāraṇā hi pātanagālanavyatirekeṇa ghanahemādigrāsapūrvakaṃ pūrvāvasthāpannatvam ityanena yat prakārāntaraṃ jāraṇālakṣaṇamuktaṃ tat cāraṇākhyajāraṇābhiprāyeṇa bodhyam ।। atha jāraṇālakṣaṇam āha drutagrāseti ।। biḍayantrādiyogena pāradodare dravībhūtasya grāsasya bījāder yaḥ parīṇāmo'vināśidṛḍhatarasaṃbandhena pāradena sahaikībhāvaḥ sā jāraṇetyucyate ।।
tasyāḥ prakārāḥ koṭiśo'tibahavaḥ santi ।। yantrādīnāṃ bahuvidhatvāt ।। te ca prakārāḥ patrajāraṇāsattvajāraṇādrutijāraṇābījajāraṇāmahābījajāraṇāsiddhabījajāraṇāsadhūmajāraṇānirdhūmajāraṇābālajāraṇāvṛddhajāraṇābaddhajāraṇābhūcarījāraṇākhecarījāraṇāprabhṛtayo rasārṇavādau savistaraṃ bodhyāḥ ।। dolāyantrasomānalayantracakrarājayantravālukāyantrajalakūrmayantrasthalakūrmayantramūṣāprabhṛtīni jāraṇayantrādīni vidyāt ।।
taptakhalve mardanaṃ tu sarvatra prākkāryam eva ।। ādiśabdena ṣaḍbindukīṭasahitamardanasṛṣṭitrayādisaṃgrahāḥ ।। kṣārairamlaiśca gandhādyair mūtraiśca paṭubhis tathā । rasagrāsasya jīrṇārthaṃ tadviḍaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
susiddhabījadhātvādijāraṇena rasasya hi । pītādirāgajananaṃ rañjanaṃ parikīrtitam ।। ato'bhrapattrajāraṇottaraṃ rāgasaṃskāraṃ lakṣayati susiddhabījeti ।। susiddhaṃ yathāvidhi sādhitaṃ yad bījam abhrakasattvadhātvādicūrṇaṃ tajjāraṇena pāradasya yā bījadhātvādyanurūpā varṇotpattis tad rañjanam ।।
tatra bījasādhanavidhistu siddhabījalakṣaṇavyākhyāyāṃ prāgukta eva ।। jāraṇāvidhistu triṃśattame'dhyāye sphuṭībhaviṣyati ।। ādiśabdo maṇirasoparasādiparigrahaḥ ।। rāgadravyodāharaṇaṃ vidhiśca rasahṛdaye ।।
yathā । jīrṇābhrako rasendro darśayati ghanānurūpiṇīṃ chāyām । kṛṣṇāṃ raktāṃ pītāṃ sītāṃ tathā saṃkarairmiśrām ।। tathā ।
krāmati tīkṣṇena rasastīkṣṇena ca jīryate kṣaṇādgrāsaḥ । hemno yonistīkṣṇaṃ rāgān gṛhṇāti tīkṣṇena ।। tadapi ca daradena hataṃ hatvā vā mākṣikeṇa ravisahitam । vāsitamapi vāsanayā ghanavaccāryaṃ ca jāryaṃ ca ।
vāsanayā vāsanauṣadhena vāsitaṃ bhāvitamityarthaḥ ।। tathā । kāntaṃ vā tīkṣṇaṃ vā kāñcīṃ vā vajrasasyakādīnām । ekatamaṃ sarvaṃ vā rasarañjane saṃkaro'pīṣṭaḥ ।।
kāñcīṃ svarṇamākṣikam ।। ādiśabdena hīrakacapalādaya upadhātavaścaikatra militā apīṣṭāḥ ।। kuṭile balamadhikaṃ rāgastīkṣṇe tu pannage snehaḥ ।। rāgasnehabalāni tu kamale śaṃsanti dhātuvidaḥ ।।
rañjanamāha susiddheti ।। śodhitasvarṇaraupyābhyāṃ tathā jīrṇatāmrādiyogena kriyāviśeṣam āśritya rasasya yat pītādirāgajananam ityanvayaḥ ।। sūte satailayantrasthe svarṇādikṣepaṇaṃ hi yat । vedhādhikyakaraṃ lohe sāraṇā sā prakīrtitā ।।
sāraṇālakṣaṇamāha sūta iti ।। sāraṇākhyatailenārdhāṃśaṃ saṃbhṛtaṃ yat sāraṇāyantraṃ tatra sthite pārade yat svarṇādikṣepaṇaṃ svarṇādibījanāgavaṅgānāṃ yat kṣepaṇaṃ vedhādhikyasiddhyarthaṃ kriyate sā sāraṇeti rasaśāstra uktā ।। pratisāraṇānusāraṇeti ca tadbhedau ।। uktaṃ caitad rasahṛdaye ।
sāritavartitasūtaḥ samānabījena milati yaḥ sāryaḥ । dviguṇena pratīsāryaḥ sa cānusāryaśca triguṇena ।। iti ।। dviguṇamapi suvarṇameva ।।
vedhādhikyaṃ vedho bhittvāntaḥpraveśaḥ so'dhiko bhavati ।। pāradasya tāmradalādau śarīrasthadhātvādiṣu ca sarvato vyāptiḥ ।। sāraṇātailaṃ pañcamādhyāyavyākhyāyāṃ prāguktameva ।। yantrādhyāye sāraṇāyantraṃ sāraṇāvidhiśca sphuṭībhaviṣyati ।।
sāraṇāmāha sūte iti ।। satailayantrasthe tailapūrṇāndhamūṣāmadhyasthite sūte rase yat svarṇādikṣepaṇaṃ svarṇādiprakṣepaḥ lohe tāmrādau ityarthaḥ vedhādhikyakaraṃ vedhasya svarṇādijananarūpavedhaśakteḥ ādhikyakaram ātiśayyajanakam ।। uktaṃ ca rasendracintāmaṇau । atha sāraṇocyate ।।
andhamūṣā tu kartavyā gostanākārasaṃnibhā ।। saiva chidrānvitā madhye gambhīrā sāraṇocitā ।। asyām eva mūṣāyāṃ tattailam apagatakalkavimalam āpūryam asminnadhikam adhastād drutabījaprakṣepasamakālam eva samāvarjanīyaḥ sūtavarastadanu sadyo mūṣānanam ācchādanīyam ।। etat tailāktakhaṇḍagranthibandhena aruṇāsitabījābhyām aśvanāsārakarmaṇā militaścet sāritaḥ samyak saṃyamitaḥ vijñātavyaḥ ।।
sāraṇārthaṃ tailamapi tatraivānveṣṭavyaṃ vistarabhayānnoddhṛtam iti ।। vyavāyibheṣajopeto dravye kṣipto rasaḥ khalu । vedha ityucyate tajjñaiḥ sa cānekavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sāraṇālakṣaṇe vedhādhikyakaram ityuktaṃ kastāvat vedha ityapekṣāyāmāha vyavāyīti nāgavallīkumārikādhustūrādivyavāyiguṇavadbheṣajasaṃyuktaḥ ityarthaḥ ।।
vyavāyilakṣaṇaṃ śārṅgadhare yathā । pūrvaṃ vyāpyākhilaṃ kāyaṃ tataḥ pākaṃ ca gacchati । vyavāyi tadyathā bhaṅgā phenaṃ cāhisamudbhavam । iti ।।
dravye svarṇādirūpeṇa pariṇinamayiṣau lohe ।। atha krāmaṇasya dravyasya sarvadā vedhasahopayogitvena samāsato viśeṣaṇamukhena krāmaṇalakṣaṇasahitaṃ vedhalakṣaṇam ekena ślokenāha vyavāyīti ।। dravye śatavedhādau yathābhāgaṃ gṛhīte mūṣāyāṃ drute kṛte prataptamātre vā tāmrarajatādau sādhyadravye kṣipto rasaḥ pārado yasmin karmaṇi sa vedha ityucyate ।। sa ca pāradaḥ kīdṛśaḥ ।।
vyavāyibheṣajopetaḥ ।। yat sevitamātraṃ tatkṣaṇa eva śarīrāntaḥsthasarvadhātuṣu sahasā sabāhyābhyantaraṃ vyāpnoti paścāt pākaṃ prāpnoti tadvyavāyi krāmaṇetyaparaparyāyaṃ ca bodhyam ।। tādṛśabheṣajopeto yogavāhī pārado'pi sevitaścet sahasā sarvaṃ dehaṃ sāntaraṃ vyāpnoti na kevalaṃ koṣṭha eva sthitiṃ karoti ।। na vā dhātuṣu kathaṃcit prāpto'pi bahiḥ saṃlagna eva tiṣṭhatīti ।।
lohāntaḥ praviśed yena dravyayogena pāradaḥ । sadyas tatkrāmaṇam iti kathitaṃ rasasiddhidam । iti krāmaṇalakṣaṇapārthakyena bodhyam ।। lepaḥ kṣepaśca kuntaśca dhūmākhyaḥ śabdasaṃjñakaḥ ।।
lepanaṃ kurute lohaṃ svarṇaṃ vā rajataṃ tathā । lepavedhaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ puṭamatra ca saurakam ।। teṣu lepavedhalakṣaṇamāha lepanamiti ।। lepanaṃ vedhasāmarthyāpādakakriyāviśeṣasiddharasenety āśayaḥ ।।
atra lepavedhe ।। saurakaṃ puṭaṃ dadyāditi śeṣaḥ sūryapakvaṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।। atha vedhabhedānāha lepa iti ।। lepeneti ।।
yasminvedhe pārado lepena lohaṃ pattrīkṛtaṃ tīkṣṇatāmrādi svarṇaṃ karoti rajataṃ vā karoti sa lepavedha ityuktaḥ ।। atra lepottaraṃ varṇotkarṣārthaṃ yat puṭaṃ deyaṃ bhavati tat puṭaṃ saukaraṃ varāhapuṭaṃ kāryam ।। asmin saṃskāre jīrṇacaturthāṃśārdhāṃśasamādibhāgair jīrṇabīja eva sārito rasa upayoktavyaḥ ।। prakṣepaṇaṃ drute lohe vedhaḥ syātkṣepasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
kṣepavedhalakṣaṇamāha prakṣepaṇamiti ।। galitasvarṇetaralauhe rasaprakṣepeṇa yat suvarṇīkaraṇaṃ sa kṣepākhyavedho jñeyaḥ ।। atha kṣepavedham āha prakṣepaṇam iti ।। dhmānena mūṣāyāṃ lohe tāmrādau drute sati krāmaṇadravyakalkasahitasya pāradasya yat prakṣepaṇaṃ sa vedhaḥ kṣepa iti khyātaḥ ।।
atra pakṣāntaram apyuktaṃ rasasāre krāmaṇakalkasahitalohe dhāmyamāne kevalaṃ pāradaṃ kṣipettatreti ।। saṃdaṃśadhṛtasūtena drutadravyāhṛtiśca yā । suvarṇatvādikaraṇaṃ kuntavedhaḥ sa ucyate ।। kuntavedhamāha saṃdaṃśeti ।।
saṃdaṃśaḥ sāṃḍāśī iti khyātaḥ saṃdaṃśayantreṇa mūrtibaddhasūtaṃ dhṛtvā drutalauhe nimajjanena tatsamparkāt svarṇādirūpeṇa pariṇatasya lauhasya yadāharaṇaṃ sa kuntavedhasaṃjñako jñeyaḥ ।। vahnau dhūmāyamāne antaḥ prakṣiptarasadhūmataḥ । svarṇādyāpādanaṃ lohe dhūmavedhaḥ sa ucyate ।। dhūmavedhamāha vahnāviti ।।
sadhūmavahnimadhye vedhasamartharasanikṣepeṇa yo dhūmaḥ nirgacchati tatsamparkād yat kiṃcillohasya svarṇādirūpeṇa yā pariṇatiḥ sa dhūmavedhaḥ ।। dhūmavedhalakṣaṇamāha vahnāviti ।। dhūmāyamāne vahnāvantarmūṣāntaḥsthatadvahnimadhye prakṣipto yo rasaḥ pāradas tatsaṃbandhidhūmasyordhvasthāpitatāmrādipatre saṃparkād yat svarṇarajatāpādanaṃ sa dhūmavedha ityabhidhīyate ।। mukhasthitarasenālpalohasya dhamanāt khalu ।
svarṇarūpyatvajananaṃ śabdavedhaḥ sa kīrtitaḥ ।। śabdavedhamāha mukheti ।। dhamanāt śabdoccāraṇādityarthaḥ phutkārādityartho vā ।। dhama dhvāne ityasmāt lyuḥ ।।
mukhamadhye vedhasamartharasaguṭikāṃ saṃsthāpya puro lauhakhaṇḍam ekaṃ dhṛtvā śabdoccāraṇe kṛte phutkāre datte vā tat lauhakhaṇḍaṃ svarṇādirūpeṇa pariṇatam ।। dhamanāt ityatra damanāt iti pāṭhe mukhamadhye vedhasamartharasaguṭikāṃ saṃsthāpya kṣudralauhakhaṇḍaṃ tannimne nidhāya ca pīḍane kṛte adhaḥsthalauhakhaṇḍaṃ yatra vedhe svarṇādirūpeṇa pariṇamet sa śabdavedhaḥ ityarthaḥ ।। siddhadravyasya sūtena kāluṣyādinivāraṇam । prakāśanaṃ ca varṇasya tadudghāṭanam īritam ।।
udghāṭanam āha siddhadravyasyeti ।। siddhadravyasya mṛtalauhāder ityarthaḥ sūtena kriyāviśeṣaniṣpannasūtasaṃyogena yat kāluṣyādinivāraṇaṃ mālinyādiproñchanaṃ varṇasya ca prakāśanam aujjvalyasaṃpādanaṃ yadvā sūtena sūtasaṃyogena siddhadravyasya māritalohādeḥ kāluṣyādinivāraṇaṃ yayā kriyayā dravyāntarasaṃyogajanitamālinyādināśanaṃ syādityevaṃ yojanīyam ।। siddhadravyasya sūtena ityatra siddhadravyeṇa sūtasya iti pāṭhe mṛtalauhādisaṃyogadvārā sūtasya yat kāluṣyādinivāraṇam ityarthaḥ ।। sūtena sabāhyābhyantaravyāptyaikībhūtasya siddhadravyasya suvarṇatvādiprāptasya tāmrādilohātmakadravyasya tadekībhūtasūtasya ca yathāsambhavaṃ yat kāluṣyādi tannivārakaṃ daśāṃśena yaccūrṇaprakṣepādi karma tad udghāṭanam itīritam ।।
kāluṣyaṃ malasaṃkīrṇatvam ।। ādiśabdena chattritvapataṅgitvadurdrāvitvadurmelitvādidoṣaḥ saṃgrāhyaḥ ।। kṣārāmlairauṣadhaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ ruddhvātiyatnataḥ । bhūmau nikhanyate yatnātsvedanaṃ saṃprakīrtitam ।।
svedanamāha kṣārāmlairiti ।। auṣadhaiḥ svedanīyauṣadhaiḥ ।। bhāṇḍaṃ rasapūrṇabhāṇḍamityarthaḥ ।। atra uṣṇavīryaiḥ kṣārāmlaiḥ saha bhūmyadhaḥsthāpanena taduṣmaṇā anagnisvedo bodhyaḥ ।।
sāraṇottaraṃ rasāyanaṃ kartuṃ kāmayamānena sādhakena pāradasya kartavyau svedasaṃnyāsākhyasaṃskārau lakṣayati kṣārāmlairiti ।। auṣadhair bhṛṅgarāṅmuṇḍī viṣṇukrāntā ityādibhiḥ svedalakṣaṇavarṇanāvasare prāguktaiḥ ।। taiśca sārdhaṃ saha pāradaṃ bhāṇḍamadhye pidhānasaṃdhirodhanādiyatnena ruddhvā tadbhāṇḍaṃ bhūmimadhye nikhanyate yasmin karmaṇi tat svedanaṃ saṃprakīrtitam ।। rasasyauṣadhayuktasya bhāṇḍaruddhasya yatnataḥ ।
mandāgniyutacullyantaḥ kṣepaḥ saṃnyāsa ucyate ।। saṃnyāsam āha rasasyeti ।। auṣadhayuktasya kṣārāmlauṣadhayuktasyetyarthaḥ ।। mandāgniyutacullyantaḥ mṛdvagniviśiṣṭacullīmadhye na tu tīvrāgniyutacullyām ityarthaḥ ।।
athauṣadhayuktasya pāradasya mṛnmayabhāṇḍasaṃpuṭitasya mandavahniyuktacullīmadhye kṣiptvā yat puṭanaṃ sa saṃnyāsa ityucyate ।। dvāvetau svedasaṃnyāsau rasarājasya niścitam । guṇaprabhāvajanakau śīghravyāptikarau tathā ।। rasanigamamahābdheḥ somadevaḥ samantāt sphuṭataraparibhāṣānāmaratnāni hṛtvā ।
vyaracayadatiyatnāttairimāṃ kaṇṭhamālāṃ kalayatu bhiṣagagryo maṇḍanārthaṃ sabhāyām ।। bhavetpaṭhitavāro'yamadhyāyo rasavādinām । rasakarmāṇi kurvāṇo na sa muhyati kutracit ।। atha yantrāṇi vakṣyante rasatantrāṇyaśeṣataḥ ।
samālocya samāsena somadevena sāmpratam ।। svedādikarma nirmātuṃ vārttikendraiḥ prayatnataḥ । yantryate pārado yasmāttasmādyantramiti smṛtam ।। dravadravyeṇa bhāṇḍasya pūritārdhodakasya ca ।
mukhasyobhayato dvāradvayaṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ ।। tayostu nikṣiped daṇḍaṃ tanmadhye rasapoṭalīm । baddhvā tu svedayedetaddolāyantramiti smṛtam ।। dolāyantramāha dravadravyeṇeti ।।
dravadravyeṇa kāñjikādisvedanadravyeṇa ।। mukhasyeti ।। bhāṇḍakandharāyāḥ prāntadvaye chidradvayaṃ kṛtvetyarthaḥ ।। tayoḥ chidrayoḥ ।।
tanmadhye daṇḍamadhye ।। svedanārheṇa kāñjikādinā kenacit draveṇa bhāṇḍārdhamāpūrya bhāṇḍakandharāprāntadvaye chidradvayaṃ kṛtvā tanmadhye daṇḍamekaṃ nidhāya tasmin rasapoṭṭalīṃ baddhvā ca evaṃ lambayet yathā bhāṇḍasthadrave sā nimajjet paraṃ tu bhāṇḍam na spṛśediti niṣkarṣaḥ ।। sāmbusthālīmukhe baddhavastre pākyaṃ niveśayet । pidhāya pacyate yatra svedanīyantramucyate ।।
atha patrapuṣpādīnāmatimṛdudravyāṇāṃ svalpasvedārthaṃ yantrāntaramāha sāmbusthālīti ।। sthālīṃ caturthāṃśajalena pūritodarāṃ jalenārdhapūritodarāṃ vā kṛtvā tasyā mukham ā samantād vastreṇa baddhaṃ yathā syāttathā mukhābaddhe vastre pākyaṃ svedyam atikomalaṃ dravyaṃ vinikṣipya nyubjaśarāvādinā pidhāyācchādya yatra pacyate tat svedanīyantramityucyate ।। asyaiva yantrasya kandukasaṃjñāṃ vakṣyati ।। aṣṭāṅgulaparīṇāhamānāhena daśāṅgulam ।
caturaṅgulakotsedhaṃ toyādhāraṃ galādadhaḥ ।। adhobhāṇḍe mukhaṃ tasya bhāṇḍasyopari vartinaḥ । ṣoḍaśāṅgulavistīrṇapṛṣṭhasyāsye praveśayet ।। pārśvayor mahiṣīkṣīracūrṇamaṇḍūraphāṇitaiḥ ।
liptvā viśoṣayetsaṃdhiṃ jalādhāre jalaṃ kṣipet । cullyām āropayed etat pātanāyantramucyate ।। athordhvapātanāyantramāha aṣṭāṅguleti ।। atha nyubjasthāpyasya viśālapṛṣṭhasya mṛtpātrasyāṅgulād adho aṅgulamitapṛṣṭhabhāgād adhobhāge toyādhāraḥ kāryaḥ ।।
katham ।। aṣṭāṅgulaparīṇāham aṣṭāṅgulagarbhavistāraṃ yathā syāttathā ।। tathānāhena bandhena saha daśāṅgulaṃ yathā syāttathā bandha ālavālaṃ tatpradeśaṃ saṃgṛhya daśāṅgulavistāram ityarthaḥ ।। evaṃ ca bandhasthaulyam aṅguladvayamitaṃ garbhavistāraścāṣṭāṅgulamitaḥ kārya ityavatiṣṭhate ।।
na ha bandhane ।। caturaṅgulocchrāyaṃ yathā syāttathā toyādhāraḥ pṛṣṭhe kārya ityarthaḥ ।। tādṛśādhāraviśiṣṭasya ṣoḍaśāṅgulavistīrṇapṛṣṭhasyoparivartinastasya bhāṇḍasyāsye'dho bhāṇḍamukhaṃ praveśayet ।। tato mukhapārśvayormahiṣīkṣīrādibhiḥ saṃdhiṃ liptvā viśoṣayet ।।
cūrṇaḥ sudhā śvetaṃ lepadravyamityarthaḥ ।। pātanāyantramīritam ।। ūrdhvapātanāyantramuktamityarthaḥ ।। pātanāyantrasya svarūpamāha aṣṭāṅguleti ।।
parīṇāhaḥ vistāraḥ paridhiriti yāvat ।। ānāhaḥ aunnatyaṃ dairghyamiti yāvat ।। utsedhaḥ upacitiḥ sthaulyamiti yāvat ।। athordhvabhājane liptasthāpitasya jale sudhīḥ ।
dīptair vanopalaiḥ kuryādadhaḥ pātaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। adhaḥpātanayantramāha asyordhveti ।। jalādhāravihīnasya vaiparītyena jale sthāpitasyāsyoktayantrasya saṃbandhi yad ūrdhvabhājanaṃ tatra liptasthāpitasya lepaṃ kṛtvā sthāpitasya pāradasya yantropari dīptairvanopalairadhaḥpātaṃ kuryāt ।। ityetad adhaḥpātanāyantram abhihitam ।।
adhaḥpātanāyantre pātanakramamāha atheti । atha uktarītyā yantranirmāṇānantaram ūrdhvabhājane uparisthādhomukhabhāṇḍodare ityarthaḥ ādau liptaṃ paścāt sthāpitaṃ tasya liptasthāpitasya rasasyeti śeṣaḥ jale adhobhāṇḍasthite iti śeṣaḥ dīptaiḥ vanotpalaiḥ vanyakarīṣāgnibhiḥ ।। jalapūrṇapātramadhye dattvā ghaṭakharparaṃ suvistīrṇam । tadupari viḍamadhyagataḥ sthāpyaḥ sūtaḥ kṛtaḥ koṣṭhyām ।।
laghulohakaṭorikayā kṛtaṣaṇmṛtsaṃdhilepayācchādya । pūrvoktaghaṭakharparamadhye aṅgāraiḥ khadirakolabhavaiḥ ।। svedanato mardanataḥ kacchapayantrasthito raso jarati । agnibalenaiva tato garbhe dravanti sarvasattvāni ।।
kacchapayantraṃ dvividhaṃ jalakacchapaṃ sthalakacchapaṃ ca ।। tatredānīṃ jalakacchapamāha jalapūrṇeti ।। ghaṭakharparaṃ khaṇḍitamukhaṃ sacchidraṃ ghaṭakhaṇḍamuttānaṃ dattvā tadupari koṣṭhīṃ mūṣāṃ chidre kiṃcitpraviṣṭabudhnāṃ nīrāviyoginīmuttānāṃ sudṛḍhaṃ niścalaṃ saṃsthāpya koṣṭhīmabhitaḥ kuḍyaṃ vidadhyāt ।। koṣṭhyāṃ biḍaṃ tanmadhye pāradaṃ ca dattvā sa samyaksthāpyaḥ ।।
tato laghulohakaṭorikayā nyubjayā taṃ pāradaṃ koṣṭhyāmācchādya mṛtkarpaṭādinā saṃdhiṃ ruddhvā tadghaṭakharparam aṅgāraiḥ karīṣādimiśraiḥ pūrṇaṃ kuryāt pūrṇaṃ tad ghaṭakharparam aṅgāraiḥ karīṣatuṣamiśraiḥ ।। garbhadravantīti sthāne garbhadrutiḥ sarvalohānāmiti pāṭhaḥ ।। evaṃ rītyā kacchapayantrasthaḥ pāradaḥ svedanato vahnitāpena mardanato biḍādinā saha pākāvasare tatraiva jātena mardanena drutaṃ grāsaṃ tridinaṃ jarati ।। evaṃ caitadyantraṃ garbhadrutipūrvakaṃ jāraṇopayogīti bhāvaḥ ।।
atra jalapūrṇapātraṃ bhūmāveva nikhātaṃ kṛtvā tanmukhe sacchidramuttānaṃ śarāvaṃ dattvā tatra chidre nīrāviyoginīṃ mūṣāṃ kācavilepitāṃ dhṛtvā tatra pāradasyādhastādupariṣṭācca gandhakaṃ dattvā pidhāyoparyupalāgninā gandhakaṃ jārayanti kecit ।। kiṃcaitadghaṭakaśarāve chidrasaṃsthitāṃ pakvamūṣāṃ kṛtvā tasyāmaṣṭāṃśabiḍāvṛtaṃ pāradaṃ dhṛtvā lohapātryāṃ saṃruddhaṃ mudritaṃ ca kṛtvā taduparyaṣṭāṅgulamānāṃ vālukāṃ vinikṣipya haṭhāttadupari dhmānena dhmātaṃ tadgarbhasambhūtaṃ rasaṃ māyūrapittaliptaṃ kāñcanaṃ grāsayantīti ।। sthalakūrmayantraṃ tu kiṃcidgartāyukte bhūtale tathaiva ghaṭakharparaṃ nyubjaṃ nidhāya saṃdhilepādi kṛtvā tadupari sarvataḥ pārśvabhāge ca puṭaṃ dadyāditi ।। tatra gartāyāṃ vanasūraṇādikandodare biḍaṃ tanmadhye sagrāsaṃ pāradaṃ dattvā tatkandaśakalenaivācchādya mṛtkarpaṭādināveṣṭya saṃśoṣya dhārayet ।।
