pṛṣṭhe cāgniṃ saṃtataṃ dinatrayaṃ dadyāt ।। antarāntarā kandaparivartanaṃ kāryaṃ yathā kando na dahyeta ।। evaṃ sthalakūrmayantreṇa jāraṇam vidadhyāditi ।। kande dagdhaprāye sati anyatrānyatra kande pūrvavattaṃ pāradaṃ dhṛtvā pācayet ।।
kacchapayantrāntargatamṛnmayapīṭhasthadīpikāsaṃsthaḥ । yasminnipatati sūtaḥ proktaṃ taddīpikāyantram ।। dīpikāyantramāha kacchapeti ।। vakṣyamāṇakacchapayantramadhyavartimṛnmayaghaṭakharpararūpapīṭhopari pradīpamekam saṃsthāpya tatra sūtaṃ sthāpayet kacchapayantrādhaḥ vahniṃ ca dadyāt evaṃ pradīpasthasūtaḥ kacchapayantre patati tat dīpikākhyaṃ yantraṃ jñeyam ।।
atha dīpikāyantramāha kacchapayantreti ।। jalapūrṇapātramadhye ghaṭakalaśamuttānaṃ nidhāya tatra koṣṭhīmakṛtvā tatsthāne mṛnmayapīṭhaṃ kṛtvā tatra dīpikāṃ nidhāya dīpaṃ prajvālya nāgasvarṇabījasahitaṃ gandhakamanaḥśilāharītālasahitaṃ ca pāradaṃ mardanena piṣṭīkṛtaṃ poṭalikāyāṃ baddhvā kacchapākāranyubjamṛtpātrodare tailamagnāṃ tāṃ poṭalīṃ dīpajvālopari yathā syāttathāvalambitāṃ baddhvā tannyubjaṃ pātraṃ nyubjaṃ nidhāya dīpoṣmaṇā nāgaṃ bhakṣayitvā pārado jalapātre'dhaḥ patati yasmin yantre taddīpikāyantramuktam ।। nāgajāraṇārthasya yantrasyopayogo bodhyaḥ ।। tato jīrṇanāgaṃ pāradaṃ bhasmamūṣāyāṃ dhmānena viyuktaṃ nāgaṃ kṛtvā tasminrase sādhakāvarabījaṃ jārayantīti ।।
dīpikāsaṃstho dīpikopari samyaksthita ityarthaḥ ।। bhāṇḍakaṇṭhādadhaś chidre veṇunālaṃ vinikṣipet । kāṃsyapātradvayaṃ kṛtvā sampuṭaṃ jalagarbhitam ।। nalikāsyaṃ tatra yojyaṃ dṛḍhaṃ taccāpi kārayet ।
yuktadravyairvinikṣiptaḥ pūrvaṃ tatra ghaṭe rasaḥ ।। agninā tāpito nālāttoye tasminpatatyadhaḥ । yāvaduṣṇaṃ bhavet sarvaṃ bhājanaṃ tāvadeva hi । jāyate rasasaṃdhānaṃ ḍekīyantramitīritam ।।
ḍekīyantramāha bhāṇḍakaṇṭhāditi ।। bhāṇḍasya kaṇṭhanimne chidramekaṃ vidhāya tatra vaṃśanirmitaṃ nalamekaṃ saṃyojya sthāpayet ।। anyacca jalapūrṇakāṃsyapātradvayena saṃpuṭamekaṃ kṛtvā bhāṇḍakaṇṭhasthanalāgraṃ tatra praveśya dṛḍhaṃ sandhirodhaṃ kuryāt ।। tato bhāṇḍamadhye nirdiṣṭadravyaiḥ saha rasaṃ kṣiptvā agnijvālā deyā tena nālacchidrānusārī rasaḥ kāṃsyapātramadhyasthajale patati ।।
evaṃ yāvat sarvaṃ pātraṃ uṣṇaṃ bhavet tāvat kuryāt ।। rasasaṃdhānaṃ rasanirgamanam ityarthaḥ ।। atha ḍhekīyantramāha bhāṇḍakaṇṭhāditi ।। adhaśchidra upakaṇṭhaṃ kṛte chidre jalagarbhitaṃ svāduśītajalagarbhitam ।।
yuktadravyaiḥ śuddhiyogyaiḥ kāñjikādibhiḥ pātanopayogidravaiśca saha saṃyukto raso ghaṭe sacchidropakaṇṭhe vahnisthite mṛnmayaghaṭe pūrvaṃ vinikṣiptaḥ kāryaḥ ।। bhājanaṃ sampuṭaghaṭakam adhobhājanam uṣṇaṃ yāvadbhaved ghaṭe tāvadagniḥ kārya ityarthaḥ ।। rasasaṃdhānaṃ pāradasya samyagādhānaṃ sthāpanamityarthaḥ ।। etadyantrasamaṃ degayantraṃ rasasāre'bhihitam ।
bṛhadbhāṇḍaṃ samādāya kukṣau ca chidrasaṃyutam । bhāṇḍe kācaghaṭīṃ kṣiptvā mukhaṃ chidre niyojayet ।। tadāsye kācanālaṃ syāttacca nālamadhomukham । ruddhvā tadā tayoḥ saṃdhimardhaṃ ca nālakaṃ dihet ।।
bhāṇḍaṃ vālukayāpūrya tasya dvāraṃ nirudhya ca । vahneḥ prajvālanaṃ tāvadyāvattannālakaṃ dravet ।। śītaṃ yantraṃ samuttārya ghaṭīṃ prakṣālayettataḥ । drāvaṃ kṣiptvā punardadyātpunaḥ pāko vidhīyate ।।
evaṃ raṅgadrutiḥ proktā degayantre'tiśobhanā । tālo nāgaḥ śilācauraḥ śulvo haṃsaśca gandhakaḥ ।। ete raṅgaṃ vimuñcanti vidrumaṃ gairikaṃ tathā । vālukādegayantreṇa picchakeśā dravanti ca ।।
iti ।। lohamūṣādvayaṃ kṛtvā dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ । īṣacchidrānvitāmekāṃ tatra gandhakasaṃyutām ।। mūṣāyāṃ rasayuktāyām anyasyāṃ tāṃ praveśayet ।
toyaṃ syātsūtakasyādha ūrdhvādho vahnidīpanam ।। jāraṇāyantramāha lohetyādi dvābhyām ।। vitastimānaṃ lauhamayamūṣādvayaṃ nirmāya tayorīṣacchidrānvitāyām ekasyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ gandhakaṃ saṃsthāpayet tataḥ rasagarbhāyāmanyasyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ pūrvoktāṃ sagandhakamūṣāṃ praveśya sūtagarbhamūṣādho jalaṃ sthāpayitvā ūrdhvādhaśca vahniṃ prajvālayediti ।। rasonakarasaṃ bhadre yatnato vastragālitam ।
dāpayetpracuraṃ yatnādāplāvya rasagandhakau ।। sthālikāyāṃ pidhāyordhvaṃ sthālīmanyāṃ dṛḍhāṃ kuru । saṃdhiṃ vilepayedyatnānmṛdā vastreṇa caiva hi ।। sthālyantare kapotākhyaṃ puṭaṃ karṣāgninā sadā ।
yantrasyādhaḥ karīṣāgniṃ dadyāttīvrāgnimeva vā ।। evaṃ tu tridinaṃ kuryāttato yantraṃ vimocayet । taptodake taptacullyāṃ na kuryācchītalāṃ kriyām ।। na tatra kṣīyate sūto na ca gacchati kutracit ।
anena ca krameṇaiva kuryādgandhakajāraṇam ।। yantraṃ vidyādharaṃ jñeyaṃ sthālīdvitayasampuṭāt । cullīṃ caturmukhīṃ kṛtvā yantrabhāṇḍaṃ niveśayet ।। tatrauṣadhaṃ vinikṣipya nirundhyādbhāṇḍakānanam ।
yantraṃ vidyādharaṃ nāma tantrajñaiḥ parikīrtitam ।। vidyādharayantramāha yantramiti ।। sthālīdvitayasampuṭāt haṇḍikādvayakṛtapuṭaviśeṣāt ।। tadeva vivṛṇoti cullīmiti ।।
adhobhāṇḍe auṣadhaṃ nikṣipya bhāṇḍāntareṇa mukhaṃ pidhāya cullyāṃ caturmukhyāṃ saṃsthāpya ca jvālā deyā ।। koṣṭhīyantramiti saṃjñāntaramasya ।। granthāntare tu vidyādharayantralakṣaṇam anyavidhaṃ tattu agre svayameva vakṣyati ।। vidyādharayantramāha ।।
tatra prathamaṃ tatsvarūpaṃ samāsata uktvānantaraṃ savistaramāha yantramiti ।। sthālīdvitayasaṃpuṭāditi ।। samasthūlānāmeva saṃpuṭaṃ bhavati na tu mahadatyalpayoriti ।। iti vakṣyamāṇaḥ sthālīyantrādasyākṛtiviśeṣaḥ sphuṭīkṛtaḥ ।।
atha vistareṇāha cullīṃ caturmukhīmiti ।। sarvatra sāmyenāgnipravṛttyarthaṃ caturmukhīm ityuktam ।। tatra yantrabhāṇḍaṃ niveśayet ।। nirundhyāt ।।
nyubjamukhena pātrāntareṇa saṃpuṭet ।। etadyantram vidyādharanāmnā śāstre parikīrtitam ।। asyopayogastu saumyavīryadravyāṇāṃ mṛdvagninā pākārthaṃ bodhyaḥ ।। ata eva vakṣyati pañcadaśādhyāye kanakasundararase dattvā vidyādhare yantre puṭedāraṇyakopalairiti ।।
ūrdhvaṃ vahniradhaścāpo madhye tu rasasaṃgrahaḥ । somānalam idaṃ proktaṃ jārayedgaganādikam ।। somānalayantramāha ūrdhvamiti ।। gaganādikam abhrādikam ।।
sthālīmadhye rasamūṣāṃ saṃsthāpya śarāveṇa mukhaṃ pidhāya mṛdvastreṇa sandhiṃ liptvā ca jalapūrṇasthālyantaropari sthālīṃ tāṃ sthāpayet śarāvopari karīṣāgniṃ ca dadyād iti ।। atha somānalayantraṃ samāsata āha ūrdhvaṃ vahniriti ।। madhya iti ।। adhaḥpātre jalaṃ tadupari uttānaṃ śarāvādi dattvā tatra laghumūṣāmuttānāṃ dhṛtvā tanmadhye biḍaṃ biḍamadhye sagrāsaṃ pāradaṃ ca dattvā dṛḍhaṃ pidhānena pidhāya tadupari kharparaṃ dattvā tatrāgnir deyaḥ ।।
iti vidhinā gaganasattvādikaṃ jārayediti ।। etadeva yantraṃ sanābhinālaṃ kṛtvāgnimadho dattvā nābhimadhye pāradaṃ sagrāsaṃ dattvā jārayediti prakārāntareṇa rasasāre abhihitam ।। tathā ca tatpāṭhaḥ । somānalasya yantrasya nābhimadhye rasaṃ kṣipet ।
dattvāṣṭāṃśaṃ biḍaṃ nābhiṃ kiṃcidamlena pūrayet ।। kṣārāmlaṃ tryūṣaṇaṃ mūtraṃ rājikā śigru citrakam । nālaṃ prapūrayed ebhir nābheścopari sādhakaḥ ।। dadyādupari yantrasya sacchidraṃ samabudhnakam ।
chidre ca dorakaṃ baddhvā amlaiḥ kharparapūraṇam ।। rasopari patedbinduḥ stokaṃ stokaṃ punaḥ punaḥ । yantrādhaḥ sthāpayedagnim ahorātratrayaṃ budhaḥ ।। tridinair jīryate grāsaṃ sūtako nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
iti ।। sacchidraṃ samabudhnakamiti kharparasya viśeṣaṇam ।। nālaṃ tu kṣārādipūritaṃ kṛtvā kharparacchidrasaṃmukham evocchritaṃ kāryamiti bhāvaḥ ।। etadeva yantraṃ nābhirahitaṃ kṛtvā vaiparītyenāgnijalasthāpanena prāptāgnīṣomākhyaṃ pāradabandhakaraṃ bhavatītyapi tadgranthe evābhihitam ।
athādho'gniruparyāpo madhye deyo raseśvaraḥ । agnīṣomākhyayantreṇa badhyate saptarātrataḥ ।। iti ।। garbhayantraṃ pravakṣyāmi piṣṭikābhasmakārakam ।
caturaṅguladīrghāṃ ca tryaṅgulonmitavistarām ।। mṛnmayīṃ sudṛḍhāṃ mūṣāṃ vartulaṃ kārayenmukham । loṇasya viṃśatirbhāgā bhāga ekastu gugguloḥ ।। suślakṣṇaṃ peṣayitvā tu vāraṃ vāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
mūṣālepaṃ dṛḍhaṃ kṛtvā lavaṇārdhamṛdambubhiḥ ।। karṣet tuṣāgninā bhūmau svedayenmṛdu mānavit । ahorātraṃ trirātraṃ vā rasendro bhasmatāṃ vrajet ।। garbhayantramāha garbhayantramiti ।।
piṣṭikā naṣṭapiṣṭīkṛtaḥ rasaḥ ityarthaḥ ।। loṇasya lavaṇasya loṇasya ityatra lohasya iti pāṭhāntaraṃ na yuktaṃ lavaṇārdhamṛdambubhiḥ iti vakṣyamāṇavākyavirodhāt ।। atra vāraṃ vāramiti padaṃ peṣayitvā tathā punaḥ punariti padaṃ mūṣālepamityanena yojanīyam ।। lavaṇārdhamṛdambubhiriti sahārthe tṛtīyā tena lavaṇārdhamṛdambubhiḥ saha loṇaguggulū peṣayitvā iti tathā viṃśatibhāgalavaṇāpekṣayā mṛdo'rdhatvamiti ca bodhyam ।।
karṣet ātape śoṣayet ।। atha garbhayantraṃ pratijānīte garbhayantramiti ।। yatra sarvaṃ yantraṃ bhūmyudara evāvasthitaṃ vidadhyāt tadgarbhayantraṃ nāma ।। tadeva spaṣṭīkaroti caturaṅguleti ।।
caturaṅguladīrghādilakṣaṇāṃ mūṣāṃ vidhāya tanmukhaṃ vartulaṃ kārayet ।। samyak pidhānasaṃdhānārthaṃ yathoktabhāgaṃ lohakiṭṭaguggulayor gṛhītvā bhāgatrayaṃ mṛdo gṛhītvaikabhāgātmakaṃ lavaṇaṃ gṛhītvā sarvametajjalena saṃmardya tena mūṣāṃ sāntarbahirvilipya tatra dhātvādikṛtapiṣṭikāṃ saṃbhṛtya samyak pidhāya bhūmimadhyagāṃ gajapuṭaparyāptāṃ gartāṃ karīṣamiśratuṣairardhapūritāṃ kṛtvā tatra mūṣāṃ dhṛtvā tadupari garākaṇṭhadaghnaṃ karīṣatuṣaireva sampūryāvaśiṣṭagartāṃ mṛttikayā sampūryāntarvāyupraveśārthaṃ kiṃcidaṅgulīsamaṃ chidraṃ vidhāyāgniṃ dattvā svedayet ।। evaṃ nirvāṇāgnituṣādiyuktyā niṣkāsya punastuṣādipūraṇādisarvamantarāntarā kuryādahorātraparyantaṃ trirātraparyantaṃ veti ।। atra govarapuṭaṃ bhūmāveva deyam ।।
taduktaṃ rasarājasundare ।। cūrṇīkṛtakarīṣāgnau bhūmāveva tu yatpuṭam । dīyate tattu kṛtibhirgovaraṃ samudāhṛtam ।। iti ।।
kharparaṃ sikatāpūrṇaṃ kṛtvā tasyopari nyaset । aparaṃ kharparaṃ tatra śanair mṛdvagninā pacet ।। pañcakṣāraistathā mūtrair lavaṇaṃ ca viḍaṃ tataḥ । haṃsapākaṃ samākhyātaṃ yantraṃ tad vārttikottamaiḥ ।।
sarasāṃ gūḍhavaktrāṃ mṛdvastrāṅgulaghanāvṛtām । śoṣitāṃ kācakalaśīṃ triṣu bhāgeṣu pūrayet ।। bhāṇḍe vitastigambhīre vālukāsupratiṣṭhitā । tadbhāṇḍaṃ pūrayettribhiranyābhiravaguṇṭhayet ।।
bhāṇḍavaktraṃ maṇikayā saṃdhiṃ limpen mṛdā pacet । cullyāṃ tṛṇasya cādāhān maṇikāpṛṣṭhavartinaḥ । etaddhi vālukāyantraṃ tadyantraṃ lavaṇāśrayam ।। vālukāyantramāha sarasāmiti ।।
sarasāṃ pāradagarbhām ।। gūḍhavaktrāṃ saṃkīrṇamukhīm ।। mṛditi ।। mṛdvastreṇa mṛlliptavastreṇa aṅgulaghanaṃ aṅgulamānotsedhaṃ yathā tathā āvṛtām ।।
triṣu bhāgeṣu pūrayet pācyarasādinā kācakalasyāḥ bhāgatrayaṃ pūrayedityarthaḥ ।। triṣu bhāgeṣviti avacchede saptamī ।। bhāṇḍe ityatra kācakalasīṃ sthāpayediti śeṣaḥ ।। vālukābhiḥ kiyān bhāgaḥ pūrayitavya ityapekṣāyāmāha tadbhāṇḍamiti ।।
tribhirityatra ।। bhāgairiti śeṣaḥ ।। tṛtīyā cātra abhede bhāṇḍasya bhāgatrayamityarthaḥ pūrayet vālukayeti śeṣaḥ anyābhiḥ vālukābhirityarthaḥ avaśiṣṭāṃśaṃ pūrayediti śeṣaḥ ।। avaguṇṭhayedityasya maṇikayā ityanena sambandhaḥ maṇikayā śarāveṇa ।।
ayamarthaḥ saṃkīrṇamukhīṃ kācakūpikāṃ mṛdvastreṇāṅgulotsedhamālipya śoṣayitvā ca tasyā bhāgatrayaṃ rasenāpūrayet tato vitastipramāṇagabhīre vālukayā tribhāgapūrṇe bhāṇḍamadhye tāṃ niveśya ūrdhvaṃ vālukayā ācchādayet tataśca śarāveṇa bhāṇḍavaktraṃ pidhāya mṛttikayā saṃdhiṃ liptvā ca tāvat pacet yāvat śarāvopari nyastaṃ tṛṇaṃ na dahediti ।। tulyalakṣaṇatvāt vālukāyantraprasaṅge lavaṇayantram apyatidiśati taditi ।। tad uktaprakāraṃ yantraṃ lavaṇāśrayam api bhavatīti śeṣaḥ lavaṇayantram api vālukāyantram bhavatītyarthaḥ ।। vālukāyantraṃ dvividhamāha surasāmiti ।।
surasāṃ granthikoṭararekhādyabhāvena sulakṣaṇāṃ ।। gūḍhavaktrām akarālamukhām adrimṛtkarpaṭādinā trivāraṃ saptavāraṃ vā kṛtenāṅgulasthūlena veṣṭitām ātape saṃśoṣitāṃ kācaghaṭīm udarasya bhāgacatuṣṭayaṃ parikalpya triṣu bhāgeṣu pūrayet ।। tasyā garbhe bhāgatrayaṃ kajjalyādinā bheṣajena pūrayet ।। evaṃ sampūritāṃ tāṃ vitastigambhīre bhāṇḍe mṛnmaye viśālakharpare pūritavālukāmadhye sthāpitāṃ kuryāt ।।
pūraṇīyavālukāyā mānamapyāha tadbhāṇḍaṃ pūrayediti ।। bhāṇḍodarasyāpi bhāgacatuṣṭayaṃ parikalpya tadbhāṇḍaṃ vālukayā tribhirbhāgairmitayā tribhāgapūraṇaparyāptayā pūrayetsaṃbharet ।। anyābhir avaśiṣṭaikabhāgamitābhir vālukābhiḥ kācakalaśīm abhitaḥ prakṣepeṇāvaguṇṭhayet ।। kaṇṭhaparyantam ācchāditāṃ kuryādityarthaḥ ।।
bhāṇḍamukhaṃ ca maṇikayā viśālanyubjamṛtpātreṇācchādya saṃdhilepādi kṛtvā cullyāṃ pacet ।। tatpacanakālamānam āha tṛṇasyeti ।। maṇikāpṛṣṭhe prakṣiptatṛṇadāhaparyantaṃ pacet ।। tṛṇadāhetyupalakṣaṇam ।।
sindūrarasādau raktavarṇotpattiparyantamapi pākasyāvaśyakatvāt ।। sa ca varṇo jñeyaḥ ।। kūpīmukhād udgataraktavarṇabāṣpadarśaneneti bodhyam ।। pañcāḍhavālukāpūrṇabhāṇḍe nikṣipya yatnataḥ ।
pacyate rasagolādyaṃ vālukāyantram īritam ।। anyavidhaṃ vālukāyantramāha pañceti ।। catvāriṃśaccharāvamitavālukāpūrṇabhāṇḍe ityarthaḥ ।। atra vālukāmadhye eva rasagolādikaṃ sthāpayet na tu kācakūpyāmiti viśeṣaḥ ।।
evaṃ lavaṇanikṣepātproktaṃ lavaṇayantrakam ।। antaḥkṛtarasālepatāmrapātramukhasya ca । liptvā mṛllavaṇenaiva saṃdhiṃ bhāṇḍatalasya ca ।। tadbhāṇḍaṃ paṭunāpūrya kṣārairvā pūrvavatpacet ।
evaṃ lavaṇayantraṃ syād rasakarmaṇi śasyate ।। antaḥ kṛtarasālepa iti ।। ālepa ityupalakṣaṇam ।। mṛdbhāṇḍe kharparasamāne viśālamukhe'ntastale nyubjaṃ sthāpanīyaṃ yallaghu tāmrapātraṃ tat pāradādigolakopari nyubjaṃ nidhāya mṛllavaṇādinā bhāṇḍatalatāmrapātramukhasaṃdhiṃ vilipya tayantrabhāṇḍaṃ lavaṇakṣārādyanyatamenāpūrya pidhānena pidhāya praharaparyantaṃ śālisphuṭanaparyantaṃ praharaparyantaṃ vā pacet ।।
evaṃvidhamapi yantraṃ lavaṇayantrākhyametad rasakarmaṇi pākamūrchanādikarmaṇi praśastaṃ syāt ।। lavaṇayantrasya prakārāntaramāha antariti ।। antas tāmrapātramadhye ityarthaḥ kṛtaḥ rasena ālepaḥ yatra tathābhūtaṃ yat tāmrapātraṃ tasya mukhaṃ tasya rasaliptodaratāmrapātramukhasya tathā bhāṇḍatalasya tāmrapātramukhopari sthāpitabhāṇḍādhobhāgasya ।। tadbhāṇḍam uparisthabhāṇḍam ।।
pūrvavat tṛṇasya cādāhād ityarthaḥ ।। tāmrapātrodare rasaṃ nikṣipya tadupari lavaṇapūrṇaṃ kṣārapūrṇaṃ vā bhāṇḍamekaṃ vinyaset tato mṛllavaṇena sandhiṃ ruddhvā pacet iti ।। lohanālagataṃ sūtaṃ bhāṇḍe lavaṇapūrite । niruddhaṃ vipacetprāgvan nālikāyantram īritam ।।
nālikāyantramāha loheti ।। lauhamayanālamadhye pāradam āpūrya chidrarodhaṃ kṛtvā ca lavaṇapūritabhāṇḍāntaḥ nālaṃ taṃ nirundhyāttato maṇikayā bhāṇḍavaktram ācchādya ālipya ca sandhiṃ tāvat pacet yāvat śarāvoparisthaṃ tṛṇaṃ na dahet iti ।। vālukāgūḍhasarvāṅgāṃ garte mūṣāṃ rasānvitām । dīptopalaiḥ saṃvṛṇuyād yantraṃ tad bhūdharāhvayam ।।
atha bhūdharayantramāha vāluketi ।। garte rājahastamātragambhīre garte hastamātrāyāmavistāre caturasre vartule vā tādṛśe garte rasānvitāṃ pāradagarbhitāṃ mallamūṣāṃ vālukāgūḍhasarvāṅgāṃ nidhāya gartakaṇṭhaparyantaṃ vālukayā prapūryopari kiṃcitpārśve ca dīptavanyopalaiḥ saṃvṛṇuyādācchādayet ।। samantato vanyopalairācchādya jvālayedityarthaḥ ।। atra pāradasya yantraṇamātraṃ vālukāyāṃ bhūmāveva vahnistūparyeva garbhayantre sarvameva bhūgarbhe ।।
bhūdharapuṭe tu na vālukāsaṃbandhaḥ ।। iti trayāṇāṃ yantrapuṭānāṃ viśeṣo bodhyaḥ ।। śarāvasampuṭāntasthaṃ karīṣeṣv agnimānavit । paceccullyāṃ dviyāmaṃ vā rasaṃ tat puṭayantrakam ।।
puṭayantramāha śarāveti ।। karīṣeṣu pacet athavā agnimānavid dviyāmaṃ cullyām aṅgāreṣu paced yojyam ।। atha puṭayantramāha śarāveti ।। bhūmitale karīṣarāśiṃ kṛtvā tatra śarāvasaṃpuṭitaṃ pāradaṃ ca dhṛtvāgnimānavidvaidyo ghāṭikādvayaparyantaṃ pacet ।।
atyantasaṃnihitāgnisaṃyogāt ।। athavā cullyāṃ karīṣāgniṃ dattvādhiśritakharpare śarāvasaṃpuṭitaṃ rasaṃ dhṛtvā kharparamukhamācchādya yāmaparyantaṃ dviyāmaṃ vā pacet ।। dūratarāgnisaṃyogāt ।। evaṃ nyūnādhikaḥ pacanakālo rasayogidravyādyudgamaśālitvāvayavaśaithilyakāṭhinyādyanurodhena svabuddhyaiva tarkya iti bhāvaḥ ।।
ṣoḍaśāṅgulavistīrṇaṃ hastamātrāyataṃ samam । dhātusattvanipātārthaṃ koṣṭhīyantram iti smṛtam ।। koṣṭhīyantramāha ṣoḍaśeti ।। atra samamiti padena militabhāṇḍadvayasya ṣoḍaśāṅgulatvādi bodhyam evaṃ ca vitastipramāṇadīrghasya aṣṭāṅgulavistīrṇasya ca adhobhāṇḍasya mukhopari tāvanmānaṃ bhāṇḍāntaram adhomukhaṃ saṃsthāpya adho dṛḍhāṅgārair bhastrayā dhamet tena dhātusattvaṃ nirgacchatīti ।।
atrisaṃhitāyām etacchlokānantaram asyaivāparāṃśaḥ paṭhitaḥ tadyathā ।। paripūrṇaṃ dṛḍhāṅgārairadho vātena koṣṭhake । mātrayā jvālamārgeṇa jvālayecca hutāśanam ।। iti ।।
atha koṣṭhīyantramāha ṣoḍaśāṅguleti ।। dhātusattveti ।। viśiṣṭadhātūnāṃ tāpyagairikavimalādīnām anudgamaśālināṃ mṛdūnāṃ ca sattvasya nipātārtham etadyantraṃ vidyāt ।। asyāṃ koṣṭhyāṃ madhya ucitāṃ dhātugarbhitāṃ vṛntākādimūṣāṃ saṃsthāpya kokilair mūṣām uparyuparibhāvena pārśvataśca sampūrya yathocitaṃ dhamet ।।
laghubhastrikādinetyarthaḥ ।। koṣṭhīyantre sattvanipātanārhā dhātava udāhṛtāśca rasasāre । vaikrāntaṃ sasyakaṃ tāpyaṃ kāntābhre vimalaṃ giriḥ । gairikā tutthakaṃ caiva rājāvarto viśeṣataḥ ।।
eṣām uparasānāṃ ca koṣṭhe sattvanipātanam । iti ।। yatra lohamaye pātre pārśvayorvalayadvayam । tādṛk svalpataraṃ pātraṃ valayaprotakoṣṭhakam ।।
pūrvapātropari nyasya svalpapātre parikṣipet । rasaṃ saṃmūrchitaṃ sthūlapātram āpūrya kāñjikaiḥ ।। dviyāmaṃ svedayedeva rasotthāpanahetave । etatsyād valabhīyantraṃ rase ṣāḍguṇyakārakam ।
sūkṣmakāntamaye pātre rasaḥ syādguṇavattaraḥ ।। valabhīyantramāha yatreti ।। valayadvayaṃ valayaṃ kaḍā āṃṭā iti khyātaṃ ।। tādṛk lohamayam ।।
valayeti ।। valaye bṛhatpātrasthavalaye protam ābaddhaṃ koṣṭhaṃ madhyadeśo yasya tādṛśam ।। ayamartho bṛhadākāraṃ kāntalauhamayaṃ pātramekaṃ nirmāya tasyāntargalād adhaḥpārśvadvaye valayadvayaṃ saṃyojanīyaṃ kṣudrākāram aparamapi tathāvidhaṃ pātramekaṃ kṛtvā bṛhatpātrasthe valaye aspṛṣṭatalabhāgaṃ yathā tathā ābadhya tatra mūrchitarasaṃ parikṣipet kāñjikena sthūlapātraṃ ca pūrayediti ।। rase ṣāḍguṇyakārakaṃ ṣāḍguṇyaṃ vidyā vitarko vijñānaṃ smṛtistatparatā kriyā ityuktaṣaḍguṇapradaśaktijanakam evaṃvidharasopayoktā uktaṣāḍguṇyasiddhiṃ labhate ityarthaḥ ।।
atha khalacarīyantramāha yatreti ।। yantrabhūte lohapātra ābhyantaropakaṇṭhe pārśvayor avasañjanārthaṃ valayadvayaṃ kāryaṃ ।। valayamadhye tu praveśārhakoṣṭhakaṃ lauhaṃ svalpapātramanyadvidhāya mūrchitarasagarbhitaṃ tatsvalpapātraṃ praveśya valayayor avasajjitaṃ kṛtvā sthūlapātre kāñjikaṃ prabhūtaṃ dattvā cullyāṃ mandāgninā praharaparyantaṃ svedayet ।। tena pārada utthāya kāñjikadrave praviśya tiṣṭhati ata evāsya yantrasya jalāhāryayantram ityapi nāmāntaraṃ kāñjikajalena svalpapātrād rasasya hriyamāṇatvāditi ।।
mūrchito rasa utthāya khale'ṅgaṇe carituṃ śaknotyaneneti vyutpattyā khalacarītyapi nāma ।। atra yatsvalpaṃ pātraṃ tatkāntamayaṃ kṛtvā yantre tatpātramadhye pārado dhṛtaśced atiśayena guṇavānbhavati ।। uktaṃ ca rasārṇave । na sūtena vinā kāntaṃ na kāntena vinā rasaḥ ।
kāntasūtasamāyogāt prayogo dehadhārakaḥ ।। iti ।। kṣipedrasaṃ ghaṭe dīrghanatādhonālasaṃyute । tannālaṃ nikṣipedanyaghaṭakukṣyantare khalu ।।
tatra ruddhvā mṛdā samyagvadane ghaṭayoratha । adhastādrasakumbhasya jvālayettīvrapāvakam ।। itarasminghaṭe toyaṃ prakṣipetsvādu śītalam । tiryakpātanam etaddhi vārttikair abhidhīyate ।।
tiryakpātanayantramāha kṣipediti ।। dīrghanatādhonālasaṃyute dīrghākāraṃ nataṃ nimnābhimukhaṃ ca yat adhonālaṃ tena saṃyute ।। ayaṃ vidhiḥ ekasmin ghaṭe rasaṃ nidhāya tasya udarādho dīrgham adholambitaṃ nālamekaṃ saṃyojya dvitīyaghaṭodarasthacchidre nālāgraṃ praveśya mṛdvastreṇa sandhimālipya ca ghaṭayormukham api tathā limpet rasakumbhādhaśca tīvrāgniṃ prajvālayet dvitīyaghaṭe svāduśītalaṃ jalaṃ ca prakṣipet iti ।। atha tiryakpātanayantramāha kṣipedrasamiti ।।
natādhonāleti natopakaṇṭhacchidrasaṃlagnādhonālasaṃyute ।। anyaghaṭaḥ pārśve nimnadeśe sthitaḥ ।। tato ghaṭayorvadane ruddhvā pidhānābhyāṃ pidhāya saṃdhilepādi kṛtvādho ghaṭayor vadanayor adhaḥsthitanalikāyojitacchidrayor api saṃdhilepaṃ kṛtvā jvālayet ।। ghaṭāntare tāpotpattiparyantaṃ pāradaśuddhyartham etadyantrasyopayogo bodhyaḥ ।।
caṣakaṃ vartulaṃ lauhaṃ vinatāgrordhvadaṇḍakam । etaddhi pālikāyantraṃ balijāraṇahetave ।। pālikāyantramāha caṣakamiti ।। caṣakaṃ darvīsamānaṃ pātram ।।
tattu na tiryagdaṇḍaṃ kiṃtu vinatāya ucchrito daṇḍo yasya tathoktam ।। etadyantraṃ sadhūmagandhakajāraṇopayogi tathā bhairavanāthoktaparpaṭyādividhau copayokṣyate ।। pālikāyantramāha caṣakamiti ।। vinatam agraṃ yasya tat nyubjīkṛtāgrabhāgam ūrdhvam uccaiḥkṛtaṃ daṇḍaṃ yasya tad unnatadaṇḍaṃ vinatāgraṃ ca tad ūrdhvadaṇḍaṃ ceti vinatāgrordhvadaṇḍakaṃ lauhaṃ lohamayaṃ vartulaṃ golākāraṃ caṣakaṃ kaṭorikā kāryamiti śeṣaḥ ।।
caṣakaśabdasya madyapānapātrārthakatve'pi pātramātrārthakatvaṃ prāgeva pradarśitam ।। balijāraṇahetave gandhakajāraṇārtham ।। catuṣprasthajalādhāraś caturaṅgulikānanaḥ । ghaṭayantram idaṃ proktaṃ tadāpyāyanakaṃ smṛtam ।।
ghaṭayantramāha caturiti ।। ṣoḍaśaśarāvamitajaladhāraṇasamarthaḥ caturaṅgulavistṛtamukhaviśiṣṭaśca ghaṭaḥ ghaṭayantramiti niṣkarṣaḥ ।। āpyāyanakaṃ rasādīnāṃ tarpaṇaṃ ṣāḍguṇyasaṃpādanamiti yāvat ।। āpyāyanakam ityatra utthāpanakam iti pāṭhe rasotthāpanasādhanamityarthaḥ ।।
vidhāya vartulaṃ gartaṃ mallamatra nidhāya ca । vinidhāyeṣṭakāṃ tatra madhyagartavatīṃ śubhām ।। gartasya paritaḥ kuryātpālikām aṅgulocchrayām । garte sūtaṃ vinikṣipya gartāsye vasanaṃ kṣipet ।।
nikṣipedgandhakaṃ tatra mallenāsyaṃ nirudhya ca । mallapālikayormadhye mṛdā samyaṅ nirudhya ca ।। vanopalaiḥ puṭaṃ deyaṃ kapotākhyaṃ na cādhikam । iṣṭikāyantram etat syād gandhakaṃ tena jārayet ।।
iṣṭakāyantramāha vidhāyeti ।। mallaṃ śarāvapātram ।। pālikām ālavālam ।। golākāraṃ gartamekam kṛtvā tatra śarāvaṃ saṃsthāpya tadupari madhyacchidrāmiṣṭakām ekāṃ vinyaset iṣṭakāgartaṃ paritaḥ aṅgulimitonnatam ālavālam ekaṃ ca kuryāt tata iṣṭakārandhre pāradaṃ vinikṣipya randhramukhe vastraṃ tadupari gandhakaṃ ca vinyasya śarāvāntareṇa ruddhvā śarāvālavālayoḥ saṃdhiṃ mṛdā samyagālipya ca vanyakarīṣaiḥ kapotākhyapuṭaṃ dadyāditi niṣkarṣaḥ ।।
atheṣṭikāyantraṃ lakṣayati nidhāya vartulāmiti ।। mallaṃ gambhīrodaraṃ kṣudraṃ mṛnmayaṃ pātraṃ tadgartāmadhye saṃsthāpya tatraikām iṣṭikāṃ madhyagartavatīṃ ca nidhāyeṣṭikāghaṭakagartasya paritaḥ samantato'ṅgulocchrāyāṃ pālikām ālavālaṃ vidhāya tadgarte pāradaṃ kṣiptvā tadgartamukhe vastraṃ prasārya tacca dṛḍhaṃ baddhvā tadupari samabhāgaṃ gandhakaṃ dattvā nyubjamallena gartamukhaṃ ruddhvā mallapālimadhyabhāgaṃ mṛdā samyagruddhvopari vanyopalaiḥ kapotapuṭaṃ punaḥ punardeyam ।। iṣṭikayā pāradasya yantraṇād etadyantram iṣṭikāyantranāmnā kathitam ।। tena nirdhūmagandhakajāraṇaṃ kuryāt ।।
jīrṇe ca gandhake pārado raktavarṇo bhavet ।। atra drutapārade gandhakajāraṇāyāṃ gartāsye vastrācchādanaṃ vastropari gandhakaṃ ca dadyāditi vidhikramaḥ ।। yatra tu baddhasya rasasya gandhakajāraṇā kartavyā syāttadā tu pāradaṃ vastreṇa baddhvā tasyādhastād upariṣṭācca gandhakaṃ dattvā jārayedityanukto'pi viśeṣo bodhyaḥ ।। sthālikopari vinyasya sthālīṃ samyaṅ nirudhya ca ।
ūrdhvasthālyāṃ jalaṃ kṣiptvā vahniṃ prajvālayed adhaḥ । etad vidyādharaṃ yantraṃ hiṅgulākṛṣṭihetave ।। hiṅgulākṛṣṭividyādharayantramāha sthālikoparīti ।। sthālīmityatra ūrdhvamukhīmiti śeṣo bodhyaḥ ।।
atra hiṅgulākṛṣṭiprakārasya anuktatvāt granthāntaroktastatprakāraḥ pradarśyate tadyathā jambīrādirasaśodhitahiṅgulam adhaḥsthālyāṃ parṇopari saṃsthāpya kaṭhinīghṛṣṭatalabhāgām uttānāṃ sthālīmaparāṃ tadupari dattvā mṛdambarādibhiḥ saṃdhim ālipya ca adho jvālā deyā ūrdhvasthālyāṃ jalaṃ ca uṣṇe ca tasmin tat nikṣipya punardeyam evaṃ triṃśadvāraṃ kuryāt ।। granthāntare'sya ūrdhvapātanamiti nāmāntaram ।। kṛcidetad anantaraṃ । rasaṃ saṃmūrchitaṃ sthūlapātram āpūrya kāñjikaiḥ ।
dviyāmaṃ svedayedenaṃ rasotthāpanahetave ।। ityadhikaḥ pāṭho vidyate ।। atha hiṅgulākṛṣṭividyādharayantramāha sthālikopari vinyasyeti ।। antastale nihitaśuṣkahiṅgulāyā viśālamukhāyāḥ sthālikāyā uparyuttānāmeva laghusthālīṃ vinyasya sthāpayitvā saṃdhilepādinā ruddhvordhvasthālyāṃ kiṃcicchītalajalaṃ punaḥ punardadyāt ।।
adhaścullyāṃ vahniṃ jvālayetpraharatrayaparyantam ।। etadyantraṃ pāradasya hiṅgulād viyujyordhvapātratala ākṛṣṭikaraṃ syāt ।। etadākṛṣṭarasasya ṣoḍaśādhyāye caṇḍasaṃgrahagadaikakapāṭavidhāvanyatra copayogaṃ vakṣyati ।। yantrasthālyupari sthālīṃ nyubjāṃ dattvā nirundhayet ।
yantraṃ ḍamarukākhyaṃ tadrasabhasmakṛte hitam ।। atha ḍamaruyantramāha pāradauṣadhagarbhitayantrasthālyupari nyubjāmeva sthālīṃ nidhāya nirundhayet ।। mṛtkarpaṭādinā saṃdhirodhaṃ kuryāt ।। yantrasyādhastād agniḥ kāryaḥ ।।
etad yantraṃ ḍamarukākhyam ūrdhvatalagapāradabhasmakarmaṇyupayujyate ।। mallamadhye caredgartaṃ tatra sūtaṃ sagandhakam । gartasya paritaḥ kuḍyaṃ prakuryādaṅgulocchritam ।। tataś cācchādayet samyag gostanākāramūṣayā ।
samyak toyamṛdā ruddhvā samyagatrocyamānayā ।। lehavat kṛtababbūlakvāthena parimarditam । jīrṇakiṭṭarajaḥ sūkṣmaṃ guḍacūrṇasamanvitam । iyaṃ hi jalamṛt proktā durbhedyā salilaiḥ khalu ।।
khaṭikāpaṭukiṭṭaiśca mahiṣīdugdhamarditaiḥ । vahnimṛtsnā bhaved ghoravahnitāpasahā khalu ।। etayā mṛtsnayā ruddho na gantuṃ kṣamate rasaḥ । vidagdhavanitāprauḍhapremṇā ruddhaḥ pumāniva ।।
nandī nāgārjunaścaiva brahmajyotir munīśvaraḥ । vetti śrīsomadevaśca nāparaḥ pṛthivītale ।। tato jalaṃ vinikṣipya vahniṃ prajvālayedadhaḥ । nābhiyantramidaṃ proktaṃ nandinā sarvavedinā ।
anena jīryate sūto nirdhūmaḥ śuddhagandhakaḥ ।। nābhiyantramāha mallamadhye iti ।। kuḍyaṃ bhittiḥ ālavālākāramiti yāvat ।। atrocyamānayā atra yantre ucyamānayā kathyamānayā toyamṛdā lehavad ityādinā vakṣyamāṇayā paribhāṣikamṛdā ityarthaḥ ।।
atra prathamaṃ samyag ācchādayed dvitīyaṃ samyak ruddhvā tṛtīyaṃ samyag ucyamānayā sambadhyate ।। toyamṛtprakāramāha lehavaditi ।। lepārthamṛttikāprastutaprasaṅgakrameṇa vahnimṛtprakāramāha khaṭiketi ।। ayaṃ vidhiḥ pātramadhye kiṃcid gartaṃ kṛtvā tatra rasagandhau niveśya gartasya caturdikṣu aṅgulocchrāyam ālavālaṃ kuryāt tato gostanākṛtimūṣayā sālavālaṃ sarasagandhakaṃ gartam ācchādya toyamṛdā sandhiṃ limpet tatastatra jalaṃ dattvā yantrādho vahniṃ dāpayed iti ।।
atha nābhiyantramāha mallamadhya iti ।। dṛḍhasthūlavistṛtamṛtpātramadhye gartaṃ kuryāt ।। tatra pāradaṃ gandhakaṃ ca nidadhyāt ।। tato gartasya samantato'ṅgulocchrāyaṃ kuḍyākāraṃ bandhaṃ kuryāt ।।
tatastaṃ gartaṃ gostanākāramūṣayā nyubjayā pidadhyāt ।। atrocyamānayā toyamṛdākhyayā mṛdā saṃdhiṃ ruddhvā saṃśoṣyoparisthitasarvamallabhāgaṃ kaṇṭhaparyantaṃ jalena pūrayet ।। yantrasyādhastācca cullyāṃ vahniṃ prajvālayedityantimaślokena saṃbandho bodhyaḥ ।। atra jalamṛcchabdabodhārthaṃ jalamṛdaṃ tatprasaṅgācca vahnimṛdaṃ ca madhyasthitagranthenāha lehavaditi ।।
ghanena babbūlatvakkaṣāyeṇa purāṇaṃ lohakiṭṭacūrṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ kaṇaṃ yathā syāttathā saṃmardya tatra guḍacūrṇaṃ samaṃ dattvā punaḥ saṃmardya kṛteyaṃ mṛjjalamṛditi khyātā ।। atha khaṭikāśvetacūrṇadravyaṃ khaḍū cāsa iti vākhyātam ।। paṭu saindhavam ।। lohakiṭṭaṃ ca sarvametanmithaḥ samaṃ gṛhītvā mahiṣīdugdhena saṃmardya vihiteyaṃ mṛdvahnimṛdākhyātā ।।
iyaṃ ca tīkṣṇaṃ vahnipātaṃ sahata ityanvarthākhyā ।। etayā ruddho rasastaruṇyā kṛtasnehena baddhaḥ puruṣaḥ ivānyatra gantuṃ na śaknoti ।। asya yantrasya jalayantramiti nāmāntaraṃ kecidvadanti ।। pāṣāṇabhedirasavidhāvasyopayogaṃ vakṣyati ।।
rasasāre pāradabandhanārthamapyasya yantrasyopayogamudājahāra ।। mūṣāṃ mūṣodarāviṣṭām ādyantaḥsamavartulām । cipiṭāṃ ca tale proktaṃ grastayantraṃ manīṣibhiḥ । sūtendrarandhanārthaṃ hi rasavidbhir udīritam ।।
grastayantramāha mūṣāmiti ।। sūtendrarandhanārthaṃ rasapākārtham ।। atha grastayantramāha mūṣāmiti ।। sthūlamūṣodare praveśayogyām ādyantamadhyabhāgeṣu tatsamavartulāṃ laghumūṣāṃ kuryāt ।।
etadyantraṃ grastayantramiti khyātam ।। anena hi svodare ruddhagatiḥ pārado grastaḥ pīḍito mārakabheṣajena mārito vā bhavati ।। kajjalīkṛtaṃ bheṣajāntareṇa saṃmarditaṃ vā pāradaṃ sthūlamūṣāntastale saṃbhṛtya tadrodhārthaṃ kiṃcillaghumūṣāṃ nyubjāṃ tadudare praveśya dṛḍhaṃ yathā syāttathā saṃdhirodhaṃ kṛtvā gajapuṭena pāradaṃ bhasmīkurvanti bhiṣajaḥ ।। randhraṇaṃ bandhanam ।।
sthālyāṃ tāmrādi nikṣipya mallenāsyaṃ nirudhya ca । pacyate sthālikādhastāt sthālīyantram idaṃ smṛtam ।। atha sthālīyantramāha sthālyāmiti ।। sthālyāṃ mṛnmayapātryāṃ tāmralohādi nikṣipya mallena niruddhamukhaṃ kṛtvā tadbheṣajaṃ sthālikādhaḥsthavahninā pacyate ityetat sthālīyantraṃ prasiddham ।।
vidhāyāṣṭāṅgulaṃ pātraṃ lauhamaṣṭāṅgulocchrayam । kaṇṭhādho hy aṅgule deśe galādhāre hi tatra ca ।। tiryaglohaśalākāśca tanvīstiryag vinikṣipet । tanūni svarṇapattrāṇi tāsāmupari vinyaset ।।
pattrādho nikṣiped vakṣyamāṇam ihaiva hi । tatpātraṃ nyubjapātreṇa chādayedapareṇa hi ।। mṛdā vilipya saṃdhiṃ ca vahniṃ prajvālayed adhaḥ । tena pattrāṇi kṛtsnāni hatāny uktavidhānataḥ ।।
rasaścarati vegena drutaṃ garbhe dravanti ca । gandhālakaśilānāṃ hi kajjalyā vā mṛtāhinā ।। dhūpanaṃ svarṇapattrāṇāṃ prathamaṃ parikīrtitam । tārārthaṃ tārapattrāṇi mṛtavaṅgena dhūpayet ।।
dhūpayecca yathāyogyairanyairuparasairapi । dhūpayantramidaṃ proktaṃ jāraṇādravyasādhane ।। dhūpayantramāha vidhāyeti ।। galādhāre śalākāsthāpanārthaṃ galadeśasthapālikāvad ādhāraviśeṣe ityarthaḥ ।।
atra prathamaṃ tiryak lohaśalākā ityanena dvitīyaṃ ca vinikṣipet ityanena sambadhyate ।। tiryak vakrākārāḥ tanvīḥ sūkṣmāḥ lohaśalākāḥ tiryak vakrabhāvena vinikṣipet ityanvayaḥ ।। tenetyādi ।। uktavidhinā hatāni kṛtsnāni patrāṇi drutaṃ garbhe dravanti tataśca rasaḥ sa svarṇapatradravaḥ vegena carati svakāryaṃ sādhayatītyarthaḥ ।।
patrādho nikṣipeddhūmamityuktaṃ kiṃtaddhūmamityāha gandheti ।। prathamaṃ śreṣṭham ।। dairghyavistārato aṣṭāṅgulamānaṃ lohapātramekaṃ kārayitvā tasya kaṇṭhādhaḥ aṅgulidvayaparimitasthāne galādhāre sūkṣmatiryaglohaśalākāḥ tiryagbhāvena vinyasya tadupari kaṇṭakavedhyasvarṇapatrāṇi sthāpayet tatpatrādhaḥ pātrābhyantare gandhakaharitālamanaḥśilābhiḥ kṛtakajjalīṃ mṛtanāgaṃ vā nikṣipya adhomukhapātrāntareṇa tat pātraṃ pidhāya mṛdādinā sandhiṃ ruddhvā ca pātrādho vahniṃ prajvālayettena saṃtaptakajjalyādito dhūmaṃ nirgatya svarṇapatre lagiṣyati patrāṇi tāni bhasmībhavanti garbhe dravanti ca ।। atha dhūpayantramāha vidhāyeti ।।
atra yathoktamānaṃ lauhaṃ pātraṃ vidhāya tatkaṇṭhādho dvyaṅgule deśe jalādhāraṃ laghupātraviśeṣaṃ nihitaṃ kuryāt ।। jaḍadravyasya dhāraṇārtham āśrayabhūtaṃ pātraṃ jalādhāraśabdavācyam ।। tatra lohaśalākāstiryaṅnidhāya tatra svarṇapatrāṇi vinyaset sthāpayet ।। teṣāmadhobhāge vakṣyamāṇaṃ dhūmadravyaṃ nikṣipet ।।
tato yantrapātram apareṇa nyubjapātreṇa chādayet ।। mṛdā saṃdhilepaṃ kṛtvā yantrasyādhastādvahniṃ kuryāt ।। uktavidhānena hatāni patrāṇi kṛṣṇāni bhavanti ।। tatastāni sarase taptakhalve yathāvidhi mardanena pārado bhakṣayati ।।
bhakṣitāni ca tāni pāradodare śīghraṃ dravanti ।। atra dhūpadravyamāha ।। pāradena sākaṃ gandhakaharitālamanaḥśilānām anyatamasya samastānāṃ vā kṛtāyāḥ kajjalyā dhūpanaṃ tayā kajjalyā bhasmīkṛtanāgena dhūpanaṃ vā svarṇapatrāṇāṃ dhūpanasaṃskārārthaṃ mukhyaṃ dhūpanadravyam udāhṛtam ।। tārārthaṃ dhūpanaṃ tūcyata iti śeṣaḥ ।।
tadāha tārapatrāṇyuktakajjalyā mṛtena vaṅgena dhūpayet ।। yathāyogyair māraṇayogyair uparasair hiṅgūlarasakamākṣikādibhir api dhūpayet ।। jāraṇādravasādhanaṃ patrāṇāṃ jāraṇopayogipāradagarbhadravasādhanam ityarthaḥ ।। sthūlasthālyāṃ jalaṃ kṣiptvā vāso baddhvā mukhe dṛḍham ।
tatra svedyaṃ vinikṣipya tanmukhaṃ prapidhāya ca ।। adhastājjvālayedagniṃ yantraṃ tatkandukābhidham । svedanīyantramityanye prāhuścedaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ ।। spaṣṭam ।।
svedanīyantratayā prāguktamapi idaṃ saṃjñāntarapradarśanārthaṃ punaruktam athavā tatra sthālyā viśeṣo noktaḥ ataḥ yā kācit sthālī eva grāhyā atra tu sthūlasthālī eva grāhyā ataḥ svedanīyantrāt asya vaiśiṣṭyam iti ।। prāguktaṃ svedanīyantrameva kandukayantranāmnāha sthūlasthālyāmiti ।। anye manīṣiṇo dhīrā vakṣyamāṇaprakāreṇa prāhuḥ yadveti ।। tatkandukayantramiti ।।
evaṃ ca teṣāṃ mate svedanīyantram asmād bhinnam eveti bhāvaḥ ।। puṣpādīnām atimṛdudravyāṇāṃ kalkāder vā svedanārtham asya yantrasyopayogo bodhyaḥ ।। yadvā sthālyāṃ jalaṃ kṣiptvā tṛṇaṃ kṣiptvā mukhopari । svedyadravyaṃ parikṣipya pidhānaṃ pravidhāya ca ।
adhastājjvālayedagniṃ yantraṃ tat kandukaṃ smṛtam ।। khallayogyā śilā nīlā śyāmā snigdhā dṛḍhā guruḥ । ṣoḍaśāṅgulakotsedhā navāṅgulakavistarā ।। caturviṃśāṅgulā dīrghā gharṣaṇī dvādaśāṅgulā ।
viṃśatyaṅguladīrghā vā syādutsedhe daśāṅgulā । khallapramāṇaṃ tajjñeyaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ syādrasakarmaṇi ।। atha khalvasaṃjñāyogyā sā śilā syāt ।। yā nīlā śyāmavarṇā vā snigdhādiguṇaviśiṣṭā ṣoḍaśāṅgulakocchrāyā tathā navāṅgulakavistārā caturviṃśāṅgulair ā samantāddīrghā ca syāt ।।
sā khalvayogyeti pūrvatra saṃbandhaḥ ।। gharṣaṇī tu dvādaśāṅguladīrghā syāt ।। punaḥ khalvaśilāmānavikalpamāha viṃśatyaṅguleti ।। athavā khalvaśilā viṃśatyaṅguladīrghā ।।
utsedha ucchrāye ca daśāṅgulā kāryeti viśeṣaḥ ।। navāṅguleti vistāramānaṃ tu prāguktameva grāhyam ।। khallayantramāha khallayogyeti ।। utsedhaḥ pārśvata unnataḥ ।।
dīrghaḥ āyāmena unnataḥ iti dīrghotsedhayor bhedaḥ ।। gharṣaṇī kaṇḍanī putrikā iti yāvat noíā iti bhāṣā ।। khallayantraṃ tridhā proktaṃ rasādisukhamardane ।। nirudgārau sumasṛṇau kāryau putrikayā yutau ।।
utsedhe sa daśāṅgulaḥ khalu kalātulyāṅgulāyāmavān vistāreṇa daśāṅgulo munimitairnimnas tayaivāṅgulaiḥ । gharṣaḥ śilāputraḥ ।। pālyāṃ dvyaṅgulivistaraśca masṛṇo atīvārdhacandropamo gharṣo dvādaśakāṅgulaśca tadayaṃ khallo mataḥ siddhaye ।। asminpañcapalaḥ sūto mardanīyo viśuddhaye ।
tattadaucityayogena khalleṣvanyeṣu yojayet ।। dvādaśāṅgulavistāraḥ khallo atimasṛṇopalaḥ । caturaṅgulanimnaśca madhye atimasṛṇīkṛtaḥ ।। mardakaś cipiṭo adhastāt sugrāhaśca śikhopari ।
ayaṃ tu vartulaḥ khallo mardane'tisukhapradaḥ ।। mardanārthaṃ dvitīyaṃ vartulakhallamāha dvādaśeti ।। mardaka iti ।। putrikā adhobhāge cipiṭavadvistīrṇā uparibhāge ca sukhena yathā dhāraṇīyā bhavati tathā kartavyā ityarthaḥ ।।
lauho navāṅgulaḥ khallo nimnatve ca ṣaḍaṅgulaḥ । mardako aṣṭāṅgulaścaiva taptakhallābhidho apyayam ।। kṛtvā khallākṛtiṃ cullīm aṅgāraiḥ paripūritām । tasyāṃ niveśya taṃ khallaṃ pārśve bhastrikayā dhamet ।।
tadantarmarditā piṣṭiḥ kṣārairamlaiśca saṃyutā । pradravatyativegena sveditā nātra saṃśayaḥ । kṛtaḥ kāntāyasā so ayaṃ bhavet koṭiguṇo rasaḥ ।। mūṣā hi krauñcikā proktā kumudī karahāṭikā ।
pācanī vahnimitrā ca rasavādibhirīryate ।। muṣṇāti doṣān mūṣā yā sā mūṣeti nigadyate ।। upādānaṃ bhavettasyā mṛttikā lohameva ca ।। mūṣāmukhaviniṣkrāntā varamekāpi kākiṇī ।
durjanapraṇipātena dhiglakṣam api māninām ।। mūṣāpidhānayorbandhe bandhanaṃ saṃdhilepanam । andhraṇaṃ randhraṇaṃ caiva saṃśliṣṭaṃ saṃdhibandhanam ।। [Ton।Lehm fṃr Tiegel]
mṛttikā pāṇḍurasthūlā śarkarā śoṇapāṇḍurā । cirādhmānasahā sā hi mūṣārtham atiśasyate । tadabhāve ca vālmīkī kaulālī vā samīryate ।। yā mṛttikā dugdhatuṣaiḥ śaṇena śikhitrakair vā hayaladdinā ca ।
lauhena daṇḍena ca kuṭṭitā sā sādhāraṇā syāt khalu mūṣikārthe ।। śvetāśmānas tuṣā dagdhāḥ śikhitrāḥ śaṇakharpare । laddiḥ kiṭṭaṃ kṛṣṇamṛtsnā saṃyojyā mūṣikāmṛdi ।। mūṣārthaṃ praśastamṛttikāmāha mṛttiketi ।।
pāṇḍurasthūlā pāṇḍuvarṇā sthūlā ca ।। athavā śoṇapāṇḍurā raktapāṇḍumiśravarṇā cirādhmānasahā dīrghakālaṃ vyāpya agnisaṃtāpaṃ prāpyāpi avidāraṇaśīlā evaṃvidhā yā śarkarā mṛttikā kaṅkararūpā mṛttikā ।। śarkarāmṛttikābhāve grāhyamṛttikāmāha taditi ।। vālmīkī kṛmiśailodbhavā mṛd uimāṭī iti vaṅgabhāṣā ।।
kaulālī kumbhakāramṛdityarthaḥ ।। hayaladdinā aśvapurīṣena ।। upādānāntarāṇyāha śvetāśmāna iti ।। śvetāśmānaḥ śvetaprastarāḥ ।।
kharparaḥ kapālakhaṇḍaḥ dagdhamṛttikā iti yāvat ।। śaṇakharpare ityatra śaṇakarpaṭe iti pāṭhe karpaṭaṃ chinnavastram ।। laddiḥ hayaladdiḥ ।। kiṭṭaṃ maṇḍūram ।।
kṛṣṇamṛtsnā kṛṣṇavarṇamṛttikā ।। mūṣikāmṛdā mūṣārthagrāhyamṛttikayā sahetyarthaḥ ।। mūṣārthaṃ praśastamṛttikāyā lakṣaṇamāha mṛttiketi ।। pāṇḍurā sthūlakaṇā śoṇamiśrapāṇḍurakaṇā vā ।।
kaulālī kulālabhāṇḍotpādanārtham upādānamṛttikā ।। atha sarvamūṣopayogisādhāraṇamṛttikām āha yā mṛttiketi ।। dagdhatuṣeti ।। caturthāṃśena dagdhatuṣayuktā pratyekaṃ tathā bhāgaiḥ śikhitraiḥ kokilair hayaladdināśvaśakṛtā ca yuktā sā praśastā ।।
mūṣikāmṛdi caturthāṃśena saṃyojyadravyāṇyāha śvetāśmāna iti ।। gāretyaparaparyāyāḥ ।। te ca dagdhā eva grāhyāḥ ।। mṛdastribhāgāḥ śaṇaladdibhāgau bhāgaśca nirdagdhatuṣopalādeḥ ।
kiṭṭārdhabhāgaṃ parikhaṇḍya vajramūṣāṃ vidadhyātkhalu sattvapāte ।। vajramūṣāmāha mṛda iti ।। mṛdaḥ pūrvoktarūpamṛttikāyāḥ ।। śaṇaladdibhāgau śaṇasya laddeśca pratyekaṃ bhāgadvayam ।।
parikhaṇḍya cūrṇayitvā ।। dagdhāṅgāratuṣopetā mṛtsnā valmīkamṛttikā । tattadviḍasamāyuktā tattadviḍavilepitā ।। tayā yā vihitā mūṣā yogamūṣeti kathyate ।
anayā sādhitaḥ sūto jāyate guṇavattaraḥ ।। yogamūṣāmāha dagdheti ।। dagdhaśabdo'tra aṅgāratuṣābhyāṃ pratyekaṃ sambadhyate ।। mṛtsnā pāṇḍurasthūlādiguṇopetā śarkarāmṛttiketyarthaḥ ।।
tattadviḍasamāyuktā sūtajāraṇārthaṃ prāṅnirūpitaviḍamiśritā ।। tattadviḍavilepitā tenaiva viḍenāliptā ।। dagdhāṅgārādiviḍāntaṃ sarvamekatra saṃnīya mūṣāṃ viracayya viḍena liptvā śuṣkīkṛtya gṛhṇīyāditi ।। atha yogamūṣāmāha dagdhagāreti ।।
dagdhā gārā vajraprasavāḥ śvetapāṣāṇā dagdhaṃ śālituṣaṃ ca pratyekaṃ caturthāṃśena taistathā tattadviḍacūrṇaiśca miśritā yā praśastā valmīkamṛttikā tayā vihitā ghaṭitā mūṣā yogamūṣeti kīrtyate ।। iyaṃ cābhrakasattvāder jāraṇāyāṃ viśiṣṭo yo yo viḍastena vilepitā tenaiva kāryā ।। atha jāraṇāyāṃ sā pāradagarbhitā koṣṭhīyantre bhastrikayā dhmātā cettayā sādhito jāritatāmrasattvādiḥ khoṭādirūpaśca pārado guṇavattaro bhavati ।। evaṃ ceyaṃ yogavāhimūṣā yogamūṣetyanvarthanāmiketi bhāvaḥ ।।
gārabhūnāgadhautābhyāṃ śaṇairdagdhatuṣairapi । samaiḥ samā ca mūṣāmṛnmahiṣīdugdhamarditā ।। krauñcikā yantramātraṃ hi bahudhā parikīrtitā । tayā viracitā mūṣā vajradrāvaṇikocitā ।।
vajradrāvaṇopayogimūṣāmāha gāreti ।। gāraśabdo'tra koṣṭhāgārikārthakaḥ nāmaikadeśenāpi nāmasākalyagrahaṇam iti nyāyāt koṣṭhāgārikā mṛttikāviśeṣaḥ kumīre pokāra moṭī iti bhāṣā ।। bhūnāgaśabdenāpi tanmṛttikā grāhyā evaṃ ca gārabhūnāgadhautābhyāṃ dhautakoṣṭhāgārikākiñculūkamṛdbhyām ।। mūṣāmṛt pūrvoktaśarkarāvālmīkikaulālyādīnām anyatamā ।।
gārādituṣāntaṃ sarvaṃ samam mṛttikā ca sarvaiḥ samānā grāhyā ।। krauñciketi ।। yantramātre hi krauñcikā saṃjñā vartate sā hi bahudhā vividhaprakārā ityanvayaḥ ।। atha hīnajātīyanātikaṭhinavajrapramukhakaṭhinapāṣāṇasattvaratnānāṃ drāvaṇakarīṃ mūṣāmāha gāreti ।।
gārāḥ śvetā vajrotpādakāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ ।। bhūnāgadhautaṃ paribhāṣādhyāyoktaṃ grāhyam ।। śaṇā dagdhatuṣāścaite mithaḥ samāḥ ।। taiḥ samā samabhāgā prāguktalakṣaṇā mūṣopādānamṛd ekatra kṛtvā mahiṣīdugdhena saṃmardya saṃskṛtā ceyaṃ mṛtkrauñcikāpakṣamātraṃ nānāvidhamūṣārūpo yo bhāgo yantratulyastannirmāṇārthaṃ praśastatvena bahuṣu grantheṣu kathitā ।।
taddhitamūṣāyāḥ sattvāharaṇādikāryeṣvagninā cirakālaparyantaṃ durbhedyatvāt ।। bhūnāgopetatvena śīghradrāvaṇopayogitvācca ।। tayā saṃskṛtayā mṛdā vihitā mūṣā śāstre vajradrāvaṇaketi khyātā ।। dugdhaṣaḍguṇagārāṣṭakiṭṭāṅgāraśaṇānvitā ।
kṛṣṇamṛdbhiḥ kṛtā mūṣā gāramūṣetyudāhṛtā । yāmayugmaparidhmānān nāsau dravati vahninā ।। gāramūṣāmāha dugdheti ।। gārasya ṣaḍguṇatvaṃ kiṭṭāṅgāraśaṇānāṃ ca pratyekam aṣṭaguṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇamṛdapekṣayā bodhyam ।।
dugdhaṃ ca mardanayogyam ।। atha gāramūṣāmāha dagdheti ।। dagdhā ye mṛttikāpekṣayā ṣaḍguṇā gārāstadviśiṣṭāstathā lohakiṭṭā aṅgārā nirvāṇāgnayaḥ kokilāḥ ।। tathā śaṇāḥ tāga iti khyātāḥ ।।
te ca pratyekaṃ caturthāṃśamitāstairyuktā yā kṛṣṇavarṇā mṛttatkṛtā mūṣā śāstre gāramūṣeti parikīrtitā ।। teṣāṃ pāṣāṇānāmatra sādhakamadhye hyadhikabhāgopetatvāditi bhāvaḥ ।। vajrāṅgāratuṣāstulyās taccaturguṇamṛttikā । gārā ca mṛttikātulyā sarvair etair vinirmitā ।
varamūṣeti nirdiṣṭā yāmamagniṃ saheta sā ।। varamūṣāmāha vajreti ।। vajraṃ tadākhyalauhaṃ pūrvoktasaṃgatyā tatkiṭṭaṃ vā bodhyam ।। atha varamūṣām āha vajreti ।।
vajro hīrakaḥ ।। tadalābhe vaikrāntaṃ grāhyam ।। aṅgārā haṭhānmṛttikādhūliprakṣepeṇa niragnayaḥ kokilāḥ ।। tathā dagdhatuṣāḥ ।।
sarve ca mithastulyabhāgāḥ ।। sarvebhyaścaturguṇā mṛttikā tattulyā gārāḥ śvetapāṣāṇāḥ ।। etannirmitā mūṣā varamūṣeti kathyate ।। varasya śreṣṭhasya mahāmūlyasya hīrakasyātra ghaṭakatvāt ।।
pāṣāṇarahitā raktā raktavargānusādhitā । mṛttayā sādhitā mūṣā kṣitikhecaralepitā । varṇamūṣeti sā proktā varṇotkarṣe niyujyate ।। varṇamūṣāmāha pāṣāṇarahiteti ।।
raktā raktavarṇā ।। raktavargānusādhitā vakṣyamāṇakusumbhādimākṣikāntavargakvāthena bhāvitā śṛtā vā ।। kṣitikhecaralepitā kṣitiśca khaṃ ca kṣitikhe tatra carataḥ iti kṣitikhecarau bhūnāgamṛt kāśīśaṃ ca yadvā kṣitisthaḥ khecaraḥ kāśīśamityarthaḥ ।। varṇotkarṣe praśastavarṇatāpādane raktavarṇajanane ityāśayaḥ ।।
atha varṇamūṣāmāha pāṣāṇeti ।। pāṣāṇā raktapāṣāṇāḥ ।। samabhāgaiśca taiḥ sahitā yā raktā raktavarṇā mṛttikā tayā sādhitā vihitā mūṣā varṇamūṣeti proktā ।। yasmādiyaṃ niyujyata upayujyate nirvāhaṇena dhātoḥ pāradasya vā raktavarṇotpādanārtham ।।
uktaṃ ca rasahṛdaye ।। nirguṇḍīrasabhāvitapuṭitaṃ śilayā vartitaṃ ślakṣṇam । tāvanmṛditapuṭitaṃ nirutthabhāvaṃ vrajedyāvat ।। tāre tannirvyūḍhaṃ yāvat pītaṃ bhavedruciram ।
hemnā samena militaṃ mātrātulyaṃ bhavet kanakam ।। iti ।। atra nirvāhaṇaṃ cāsyāṃ mūṣāyāṃ kāryam ।। raktavargaḥ śvetavargaścāsminnevādhyāye vakṣyamāṇaḥ ।।
pāṣāṇarahitā śvetā śvetavargānusādhitā । mṛt tayā sādhitā mūṣā kṣitikhecaralepitā । raupyamūṣeti sā proktā varṇotkarṣe niyujyate ।। tattadbhedamṛdodbhūtā tattadviḍavilepitā ।
dehalohārthayogārthaṃ viḍamūṣetyudāhṛtā ।। viḍamūṣāmāha tattaditi ।। tattadbhedamṛdodbhūtā śarkarādīnām anyatamamṛdā racitā ityarthaḥ ।। tattadbhedamṛdodbhūtā ityatra tattadviḍamṛdodbhūtā iti pāṭhe pūrvoktaviḍena pūrvoktamṛdā ca udbhūtā nirmitā ।।
dehalohārthayogārthaṃ dehasya lauhavad dārḍhyasampādanārthā ye yogāḥ tadarthaṃ tatkarmasampādanārtham ityarthaḥ ।। atha viḍamūṣāmāha tattadviḍamṛdudbhūteti ।। abhrasattvajāraṇasvarṇajāraṇopayogīni yāni vaḍavānalādiviḍāni yathoddiṣṭarasādibhāvitāni cūrṇāni tathā sarvalohādijāraṇopayogiviḍātmakaścūrṇaḥ paribhāṣādhyāye viḍavarṇanāvasare prāguktaḥ ।। tathā pūrvoktā nānāvidhā pāṇḍurādimṛttadudbhūtā tatsiddhā tathā tattadviḍair grāsajāraṇasādhanair viśiṣṭaiścūrṇairantarvilepitā yā mūṣā sā viḍamūṣetyucyate ।।
iyaṃ mūṣā dṛḍhakāyakararasāyanavidhau sādhanatvena dehārthā dehopayoginītyarthaḥ ।। tathā lohamāraṇopayoginī ।। ata eva lohārthā ।। tathā artho dhanaṃ tathā suvarṇādyutpādanavidhau dhātuvāde sādhanatvenārthārthā ।।
tathā kāsaghnaratnakaraṇḍakarasārśonāśakasarvalokāśrayarasaprabhṛtinānāvidharogaghnarasavidhau sādhanatvena yogārthā cetīyaṃ caturvidhakāryopayoginī bhavati ।। gārabhūnāgadhautābhyāṃ tuṣamṛṣṭaśaṇena ca । samaiḥ samā ca mūṣāmṛnmahiṣīdugdhamarditā ।। krauñcikā yantramātre hi bahudhā parikīrtitā ।
tayā viracitā mūṣā liptā matkuṇaśoṇitaiḥ ।। bālābdadhvanimūlaiśca vajradrāvaṇakrauñcikā । sahate'gniṃ caturyāmaṃ draveṇa vyādhitā satī ।। pūrvoktavajradrāvaṇopayogimūṣāyāḥ prakārāntaramāha gāreti ।।
matkuṇaḥ chārapokā iti khyātaḥ krimiviśeṣaḥ tasya śoṇitaiḥ ।। abdadhvaniḥ vanataṇḍulīyakaḥ kāṃṭānaṭe iti bhāṣā bālābdadhvanimūlaiḥ navotpannataṇḍulīyamūlaiḥ yadvā vālaḥ aśvapucchakeśaḥ tathā abdadhvanimūlaṃ taiḥ liptā ityanenānvayaḥ ।। draveṇa vyādhitā viddhā spṛṣṭā ityarthaḥ dravapūrṇā ityāśayaḥ ।। athāvyabhicāreṇa vajramātradrāvaṇārthaṃ vajramūṣāmāha gāreti ।।
vālābdeti ।। vālā narakeśāḥ ।। abdadhvanimūlaṃ tandulīyakamūlam ।। iyaṃ mūṣā dravadraveṇa vyathitā satī antaḥsthataijasadravyayogasaṃyogena bāhyāgnisaṃyogena ca saṃtataṃ pīḍitā satyapyagniṃ sahate ।।
drave dravībhāvamukhe mūṣāyā dhmānayogataḥ । kṣaṇamuddharaṇaṃ yattanmūṣāpyāyanam ucyate ।। mūṣāpyāyanamāha drave iti ।। dhmāyate aneneti dhmānamagniḥ tadyogataḥ agnisaṃyogād drave drāvaṇopayogini dravye dravībhāvamukhe dravībhavitum ārabdhe mūṣāyā yat kṣaṇam uddharaṇam agnitaḥ uttolanam avatāraṇamityarthaḥ tad āpyāyanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ sthāyitvasampādanam ityarthaḥ ।।
vṛntākākāramūṣāyāṃ nālaṃ dvādaśakāṅgulam । dhattūrapuṣpavac cordhvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ śliṣṭapuṣpavat ।। aṣṭāṅgulaṃ ca sacchidraṃ sā syād vṛntākamūṣikā । anayā kharparādīnāṃ mṛdūnāṃ sattvamāharet ।।
vṛntākamūṣāmāha vṛntāketi ।। vṛntākaṃ vārttākuḥ vārttākuphalasadṛśākārāṃ mūṣāṃ kṛtvā tatra dvādaśāṅguladīrghaṃ nālaṃ yojayet nālāgrabhāgaṃ ca dhustūrapuṣpavad uparyadho yugmarūpāvasthitam aṣṭāṅgulaṃ sacchidraṃ ca kuryāt ।। vṛntākamūṣāmāha vṛntākākāreti ।। dvādaśakāṅgulam ।।
dvādaśāṅgulaṃ dīrgham ūrdhvam uttānamūṣāyā ūrdhvatanamukhabhāgo dhattūrapuṣpavat krameṇa vistīrṇastadvadeva ca saṃśleṣeṇa tricatuṣkoṇayuto dhmānāvasare pihite'pi mukhe sati tatkoṇamārgeṇāntaḥsthadhūmasya bahirnirgamanārthaṃ koṇaghaṭanenaiva tanmukhaṃ sacchidraṃ bhavati ।। tacca mukham aṣṭāṅgulavistṛtaṃ vartulasūtraveṣṭanenāṣṭāṅgulamitam ityarthaḥ ।। mūṣā yā gostanākārā śikhāyuktapidhānakā । sattvānāṃ drāvaṇe śuddhau mūṣā sā gostanī bhavet ।।
atha gostanamūṣāmāha mūṣāyā iti ।। śikhāyukteti ।। śikharākārapidhānakasahiteyameva cāndhamūṣābhidhīyate ।। dvaṃdvitabījamelāpādividhāvasyā upayogo bodhyaḥ ।।
yatra tu nyubjayā tayācchādanaṃ kriyate tatra pidhānarahitā grāhyā ।। yathā nābhiyantre prāguktam । tataścācchādayet samyaggostanākāramūṣayā । iti ।।
nirdiṣṭā mallamūṣā yā malladvitayasampuṭāt । parpaṭyādirasādīnāṃ svedanāya prakīrtitā ।। mallamūṣāmāha nirdiṣṭeti ।। mallaṃ pidhānopayogi vistīrṇaṃ kiṃcid gabhīrodaraṃ mṛnmayaṃ pātraṃ śarāveti loke prasiddham ।।
saptaviṃśatitame'dhyāye'syā upayogaṃ vakṣyati madanasaṃjīvanarasavidhau ।। anyatrāpi prabhūtasthale caiṣopayujyate ।। tadevocyate parpaṭyādīti ।। kulālabhāṇḍarūpā yā dṛḍhā ca paripācitā ।
pakvamūṣeti sā proktā poṭṭalyādivipācane ।। pakvamūṣāmāha kulāleti ।। ghaṭakapālayoḥ pṛthak pṛthak nirmāṇārthaṃ yaḥ pratirūpaḥ saḥ kulālabhāṇḍaśabdenocyate tadrūpā ityarthaḥ ।। poṭalyādivipācane ratnagarbhapoṭalyādipāke ityarthaḥ ।।
trayodaśādhyāyoktaparpaṭīprabhṛtirasānām alpasvedasādhyānāṃ pakvamūṣāmāha kulāleti ।। vastramayapoṭalīva bheṣajagarbhitaṃ bheṣajamayamūṣā kapardikāśaṅkhādi bhūmau gajapuṭādinā pācayitum yatra pātrāntare dhriyate pākottaram ācchādanasahitaṃ ca gṛhyate ।। yathā rājayakṣmacikitsāyāṃ mṛgāṅkapoṭalīvidhau sa rasaḥ poṭalītyucyate ।। nirvaktragolakākārā puṭanadravyagarbhiṇī ।
golamūṣeti sā proktā satvaradravarodhinī ।। golamūṣāmāha nirvaktreti ।। mukhavirahitagolākārā ityarthaḥ ।। satvaradravarodhinī dravapadārthasrāvanivāriṇī ityarthaḥ ।।
madhyasthitapuṭanadravyā samyaṅniruddhānanā golākṛtimūṣā golamūṣā bodhyā ।। atha golamūṣāmāha nirvaktreti ।। gatvaradravyaṃ pāradarasakamanaḥśilāharitālaprabhṛti madhye dattvā kulālena yā nirmukhaiva vidhīyate etatsamā tāmramūṣā rasahṛdaye aṣṭādaśāvabodhe abhihitā ।। ata eva tadudāharaṇamatra nopayogi ।।
mṛnmayodāharaṇaprayogo nopalabhyate ।। tale yā kūrparākārā kramādupari vistṛtā । sthūlavṛntākavat sthūlā mahāmūṣetyasau smṛtā । sā cāyo'bhrakasattvādeḥ puṭāya drāvaṇāya ca ।।
mahāmūṣāmāha tale iti ।। kūrparākārā kūrparaḥ kaphoṇiḥ bhujamadhyasandhir ityarthaḥ tadākārā ।। atha mahāmūṣāmāha tala iti ।। ayo'bhraketi ।।
atrāyaḥśabdena kāntaṃ grāhyam ।। tasyāntaḥpītarekhāviśiṣṭasya chāgaraktena bhāvanayā śuddhasya ।। piṇḍībaddhasya koṣṭhayantrodare mūṣāyāṃ laghubhastrayā dhamanādbhavati sattvanipātanam ।। maṇḍūkākārā yā nimnatāyāmavistarā ।
ṣaḍaṅgulapramāṇena mūṣā maṇḍūkasaṃjñikā । bhūmau nikhanya tāṃ mūṣāṃ dadyātpuṭamathopari ।। maṇḍūkamūṣāmāha maṇḍūketi ।। maṇḍūkaḥ bhekaḥ tadākārā ।।
ṣaḍaṅgulapramāṇena nimnatāyāmavistarā ṣaḍaṅgulapramāṇagabhīratādairghyavistārayuktā ।। maṇḍūkamūṣāmāha maṇḍūketi ।। tadākāramūṣāyā gāmbhīryadairghyapariṇāhāḥ ṣaḍaṅgulamitāḥ kāryāḥ ।। upari mṛttikayā tām caturaṅgulamitam ācchādya bhūmipṛṣṭhoparītyarthaḥ ।।
[mūsala-।muśalamūṣā] mūṣā yā cipiṭā mūle vartulāṣṭāṅgulocchrayā । mūṣā sā mūsalākhyā syāccakribaddharase hitā ।। muṣalamūṣāmāha mūṣeti ।।
vartulā mūlād ūrdhvamiti bodhyam ।। cakribaddharase strīrogādhikārokta auṣadhaviśeṣaḥ ।। muśalamūṣāmāha mūṣeti ।। cakribaddharaso dvāviṃśādhyāye vakṣyamāṇaḥ ।।
sattvānāṃ pātanārthāya pātitānāṃ viśuddhaye । koṣṭhikā vividhākārāstāsāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate ।। alpāgnisādhyasya dravyapākasya sādhanāya mūṣā nānāvidhā uktāḥ ।। saṃprati prabhūtāgnisādhyasya dravyapākasya sādhanārthaṃ vividhāḥ koṣṭhīr vaktukāmaḥ prathamaṃ tāsāṃ prayojanamāha sattvānāmiti ।।
mūṣāmṛdaiva koṣṭhīr vidadhyād ityabhiprāyeṇaivātra koṣṭhīnāṃ mṛdviśeṣo noktaḥ ।। rasaratnākare tu mṛttikādravyāṇāṃ pramāṇamapi spaṣṭaṃ kṛtvābhihitam ।। tathā ca tadgranthaḥ । gārā dagdhāstuṣā dagdhā valmīkamṛttikā ।
ajāśvānāṃ malaṃ dagdhaṃ yāvat tat kṛṣṇatāṃ gatam ।। pāṣāṇabhedapatrāṇi kṛṣṇā mṛcca samaṃ samam । vajravallyā dravairmardyaṃ dinaṃ vā peṣayeddṛḍham ।। tena koṣṭhīr vaṅkanālā vajramūṣāśca kārayet ।
mṛnmayakośasya koṣṭhīti nāma prasiddham ।। sā ca dvividhā ।। bhūmikoṣṭhī calatkoṣṭhī ca ।। yatkoṣṭhīyantraṃ prāguditaṃ sā calatkoṣṭhīti nigadyate ।।
idānīm ucyamānāstu sarvā bhūmikoṣṭhyaḥ ।। tāśca dvividhāḥ ।। prakāśakoṣṭhī sapidhānakoṣṭhī ceti bhedena ।। rājahastasamutsedhā tadardhāyāmavistarā ।
caturasrā ca kuḍyena veṣṭitā mṛnmayena ca ।। ekabhittau careddvāraṃ vitastyābhogasaṃyutam । dvāraṃ sārdhavitastyā ca saṃmitaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ śubham ।। dehalyadho vidhātavyaṃ dhamanāya yathocitam ।
prādeśapramitā bhittir uttaraṅgasya cordhvataḥ ।। dvāraṃ copari kartavyaṃ prādeśapramitaṃ khalu । tataśceṣṭikayā ruddhvā dvārasaṃdhiṃ vilipya ca ।। śikhitraistāṃ samāpūrya dhamedbhastrādvayena ca ।
śikhitrān dhamanadravyam ūrdhvadvāreṇa nikṣipet ।। sattvapātanagolāṃśca pañca pañca punaḥ punaḥ । bhaved aṅgārakoṣṭhīyaṃ kharāṇāṃ sattvapātinī ।। aṅgārakoṣṭhikālakṣaṇamāha rājahasteti ।।
rājahastasamutsedhā hastadvayonnatā ।। rājahastasya vistṛtavyākhyā gajapuṭavyākhyāyāṃ draṣṭavyā ।। caturasrā catuṣkoṇā ।। vitastyābhogasaṃyutaṃ dvādaśāṅgulavistṛtam ।।
dvāraṃ sārdhavitastyā ca ityasya dehalyadhaḥ ityanena saṃbandhaḥ ।। dehalī dvāranimne piṇḍikā ।। prādeśapramitā aṅguṣṭhasya pradeśinyā vyāsaḥ prādeśa ucyate ityuktalakṣaṇā tarjanīsahitavistṛtāṅguṣṭhapramāṇā ।। uttaraṅgasya dvārordhvasthadāruṇaḥ ।।
hastadvayotsedhaṃ hastamitāyāmavistāraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ samantāt mṛnmayabhittiveṣṭitaṃ ca cullyākāramekaṃ mārttikaṃ yantraṃ kṛtvā tasya ekabhittau vitastivistaraṃ dvāraṃ dvārapiṇḍikādhaḥ aṣṭādaśāṅgulamānaṃ dvārāntaraṃ ca kuryāt ।। dvārordhvabhāge aṅguṣṭhatarjanyor madhyavat vistṛtāṃ bhittiṃ sthāpayitvā tadupari tadvadvistṛtaṃ dvāramanyat vidadhyāt tataḥ iṣṭakayā dvārasandhiṃ ruddhvā ālipya ca koṣṭhīmaṅgāraiḥ paripūrya dvābhyāṃ bhastrābhyāṃ dhamet ।। bhasmībhūte ca aṅgāre punarapi aṅgāraṃ sattvapātanagolādikaṃ ca pañca pañca kṛtvā ūrdhvadvāreṇa punaḥ punaḥ nikṣipet ।। iyam aṅgārakoṣṭhī kharadravyāṇāṃ sattvapātane śubhā jñeyā ।।
prathamaṃ sapidhānakoṣṭhīmāha rājahasteti ।। sapādahastastriṃśadaṅgulātmakastanmita utsedha ucchrayo yasyāstathoktā ।। tadardhamātrau dairghyavistārau yasyāstathoktā ।। tathā caturasrā catuṣkoṇā sarvato dārḍhyāya mṛnmayena kuḍyena bhittyā bahirveṣṭitā kāryā ।।
tena catasṛṣu dikṣu catasro bhittayaḥ sambhavanti ।। ekabhittāviti sāmānyata uktamapi yogyatayā pūrvabhittau paścimabhittau veti viśeṣārthe paryavasyati ।। tasyāṃ diśi sthitāyāṃ bhittau dvāraṃ vitastyā saṃmitaṃ kāryam ।। yadvitastimitaṃ dīrghaṃ sūtraṃ tadvartulaṃ nidhāyāntaravakāśo yāvān sambhavati tanmitaṃ vartulaṃ caturaṅgulamitam ityarthaḥ ।।
antaḥsthitajvālāyāḥ sattvanirgamakālabodhikāyāḥ parīkṣārthaṃ caret kuryāt ।। tadarthaṃ prakāśa āvaśyakaḥ ।। sa tu prācyāṃ pratīcyāṃ vādhikyena labhyata iti prakāśayogyatvād viśiṣṭā digevātra gṛhītā ।। taddvārasyādhobhāgo dehalī dvāradehasaṃrakṣikā sā dvitryaṅgulamitā kāryā ।।
tādṛgdehalyā adhobhāge bhūtalaṃ saṃlagnaṃ pūrvavadeva sārdhavitastimitasūtreṇa paricchinnam arthāt ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ vartulaṃ dvāraṃ bhastrāyojanāya kāryam ।। atra vitastidīrghā tāvad bhittireva sārdhavitastidīrghā ca dvāradvayārthaṃ paryāptā na bhavati ।। ata uktaṃ sūtramitaṃ vartulaṃ ceti ।। kecittu kramanimnabhūminikhātatiryaggartābhāgo'pi sārdhavitastimānārthaṃ saṃgrāhya iti noktasūtradairghyamānāpekṣā lohakārāṇāṃ tathaiva saṃpradāyo'pi saṃprati dhmānavidhau dṛśyata iti vadanti ।।
tattu nocitam ।। tādṛśagartābhāgasya pātālakoṣṭhikāyāṃ vakṣyamāṇatvāt ।। ūrdhvabhāge koṣṭhikāyā uttarāṅgasyordhvāṅgasya ca kartavyā yā bhittiḥ sā caturvidhāpi prādeśapramitā daśāṅgulamitaivārthācchikhākāravat saṃkucitā kāryā ।। śikhāsthāna ūrdhvaṃ dvāraṃ tu prādeśamitāyāmavistāram eva kāryam ।।
tatastaddvāraṃ ceṣṭikayā ruddhvā prāguktavitastimitaṃ dvāraṃ ca kokilaiḥ samāpūrya dhamet ।। kiṃ kṛtvā ruddhvā dhamettadāha prathamaṃ śikhitrān kokilān dhmānārham abhrakādidravaṃ cordhvadvāreṇa krameṇa nikṣipet ।। kiṃ tad dhmānadravyaṃ piṇḍīkṛtaṃ bhāgaśaḥ sakṛdeva vā nikṣiped ityākāṅkṣāyāmāha sattvapātanagolān iti ।। punaḥ punaḥ pratiprakṣepakālāvasaraṃ saṃtataṃ dhmātvā yadāṅgārāḥ kārśyaṃ prāpnuyuḥ śvetabhasmāvṛtāśca bhaveyustadā punaḥ kokilān dattvā punardhamanaṃ kāryam ।।
evaṃ bhastrādvayena praharaparyantaṃ saṃtataṃ dhmānena prāyaḥ kaṭhinadravyāṇāṃ sattvanirgamanakālaḥ samupajāyate ।। paraṃ tu nāyaṃ kālaḥ sattvanirgamanajñāpakaḥ svātantreṇa kiṃtu śuklā vahnijvālaiva jñāyamānā ।। uktaṃ hi paribhāṣādhyāye । yadā hutāśo dīptārciḥ śuklotthānasamanvitaḥ ।
śuddhāvartastadā jñeyaḥ sa kālaḥ sattvanirgame । iti ।। tadā sphuṭipiṇḍīr bahir niṣkāsya kiṭṭaṃ pṛthakkṛtya gurumārgeṇa sattvamātraṃ grāhyam ।। atha dvitīyaḥ sattvapiṇḍānāṃ prakṣepakālaḥ prāpnotīti bodhyam ।।
atha mṛdudravyāṇāṃ sattvapātārtham alpadhmānāpekṣā ।। dṛḍhabhūmau caredgartaṃ vitastyā saṃmitaṃ śubham । vartulaṃ cātha tanmadhye gartamanyaṃ prakalpayet ।। caturaṅgulavistāranimnatvena samanvitam ।
gartāddharaṇiparyantaṃ tiryaṅnālasamanvitam ।। kiṃcit samunnataṃ bāhyagartābhimukhanimnagam । mṛccakrīṃ pañcarandhrāḍhyāṃ garbhagartodare kṣipet ।। āpūrya kokilaiḥ koṣṭhīṃ pradhamed ekabhastrayā ।
pātālakoṣṭhikā hy eṣā mṛdūnāṃ sattvapātinī । dhmānasādhyapadārthānāṃ nandinā parikīrtitā ।। pātālakoṣṭhikāmāha dṛḍhabhūmāviti ।। kaṭhinamṛttikāyāṃ vitastimānaṃ vartulaṃ gartam ekaṃ kṛtvā tanmadhye caturaṅgulavistāraṃ caturaṅgulagabhīraṃ gartād bhūpṛṣṭhaparyantayāyivakrākṛtinālasaṃyuktam īṣaducchritaṃ ca gartamanyaṃ kuryāt ।।
tataḥ abhyantaragartamadhye pañcarandhrasaṃyuktāṃ mṛccakrīṃ sthāpayitvā aṅgāraiḥ koṣṭhīṃ paripūrya ca ekabhastrayā pradhamet ।। mṛdudravyāṇāṃ sattvapātanārtham iyaṃ pātālakoṣṭhīti jñeyamiti niṣkarṣaḥ ।। atastadupayogikoṣṭhīviśeṣamāha dṛḍhabhūmāviti ।। tatra dvādaśāṅgulaṃ gartaṃ vidhāya tattalamadhye caturaṅgulagāmbhīryavistāram anyaṃ vartulaṃ gartaṃ kṛtvā garbhagartatalam ārabhya pṛṣṭhabhāgaparyantaṃ bāhyagartābhimukhaṃ tatsallagnaṃ kiṃcitsamunnataṃ tiryaṅnālasamanvitaṃ dvāraṃ vidhāya garbhagartopari mṛccakrīṃ pañcarandhraviśiṣṭāṃ vāyor ūrdhvagamanārthaṃ kṣipet ।।
taduparyaṅgārāṃstadupari sattvapātanagolāṃśca nikṣipya sarvāṃ koṣṭhīṃ kokilaiḥ pūrayitvaikabhastrayā dhamet ।। eṣā pātālakoṣṭhiketyucyate ।। dvādaśāṅgulanimnā yā prādeśapramitā tathā । caturaṅgulataścordhvaṃ valayena samanvitā ।।
bhūricchidravatīṃ cakrīṃ valayopari nikṣipet । śikhitrāṃstatra nikṣipya pradhamed vaṅkanālataḥ । gārakoṣṭhīyam ākhyātā mṛṣṭalohavināśinī ।। adhodhmānaviśiṣṭāṃ koṣṭhīmuktordhvadhamanaviśiṣṭāṃ koṣṭhīmāha dvādaśeti ।।
prādeśāyāmavistārā koṣṭhī bhūtalopari kāryā ।। sā ca talabhāgam ārabhyopari caturaṅgulabhāgaṃ vihāya tadupari valayena kaṭakena samanvitāṃ tāṃ kṛtvā valayopari prabhūtacchidrayuktāṃ cakrīṃ nikṣipya tatra kokilāṃśca dattvā vaṅkanālataḥ pradhamet ।। mṛttikāpekṣayā adhikagārabhāgamiśritamṛdupādāneyaṃ koṣṭhī gārakoṣṭhītyucyate ।। iyaṃ kāṃsyarītipramukhaṃ yatsṛṣṭalohaṃ tanmadhye saṃsargaghaṭakayor madhya ekasyāvaśeṣakarī dvitīyaṃ vināśyetyarthaḥ ।।
gārakoṣṭhīmāha dvādaśeti ।। dvādaśāṅgulagabhīrā prādeśapramāṇavistāraviśiṣṭā koṣṭhī ekā kāryā tasyā ūrdhvaṃ caturaṅgule valayākāram ālavālam ekaṃ dattvā tadupari bahucchidrāṃ cakrīṃ nidhāya aṅgāraṃ nikṣipya ca vaṅkanālena pradhamet iti ।। mṛṣṭalohavināśinī śodhitalauhamāriṇī ityarthaḥ ।। mūṣāmṛdbhir vidhātavyam aratnipramitaṃ dṛḍham ।
adhomukhaṃ ca tadvaktre nālaṃ pañcāṅgulaṃ khalu । vaṅkanālam idaṃ proktaṃ dṛḍhadhmānāya kīrtitam ।। gārakoṣṭhikāyāṃ vaṅkanālam ityuktaṃ kiṃ tat vaṅkanālam ityāśaṃsāyāmāha mūṣāmṛdbhiriti ।। śarkarādīnām anyatamābhiḥ mūṣopayogimṛdbhiḥ aratnipramitaṃ dṛḍhaṃ nālaṃ kṛtvā tanmukhe pañcāṅgulapramāṇam adhomukhaṃ nālam ekaṃ yojayet dṛḍhadhmānāya tad vaṅkanālaṃ veditavyam ।।
[mūṣākoṣṭhī।tiryakpradhamanakoṣṭhī] koṣṭhī siddharasādīnāṃ vidhānāya vidhīyate । dvādaśāṅgulakotsedhā sā budhne caturaṅgulā । tiryakpradhamanāsyā ca mṛdudravyaviśodhinī ।।
atha siddharasānāṃ khoṭabaddhādīnām abhrakādisattvānāṃ ca kācaṭaṅkaṇasauvīrādinā śodhayituṃ sādhanabhūtāṃ koṣṭhīmāha dvādaśāṅguleti ।। asyāṃ koṣṭhyāṃ sthāpitamūṣāmadhye siddharasādi prakṣipya saṃtatadhmānāvasare antarāntarā muhuḥ kācacūrṇādi dattvā dhamet ।। mṛdudravyaṃ sattvādi ।। iyaṃ koṣṭhī budhnabhāgamārabhya mukhabhāgaparyantaṃ kramavistṛtā prādeśapramitavartulamukhī kāryetyanuktamapi bodhyam ।।
pūrvasyāstathāmānamukhasyoktatvāt ।। rasādidravyapākānāṃ pramāṇajñāpanaṃ puṭam । neṣṭo nyūnādhikaḥ pākaḥ supākaṃ hitam auṣadham ।। lohāderapunarbhāvo guṇādhikyaṃ tato agratā ।
anapsu majjanaṃ rekhāpūrṇatā puṭato bhavet ।। puṭād grāvṇo laghutvaṃ ca śīghravyāptiśca dīpanam । jāritādapi sūtendrāllohānām adhiko guṇaḥ ।। yathāśmani viśed vahnir bahiḥsthapuṭayogataḥ ।
cūrṇatvāddhi guṇāvāptistathā loheṣu niścitam ।। saṃprati mūṣākoṣṭhyapekṣyādhikatarāgnijanakapuṭān vaktuṃ teṣāṃ prayojanamāha raseti ।। rasalohaprabhṛtikaṭhoradravyāṇāṃ samyakpāko bheṣajārthamapekṣyate ।। sa ca pākaḥ kriyārūpastulayā parimāṇena vā paricchettuṃ na śakyate ।।
supākasya pramāṇabodhakaṃ puṭam evāgnidīpakopalatuṣagorvarasaṃpūryagartādiviśeṣa eva sambhavati ।। etadgartāpūritopalāgninaikaḥ supāko'bhavaditi tatpuṭaviśeṣāvṛttiḥ kāryā ।। yathoktaguṇalābhaparyantamiti bhāvaḥ ।। nyūnapākena gandhavarṇarasasparśaḥ samyaṅna jāyate ।।
adhipākena tu dravyaṃ niḥsāraṃ dagdhaṃ bhavatyodanavat ।। atha puṭasya yogato guṇāṃllohasthān āha lohāderiti ।। apunarbhāvo na prākṛtasvarūpāpādanaṃ pañcamitrasaṃskāreṇāpi ।। guṇādhikyamāmāvasthāpanne tasmin bhakṣite jāṭharāgnyapākena rogavārakā guṇāstathā puṣṭyādayo mārdavādayaścānudbhūtāsteṣām udbhavenādhikyābhāsaḥ ।।
tena cāgratā śreṣṭhatādhikamūlyatā ।। tathāpsu prakṣiptasya tasya na majjanam uparitaraṇam ।। aṅgulibhyāṃ pīḍitasya tasya sūkṣmāṅgulirekhāsu praviṣṭatvaṃ ca ।। abhrakavajraharitālādirūpapāṣāṇaviśeṣeṣu tu laghutvādayo guṇāḥ puṭātprādurbhavanti ।।
kiṃ bahunā guṇavarṇanena ।। yatra guṇāḥ sarve sambhūyotkaṭā nivasanti tasmāt pāradādapi jīrṇarasoparasamaṇilohāt susiddhānāṃ lohānāṃ guṇā yathāvidhisevino narasya śarīre'dhikā eva ।। bhūriphalayuto'pi siddharasasya hi krāmaṇārthaṃ kiṃcitsphuṭitayauvanā kāminī saṃnihitāpekṣyate bhāṣaṇacumbanāliṅganārthaṃ tatstanābhyāmaṅgamardanārthaṃ ca ।। tadasaṃnidhau sarvaśarīre krāmaṇābhāvena na manmathaḥ ।।
sāṃnidhye tu pramādena maithunam ।। tataśca māraṇam āpadyate ।। kiṃca rasasevino varṣaparyantaṃ parihāraviśeṣaḥ ।। ādau kṣetrīkaraṇaṃ cāvaśyakam ।।
pāradasiddhāvanubhūtasarvakriyāsādhakaḥ prabhūtadravyādisaṃpaccāpekṣyate ।। ata eva nātinirapāyasya lohasya guṇānām ādhikyamupacaryate ।। nanu pāṣāṇato'pi kaṭhināṇāṃ lohaviśeṣāṇāṃ nāvayavaviśleṣa iti katham uktalābha ityāśaṅkya nidarśanena punarlohaguṇān dṛḍhīkaroti yathāśmanīti ।। antaragnipraveśena sarvaṃ sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।।
nimnavistarataḥ kuṇḍe dvihaste caturasrake । vanotpalasahasreṇa pūrite puṭanauṣadham ।। krauñcyāṃ ruddhaṃ prayatnena piṣṭikopari nikṣipet । vanotpalasahasrārdhaṃ krauñcikopari vinyaset ।
vahniṃ prajvālayettatra mahāpuṭamidaṃ smṛtam ।। saṃprati gartāviśeṣaṃ mahāpuṭamāha bhūmimadhya iṣṭikādibhiḥ kṛte kuḍye kuḍyamaye garte gāmbhīryavistārābhyāṃ dvihaste tathā catuṣkoṇe tādṛggarte vanyacchagaṇaiḥ sahasrasaṃkhyākaiḥ pūrite sati śarāvasaṃpuṭitaṃ bheṣajaṃ piṣṭikopari pūritacchagaṇopari sthāpayet ।। tādṛśamūṣikoparyardhasahasraṃ chagaṇānāṃ pūrayet ।। tato dīpayet ।।
rājahastapramāṇena caturasraṃ ca nimnakam । pūrṇaṃ copalasāṭhībhiḥ kaṇṭhāvadhyatha vinyaset ।। vinyasetkumudīṃ tatra puṭanadravyapūritām । pūrṇacchagaṇato ardhāni giriṇḍāni vinikṣipet ।
etadgajapuṭaṃ proktaṃ mahāguṇavidhāyakam ।। atha gajapuṭamāha rājahasteti ।। rājahastastriṃśadaṅgulimitaḥ ।। tanmitaṃ nimnaṃ gambhīraṃ tanmitavistāraṃ ca gartaṃ bodhyaṃ ।।
nimnamityatra vistāraśabdo luptanirdiṣṭaḥ ।। tadupalaśāṭhībhiḥ kaṇṭhaparyantaṃ pūrayet ।। upalāḥ kaṭhinā mahānto vanyacchagaṇāstato alpadehāḥ śāṭhyaḥ ।। tatra mūṣāṃ bheṣajagarbhitāṃ vinyasya pūrvavinyastacchagaṇato'rdhamānāni giriṇḍāni vanyacchagaṇāni vinikṣipet ityetadgajapuṭākhyaṃ matam ।।
itthaṃ cāratnike kuṇḍe puṭaṃ vārāhamucyate ।। puṭaṃ bhūmitale tattadvitastidvitayocchrayam । tāvacca talavistīrṇaṃ tatsyātkukkuṭakaṃ puṭam ।। atha kukkuṭapuṭamāha ।।
bhūmipṛṣṭhabhāge kuḍyena nirmitaṃ caturviṃśatyaṅgulocchrāyaṃ tāvanmānameva tale mukhe ca vistṛtametādṛśaṃ yadgartaṃ bheṣajaṃ paktumupalādibhiḥ pūryate tatkukkuṭapuṭasaṃjñaṃ bhavati ।। kukkuṭapuṭamāha puṭamiti ।। vitastidvitayocchrayaṃ hastapramāṇonnatam ।। tāvacca talavistīrṇaṃ adhobhāge'pi hastapramāṇavistṛtam ।।
etattu bhūmerupari eva kāryaṃ na tu gartaṃ khanitvā ।। yatpuṭaṃ dīyate bhūmāv aṣṭasaṃkhyair vanopalaiḥ । baddhvā sūtārkabhasmārthaṃ kapotapuṭamucyate ।। yacca gartaṃ bhūmitale mṛdādibhiḥ kṛtamaṣṭasaṃkhyairvanopalairdīyate jvālayā prajvalitaṃ kriyate baddhapāradasya bhasmakaraṇārthaṃ tatkapotapuṭamucyate ।।
baddhvā mūṣāyāṃ ruddhvetyarthaḥ ।। sūtārkabhasmārthaṃ rasabhasmārthaṃ tāmrabhasmārthaṃ ca ।। goṣṭhāntargokṣurakṣuṇṇaṃ śuṣkaṃ cūrṇitagomayam । govaraṃ tatsamādiṣṭaṃ variṣṭhaṃ rasasādhane ।।
govarairvā tuṣairvāpi puṭaṃ yatra pradīyate । tadgovarapuṭaṃ proktaṃ rasabhasmaprasiddhaye ।। gorvaraistuṣairvā yatra gajapuṭagartāyāṃ puṭaṃ dīyate bheṣajaṃ pakvaṃ kriyate tadgorvarapuṭamucyate ।। sthūlabhāṇḍe tuṣāpūrṇe madhye mūṣāsamanvite ।
vahninā vihite pāke tadbhāṇḍapuṭamucyate ।। adhastādupariṣṭācca krauñcikācchādyate khalu । vālukābhiḥ prataptābhiryatra tadvālukāpuṭam ।। vahnimitrāḥ kṣitau samyaṅnikhanyād dvyaṅgulādadhaḥ ।
upariṣṭātpuṭaṃ yatra puṭaṃ tad bhūdharāhvayam ।। vahnimitrāḥ mūṣāḥ dīrghakālaṃ vahninā sahāvasthānāt asyā vahnimitratvaṃ jñātavyam ।। spaṣṭamanyat ।। atha bhūdharapuṭamāha vahnimitrāmiti ।।
vahnimitrā mūṣā śarāva iti yāvat ।। jayasundarādirasavidhāvasyā upayogo bodhyaḥ ।। ūrdhvaṃ ṣoḍaśikāmūtraistuṣairvā govaraiḥ puṭam । yatra tallāvakākhyaṃ syāt sumṛdudravyasādhane ।।
atha lāvakapuṭamāha ūrdhvamiti ।। śarāvākāramūṣāṃ saṃpuṭitāṃ bhūmau nidhāya tadupari ṣoḍaśavanopalamitais tuṣair gorvarair vā yatpuṭaṃ dīyate pākaḥ kriyate tallāvakam iti khyātam ।। ṣoḍaśa eva ṣoḍaśikā ।। sā saṃkhyā cātra vanyopalānāmeva grāhyā ।।
tanmātrais tadvanyacchagaṇatulitair ityarthaḥ ।। anuktapuṭamāne tu sādhyadravyabalābalāt । puṭaṃ vijñāya dātavyam ūhāpohavicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। puṭānāṃ hi prāyo vanyacchagaṇasādhyatvāttadupasthitiḥ ।।
atha kumbhapuṭaṃ granthāntaroktaṃ vakṣyāmi । mṛdghaṭe bahurandhrāṇi kṛtvāṅgulasamāni vai । catvāriṃśattatastasmiñśītamulmukacūrṇakam ।। ardham āpūrayitvā ca mukhe dadyāccharāvakam ।
karpaṭena mṛdā liptvā chāyāśuṣkaṃ ca kārayet ।। tasminnaṅgārakān kṣiptvā cullyāṃ vā ceṣṭikāsu ca । nidhāya tridinācchītaṃ gṛhītvauṣadhimāharet ।। etat kumbhapuṭaṃ jñeyaṃ kathitaṃ śāstradarśibhiḥ ।
iti ।। piṣṭakaṃ chagaṇaṃ chāṇam utpalaṃ copalaṃ tathā । giriṇḍopalasāṭhī ca varāṭī chagaṇābhidhāḥ ।। suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ trapu sīsakam āyasam ।
ṣaḍetāni ca lohāni kṛtrimau kāṃsyapittalau ।। lavaṇāni ṣaḍ ucyante sāmudraṃ saindhavaṃ viḍam । sauvarcalaṃ romakaṃ ca cūlikālavaṇaṃ tathā ।। kṣāratrayaṃ samākhyātaṃ yavasarjikaṭaṅkaṇam ।।
palāśamuṣkakakṣārau yavakṣāraḥ suvarcikā । tilanālodbhavaḥ kṣāraḥ saṃyuktaṃ kṣārapañcakam ।। ghṛtaṃ guḍo mākṣikaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ madhuratrayam ।। tumbinī kaṭutumbī saralakāṣṭhaṃ vā ।।
kaṅguṇī tumbinī ghoṣā karīraśrīphalodbhavam । kaṭuvārttākasiddhārthasomarājīvibhītajam ।। atasījaṃ mahākālīnimbajaṃ tilajaṃ tathā । apāmārgāddevadālīdantītumburuvigrahāt ।।
aṅkolonmattabhallātapalāśebhyas tathaiva ca । etebhyastailamādāya rasakarmaṇi yojayet ।। jambūkamaṇḍūkavasā vasā kacchapasambhavā । karkaṭīśiśumārī ca gośūkaranarodbhavā ।
ajoṣṭrakharameṣāṇāṃ mahiṣasya vasā tathā ।। mūtrāṇi hastikarabhamahiṣīkharavājinām । go'jāvīnāṃ striyaḥ puṃsāṃ puṣpaṃ bījaṃ tu yojayet ।। māhiṣāmbu dadhi kṣīraṃ sābhighāraṃ śakṛdrasaḥ ।
tatpañcamāhiṣaṃ jñeyaṃ tadvacchāgalapañcakam ।। amlavetasajambīranimbukaṃ bījapūrakam । amlīkaṃ tintiḍīphalam ।। cāṅgerī caṇakāmlaṃ ca amlīkaṃ koladāḍimam ।।
ambaṣṭhā tintiḍīkaṃ ca nāgaraṃ rasapattrikā । rasapattrikā kapitthāmlam ।। karavandaṃ tathā cānyadamlavargaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। caṇakāmlaśca sarveṣāmeka eva praśasyate ।
amlavetasamekaṃ vā sarveṣāmuttamottamam । rasādīnāṃ viśuddhyarthaṃ drāvaṇe jāraṇe hitam ।। koladāḍimavṛkṣāmlacullikācukrikārasaḥ । pañcāmlakaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ taccoktaṃ cāmlapañcakam ।।
iṣṭikā gairikā loṇaṃ bhasma valmīkamṛttikā । rasaprayogakuśalaiḥ kīrtitāḥ pañcamṛttikāḥ ।। śṛṅgīkaṃ kālakūṭaṃ ca vatsanābhaṃ sakṛtrimam । pittaṃ ca viṣavargo ayaṃ sa varaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
rasakarmaṇi śasto'yaṃ tadbhedanavidhāv api । ayuktyā sevitaścāyaṃ mārayatyeva niścitam ।। lāṅgalī viṣamuṣṭiśca karavīraṃ jayā tathā । nīlakaḥ bhallātakaḥ ।।
nīlakaḥ kanako'rkaśca vargo hy upaviṣātmakaḥ ।। hastyaśvavanitā dhenurgardabhī chāgikāvikā । uṣṭrikodumbarāśvatthabhānunyagrodhatilvakam ।। dugdhikā snugguṇaś caiva tathaivottamakaṇṭikā ।
uttamakaṇṭikā eraṇḍaviśeṣaḥ vāgā bhereṇḍā jāmālagoṭā iti ca bhāṣā yadvā uttamakaṇṭikā ।। eṣāṃ dugdhair vinirdiṣṭo dugdhavargo rasādiṣu ।। pārāvatasya cāṣasya kapotasya kalāpinaḥ । gṛdhrasya kukkuṭasyāpi vinirdiṣṭo hi viḍgaṇaḥ ।
śodhanaṃ sarvalohānāṃ puṭanāllepanāt khalu ।। kusumbhaṃ khadiro lākṣā mañjiṣṭhā raktacandanam । akṣī ca bandhujīvaśca tathā karpūragandhinī । karpūragandhinī karpūragandhiharidrāviśeṣaḥ ।। -d
mākṣikaṃ ceti vijñeyo raktavargo atirañjanaḥ ।। kiṃśukaḥ karṇikāraśca haridrādvitayaṃ tathā । pītavargo ayamādiṣṭo rasarājasya karmaṇi ।। tagaraḥ kuṭajaḥ kundo guñjā jīvantikā tathā ।
sitāmbhoruhakandaśca śvetavarga udāhṛtaḥ ।। kadalī kāravellī ca triphalā nīlikā nalaḥ । paṅkaḥ kāsīsabālāmraṃ kṛṣṇavarga udāhṛtaḥ ।। raktavargādivargaiśca dravyaṃ yajjāraṇātmakam ।
bhāvanīyaṃ prayatnena tādṛgrāgāptaye khalu ।। kācaḥ mṛttikāviśeṣaḥ sa ca kṣārarasaḥ uṣṇavīryaḥ añjanāddṛṣṭikārakaḥ viḍākhyalavaṇo vā ।। śiprā śuktiviśeṣaḥ ityarthaḥ ।। kācaṭaṅkaṇaśiprābhiḥ śodhanīyo gaṇo mataḥ ।।
sattvānāṃ baddhasūtasya lohānāṃ malanāśanaḥ । kāpālīkaṅguṇadhvaṃsī rasavādibhir ucyate ।। śodhanīgaṇaṃ tadupayogaṃ cāha kācaṭaṅkaṇasauvīrairiti ।। sauvīraṃ añjanaviśeṣam ।।
ayaṃ gaṇaḥ sūtasya khoṭabaddhādirūpasyābhrakasattvādīnāṃ ca yo guṇo vaṅgakāpālikā nāgakāpālikā kālikādir doṣātmakastaddhvaṃsī ।। ata evāyaṃ rasavādibhir iṣyate ।। mahiṣī meṣaśṛṅgī ca kaliṅgo dhavabījayuk । śaśāsthīni ca yogo'yaṃ lohakāṭhinyanāśanaḥ ।।
guḍagugguluguñjājyasāraghaiṣ ṭaṅgaṇānvitaiḥ । durdrāvākhilalohāder drāvaṇāya gaṇo mataḥ ।। kṣārāḥ sarve malaṃ hanyur amlaṃ śodhanajāraṇam । māndyaṃ viṣāṇi nighnanti snaigdhyaṃ snehāḥ prakurvate ।।
ṣaṭ truṭyaś caikalikṣā syāt ṣaḍ likṣā yūkam ucyate । ṣaḍyūkāstu rajaḥsaṃjñaṃ kathitaṃ tava suvrate ।। ṣaḍrajaḥ sarṣapaḥ sākṣātsiddhārthaḥ sa ca kīrtitaḥ । ṣaṭsiddhārthena deveśi yavastvekaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
ṣaḍyavair ekaguñjā syāttriguñjo valla ucyate । ṣaḍbhireva tu guñjābhirmāṣa ekaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । māṣā dvādaśa tolaḥ syādaṣṭau tolāḥ palaṃ bhavet ।। truṭiḥ syādaṇubhiḥ ṣaḍbhistairlikṣā ṣaḍbhirīritā ।
tābhiḥ ṣaḍbhirbhaved yūkā ṣaḍyūkās tad rajaḥ smṛtam ।। ṣaḍrajaḥ sarṣapaḥ proktastaiḥ ṣaḍbhiryava īritaḥ । ekā guñjā yavaiḥ ṣaḍbhirniṣpāvastu dviguñjakaḥ ।। syādguñjātritayaṃ vallo dvau vallau māṣa ucyate ।
dvau māṣau dharaṇaṃ te dve śāṇaniṣkakalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। niṣkadvayaṃ tu vaṭakaḥ sa ca kola itīritaḥ । syātkolatritayaṃ tolaḥ karṣo niṣkacatuṣṭayam ।। udumbaraṃ pāṇitalaṃ suvarṇaṃ kavalagrahaḥ ।
akṣaṃ biḍālapadakaṃ śuktiḥ pāṇitaladvayam ।। śuktidvayaṃ palaṃ kecidanye śuktitrayaṃ viduḥ । tadeva kathitaṃ muṣṭiḥ prakuñco bilvamityapi ।। paladvayaṃ tu prasṛtaṃ taddvayaṃ kuḍavo'ñjaliḥ ।
kuḍavau mānikā tau syātprastho dve mānike smṛtaḥ ।। prasthadvayaṃ śubhaṃ tau dvau pātrakaṃ dvayamāḍhakam । taiś caturbhir ghaṭonmānanalvanārmaṇaśūrpakāḥ ।। droṇasya śabdāḥ paryāyāḥ palānāṃ śatakaṃ tulā ।
catvāriṃśatpalaśatatulā bhāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। rasārṇavādiśāstrāṇi nirīkṣya kathitaṃ mayā । rasopayogi yat kiṃcid diṅmātraṃ tatpradarśitam ।। adhunā rasarājasya saṃskārān sampracakṣmahe ।।
syātsvedanaṃ tadanu mardanamūrchane ca utthāpanaṃ patanarodhaniyāmanāni । saṃdīpanaṃ gaganabhakṣaṇamānamatra saṃcāraṇā tadanu garbhagatā drutiśca ।। bāhyā drutiḥ sūtakajāraṇā syād grāsastathā sāraṇakarma paścāt । saṃkrāmaṇaṃ vedhavidhiḥ śarīre yogas tathāṣṭādaśadhātra karma ।।
na yojyo marmaṇi chinne na ca kṣārāgnidagdhayoḥ ।। śuddhaḥ sa mṛdvagnisaho mūrchito vyādhināśanaḥ ।। niṣkampavegas tīvrāgnāv āyurārogyado mṛtaḥ ।। viṣaṃ vahnirmalaśceti doṣā naisargikāstrayaḥ ।
rase maraṇasaṃtāpamūrchānāṃ hetavaḥ kramāt ।। viṣamiti ।। ete doṣā naisargikāḥ ।। tadviyogakaraṇaṃ doṣāntarāpekṣayātidurghaṭam iti svābhāvikā ityupacaryante ।।
vastutastu devaprārthitamahādevena teṣāṃ saṃbandhaḥ pārade yojita iti bhāvaḥ ।। yogikau nāgavaṅgau dvau tau jāḍyādhmānakuṣṭhadau ।। yogikau doṣāvāha yaugikāviti ।। nikaṭavartināgavaṅgakhaniyogena miśraṇājjāto nāgākhya eko doṣo vaṅgākhya ekaśceti to dvau jāḍyamādhmānaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ ca kurutaḥ ।।
aupādhikāḥ punaścānye kīrtitāḥ saptakañcukāḥ । bhūmijā girijā vārjās te ca dve nāgavaṅgajau ।। upādhinā saṃnihitavastusaṃbandhamātreṇa vastuni bahireva vyāpya tiṣṭhanti kiṃcit kālāvasthāyinaśca ye doṣāste aupādhikāḥ ।। te ca saptavidhāḥ ।।
kañcukākhyayā śāstra uditāḥ ।। teṣāṃ madhye bhūmijā ekaprakārāḥ ।। teṣām avāntarabhedena śāstre anupayogānnāmato anādṛtena bahuvacanam ।। girijā ekavidhāḥ ।।
vārjā jalajāścānyavidhāḥ ।। tathā nāgena vaṇijādibhir miśrīkṛtena jātau doṣau dvau ।। vaṅgajāvapi dvau ।। ityevaṃ sapta kañcukāḥ pūrvoktāśca pañca doṣāḥ ।।
itthaṃ pārade dvādaśa doṣā rasajñaiḥ proktāḥ ।। dvādaśaite rase doṣāḥ proktā rasaviśāradaiḥ ।। parpaṭī pāṭanī bhedī drāvī malakarī tathā । andhakārī tathā dhvāṅkṣī vijñeyāḥ sapta kañcukāḥ ।।
parpaṭyādi sapta kañcukānāṃ saṃjñāḥ tatra parpaṭīsadṛśaśoṣakatvāt parpaṭī parpaṭī yathā śoṣiṇī grāhiṇī ca pāradasya parpaṭyākhyakañcuko'pi naradehe tatkriyājananī vidārakatvāt pāṭanī malabhedakatvād bhedinī śārīradhātūnāṃ dravatvasaṃpādanād drāvī doṣavardhakatvāt malakarī andhatvajananād andhakārī dhvāṅkṣo yathā karkaśasvaro bhavati tathā svarapāruṣyajananād dhvāṅkṣīti jñeyam ।। uktasaptakañcukānāṃ krameṇa nāmāntarāṇyāha parpaṭīti ।। rasopari parpaṭī parpaṭākārā bhavati ।। sā parpaṭītyucyate ।।
pāṭanī tvacovidāraṇakarī ।। bhedī tvaci randhrakarī ।। drāvī lohādidravakarī ।। malakarī vātādidoṣakarī ।।
andhakārī kṛṣṇatvakarī ।। dhvāṅkṣī kālimā ।। bhūmijāḥ kurvate kuṣṭhaṃ girijā jāḍyameva ca । vārijā vātasaṃghātaṃ doṣāḍhyaṃ nāgavaṅgayoḥ ।।
tasmāt sūtavidhānārthaṃ sahāyairnipuṇairyutaḥ । sarvopaskaramādāya rasakarma samārabhet ।। dve sahasre palānāṃ tu sahasraṃ śatameva vā । aṣṭāviṃśat palānyeva daśa pañcaikameva vā ।।
palārdhenaiva kartavyaḥ saṃskāraḥ sūtakasya ca । sudine śubhanakṣatre rasaśodhanamārabhet ।। tryūṣaṇaṃ lavaṇāsūryau citrakārdrakamūlakam । kṣiptvā sūto muhuḥ svedyaḥ kāñjikena dinatrayam ।।
gṛhadhūmeṣṭikācūrṇaṃ tathā dadhi guḍānvitam । lavaṇāsurīsaṃyuktaṃ kṣiptvā sūtaṃ vimardayet ।। ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ tu tad dravyaṃ sūtamānān niyojayet । sūtaṃ kṣiptvā samaṃ tena dināni trīṇi mardayet ।।
jīrṇābhrakaṃ tathā bījaṃ jīrṇasūtaṃ tathaiva ca । nairmalyārthaṃ hi sūtasya khalle dhṛtvā vimardayet ।। gṛhṇāti nirmalo rāgān grāse grāse vimarditaḥ । mardanākhyaṃ hi yatkarma tatsūtaguṇakṛd bhavet ।।
gṛhakanyā malaṃ hanyāttriphalā vahnināśinī । citramūlaṃ viṣaṃ hanti tasmād ebhiḥ prayatnataḥ ।। miśritaṃ sūtakaṃ dravyaiḥ saptavārāṇi mūrchayet । itthaṃ saṃmūrchitaḥ sūto doṣaśūnyaḥ prajāyate ।।
asmādvirekāt saṃśuddho rasaḥ pātyastataḥ param । uddhṛtaḥ kāñjikakvāthāt pūtidoṣanivṛttaye ।। tāmreṇa piṣṭikāṃ kṛtvā pātayedūrdhvabhājane । vaṅganāgau parityajya śuddho bhavati sūtakaḥ ।।
śulvena pātayet piṣṭīṃ tridhordhvaṃ saptadhā tv adhaḥ ।। triphalāśigruśikhibhir lavaṇāsurīsaṃyutaiḥ । naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ rasaṃ kṛtvā lepayeccordhvabhājane । tato dīptairadhaḥ pātamutpalaistatra kārayet ।।
haridrāṅkolaśampākakumārītriphalāgnibhiḥ । śampākaḥ āragvadhaḥ ।। taṇḍulīyakavarṣābhūhiṅgusaindhavamākṣikaiḥ ।। piṣṭaṃ rasaṃ salavaṇaiḥ sarpākṣyādibhireva vā ।
pātayed athavā devi vraṇaghno yakṣalocanaiḥ ।। itthaṃ hy adhaūrdhvapātena pātito asau yadā bhavet । tadā rasāyane yogyo bhaved dravyaviśeṣataḥ ।। athavā dīpakayantre nipātitaḥ sarvadoṣanirmuktaḥ ।।
tiryakpātanavidhinā nipātitaḥ sūtarājastu । ślakṣṇīkṛtam abhradalaṃ rasendrayuktaṃ tathāranālena ।। khalle dattvā mṛditaṃ yāvat tan naṣṭapiṣṭatām eti । kuryāt tiryakpātanapātitasūtaṃ krameṇa dṛḍhavahnim ।।
saṃsvedyaḥ pātyo asau na patati yāvad dṛḍhaś cāgnau । tadāsau śudhyate sūtaḥ karmakārī bhaveddhruvam ।। mardanair mūrchanaiḥ pātair mandaḥ śānto bhaved rasaḥ ।। sṛṣṭyambujair nirodhena tato mukhakaro rasaḥ ।
svedanādivaśātsūto vīryaṃ prāpnotyanuttamam ।। niyamyo'sau tataḥ samyak capalatvanivṛttaye । karkoṭīphaṇinetrābhyāṃ vṛścikāmbujamārkavaiḥ । samaṃ kṛtvāranālena svedayecca dinatrayam ।।
maricair bhūkhagayuktair lavaṇāsurīśigruṭaṅkaṇopetaiḥ । kāñjikayuktaistridinaṃ grāsārthī jāyate svedāt ।। trikṣārasindhukhagabhūśikhiśigrurājītīkṣṇāmlavetasamukhair lavaṇoṣaṇāmlaiḥ । nepālatāmradalaśoṣitamāranāle sāmlāsavāmlapuṭitaṃ rasadīpanaṃ tat ।।
svedayedāsavāmlena vīryatejaḥpravṛddhaye । yathopayogaṃ svedyaḥ syān mūlikānāṃ raseṣu ca ।। sarpākṣī kṣīriṇī vandhyā matsyākṣī śaṅkhapuṣpikā । kākajaṅghā śikhiśikhā brahmadaṇḍyākhukarṇikā ।।
varṣābhūḥ kambukī dūrvā sairyakotpalaśimbikāḥ । śatāvarī vajralatā vajrakandāgnikarṇikā ।। śvetārkaśigrudhattūramṛgadūrvārasāṅkuśāḥ । rambhā raktābhanirguṇḍī lajjāluḥ suradālikā ।।
maṇḍūkaparṇī pātālī citrakaṃ grīṣmasundarā । kākamācī mahārāṣṭrī haridrā tilaparṇikā ।। jātī jayantī śrīdevī bhūkadambaḥ kusumbhakaḥ । kośātakī nīraṃ kaṇā lāṅgalī kaṭutumbikā ।।
cakramardo amṛtā kandaḥ sūryāvarteṣu puṅkhikā । vārāhī hastiśuṇḍī ca prāyeṇa rasamūlikāḥ ।। rasasya bhāvane svede mūṣālepe ca pūjitāḥ । ityaṣṭau sūtasaṃskārāḥ samā dravye rasāyane ।
kāryāste prathamaṃ śeṣā noktā dravyopayoginaḥ ।। pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyākān rasabandhān pracakṣmahe । yena yena hi cāñcalyaṃ durgrahatvaṃ ca naśyati । rasarājasya samprokto bandhanārtho hi vārttikaiḥ ।।
atha prathamādhyāye mūrchitvā harati rujam itipadyoktā viṣayāstraya evātra granthe vaktavyāḥ ।। mūrchanaṃ bandhanaṃ māraṇaṃ ca ।। tatra mūrchanaṃ tu mardanapūrvakaṃ puṭena prāguktameva ।। yantramūrchanaṃ tvasminnadhyāye dehopayogisarvabandhottaraṃ vakṣyāmi ।।
dvitīyo viṣayo'tra bandharūpo varṇyate ।। pañcaviṃśatīti ।। nanu granthāntare pāṭakhoṭajalūkābhasmeti bandhaścaturvidha evākhyātaḥ ।। atra tu pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyāka iti pratijānāti ।।
etadviruddhamiva bhātītyāśaṅkya cāñcalyadurgrahatvābhāvarūpasāmānyasya sarvabandheṣu sattve'pi bandhajanakakāraṇabhedānurodhena bandhabhedo'pi vārtikairādṛta ityāha yena yeneti ।। haṭhāroṭau tathābhāsaḥ kriyāhīnaśca piṣṭikā । kṣāraḥ khoṭaśca poṭaśca kalkabandhaśca kajjaliḥ ।। sajīvaścaiva nirjīvo nirbījaśca sabījakaḥ ।
śṛṅkhalādrutibandhau ca bālakaśca kumārakaḥ ।। taruṇaś ca tathā vṛddho mūrtibaddhas tathāparaḥ । jalabandho agnibandhaśca susaṃskṛtakṛtābhidhaḥ । mahābandhābhidhaśceti pañcaviṃśatir īritāḥ ।।
kecidvadanti ṣaḍviṃśo jalūkābandhasaṃjñakaḥ । sa tāvanneṣyate dehe strīṇāṃ drāve'tiśasyate ।। haṭho rasaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ samyak śuddhivivarjitaḥ । sa sevito nṛṇāṃ kuryān mṛtyuṃ vā vyādhimuddhatam ।।
pāradam āpaṇād ānīya nimbūrasena saṃmardya gālayitvā mayūratutthādisamabhāgaṃ caturthāṃśaṃ vā tatra dattvā mardanena baddho rasaḥ kriyate ।। sa sevitaścen mṛtyuṃ kuryādvyādhiṃ vā ।। suśodhito rasaḥ samyagāroṭa iti kathyate । sa kṣetrīkaraṇe śreṣṭhaḥ śanairvyādhivināśanaḥ ।।
āroṭalakṣaṇam āha suśodhita iti ।। trividhapātanena śuddhaṃ paścācchuddhaṃ cūrṇīkṛtam abhrakadalaṃ samabhāgaṃ dattvā kāñjikena mardanapūrvakaṃ pāradaṃ naṣṭapiṣṭaṃ kṛtvordhvādhastiryakpātanenāsakṛtkṛtenāgnisahaḥ pārada āroṭa iti nigadyate ।। taṃ ca mākṣīkaśilājatulohacūrṇapathyākṣaviḍaṅgaghṛtamadhubhiḥ saṃyutaṃ kṛtvā kṣetrīkaraṇāya yuñjīteti rasahṛdaye ।। mākṣīkasahito naṣṭapiṣṭirūpaḥ pātanenāgnisthāyyapi pārado'pi āroṭa iti kathyate ।।
puṭito yo raso yāti yogaṃ muktvā svabhāvatām । bhāvito dhātumūlādyair ābhāso guṇavaikṛteḥ ।। ābhāsabandhamāha puṭita iti ।। dhātumūlādyaiḥ prāguktasvarṇādidhātubhistathā sarpākṣyādimūlikābhiḥ bhāvitaḥ puṭitaśca rasaḥ guṇavaikṛteḥ dravyāntarasaṃyogena svābhāvikaguṇaviparyayāt svabhāvatāṃ svābhāvikaguṇādikaṃ muktvā yogaṃ yogavāhitāṃ yāti sa ābhāsaḥ kathyate iti śeṣaḥ ।।
ābhāsalakṣaṇamāha yaḥ pārado dhātubhir manaḥśilāgandhakādibhistathā mūlikādyaiḥ sarpākṣyādimūlikābhiḥ patrapuṣpādibhiśca saha bhāvito dravaṃ dattvā marditastato bhūdharayantre puṭena puṭito bhasmīkṛtaḥ svabhāvataḥ svabhāvaṃ cāñcalyadurgrahatvādi muktvā dhātvādiyogaṃ yāti tattadroganāśakayogaguṇaṃ ca yāti guṇaprado bhavati ।। alpakālaparyantaṃ tataḥ pathyasevino'pi narasya guṇavaikṛte sati guṇavikriyāyāṃ satyāṃ sa baddhapārada ābhāsa iti kīrtitaḥ ।। guṇābhāsakaratvāt ।। vikṛtireva vaikṛtam ।।
asaṃśodhitalohādyaiḥ sādhito yo rasottamaḥ । kriyāhīnaḥ sa vijñeyo vikriyāṃ yātyapathyataḥ ।। tīvrātape gāḍhatarāvamardātpiṣṭī bhavetsā navanītarūpā । sa rasaḥ piṣṭikābandho dīpanaḥ pācanastarām ।।
śaṅkhaśuktivarāṭādyair yo asau saṃsādhito rasaḥ । kṣārabandhaḥ paraṃ dīptipuṣṭikṛcchūlanāśanaḥ ।। śaṅkhaśuktīti ।। bhasmīkṛtānāṃ śaṅkhaśuktyādīnāṃ vṛkṣakṣārādīnāṃ ca mūṣāṃ kṛtvā tatsaṃpuṭe pāradaṃ prakṣipya saṃpuṭitaḥ pārado laghupuṭadānena bhasmībhavatīti kṣārabandho asāvagnidīptyādikṛd bhavet ।।
kṣārabandhamāha śaṅkheti ।। saṃsādhitaḥ mardanapuṭanādibhiḥ susampāditaḥ ।। spaṣṭam anyat ।। bandho yaḥ khoṭatāṃ yāti dhmāto dhmātaḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet ।
khoṭabandhaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ śīghraṃ sarvagadāpahaḥ ।। khoṭabandhamāha bandha iti ।। khoṭatāṃ vahnistho'pi anuḍḍayanasvabhāvatāṃ yaduktam । agnimadhye yadā tiṣṭhet khoṭabaddhasya lakṣaṇam ।
iti ।। dhmāto dhmātaḥ bhastrayā punaḥ punar ādhmāpita ityarthaḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet dravyāntareṇa saha ekībhāvāt adarśanatāṃ gacchedityarthaḥ ।। atha khoṭabandhamāha bandha iti ।। khoṭakaraṇaprakārastu rasasāra uvāca ।
bandhane yāśca vikhyātā aṣṭāveva mahauṣadhīḥ । tābhiṣṭaṅkaṇayuktābhir bhāvayecca raseśvaram । tābhir viliptamūṣāyāṃ dhamanāt khoṭatāṃ vrajet ।। iti ।।
sa evātidhmānāt kṣayaṃ gacchati ।। sa ca khoṭabandho bodhyaḥ ।। atra pārado jīrṇaṣaḍguṇagandho grāhyaḥ ।। abhrakadānena piṣṭīkṛto vā grāhyaḥ ।।
somavallīrase piṣṭvā dāpayecca puṭatrayam । somavallīrasenaiva saptavārāṃśca bhāvayet ।। tadabhraṃ mṛdbhāṇḍe dadyād rasena saha saṃyutam । mūlaṃ tu śarapuṅkhāyā gavyakṣīreṇa gharṣayet ।।
kalkena melayet sūtaṃ gaganaṃ ca tadadhordhvagam । sthāpayed ravitāpe tu nirmukho grasate kṣaṇāt । jāyate piṣṭikā śīghraṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। iti ।।
piṣṭībandhastu khoṭaka iti varṇanād atra piṣṭikārūpam ucyate ।। khoṭalakṣaṇaṃ granthāntare tu । dhmāto druto bhavet khoṭa āhataścūrṇatāṃ vrajet । punar dhmāto drutaḥ khoṭa iti khoṭasya lakṣaṇam ।।
ghanasattvapādajīrṇaḥ kāntapādajīrṇaḥ samatīkṣṇajīrṇaścedvāyaṃ kṣetrīkaraṇārtham api praśastaḥ ।। drutakajjalikā mocāpattrake cipiṭīkṛtā । sa poṭaḥ parpaṭī saiva bālādyakhilaroganut ।। pāṭabandhaṃ lakṣayati druteti ।।
adho'gninā kaṭāhe tāpena drutā jātadravā yā kajjalī sā tatkṣaṇe kadalīdale prakṣipya taddalenācchādya pīḍanena cipiṭīkṛtā pāṭabandhaḥ parpaṭikābandhaśceti khyātā bālavṛddhādīnām anupānabhedena sarvarogaghnī ।। svedādyaiḥ sādhitaḥ sūtaḥ paṅkatvaṃ samupāgataḥ । kalkabaddhaḥ sa vijñeyo yogoktaphaladāyakaḥ ।। yogoktaphaladāyakaḥ yasmin yoge sa prayojyaḥ tasya phalautkarṣyaprada ityarthaḥ athavā svedanamardanārthaṃ gṛhītakalkadravyāṇām upayoge yat phalaṃ tatphalaprada ityarthaḥ ।।
kajjalī rasagandhotthā suślakṣṇā kajjalopamā । tattadyogena saṃyuktā kajjalībandha ucyate ।। kajjalībandhamāha kajjalīti ।। suślakṣṇā cikkaṇā ।।
tattadyogena saṃyuktā rasagandhakaśodhakadravyasaṃyogena śuddhā ityarthaḥ ।। kajjalībandhaṃ lakṣayati ।। tattadyogena rogavārakaviśiṣṭauṣadhīmiśraṇamardanayogena yuktā satī kajjalībandha ucyate ।। atra tattadyogena saṃyukteti na lakṣaṇaghaṭakam ।।
tena vinā kajjalyāḥ siddhatvāt ।। kiṃtu yogavāhitveneyaṃ sarvaroganāśiketi bodhanāya taduktiḥ ।। bhasmīkṛto gacchati vahniyogād rasaḥ sajīvaḥ sa khalu pradiṣṭaḥ । saṃsevito'sau na karoti bhasmakāryaṃ javād rogavināśanaṃ ca ।।
sajīvabaddham āha bhasmīkṛteti ।। tāmbūlīdalarasamarditaḥ paścād vandhyākarkoṭakīkandamadhye prakṣipya saṃpuṭito bahir mṛdvastrābhyāṃ saṃpuṭito bhūmau gajapuṭena puṭito bhasmībhavati ।। evaṃ prakārāntareṇāpi bhasmīkṛtaḥ pārado'gnau pātre dhṛtaścedākāśe gacchati ।। pakṣacchedābhāvāt ।।
bhasmakāryaṃ jarāmaraṇābhāvarūpaṃ sa tu na karoti ।। vyādhināśamapi na ।। jīrṇābhrako vā parijīrṇagandho bhasmīkṛtaścākhilalohamauliḥ । nirjīvanāmā hi sa bhasmasūto niḥśeṣarogān vinihanti sadyaḥ ।।
nirjīvabandhamāha jīrṇābhraka iti ।। jīrṇābhrakaḥ grāsīkṛtābhra ityarthaḥ ।। parijīrṇagandhaḥ samyaggrāsitagandhaka ityarthaḥ ।। akhileti ।।
akhilānāṃ sarveṣāṃ lohānāṃ svarṇādīnāmityarthaḥ mauliḥ śirobhūṣaṇasvarūpaḥ sarvalohopayoge ye guṇā bhavanti tebhyo'pyadhikaguṇaprada ityarthaḥ ।। vahniyoge'pi nirgamanāsāmarthyāt asya nirjīvatvaṃ bodhyam ।। rasastu pādāṃśasuvarṇajīrṇaḥ piṣṭīkṛto gandhakayogataśca । tulyāṃśagandhaiḥ puṭitaḥ krameṇa nirbījanāmā sakalāmayaghnaḥ ।।
nirbījabandhaṃ lakṣayati rasastviti ।। atra suvarṇaṃ na tu bījīkṛtaṃ kiṃtu śuddhaṃ jāraṇāyantre saṃskṛtaṃ pattrarūpaṃ grāhyam ।। piṣṭīkṛto dvādaśāṃśe pārada ekāṃśaṃ gandhakaṃ truṭiśo muhur dattvāmlena saṃmarditastatastulyāṃśagandhaiḥ krameṇa puṭitaḥ prathamaṃ gandhakaṃ caturthāṃśaṃ dattvā bhūdharayantre puṭitastato'rdhāṃśaṃ gandhakaṃ dattvā tathā puṭitastataḥ pādonaṃ gandhakaṃ dattvā puṭitastadūrdhvaṃ samabhāgamitaṃ dattvā puṭita iti kramaśabdārthaḥ ।। gandhair iti bahuvacanam atantram ।।
piṣṭīkṛtair abhrakasattvahematārārkakāntaiḥ parijārito yaḥ । hatastataḥ ṣaḍguṇagandhakena sabījabaddho vipulaprabhāvaḥ ।। vajrādinihataḥ sūto hataḥ sūtaḥ samo'paraḥ । śṛṅkhalābaddhasūtastu dehalohavidhāyakaḥ ।
citraprabhāvāṃ vegena vyāptiṃ jānāti śaṃkaraḥ ।। vajreṇa bhasmīkṛtena cūrṇīkṛtena vā nihato mārito yaḥ sūtastanmadhye māritam anyaṃ sūtakam api nikṣipet ।। so'pi raso baddhaḥ khoṭarūpaḥ śṛṅkhalābaddha ityucyate ।। etanmāraṇaprakārastu rasārṇave uktaḥ ।।
śṛṅkhalābandhamāha vajrādīti ।। vajrādinihataḥ hīrakādisahayogena māritaḥ sūtaḥ tadvā samaḥ samaparimitaḥ aparaśca hataḥ prakārāntareṇa māritaḥ sūtaḥ śṛṅkhalābaddhasūtaḥ ubhayor mardanād iti śeṣaḥ ।। citraprabhāvām alaukikasāmarthyāṃ vegena vyāptiṃ śṛṅkhalābandhasūtasya dehe iti śeṣaḥ ।। yukto'pi bāhyadrutibhiśca sūto bandhaṃgato vā bhasitasvarūpaḥ ।
