sa rājikāpādamito nihanti duḥsādhyarogān drutibaddhanāmā ।। atha drutibaddham āha yukto'pīti ।। bījānāṃ jāraṇena yadi raso mahāprabhāvo bhavatīti tanna citram ।। rasoparasadhātūnāṃ yā bahirdrutayas tābhir yukto'pi tābhir jārito'pi pārado baddhamātro bandhottaraṃ bhasmīkṛto vā drutibaddhanāmā sarṣapacaturthāṃśamātrayā sevitaścedduḥsādhyarogān nihanti ।।
drutibandhamāha yukta iti ।। bāhyadrutibhiḥ rasasya dravatvasampādakakriyāviśeṣaiḥ yuktaḥ api bandhaṃ gataḥ bandhanatāṃ prāptaḥ vā athavā bhasitasvarūpaḥ bhasmībhūtaḥ sūtaḥ drutibaddhanāmā jñeyaḥ ।। saḥ drutibaddhasūtaḥ rājikā rāī iti khyātaḥ raktavarṇasarṣapaviśeṣaḥ tasyāḥ pādamitaḥ caturthabhāgaparimitaḥ ।। samābhrajīrṇaḥ śivajastu bālaḥ saṃsevito yogayuto javena ।
rasāyano bhāvigadāpahaśca sopadravāriṣṭagadānnihanti ।। bālākhyabaddhaṃ lakṣayati sameti ।। abhraṃ kṛṣṇavajrābhrasattvam ।। śivajaḥ pāradaḥ ।।
samābhrajīrṇaścatuḥṣaṣṭidvātriṃśatṣoḍaśādibhāgakrameṇa ।। asyopayogaḥ pattralepe'pi bodhyaḥ ।। harodbhavo yo dviguṇābhrajīrṇaḥ sa syātkumāro mitataṇḍulo'sau । triḥ saptarātraiḥ khalu pāparogasaṃghātaghātī ca rasāyanaṃ ca ।।
caturguṇavyomakṛtāśano asau rasāyanāgryas taruṇābhidhānaḥ । sa saptarātrāt sakalāmayaghno rasāyano vīryabalapradātā ।। yasyābhrakaḥ ṣaḍguṇito hi jīrṇaḥ prāptāgnisakhyaḥ sa hi vṛddhanāmā । dehe ca lohe ca niyojanīyaḥ śivādṛte ko asya guṇān pravakti ।।
yo divyamūlikābhiśca kṛto'tyagnisaho rasaḥ । vinābhrajāraṇātsa syānmūrtibandho mahārasaḥ ।। ayaṃ hi jāryamāṇastu nāgninā kṣīyate rasaḥ । yojitaḥ sarvayogeṣu niraupamyaphalapradaḥ ।।
mūrtibaddhaṃ lakṣayati ya iti ।। divyamūlikāścatuḥṣaṣṭimūlikāḥ prāguktāstābhistadrasena mardanasvedanādinā pakṣacchedāt ।। abhrajāraṇād vināpyatyagnisaho baddhaḥ kṛto dravyāntarānabhivyāptyā kevalaṃ dehenaiva baddho mūrtibaddha ityucyate ।। tathā vaikrāntavajrasaṃsparśāt ।।
tena cūrṇīkṛtena saha mardanādapi raso baddho bhavatīti so'pi mūrtibaddha ityucyate ।। evaṃ ca mūrtibandho dvividhaḥ sambhavati ।। śilātoyamukhaistoyair baddho asau jalabandhavān । sa jarārogamṛtyughnaḥ kalpoktaphaladāyakaḥ ।।
jalabandhaṃ lakṣayati ।। śilātoyamukhaiḥ śilātoyacandratoyapramukhair jalaiḥ saha mardanādinā baddhaḥ pārado jalabaddha iti kīrtitaḥ ।। kalpokteti ।। pāradakalpoktaphaletyarthaḥ ।।
etasya jalasya vistaro rasārṇave spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ ।। kṣiptaṃ jale bhavet kāṣṭhaṃ śilābhūtaṃ ca dṛśyate । bahirantaśca deveśi vedhakaṃ tat prakīrtitam ।। hiṅgulaṃ haritālaṃ ca gandhakaṃ ca manaḥśilā ।
eṣāṃ gandhāpahāraṃ yat kurute tacca vedhakam ।। kevalo yogeṣu vā dhmātaḥ syādguṭikākṛtiḥ । akṣīṇaścāgnibaddho'sau khecaratvādikṛt sa hi ।। agnibandhamāha kevala iti ।।
kevalaḥ dravyāntarāsaṃyukta ityarthaḥ ।। yogayuktaḥ dravyāntarasaṃyuktaḥ ।। dhmātaḥ agnau saṃtaptaḥ ।। akṣīṇaḥ agnitāpe'pi yathāmātrāyāṃ sthitaḥ na tu kiṃcid apyūnaḥ ।।
khecaratvādikṛt mukhe dhṛtaḥ nabhogatisāmarthyapradaḥ ityarthaḥ ।। uddeśagranthe jalabandho'gnibandhaśca susaṃskṛtakṛtābhidhaḥ ityanena agnibandhānantaraṃ mahābandhācca prāk susaṃskṛtakṛtākhyabandhāntarasya samullekho vidyate vivaraṇagranthe tu tadullekhādarśanāt bandhaḥ saḥ lipikarapramādāt pramādāntarādvā adarśanatāṃ gata iti manye ।। kiṃca susaṃskṛtakṛtābhidhaḥ ityasya agnibandhasya viśeṣaṇatvamapi na yujyate tathātve bandhasya caturviṃśatisaṃkhyatvāt pañcaviṃśatisaṃkhyākān rasabandhān pracakṣmahe iti pratijñāhānyāpatteriti ।। athāgnibaddhaṃ pāradamāha kevala iti ।।
ādau ṣaḍguṇenābhrakajāraṇenāgnisahaḥ pārado maṇijīrṇaḥ pātanāyantreṇotthāpitaḥ sa druto bhavati ।। sa ca kevalastīkṣṇalohayukto vā dhmātaḥ san guṭikākṛtiścāgnāvakṣayaśca bhavati ।। ata evāyam agnibaddha ityucyate ।। ayaṃ mukhe dhṛtaścet puruṣasyākāśagāmitvaśastrāgnyabhedyatvasāyujyasārūpyādimuktikaro bhavet ।।
viṣṇukrāntāśaśilatākumbhīkanakamūlakaiḥ । viśālānāginīkandavyāghrapādīkuruṇṭakaiḥ ।। vṛścikālībhaśuṇḍībhyāṃ haṃsapādā sahāsuraiḥ । aprasūtagavāṃ mūtraiḥ piṣṭaṃ vā kulake pacet ।।
pakvamevaṃ mṛtair lohairmarditaṃ vipaced rasam । yantreṣu mūrchā sūtānāmeṣa kalpaḥ samāsataḥ ।। nibiḍaḥ nonnatānataḥ samānasarvāvayavaḥ ityarthaḥ ।। hemnā vā rajatena vā sahacaro dhmāto vrajatyekatām akṣīṇo nibiḍo guruśca guṭikākāro atidīrghojjvalaḥ ।
nirbandhaḥ yathāyatham asaṃpāditabandhanakriyaḥ cet kṣaṇāt dravati agnau iti śeṣaḥ ।। cūrṇatvaṃ paṭuvat prayāti nihato ghṛṣṭo na muñcenmalaṃ nirgandho dravati kṣaṇāt sa hi mahābandhābhidhāno rasaḥ ।। mahābandhamāha hemnā veti ।। atra hema caturthāṃśam ardhāṃśaṃ vā grāhyam ।।
rajatamapi tathaiva ।। bandhauṣadhiliptavajramūṣāmadhye tayor anyatareṇa yukto dhmāto'gnibaddha eva pārado vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇaviśiṣṭaḥ susaṃskṛtakṛtasaṃjñāṃ mahābandhasaṃjñāṃ ca labhate ।। tānyeva lakṣaṇāny āha dhmāto vrajatyekatām ityādinā ।। paṭuvat ।।
saindhavatulyaṃ cūrṇatvaṃ yāti ।। nihataḥ saṃdravati ।। agniyogāditi śeṣaḥ ।। sūte garbhaniyojitārdhakanake pādāṃśanāge'thavā pañcāṅguṣṭhakaśālmalīkṛtamadāśleṣmātabījais tathā ।
tadvat tejinīkolakākhyaphalajaiś cūrṇaṃ tilaṃ pattrakaṃ tapte khallatale nidhāya mṛdite jātā jalūkā varā ।। saiṣā syātkapikacchūromapaṭale candrāvatītailake candre ṭaṅkaṇakāmapippalījale svinnā bhavet tejinī । tapte khallatale vimardya vidhivadyatnādvaṭī yā kṛtā sā strīṇāṃ madadarpanāśanakarī khyātā jalūkā varā ।। bālye cāṣṭāṅgulā yojyā yauvane ca daśāṅgulā ।
dvādaśaiva pragalbhānāṃ jalaukā trividhā matā ।। dhṛtvā sūtamukhe pātraṃ meṣīkṣīraṃ pradāpayet । sthāpayedātape tīvre vāsarāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ ।। dvitīyātra mayā proktā jalaukā drāvaṇe hitā ।
puruṣāṇāṃ sthitā mūrdhni drāvayedbījam adbhutam ।। munipattrarasaṃ caiva śālmalīvṛntavāri ca । jātīmūlasya toyaṃ ca śiṃśapātoyasaṃyutam ।। śleṣmātakaphalaṃ caiva triphalācūrṇam eva ca ।
kokilākṣasya cūrṇaṃ ca pāradaṃ mardayed budhaḥ ।। jalūkā jāyate divyā rāmājanamanoharā । sā yojyā kāmakāle tu kāmayetkāminī svayam ।। triphalābhṛṅgamahauṣadhamadhusarpiśchāgadugdhagomūtre ।
nāgaṃ saptaniṣiktaṃ samarasajāritaṃ jalūkā syāt ।। bhānusvaradinasaṃkhyāpramāṇasūtaṃ gṛhītadīnāram । aṅkolarājavṛkṣakakanyārasataśca śodhanaṃ kuryāt ।। śaśirekhāvaravarṇinīsakokilākṣāpāmārgakanakānām ।
cūrṇaiḥ sahaikaviṃśatidināni saṃmardayet samyak ।। niśāyāḥ kāñjikaṃ yūṣaṃ dattvā yonau praveśayet । bālamadhyamavṛddhāsu yojyā vijñāya tatkramāt । nīrasānāmapi nṝṇāṃ yoṣā syātsaṃgamotsukā ।।
rasabhāgaṃ catuṣkaṃ ca vaṅgabhāgaṃ ca pañcamam । surasārasamaṃ yuktaṃ ṭaṅkaṇena samanvitam ।। tridinaṃ mardayitvā ca golakaṃ taṃ rasodbhavam । liṅgāgre yoninikṣiptaṃ yāvad āyurvaśaṃkaram ।।
karpūrasūraṇasubhṛṅgasumeghanādair nāgaṃ niṣicya tu mitho valayed rasena । liṅgasthitena valayena nitambinīnāṃ svāmī bhavatyanudinaṃ sa tu jīvahetuḥ ।। ṭaṅkaṇapippalikābhiḥ sūraṇakarpūramātuluṅgarasaiḥ । kṛtvā svaliṅgalepaṃ yoniṃ vidrāvayet strīṇām ।।
agnyāvartitanāge harabījaṃ nikṣipettato dviguṇam । munikanakanāgasarpair dantyātha siñcyācca tanmadhyam ।। takreṇa mardayitvā gaṇena madanavalayaṃ kuryāt । ratisamaye vanitānāṃ ratigarvavināśanaṃ kurute ।।
vyāghrībṛhatīphalarasasūraṇakandaṃ ca caṇakapattrāmlam । kapikacchuvajravallīpippalikāmlikācūrṇam ।। agnyāvartitanāgaṃ navavāraṃ mardayeddhimairdravyaiḥ । smaravalayaṃ kṛtvaitadvanitānāṃ drāvaṇaṃ kurute ।।
palāśabījakaṃ raktajambīrāmlena sūtakam । sajīvaṃ marditaṃ yantre pācitaṃ mriyate dhruvam ।। kharamañjari bījānvitapuṣkarabījaiḥ sucūrṇitaiḥ kalkam । kṛtvā sūtaṃ puṭayed dṛḍhamūṣāyāṃ bhavedbhasma ।।
kākodumbarikāyā dugdhena subhāvito hiṅguḥ । mardanapuṭanavidhānātsūtaṃ bhasmīkarotyeva ।। devadālīṃ harikrāntāmāranālena peṣayet । taddravaiḥ saptadhā sūtaṃ kuryānmarditamūrchitam ।।
tatsūtaṃ kharpare dadyāddattvā dattvā tu taddravam । cullyopari pacec cāhni bhasma syāllavaṇopamam ।। apāmārgasya bījāni tathairaṇḍasya cūrṇayet । taccūrṇaṃ pārade deyaṃ mūṣāyām adharottaram ।
ruddhvā laghupuṭaiḥ pacyāc caturbhir bhasmatāṃ nayet ।। kaṭutumbyudbhave kande garbhe nārīpayaḥplute । saptadhā sveditaḥ sūto mriyate gomayāgninā ।। aṅkolasya śiphāvāripiṣṭaṃ khalle vimardayet ।
sūtaṃ gandhakasaṃyuktaṃ dinānte taṃ nirodhayet । puṭayedbhūdhare yantre dinānte sa mṛto bhavet ।। vaṭakṣīreṇa sūtābhrau mardayetpraharatrayam । pācayettena kāṣṭhena bhasmībhavati tadrasaḥ ।।
athāturo rasācāryaṃ sākṣāddevaṃ maheśvaram । sādhitaṃ ca rasaṃ śṛṅgadantaveṇvādidhāritam ।। arcayitvā yathāśakti devagobrāhmaṇānapi । parṇakhaṇḍe dhṛtaṃ sūtaṃ jagdhvā syādanupānataḥ ।।
ghṛtasaindhavadhānyakajīrakārdrakasaṃskṛtam । taṇḍulīyakadhānyakapaṭolālambuṣādikam ।। gojīrṇaśālyannaṃ gavyaṃ kṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ dadhi । haṃsodakaṃ mudgarasaḥ pathyavargaḥ samāsataḥ ।।
bṛhatī bilvakūṣmāṇḍaṃ vetrāgraṃ kāravellakam । māṣaṃ masūraṃ niṣpāvaṃ kulatthaṃ sarṣapaṃ tilam ।। laṅghanodvartanasnānatāmrasurāsavān । ānūpamāṃsaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ bhojanaṃ kadalīdale ।
kāṃsye ca guruviṣṭambhi tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ ca bhṛśaṃ tyajet ।। kaṇṭārīphalakāñjikaṃ ca kamaṭhas tailaṃ tathā rājikām । nimbūkaṃ katakaṃ kaliṅgakaphalaṃ kūṣmāṇḍakaṃ karkaṭī । kārī kukkuṭakāravellakaphalaṃ karkoṭikāyāḥ phalam ।
vṛntākaṃ ca kapitthakaṃ khalu gaṇaḥ proktaḥ kakārādikaḥ ।। devīśāstroditaḥ so ayaṃ kakārādigaṇo mataḥ । śāstrāntaravinirdiṣṭaḥ kathyate'nyaprakārataḥ ।। kaṅguḥ kandukakolakukkuṭakalakroḍāḥ kulatthāstathā ।
kaṇṭārī kaṭutailakṛṣṇagalakaḥ kūrmaḥ kalāyaḥ kaṇā । karkāruśca kaṭhillakaṃ ca katakaṃ karkoṭakaṃ karkaṭī kālī kāñjikameṣakādikagaṇaḥ śrīkṛṣṇadevoditaḥ ।। yasminrase ca kaṇṭhoktyā kakārādirniṣedhitaḥ । tatra tatra niṣeddhavyaṃ tadaucityamato'nyataḥ ।।
udgāre sati dadhyannaṃ kṛṣṇamīnaṃ sajīrakam । abhyaṅgam anilakṣobhe tailair nārāyaṇādibhiḥ ।। aratau śītatoyena mastakopari secanam । tṛṣṇāyāṃ nārikelāmbu mudgaṃ saśarkaram ।।
drākṣādāḍimakharjūrakadalīnāṃ phalaṃ bhajet । rasavīryavivṛddhyarthaṃ dadhikṣīrekṣuśarkarāḥ । śītopacāram anyaṃ ca rasatyāgavidhau punaḥ ।। bhakṣayed bṛhatīṃ bilvaṃ sakṛtsādhāraṇo vidhiḥ ।।
jvarasya raktapittasya kāsasya śvāsahidhmayoḥ । vaisvaryasya kṣayasyāpi tathārocaprasekayoḥ ।। chardihṛdrogayoś caiva tṛṣṇāmadyodbhavārśasām । udāvartātisārāṇāṃ grahaṇyartipravāhiṇoḥ ।।
visūcyā vahnimāndyasya mūtrakṛcchrāśmarujām । mehasya somarogasya piṭikānāṃ ca vidradheḥ ।। vṛddhigulmādirogāṇāṃ śūlānāmudarasya ca । pāṇḍuśophavisarpāṇāṃ kuṣṭhaśvitranabhasvatām ।।
vātāsrasyāvṛtānāṃ ca vandhyānāṃ garbhiṇīrujām । sūtikābālarogāṇām unmāde apasmṛtāv api ।। netraroge karṇaroge nāsārogāsyarogayoḥ । śiraḥsaṃjātarogeṣu vraṇe bhaṅge bhagaṃdare ।।
granthyādau kṣudrarogeṣu guhyaroge viṣeṣu ca । jarāyāstvanapatyānāṃ bījapoṣaṇahetave ।। paripāṭyānayā sarvaṃ rogāṇāṃ hi cikitsanam । rasalohaviṣair atra yogairvakṣye yathāgamam ।।
romāñcakampau vadane madhutvamujjṛmbhaṇaṃ mastakatodadāhau । vātajvarasyoktam idaṃ hi lakṣma bhuktottaraṃ syādyadi śaśvadeva ।। virekaśoṣāsyakaṭutvatīvratāpapralāpabhramamūrchanāni । etāni pittajvaralakṣaṇāni vamiḥ satṛṣṇāṅgavidāhitā ca ।।
kāsaśvāsau mukhe jāḍyaṃ mādhuryaṃ bahunidratā । prasvedaḥ svalpadāhaśca śleṣmajajvaralakṣaṇam ।। miśritaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ yattu dvayos triṣu bhavecca tat ।। vimarditābhyāṃ rasagandhakābhyāṃ nīreṇa kuryādiha golakaṃ tam ।
bhāṇḍe navīne viniveśya paścāttadgolakasyopari tāmrapātram ।। sārdhaṃ muhūrtaṃ vinirudhya dhīmān uddīpayed dīptakṛśānunāsya । adhastataḥ sidhyati parpaṭīyaṃ navajvarāraṇyakṛśānumeghaḥ ।। vilipya pūrvaṃ rasanāṃ ca tāludeśaṃ ca sindhūdbhavajīrakārdraiḥ ।
vallonmitāṃ cārdrakatoyamiśrām enāṃ niyojya sthagayet paṭena ।। gharmodgamo yāvadataḥ paraṃ ca takraudanaṃ pathyamiha prayojyam । kuryāddinānāṃ tritayaṃ yadītthaṃ jvarasya śaṅkāpi tadā bhavetkim ।। sūtārkagandhacapalājayapālatiktāpathyātrivṛcca viṣatindukajān samāṃśān ।
saṃbhāvya vajripayasā madhunā trivallas trailokyaḍambararaso abhinavajvaraghnaḥ ।। pādāṃśakaṃ sāraraviḥ samāṃśagandho vipakvaḥ svakaṣāyapiṣṭaḥ । rasaḥ kramānmāṣamito anilādijvareṣu nāmnā kila meghanādaḥ ।। daradajaladayuktaṃ śuddhasūtaṃ ca gandhaṃ praharamatha supiṣṭaṃ vallayugmaṃ ca dadyāt ।
jvaragajaharisaṃjñaṃ śṛṅgaverodakena prathamajanitadāhī kṣīrabhaktena bhojyaḥ ।। saṃtaptasīsabhāgaṃ ca pāradaṃ gandhakaṃ kaṇām । samabhāgaṃ pṛthak tatra melayecca yathāvidhi ।। jambīrasya rase sarvaṃ mardayecca dinatrayam ।
meghanādakumāryośca rase cāpi dinatrayam ।। dinadvayamajāmūtre gavāṃ mūtre dinatrayam । bhāvayecca yathāyogyaṃ tasminnetāni dāpayet ।। saindhavaṃ citrakaṃ bhāgaṃ sauvarcalalavaṇaṃ tathā ।
tena sammelanaṃ kṛtvā bhāvayecca punaḥ punaḥ ।। anena vidhinā samyak siddho bhavati tadrasaḥ । śarkarāghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ dadyādvallatrayaṃ rasam ।। godhūmasyaudanaṃ pathyaṃ māṣasūpaṃ ca vāstukam ।
dhātrīphalasamāyuktaṃ sarvajvaravināśanam । dīpikārasa ityeṣa tantrajñaiḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। pāradaṃ rasakaṃ tālaṃ tutthaṃ gandhakaṭaṅkaṇam । sarvametatsamaṃ śuddhaṃ kāravallyā dravairdinam ।।
mardayettena kalkena tāmrapātrodaraṃ limpet । aṅgulārdhārdhamānena taṃ pacetsikatāhvaye ।। yantre yāvatsphuṭantyevaṃ vrīhayastasya pṛṣṭhataḥ । tataḥ suśītalaṃ grāhyaṃ tāmrapātrodarād bhiṣak ।।
śītabhañjī raso nāma cūrṇayenmaricaiḥ samam । māṣaikaṃ parṇakhaṇḍena bhakṣayennāśayejjvaram । tridinair viṣamaṃ tīvramekadvitricaturthakam ।। sūtatālaśilāstulyā mardayetkarkaṭīrase ।
tāmrapātre vinikṣipya tatkalkaṃ kajjalīkṛtam ।। vipacedvālukāyantre yathoktavidhinā tataḥ । dadyānmaricacūrṇena māṣamātraṃ bhiṣagvaraḥ ।। prapibeduṣṇatoyasya culukaṃ śītakajvare ।
śītabhañjī rasaḥ so ayaṃ śītajvaranivāraṇaḥ ।। kūṣmāṇḍacūrṇatilajaiḥ praviśuddhatālaṃ gāḍhaṃ vimardya suṣavīsalilena tulyam । sūtena hiṅgulabhuvā sikatākhyayantre golaṃ vidhāya parivṛttakapālamadhye ।। pattreṇa taṃ dinapateśca pidhāya ruddhvā saṃdhiṃ tayorguḍasudhākhaṭikāśivābhiḥ ।
vahnau pacenmṛduni pātraśiraḥsthaśālīvaivarṇyamātram avadhiṃ pravidhāya dhīmān ।। vallaṃ tataḥ surasamiśramamuṣya dadyāt sarpiḥ sitākaṇapayomadhu cānupeyam । jetuṃ jvarān praviṣamān iha vāntiśāntyai maulau suśītalajalasya dadīta dhārām ।। athāmayāntaṃ rasarājamaulibhūṣāmaṇiṃ taṃ mṛtajīvanākhyam ।
sudhāraseneva rasena yena saṃjīvanaṃ syāt sahasāturāṇām ।। rasahiṅgulajepālair vṛddhyā dantyambumarditaiḥ । dinārdhena jvaraṃ hanyādguñjaikaṃ sitayā saha ।। śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ viṣaṃ gandhaṃ dhūrtabījaṃ tribhiḥ samam ।
caturbhiśca samaṃ vyoṣaṃ cūrṇīkṛtya nidhāpayet ।। dantabhāṇḍe atha vā śārṅge kāṣṭhe naiva kadācana । vātaśleṣmajvare deyaṃ dvaṃdvaje vā tridoṣaje ।। rasena śṛṅgaverasya jambīrasyāthavā punaḥ ।
guñjādvayaṃ ca jīrṇe'smindadhibhaktaṃ prayojayet ।। ekadvitridinairhanyāj jvarān doṣakrameṇa tu । mahājvarāṅkuśo nāma raso'yaṃ śambhunoditaḥ ।। tālaṃ tāmrarajo rasaśca gaganaṃ gandhaśca nepālakaṃ dīnārapramitaṃ tadardhamuditaṃ ṭaṅkaṃ śilāmākṣikam ।
dīnāradvitayaṃ viṣasya śikhinaḥ piṣṭvā rasaiḥ pācito yaścintāmaṇivajjvaraughavijayī nāmnā tu mṛtyuṃjayaḥ ।। tālaṃ tāmram ayorajaśca capalā tutthābhrakaṃ kāntakaṃ nāgaṃ syācca samāṃśakaṃ sumṛditaṃ mūlaṃ ca paunarnavam । bhṛṅgīkāsaharīpunarnavāmahāmandārapattrodbhavaiḥ kalkaṃ vālukayantrapācitam idaṃ sarvajvarasyāntakṛt ।। tutthena tulyaḥ śivajaśca gandho jambīranīreṇa vimardanīyaḥ ।
dinatrayaṃ melaya tena tulyaṃ vyoṣaṃ tataḥ sidhyati candrasūryaḥ ।। vallo vijetuṃ viṣamāvalambi dalena deyo bhujagākhyavallyāḥ । dugdhaṃ hitaṃ syādiha śṛṅgaverarasena śaityeṣu niṣevaṇīyaḥ ।। takraṃ sagarbhājvaraśūlayostu drākṣāmbunā pathyamanantaroktam ।
rodhaṃ varāyāḥ salilena śūlaṃ jambīranīreṇa varājalena ।। apasmṛtāv atra niyojanīyamabhyañjanaṃ bimbapayobhavābhyām । ghṛtaudanaṃ syādiha bhojanāya jambīranīreṇa nihanti gulmam ।। hiṅgvamlikānimburasena deyaṃ plīhodare syādiha takrabhaktaḥ ।
stambhārthamasminsasitaṃ payaḥ syād guḍo niyojyo vamanapraśāntyai ।। aśītir yasya varṣāṇi vasuvarṣāṇi yasya vā । viṣaṃ tasya na dātavyaṃ dattaṃ ced doṣakārakam ।। meghapāradagandhāśmaviṣavyoṣapaṭūni ca ।
jīrakadvayametāni samabhāgāni kārayet ।। sinduvārarasenāpi laśunasya rasena ca । apāmārgarasenāpi saptarātraṃ vimardayet ।। tatpakvaṃ vālukāyantre guñjāmātraṃ prayojayet ।
sanāgavallīmaricaṃ tataḥ śītāmbu pāyayet ।। umāprasādano nāma rasaḥ śītajvarāpahaḥ । cāturthikaṃ trirātraṃ vā nāśayet kimutāparān ।। ṭaṅkaṇaṃ rasagandhau ca samabhāgānprakalpayet ।
nepālaṃ dviguṇaṃ dattvā mardayet khallamadhyataḥ ।। ślakṣṇatāṃ yāti tadyāvattāvattanmardayecchanaiḥ । saindhavaṃ maricaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ciñcākṣāraṃ samākṣikam ।। tattulyam etat kṛtvātha nimbūtoyena mardayet ।
caṇapramāṇavaṭikām bhakṣayeddivasatrayam ।। aikāhikaṃ dvyāhikaṃ ca tryāhikaṃ ca caturthakam । sarvajvaravināśāya jvarāṅkuśa iti smṛtaḥ ।। abhrakaṃ gandhakaṃ sūtaṃ tolakaikaṃ pṛthakpṛthak ।
gṛhītvā viṣatolārdhaṃ tolārdhaṃ tintiḍīphalam ।। etatsarvaṃ samaṃ kṛtvā mardayet khallamadhyataḥ । ślakṣṇatāṃ yāti tadyāvat tāvat saṃmardayecchanaiḥ ।। vistāre pariṇāhe ca gartāṃ kṛtvā ṣaḍaṅgulām ।
phaṇivallīdalānyantargartāyāṃ prakṣipennaraḥ ।। parṇeṣu sūtakalkaṃ taṃ gartāyāṃ sthāpayed dṛḍham । kalkād upari tatparṇair gartāvaktraṃ prapūrayet ।। gartāyāṃ tu tato deyaṃ puṭamāraṇyakotpalaiḥ ।
svāṅgaśītalatāṃ jñātvā samākarṣettataḥ param ।। sūtaliptadalaiḥ sārdhaṃ kalkaṃ khalle vimardayet । tolārdhamamṛtaṃ kṣiptvā tolārdhaṃ tintiḍīphalam ।। sthāpayetkhallitaṃ kalkaṃ yojayed guñjamātrayā ।
śṛṅgaverāmbhasā yuktaṃ tīkṣṇacitrakasaindhavaiḥ ।। saṃnipāte tathā vāte tridoṣe viṣamajvare । agnimāndye grahiṇyāṃ ca tathā deyo'tisāriṇi ।। bhojanaṃ dadhibhaktaṃ ca rase'smin saṃprayojayet ।
vyādhyādikaṃ yathā kuryādudakaṃ ḍhālayet tataḥ ।। eṣa yogavaraḥ śrīmānprāṇināṃ prāṇadāyakaḥ । cintāmaṇiritikhyāto rasaḥ sarvāṅgasundaraḥ ।। sūtendraṃ parimardya pañcapaṭubhiḥ kṣārais tribhis taṃ tataḥ piṇḍe hiṅgumahauṣadhāsurīmaye saṃsvedya dhānyodake ।
nirguṇḍyambuhutāśamanthatilaparṇyunmattabhṛṅgārdrakaṃ kāmātāgirikarṇikāplavadalāpañcāṅgulotthair jalaiḥ ।। sūtendreṇa samair vimardya sahajaiḥ pittaistato bhāvayed daṃṣṭricchāgalulāyamatsyaśikhināṃ sā saṃnipātāñjayet । vikhyātā bhuvi lokanāthaguṭikā mārīcamātrā hitā syādasyāḥ sahitaṃ dadhīkṣuśakalaṃ vīryaṃ bhavecchītalam ।। vajravaikrāntayor bhasma pratyekaṃ niṣkasammitam ।
śṛṅgīviṣaṃ dviniṣkaṃ ca triniṣkaṃ cūlikāpaṭu ।। pañcaniṣko'gnijāraśca sarvamekatra melayet । tāvadbhasma rasaṃ yāvanmardayed divasatrayam ।। śārṅgaṣṭādikavargasya kṣāranīreṇa bhāvayet ।
trayoviṃśativārāṇi vimardya ca viśoṣya ca ।। tato vimardya divasaṃ kṣiped dantakaraṇḍake । mṛtasaṃjīvanākhyo ayaṃ sūcikābharaṇo rasaḥ ।। saṃnipātena tīvreṇa mumurṣor bhūgatasya ca ।
tāluni vṛścayitvātha rasamenaṃ vinikṣipet ।। sūcyātisūkṣmayā toyabhinnayātiprayatnataḥ । tatastailena taṃ liptvā nirvāte saṃniveśayet ।। tato ardhapraharād ūrdhvaṃ muktamūtrapurīṣakam ।
labdhasaṃjñaṃ pratāpāḍhyaṃ dolayantaṃ śiro muhuḥ ।। āyuṣmantaṃ vijānīyādanyathā cānyathā khalu । tataḥ śītāmbusampūrṇe kaṭāhe taṃ niveśayet ।। tatra cotkvathitaṃ toyam apanīyāparaṃ kṣipet ।
yācamānam amuṃ paścāt pāyayet sasitaṃ payaḥ ।। dadhi vā sitayopetaṃ nārikelajalaṃ tathā । rambhāphalāni dadyācca mriyate so anyathā khalu ।। labdhasaṃjñaṃ prabhāṣantaṃ yācamānaṃ phalādikam ।
tasmādākṛṣya tailāktaṃ tailaṃ piṣṭvāpanīya ca ।। lepayedgandhakarpūrair ā pādatalamastakam । ityādiśiśirair dravyaiḥ saptarātram upācaret ।। karṇākṣināsikāvaktre kṣipet potāśrayaṃ muhuḥ ।
aṣṭame ahani samprāpte dardurīmūlajaṃ rasam ।। sasitaṃ pāyayed vegam avatārayituṃ rasam । rase'vatārite paścād yatheṣṭaṃ bhojanaṃ dadhi ।। śvāsocchvāsayutaṃ cānyair muktajīvanalakṣaṇaiḥ ।
kaṭāhe jalasampūrṇe nikṣiped bodhalabdhaye ।। labdhabodhaṃ tamākṛṣya pūrvavat samupācaret । jīvitvā yāvad āyuṣyaṃ mriyate tadanantaram ।। saṃnipāte mahāghore majjantaṃ mṛtyusāgare ।
uddharettasya dharmasya brahmāpyantaṃ na vindati ।। saṃnipātamahāmṛtyubhayanirmuktamānavaḥ । api sarvasvadānena prāṇācāryaṃ prapūjayet ।। anyathā narake tāvad yāvat kalpavikalpanā ।
ityājñā śāṃkarī jñeyā śambhunā parikīrtitā ।। prakāśā naiva kartavyā rasottaraṇamūlikā । śāstraṃ vinā prayacchante mandā vittābhikāṅkṣayā । guruprasādam āsādya saṃnipāte prayujyatām ।।
śārṅgaṣṭā ca tathā vyāghrī karīras tilaparṇikā । indravāruṇikā mustā haridrāṅkolamūlikā ।। apāmārgaḥ kaṇā svarṇaṃ kaṭutumbī ca tintiḍī । śārṅgaṣṭādikavargo ayaṃ saṃnipātaharaḥ param ।।
sūtaṃ gandhakatālakaṃ maṇiśilāṃ tāpyaṃ lavaṃ tutthakaṃ jepālaṃ viṣaṭaṅkaṇaṃ madhuphalaṃ kṛtvā samāṃśaṃ dṛḍham । kṛtvā kajjalikāṃ viṣolbaṇaphaṇeḥ pittaiśca saṃbhāvayet kṣiptvā sīsakakūpike rasavaraṃ sūcīmukhaṃ nāmataḥ ।। brahmadvāri vikīrṇalohitalave guñjaikamātraṃ daded dattvā sampuṭabaddhatandrikadhanurvāte saśākhāhime । kāsaṃ śvāsamarocakaṃ pralapanaṃ kampaṃ ca hikkāturaṃ mūkatvaṃ badhiratvam unmadam apasmāraṃ jayet tatkṣaṇāt ।।
rasagandhakatāmrābhraṃ lāṅgalīvahnirāmaṭham । vandhyāpaṭolanirguṇḍīsugandhānimbapallavāḥ ।। pāṭhākṣāratrayaṃ kṣveḍaboladhattūrataṇḍulaiḥ । śṛṅgīmadhukasāraṃ ca jambīrāmlena mardayet ।।
kuryāddhi niṣkamānena vaṭikā sā niyacchati । sasvedadāhābhinyāsaṃ saṃnipātagajāṃkuśaḥ ।। sasārā vaiṣṇavī senā acalā kādi kaṅkaṇā । rāgarudropamopetā prauḍhā mastakaśālinī ।।
tribhāgaṃ tālakaṃ vidyād ekabhāgaṃ tu pāradam । tadardhaṃ gandhakaṃ caiva tadardhaṃ tu manaḥśilā ।। kāravallīdalarasair mardayet tatpraharatrayam । pācito vālukāyantre cāturthikaharo rasaḥ ।।
syād rasena samāyukto gandhakaḥ sumanoharaḥ । hiyāvallitriguṇito nirguṇḍīrasamarditaḥ ।। saptavārāṇi tad yojyam ārdrakasvarasena tu । saṃtatādijvaraṃ hanyāccāturthikagajāṃkuśaḥ ।।
tāpyatālakajepālavatsanābhamanaḥśilāḥ । tāmragandhakasūtaṃ ca musalīrasamarditaḥ । mṛtyuṃjaya iti khyātaḥ kukkuṭīpuṭapācitaḥ ।। valladvayaṃ prayuñjīta yatheṣṭaṃ dadhibhojanam ।
navajvaraṃ saṃnipātaṃ hanyādeṣa mahārasaḥ ।। śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ viṣaṃ gandhaṃ maricaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ kaṇām । mardayed dhūrtajadrāvair dinam ekaṃ tu śoṣayet ।। pañcavaktro raso nāma dviguñjaḥ saṃnipātajit ।
arkamūlakaṣāyaṃ ca satryūṣam anupāyayet । dadhyodanaṃ hitaṃ tatra jalayogaṃ ca kārayet ।। rasagandhakatulyāṃśaṃ dhattūraphalajadravaiḥ । mardayed dinamekaṃ tu tattulyaṃ trikaṭu kṣipet ।
unmattākhyo raso nāmnā nasye syātsaṃnipātajit ।। nistvagjepālajaṃ bījaṃ daśaniṣkaṃ pracūrṇayet । maricaṃ pippalīṃ sūtaṃ pratiniṣkaṃ vimiśrayet ।। bhāvyaṃ jambīrajairdrāvaiḥ saptāhaṃ tat prayatnataḥ ।
saṃnipātaṃ nihantyāśu añjane yaḥ śivaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। madanaphalaṃ viḍalavaṇaṃ sarṣapāḥ pratiniṣkadvayam । cūrṇayitvā triphalākvāthena saṭaṅkaṇaṃ pibet ।। kuṣṭhe jvare kāmalāyāṃ kaṇṭharoge hy ajīrṇake ।
nasye ca girikarṇyutthabījaikaṃ śītavāriṇā ।। pratyekaṃ rasagandhayor dvipalayoḥ kṛtvā maṣīṃ śuddhayor ramyāṃ mlecchalulāyalocanamanodhātrīprakuñcatrayam । pathyāyā badaratrikaṃ trikaṭu ṣaṭśāṇaṃ vacā dharmiṇī vellāmbhodharapattrakadviradakiñjalkāśvagandhāhvayam ।। piṣṭvaitat samasāram akhilaṃ karṣonmitaṃ nyasya tat pronmardyārdhakarañjakāmṛtayutaṃ sāgastikatryūṣaṇaiḥ ।
bhūdhātrīvijayāsaritpatiphalaṃ jvālāmukhīmārkavaiḥ pratyekaṃ vidadhīta niścalamatiḥ sapta kramādbhāvanāḥ ।। pittairatho pañca vidhāya pañcabhiḥ karañjapattrāmṛtadhūpanaṃ tataḥ । dattvārdrakasya svarasena taṇḍulākṛtiṃ vidadhyādguṭikāṃ bhiṣagvaraḥ ।। deyaikā saṃnipāte pratihataviṣaye mohanetraprasuptyoḥ syādgulme sājamodā pavanavikṛtiṣu tryūṣaṇena grahaṇyām ।
dātavyā jīrakeṇa dvipaturaganṛṇāṃ prāṇasaṃrakṣaṇāya kāyāmbhodhir etaṃ rasakasamarasaṃ vaidyanātho'bhyadhatta ।। gandhakābhrasamaḥ sūto vārāhīrasamarditaḥ । pācito vālukāyantre triphalāvyoṣacitrakaiḥ ।। trikṣāraṃ pañcalavaṇahiṅgugugguludīpyakaiḥ ।
sajīrakaiḥ sendrayavaiḥ pṛthagrasasamairyutaḥ ।। māṣamātro'nupānena dvipalasyoṣṇavāriṇaḥ । abhinyāsānalabhraṃśagrahaṇīpāṇḍugulminām ।। kuryātprāṇaparitrāṇamataḥ prāṇeśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।
vyādhivṛddhau prayogo'sya dvau vārau vaidyasaṃmataḥ ।। rasāyovyoṣakaṅkuṣṭhaśilātālābhrahiṅgulān । kumbhyagnibhṛṅgamārītaṇḍulīyakamākṣikān ।। hastiśuṇḍīyutāṃs tulyāṃs tadardhaśivagandhakān ।
tryaham ārdrāmbunā piṣṭvā kūpīsthaṃ vālukāgninā ।। jayājambīranirguṇḍīcāṅgerīvāri nikṣipet । paktvā caturdaśāhāni piṣṭvārdrāktaṃ viśoṣayet ।। mṛtasaṃjīvanākhyo'yaṃ raso vallamito aśitaḥ ।
drāg jayedauṣadhaṃ saṃnipātādīn sakalān gadān ।। rasabhāgo bhavedeko gandhako dviguṇo mataḥ । viṣatālakakaṅkuṣṭhaśilāhiṅgulalohakam ।। vahnitrikaṭubhṛṅgāhvahemamākṣikamabhrakam ।
hastiśuṇḍī viṣaṃ kumbhī taṇḍulīyakatāmrakau ।। eṣāṃ pratyekamekaikaṃ bhāgamādāya cūrṇayet । ārdrakasya draveṇaiva mardayecca dinatrayam ।। jambīrasya raso grāhyaḥ palatrayaparīkṣitaḥ ।
triphalāyāśca nirguṇḍyāḥ pratyekaṃ ca palatrayam ।। rasasya palamātraṃ tu cāṅgeryāḥ parikīrtitam । kācakūpyāṃ vinikṣipya yantre kṣiptvā prayatnavān ।। uddhṛtyārdrakaniryāsair mardayitvā viśoṣayet ।
mṛtasaṃjīvano nāma raso'yaṃvidito bhuvi । guñjādvayaṃ dadītāsya saṃnipātāpanuttaye ।। vaṅgaṃ nāgaṃ ca sūtaṃ ca nepālaṃ gandhakaṃ tathā । śulbaṃ viṣaṃ samāṃśena rasenārdreṇa mardayet ।।
punar mardyeta nirguṇḍyāś cāṅgeryā rasamarditaḥ । vallaprayogeṇa raso'yaṃ saṃnipātanut ।। gandhakaṃ ca rasaṃ śuddhaṃ pratyekaṃ karṣasammitam । ekatra kajjalīṃ kṛtvā tataḥ kurvīta golakam ।।
navabhāṇḍe vinikṣipya tāmrapātreṇa gopayet । dṛḍhaṃ nirudhya tat pātramagnāvāropayet tataḥ ।। vrīhisphuṭanamātreṇa svāṅgaśītaṃ samuddharet । navajvare prayuñjīta rasaṃ parpaṭikāhvayam ।।
ārdrakasya rasenaiva trivallaṃ tridinaṃ bhiṣak । jvaritaṃ chādayedgāḍhaṃ yāvatsvedaḥ samudbhavet ।। takrabhaktaṃ bhavetpathyaṃ jvaramuktasya dehinaḥ । navajvarārir ityeṣa rasaḥ paramadurlabhaḥ ।
vātajvare viśeṣeṇa rasaḥ sādhāraṇo mataḥ ।। ṭaṅkaṇaṃ rasagandhau ca maricāni samāṃśakam । sarvaṃ jambīranīreṇa dināni trīṇi mardayet ।। saṃśoṣya śarkarāyuktaṃ matsyapittena bhāvayet ।
bhāvitaṃ tadrasaṃ siddhamārdrakasvarasaistryaham ।। vallaṃ vāratrayaṃ deyaṃ pānārthaṃ vāri śītalam । takrabhaktaṃ bhavetpathyaṃ vṛntākaphalasaṃyutam । sarvān navajvarān hanti raso'yaṃ jalamañjarī ।।
kāntasya kaṇṭavedhyānāṃ pātrāṇāṃ bhasma kārayet । tatsamaśca raso gandhaṣṭaṅkaṇo nimbavāriṇā । tataḥ saṃpeṣya tatkalkaṃ mardayettridinaṃ punaḥ ।। rasatulyena matsyasya pittena paribhāvayet ।
siddhaḥ kāntaraso hy eṣa prayojyo abhinavajvare । śṛṅgaverānupānena mātrayā bhiṣaguttamaiḥ ।। rasagandhau tathā vaṅgam abhrakaṃ samabhāgataḥ । melayitvātha vaṅgena samaṃ sūtaṃ vimardayet ।।
tatraikīkṛtya gandhābhre peṣyaṃ jambīravāriṇā । sāmānyaṃ puṭam ādadyāt saptadhā sādhitaṃ rasam ।। kumāryā citrakeṇāpi bhāvayitvātha saptadhā । guḍena jīrakeṇāpi jvare jīrṇe prayojayet ।।
kāse śvāse kumāryā ca triphalākvāthayogataḥ । unmādaṃ ca dhanurvātam amṛtākvāthayogataḥ । ityevaṃ rogatāpaghno rasaś candrodayābhidhaḥ ।। nāgaṃ vaṅgaṃ rasaṃ tāmraṃ gandhakaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ tathā ।
viṣaṃ ca nepālaṃ haritālaṃ samaṃ tathā ।। vaṭakṣīreṇa saṃmardya sarvaṃ kuryāttu golakam । taṃ golakaṃ bhāṇḍamadhye pācayeddīpavahninā ।। taṃ golaṃ śītalaṃ kṛtvā bhṛṅgarājena mardayet ।
ārdrakasya rasenāpi mardayecca punaḥ punaḥ ।। caṇapramāṇavaṭakān rasenārdrasya dāpayet । guñjādvayapramāṇena jvaraṃ jīrṇaṃ haratyasau ।। haraśca gandhakaṃ caiva kunaṭī ca samaṃ samam ।
mardyaṃ karkoṭikāyāśca rasena viniyojayet ।। navajvaramurāriḥ syādvallaṃ śarkarayā saha । taṇḍulīyarasenānupānaṃ śarkarayāpi vā । guñjādvayapramāṇena jvarānhanti navānhaṭhāt ।।
kaṭvamlatīkṣṇalavaṇoṣṇavidāhirūkṣaiḥ pittaṃ praduṣṭam aśanair atisevitais taiḥ । saṃdūṣya raktam amunobhayamārgavarti niryātyasṛksthalayakṛtplihato atimātram ।। pāradaṃ hiṅgulukaṃ ca ūrdhvayantreṇa melayet । kukkuṭāṇḍarasaṃ bhāgaṃ ṭaṅkaṇakṣāram eva ca ।।
gandhakasya tathā bhāgaṃ ghṛtena parimardayet । siddhaṃ rasaṃ samādāya jīratoyena dāpayet ।। dināni trīṇi māṣaṃ ca grahaṇīraktadoṣajit । jvaradāhavināśaṃ ca raktapittavināśanam ।।
pratyekaṃ tolamānena sūtakaṃ tāmrabhasmakam । dināni trīṇi guṭikāṃ kṛtvā cāgnau vinikṣipet ।। tataḥ śuṣkaṃ samādāya punareva ca mardayet । samastaiḥ samagandhaiśca kṛtvā kajjalikāṃ ca taiḥ ।।
mustādāḍimadūrvābhiḥ ketakīstanavāribhiḥ । sahadevyāḥ kumāryāśca parpaṭasyāpi vāriṇā ।। rāmaśītalikātoyaiḥ śatāvaryā rasena ca । bhāvayitvā prayatnena divase divase pṛthak ।।
tiktaṃ guḍūcikāsattvaṃ parpaṭīśīramāgadhīḥ । śṛṅgāṭaṃ sārivā caiṣāṃ samānaṃ sūkṣmacūrṇakam ।। drākṣādikakaṣāyeṇa saptadhā paribhāvayet । tataḥ potāśrayaṃ kṣiptvā vaṭyaḥ kāryāścaṇopamāḥ ।।
ayaṃ candrakalānāmā rasendraḥ parikīrtitaḥ । sarvapittagadadhvaṃsī vātapittagadāpahaḥ ।। antarbāhyamahādāhavidhvaṃsanamahākṣamaḥ । grīṣmakāle śaratkāle viśeṣeṇa praśasyate ।।
kurute nāgnimāndyaṃ ca mahātāpajvaraṃ haret । śramaṃ mūrchāṃ haratyāśu strīṇāṃ raktamahāsravam ।। ūrdhvādho raktapittaṃ ca raktavāntiṃ viśeṣataḥ । mūtrakṛcchrāṇi sarvāṇi nāśayennātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
paṭolamāyasaṃ cūrṇaṃ sūtendraṃ samacāritam । lohārivargasaṃghṛṣṭaṃ raktapittaharaṃ param ।। vṛṣādalānāṃ svarasasya karṣaṃ rasendraguñjāmadhuśarkarāyutam । lihanprabhāte manujo nihanyād duḥkhākaraṃ dāruṇaraktapittam ।।
sapaṭolakahiṅgūlaḥ sakṣaudro raktapittanut ।। navanītaṃ sitā lājā drākṣayā saha bhakṣayet ।। mastake ca ghṛtaṃ dadyādraktapittaharaṃ param ।। drākṣāvāsāyutaṃ kvāthaṃ śarkarābhāvitaṃ pibet ।।
vāsārasaṃ sitākṣaudrairlājānvā śarkarāsamān । bhakṣayan raktapittārtas tṛṣṇādāhajvaraṃ jayet ।। dhātrīcūrṇaṃ sitāyuktaṃ bhakṣayedraktapittanut ।। doṣāḥ śoṣamano'bhitāpakupitāḥ kurvanti kāsaṃ tataḥ pītaṃ pūtikaphaṃ pratīpanayanaḥ pūyopamaṃ ṣṭhīvati ।
śītoṣṇecchur akāraṇena bahubhuk snigdhaprasannānanaḥ pārśvārtyalpabalakṣayākṛtir api prādurbhavatyanyathā ।। sārkatīkṣṇābhrako agastyakāsamardavarārasaiḥ । mardito vetasāmlena piṇḍitaḥ kāsanāśanaḥ ।। tāre piṣṭaśilāṃ kṣiptvā haritālāccaturguṇām ।
vāsāgokṣurasārābhyāṃ mardayet praharadvayam ।। prasvinno vālukāyantre guñjādvitayasaṃmitaḥ । kāsaṃ trikaṭunirguṇḍīmūlacūrṇayuto haret ।। bhūnāgābhrakayoḥ sattvaṃ kāntahemābhrarūpyakam ।
muktāphalāni ratnāni tāpyaṃ vaikrāntameva ca ।। bhasmīkṛtamidaṃ sarvaṃ pṛthaṅ māṣamitaṃ matam । niṣkamātramitaṃ śuddhaṃ rājāvartarajastathā ।। etatsarvaṃ samaṃ yojyaṃ mardayitvāmlavetasaiḥ ।
ruddhvā mūṣodare koṣṭhyāṃ dhamedākāśadarśanam ।। śatavāraṃ dhamedevaṃ mardayitvāmlavetasaiḥ । tataḥ saṃcūrṇite cāsminmuktābhasma dviśāṇakam ।। maricaṃ pañca śāṇeyaṃ kṣiptvā saṃmardya yatnataḥ ।
ramye karaṇḍake kṣiptvā sthāpayet tadanantaram ।। so ayaṃ ratnakaraṇḍako rasavaro madhvājyasaṃkrāmaṇo hanyācchvāsagadaṃ jvaraṃ grahaṇikāṃ kāsaṃ ca hidhmāmayam । śūlaṃ śoṣamahodaraṃ bahuvidhaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ ca hanyād gadān balyo vṛṣyakaraḥ pradīpanatamaḥ svasthocito vegavān ।। śuddhasūtasya bhāgaikaṃ bhāgaikaṃ śuddhagandhakam ।
bhāgatrayaṃ mṛtaṃ tāmraṃ maricaṃ pañcabhāgikam ।। mṛtābhrasya caturbhāgaṃ bhāgamekaṃ viṣaṃ kṣipet । bhūtāṅkuśasya bhāgaikaṃ sarvaṃ cāmlena mardayet ।। yāmaṃ bhūtāṅkuśo nāma māṣaikaṃ vātakāsajit ।
anupānaṃ lihetkṣaudrairvibhītakaphalatvacaḥ । pittakāsāruciśvāsakṣayakāsāṃśca nāśayet ।। rasabhasma viṣaṃ tulyaṃ gandhakaṃ dviguṇaṃ matam । bolatālakavāhlīkakarkoṭīmākṣikaṃ niśā ।।
kaṇṭakārī yavakṣāralāṅgalīkṣārasaindhavam । madhūkasāraṃ saṃcūrṇya saptāhaṃ cārdrakadravaiḥ ।। guṭikāṃ badarākārāṃ śleṣmakāsāpanuttaye । bhakṣayed bolabaddho ayaṃ rasaḥ saśvāsapāṇḍujit ।।
rasagandhakapippalyo harītakyakṣavāsakam । ṣaḍuttaraguṇaṃ cūrṇaṃ babbulakvāthabhāvitam ।। ekaviṃśativārāṇi śoṣayitvā vicūrṇayet । bhakṣayenmadhunā hanti kāsam agniraso hy ayam ।।
trikaṭu triphalā cailā jātīphalalavaṃgakam । eteṣāṃ samabhāgānāṃ samaḥ pūrvaraso bhavet ।। sampūryāloḍayet kṣaudre bhakṣyo niṣkadvayaṃ dvayam । svayam agniraso nāmnā kṣayakāsanikṛntanaḥ ।।
bhṛṅgarājasya pattrāṇi madhunā cūrṇitāni hi । golakaṃ dhārayedvaktre kāsaviṣṭambhaśāntaye ।। arkairaṇḍasya pattrāṇāṃ rasaṃ pītvā ca kāsajit ।। dantīmūlasya dhūmaṃ vā nirguṇḍyā vā pibejjayet ।।
indravāruṇikāmūlaṃ bhṛṅgīkṛṣṇātilaiḥ saha । bhakṣayet kṣayakāsārto niṣkamātraṃ praśāntaye ।। śleṣmoparuddhamanaḥ pavano atiduṣṭaḥ saṃdūṣayannanu jalānnavahāś ca nāḍīḥ । āmāśayodbhavam imaṃ vidadhāty urasthaḥ śvāsaṃ ca vakragamano hi śarīrabhājām ।।
indravāruṇikāmūlaṃ devadāru kaṭutrayam । śarkarāsahitaṃ khāded ūrdhvaśvāsapraśāntaye ।। sūtārdhaṃ gandhakaṃ mardyaṃ yāmaikaṃ kanyakādravaiḥ । dvayoḥ samaṃ tāmrapattraṃ pūrvakalkena melayet ।।
dinaikaṃ haṇḍikāyantre pakvamādāya cūrṇayet । sūryāvartaraso hy eṣa dviguñjaḥ śvāsajit bhavet ।। sūtaḥ ṣoḍaśa tatsamo dinakarastasyārdhabhāgo baliḥ sindhustasya samaḥ susūkṣmamṛditaḥ ṣaṭ pippalī cūrṇitaḥ । jambīrasvarasena marditam idaṃ taptaṃ supakvaṃ bhavet kāsaśvāsasagulmaśūlajaṭharaṃ pāṇḍuṃ lihannāśayet ।।
sādhāraṇaṃ tu vaṭakaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tattvataḥ । pāradaṃ gandhakaṃ caiva palamekaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।। palatrayaṃ trikaṭukaṃ vaṅgam ekapalaṃ kṣipet । sarvam ekatra saṃyojya dināni trīṇi mardayet ।।
gomūtreṇa tathā trīṇi dināni parimardayet । akṣapramāṇavaṭakaṃ chāyāśuṣkaṃ tu kārayet ।। nityamekaṃ tu vaṭakaṃ dināni triṃśadeva ca । śvāsakāsajvaraharam agnimāndyārucipraṇut ।।
rasabhāgo bhavedeko gandhako dviguṇo mataḥ । tribhāgā pippalī grāhyā caturbhāgā harītakī ।। vibhītaḥ pañcabhāgastu vāsā ṣaḍguṇitā bhavet । bhārṅgīsaptaguṇā grāhyā sarvaṃ cūrṇaṃ prakalpayet ।।
babbulakvātham ādāya bhāvayed ekaviṃśatiḥ । vibhītakapramāṇena madhunā guṭikāṃ caret ।। ekaikāṃ bhakṣayetprātarvaṭī saptāmṛtābhidhā । śvāsakāsādikaṃ vyādhiṃ tatkṣaṇānnāśayed iyam ।।
sūtaṃ śulbaṃ sulohaṃ balim amṛtayutaṃ tritrikaṃ reṇukābdaṃ gaṇḍīraṃ kesarāgniṃ dviguṇaguḍayutaṃ mardayitvā samastam । kuryāt kolāsthimātrān suruciravaṭakān bhakṣayet prāgdinādau pathyāsīsarvarogān harati ca nitarāṃ nīlakaṇṭhābhidhānaḥ ।। tāratāmrarasapiṣṭikā śilā gandhatālasamabhāgikaṃ rasaiḥ । āṭarūṣasurasārdrasambhavair mardaya prakuru golakaṃ tataḥ ।।
mṛtsnayā ca pariveṣṭya golakaṃ yāmayugmam atha bhūdhare pacet । gandhakena kuru tatsamaṃ tataś cāṭarūṣakaṭukair vibhāvayet ।। śvāsakāsakarikesarīraso vallayasya parisevayed budhaḥ ।। rasagandhakatāmrābhraṃ kaṇāśuṇṭhyūṣaṇaṃ samam ।
bhūtam ekaṃ viṣaṃ caikaṃ sūryaḥ kāsādināśanaḥ ।। gandhakaṃ maricaṃ sājyaṃ pibecchvāsakaphāpaham । śilā hiṅgu viḍaṅgaṃ ca maricaṃ kuṣṭhasaindhavam । madhvājyābhyāṃ lihet karṣaṃ śvāsakāśakaphāpaham ।।
vidāhiguruviṣṭambhirūkṣābhiṣyandibhojanaiḥ । śītapānāśanasthānarajodhūmātapānilaiḥ । vyāyāmakarmabhārādhvavegāghātāpatarpaṇaiḥ । hikkā śvāsaśca kāsaśca nṛṇāṃ samupajāyate ।
rasagandhakadhānyābhratālatāpyopalaṃ kramāt । bhāgavṛddhaṃ vacākuṣṭhaharidrākṣāracitrakaiḥ ।। sapāṭhā lāṅgalī vyoṣasaindhavākṣaviṣaiḥ samam । bhāvitaṃ bhṛṅganīreṇa hikkāvaisvaryakāsanut ।।
pakvatāmre rasaḥ piṣṭo balinā hidhmināṃ hitaḥ ।। cūrṇaṃ pāṭhendravāruṇyorbhāṇḍe dattvātha kunaṭīm । tatpṛṣṭhe śuddhasūtaṃ ca kunaṭyaṃśaṃ pradāpayet ।। sūtārdhaṃ kunaṭīcūrṇaṃ tasyārdhaṃ pūrvamūlikā ।
cūrṇaṃ dattvā paceccullyā yāmāṣṭa mṛduvahninā । śilāpūto raso nāma hanti hikkāṃ triguñjakaḥ ।। mṛtasūtaṃ mṛtaṃ tāmraṃ hiṅgu puṣkaramūlakam । saindhavaṃ gandhakaṃ tālaṃ kaṭukaṃ cūrṇayet samān ।।
devadālīpunarnavayor nirguṇḍīmeghanādayoḥ । tiktakoṣātakīdrāvair dinaikaṃ mardayed dṛḍham ।। māṣamātraṃ lihet kṣaudraiḥ rasaṃ manthānabhairavam । kapharogapraśāntyarthaṃ nimbakvāthaṃ pibedanu ।।
viśvāditrikanirgatadravaniśā kīrapriyotthaṃ dalaṃ nīlagrīvagalālayaṃ surapates tārtīyanetrābhidham । vidvatpuñjavatī kṛmipratibhaṭaṃ nirguṇḍikāvāriṇā tulyāṃśāś caṇakapramāṇavaṭikāḥ saśvāsakāsaghnikāḥ ।। kvāthaṃ rāsnābṛhatyagnibalādugdhaiś ca pāyayet ।। hikvinaṃ pāyayed dhūmaṃ pattraiḥ śikhiniśodbhavaiḥ ।।
karṣaikaṃ gandhakaṃ śuddhaṃ ghṛtaiś coṣṇodakaiḥ pibet । kaphaṃ hantyatha vā kṣaudraiḥ pañcavaktrarasaḥ khalu ।। atyuccabhāṣaṇaviṣādhyayanābhighātasaṃdūṣaṇaiḥ prakupitāḥ pavanādayas tu । srotaḥsu te svaravaheṣu gatāḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ hanyuḥ svaraṃ bhavati cāpi hi ṣaḍvidhaḥ saḥ ।।
rasaṃ dviguṇagandhena mardayitvā sabhṛṅgakam । lohapātre ghṛtābhyakte drāvitaṃ badarāgninā ।। ūrdhvādho gomayaṃ dattvā kadalyāḥ komale dale । snigdhayā lohadarvyā ca parpaṭākāratāṃ nayet ।।
lohapātre vinikṣiptā lohaparpaṭikā bhavet । tāmrapātre vinikṣiptā tāmraparpaṭikā bhavet ।। parpaṭīrasamāha rasaṃ dviguṇeti ।। sabhṛṅgakaṃ bhṛṅgarājarasena mardayitvā taptaṃ drāvitaṃ tadgomayoparisthe kadale snigdhayā lohadarvyā prakṣipya tadupari kadalīdale nyubje gomayaṃ dattvā karatalādinā nipīḍya parpaṭākāraṃ kuryāt ।।
kadalīdalasthāne snigdhe lohapatre vinikṣiptā cellohaparpaṭikā bhavet ।। athavā tāmrapatre snigdhe vinikṣiptā tāmraparpaṭikā bhavet ।। rasopari tu kadalīdalādyeva deyam ।। viṣapādaṃ ca yuñjīta tatsādhyeṣvāmayeṣu ca ।
surasāyā jayantyāś ca kanyakāṭarūṣakayoḥ ।। triphalāyā muner bhārṅgyā muṇḍyās trikaṭucitrayoḥ । bhṛṅgarājasya vahneśca pratyahaṃ dravabhāvitam ।। ārdrakasya rasenāpi saptadhā bhāvayetpunaḥ ।
aṅgāraiḥ svedayed īṣat parpaṭarasam uttamam ।। guñjāṣṭakaṃ dadītāsya tāmbūlīpattrasaṃyutam । pippalīdaśakaiḥ kvāthaṃ nirguṇḍyāś cānupāyayet । svarabhaṅge kaphe śvāse prayojyaḥ sarvadā rasaḥ ।।
trikaṇṭakasya mūlāni śuṇṭhīṃ saṃkṣudya nikṣipet । ajākṣīre sanīrārdhaṃ yāvatkṣīraṃ vipācayet ।। tatkṣīraṃ pāyayedrātrau sakaṇaṃ bhojane api ca । kūṣmāṇḍaṃ varjayecciñcāṃ vṛntākaṃ karkaṭīm api ।।
āranālaṃ ca tailaṃ ca saṃsargaṃ ca vivarjayet । māsatrayaṃ ca seveta kāsaśvāsanivṛttaye ।। sajīrahiṅgukavyoṣaiḥ śamayed grahaṇīṃ rasaḥ । daśamūlāmbhasā vātajvaraṃ trikaṭunā kapham ।।
jvaraṃ madhukasāreṇa pañcakolena sarvajam । yakṣmāṇaṃ madhupippalyā gomūtreṇa gudāṅkurān ।। śūlam eraṇḍatailena pāṇḍuśophaṃ sagugguluḥ । kuṣṭhāni bhṛṅgabhallātavākucī pañcanimbakaiḥ ।।
dhattūrabījasaṃyogānmehonmādavināśinī । apasmāraṃ nihantyāśu vyoṣanimbudalaiḥ saha ।। stanaṃdhayaśiśūnāṃ tu raso'yaṃ nitarāṃ hitaḥ । pathyākṣacūrṇādivaśād vyādhīṃś cānyān sudustarān ।।
sajātīphalaśītodaṃ yojayetparpaṭīrasam । pittājīrṇe śiraś cāsya śītatoyena secayet ।। nasyaṃ niṣṭhīvanaṃ dhūmaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ vamanarecanam । annaṃ rūkṣālpatīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ kaṭutiktakaṣāyakam ।
cirakālasthitaṃ madyaṃ yojayetkapharogiṇe ।। agnimāndyaṃ jvaraḥ śaityaṃ vāntiḥ śoṇitapūyayoḥ । sattvahāniśca daurbalyaṃ rājarogasya lakṣaṇam ।। rasasya tulyabhāgena hemabhasma prakalpayet ।
tālakaṃ gandhakaṃ tutthaṃ mākṣikaṃ rasakaṃ śilām ।। rasasāmyena yuñjīta tutthaṃ bhasmīkṛtaṃ nyaset । vahnau bhasmīkṛtaṃ cetthaṃ mayūrakasututthakam ।। kiṃciṭ ṭaṅkaṇakaṃ dattvā mārjārasya viśā yutam ।
prathamaṃ puṭayed dadhnā dvitīyaṃ madhunā saha ।। tālakaṃ śodhayedagre kūṣmāṇḍakṣārapācanāt । taile pacettataḥ samyak cūrṇe vā pariśodhayet ।। gandhakaṃ śodhayeddugdhe rasakaṃ naravāriṇā ।
mākṣikaṃ sindhusaṃyuktaṃ bījapūrarase pacet ।। jayantīdravasampiṣṭāṃ śilāṃ tatraiva pācayet । ekīkṛtya tataḥ sarvam arkakṣīreṇa mardayet ।। jayantībhṛṅgarājābhyāṃ vāsāpāṭhākṛśānubhiḥ ।
agastilāṅgalībhyāṃ ca pratyekaṃ divasaṃ śanaiḥ ।। tatastu golakaṃ baddhvā pacetpūrvavadāhṛtaḥ । cūrṇayitvā tataḥ samyag bhāvayedārdrakāmbunā ।। saptadhā vyoṣaniryāsai rasaḥ kanakasundaraḥ ।
guñjādvayaṃ trayaṃ vāsya rājayakṣmāpanuttaye ।। madhunā pippalībhiśca maricairvā ghṛtānvitaiḥ । lehayedrogiṇaṃ vaidyo balāvasthāviśeṣavit ।। jayapālarajobhirvā śuṇṭhyā gavyaghṛtāktayā ।
dadīta śūline prājño gulmine ca viśeṣataḥ ।। kādivarjyaṃ caretpathyaṃ hṛdyaṃ balyaṃ ca pūrvavat । sannipāte dadītainamārdrakadravasaṃyutam । guḍūcītriphalākvāthaiḥ saṃskṛto guggulurvaraḥ ।।
rasabhasma trayo bhāgā bhāgaikaṃ hemabhasmakam । mṛtatāmrasya bhāgaikaṃ śilāgandhakatālakam ।। pratibhāgadvayaṃ śuddhamekīkṛtya vicūrṇayet । varāṭānpūrayettena ajākṣīreṇa ṭaṅkaṇam ।।
piṣṭvā tena mukhaṃ ruddhvā mṛdbhāṇḍe tannirodhayet । śuddhaṃ gajapuṭe pacyāccūrṇayetsvāṅgaśītalam ।। raso rājamṛgāṅko'yaṃ caturguñjaḥ kṣayāpahaḥ । daśapippalikākṣaudrairmaricaikonaviṃśatiḥ ।
saghṛtairdāpayedvaidyo rogarājapraśāntaye ।। śaṅkhasya valayānniṣkaṃ caturniṣkaṃ varāṭakam । niṣkārdhaṃ nīlatutthasya sarvatulyaṃ tu gandhakam ।। gandhatulyaṃ mṛtaṃ nāgaṃ nāgatulyaṃ mṛtaṃ rasam ।
ṭaṅkaṇaṃ rasatulyaṃ syānmardyaṃ pācyaṃ mṛgāṅkavat । rājayakṣmaharaḥ so'yaṃ nāmnā śaṅkheśvaro mataḥ ।। śaṅkhanābhiṃ gavāṃ kṣīraiḥ peṣayenniṣkaṣoḍaśa । tena mūṣā prakartavyā tanmadhye bhasmasūtakam ।।
niṣkārdhaṃ gandhakāttrīṇi cūrṇīkṛtya vinikṣipet । ruddhvā tadveṣṭayedvastre mṛttikāṃ lepayedbahiḥ ।। śoṣyaṃ gajapuṭe pacyānmūṣayā saha cūrṇayet । guñjaikamanupānena kṣayaṃ hanti mṛgāṅkavat ।।
dviniṣkaṃ bhasma sūtasya niṣkaikaṃ svarṇabhasmakam । śuddhagandhakaniṣkau dvau cūrṇayitvā citrakadravaiḥ ।। dviyāmānte viśoṣyātha tena pūryā varāṭikāḥ । varāṭānmṛṇmaye bhāṇḍe ruddhvā gajapuṭe pacet ।।
svāṅgaśītaṃ vicūrṇyātha poṭalīṃ hemagarbhitām । mṛgāṅkavaccaturguñjaṃ bhakṣitaṃ rājayakṣmanut ।। svayamagnirasaṃ khādettriniṣkaṃ rājayakṣmanut ।। bhasmasūtābhralohānāṃ śilājatuviṣaṃ samam ।
guḍūcītriphalākvāthaiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ gugguluṃ tathā ।। mṛtaṃ nepālatāmraṃ ca sūtasthāne niyojayet । ekīkṛtya dviguñjaṃ tadbhakṣayedrājayakṣmanut ।। pañcāmṛtaraso nāma hyanupānaṃ ca pūrvavat ।।
haretkṣīrājagandhābhyāṃ jayantī vā kṣayāpahā ।। tulyaṃ pāradagandhakaṃ trikaṭukaṃ tābhyāṃ rajaḥ kambujaṃ taistulyaṃ ca bhavetkapardabhasitaṃ syātpāradāṭṭaṅkaṇam । pādāṃśaṃ sakalaiḥ samānamaricaṃ lihyātkramātsājyakaṃ yāvanniṣkamitaṃ bhavetpratidinaṃ māsātkṣayaḥ śāmyati ।। rasasya bhasmanā hema pādāṃśena prakalpayet ।
gandhakaṃ dviguṇaṃ dattvā mardayeccitrakāmbunā ।। carācarāsye sampūrya ṭaṅkaṇena nirudhya ca । bhāṇḍe cūrṇapralipte'tha kṣiptvā rundhīta mṛtsnayā ।। śoṣayitvā puṭedgarte'ratnimātre aparāhṇake ।
svāṅgaśītalam uddhṛtya cūrṇayitvātha vinyaset ।। eṣa lokeśvaro nāma puṣṭivīryavivardhanaḥ । guñjācatuṣṭayaṃ sājyaṃ maricaiśca samanvitam ।। khādetparamayā bhaktyā lokeśe sarvadarśinī ।
aṅgakārśye'gnimāndye ca raso'yaṃ kāsahikkayoḥ ।। marīcairghṛtasaṃyuktaiḥ pradātavyo dinatrayam । lavaṇaṃ varjayettatra sājyaṃ sadadhi bhojanam ।। ekaviṃśaddinaṃ yāvanmaricaṃ saghṛtaṃ pibet ।
pathyaṃ mṛgāṅkavaddeyaṃ śayītottānapādataḥ ।। vamane sampravṛtte tu guḍūcīdravamāharet । madhunā pāyayetsārdhaṃ dagdhavṛntākamāśayet ।। snānaṃ śītalatoyena mūrdhni dhārāṃ vinikṣipet ।
jāte śleṣmavikāre tu kadalīphalamāharet ।। bhṛṣṭvā tanmaricaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhojayecchleṣmanuttaye । ārdrakaṃ madhumiśraṃ vā guḍārdrakamatho'pi vā ।। bhṛṣṭvā kustumbarīmāṣānnistuṣāṃścūrṇayettataḥ ।
śarkarāghṛtasammiśrāndadītāruciśāntaye ।। bhṛṣṭvā kustumbarīṃ samyag ghṛte śarkarayā pibet । elāṃ maricasaṃyuktāṃ yāvad vāntiḥ praśāmyati ।। ajamodaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ ca piṣṭvā takreṇa pāyayet ।
kṛmikopapraśāntyarthaṃ kvāthaṃ vātaghnamustayoḥ ।। saṃskṛtya dugdhikāṃ vahnau vireke ca prayojayet । īṣadbhṛṣṭvā jayācūrṇaṃ madhunā khādayenniśi ।। aṅgatode ghṛtenāṅgaṃ mardayitvoṣṇavāriṇā ।
snāpayedrogiṇaṃ vaidyo lokanāthaṃ rasaṃ smaran ।। śaṃkhasya valayaṃ niṣkaṃ caturniṣkaṃ varāṭikāḥ । karṣāṃśaṃ nīlatutthaṃ ca tālaṃ gandhāśmaṭaṅkaṇam ।। tutthaṃ nāgarasaṃ cārdhaṃ niṣkāṃśaṃ pūrvavatpuṭet ।
varāṭacūrṇaṃ maṇḍūrakalpitālepane pacet ।। asyārdhamāṣaṃ maricārdhamāṣaṃ tāmbūlavallīrasabhāvitaṃ ca । tatpatraliptaṃ madhunāvalihyāddhaiyaṅgavīnena ghṛtena vāpi ।। nāḍīmārge nirgate cālpamalpaṃ pathyaṃ bhojyaṃ lokanāthopadiṣṭam ।
yāme yāme caivam ā maṇḍalāntāt siddhaṃ sadyaḥ śoṣajidvaidyanāthaḥ ।। adhyardhaniṣkau rasatutthabhāgau pṛthakpṛthaggandhakaṭaṅkakarṣam । śaṃkhasya karṣaṃ mṛtatāmrato dvau varāṭikānāṃ nava sampuṭasthān ।। paktvā pacedarkadaladravārdrān bhūyo ardhabhāgena karīṣakāṇām ।
asyārdhapādaṃ maricārdhabhāgaṃ gandhāśmaniṣkaṃ ca ghṛtena lihyāt ।। aśnīyātpūrvavatpathyaṃ vāsarāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ । lokanātharaso nāmnā rogarājanikṛntanaḥ ।। ayorajo viṃśatiniṣkamānaṃ vibhāvitaṃ bhṛṅgarasāḍhakena ।
dhattūrabhārṅgitriphalārasārdraṃ tulyāṃśatāpyaṃ vipacetpuṭeṣu ।। sūtaṃ ca niṣkaṃ samabhāgatutthaṃ gandhopalau dvau caturo varāṭān । paktvā puṭāgnau samalohacūrṇānpacettathā pūrvarasairvimiśrān ।। cūrṇe'sminmaricāḥ sapta tutthaṭaṅkaṇayordaśa ।
saṃsṛjet tat pṛthaṅniṣkān prāṇanāthāhvayoditaḥ ।। ardhapādo rasādbhakṣyaḥ kevalādrājayakṣmibhiḥ । śoṣodarārśograhaṇījvaragulmādyupadrutaiḥ ।। karṣaṃ kharparasattvasya ṣaṇmāse hemni vidrute ।
ṣaṇniṣkasūtaṃ gandhāśmanyaṣṭaniṣke praveśitam ।। pravālamuktāphalayoścūrṇaṃ hemasamāṃśayoḥ । kramāddvitricaturniṣkaṃ mṛtāyaḥ sīsabhāskaram ।। cāṅgeryamlena yāmāṃstrīnmarditaṃ cūrṇitaṃ pṛthak ।
dvau niṣkau nīlavaṭakavyomāyaskāntatālakāt ।। aṅkollakaṅguṇībījatutthebhyaś caturaḥ pṛthak । aṣṭau ca ṭaṃkaṇakṣārādvarāṭānāṃ ca viṃśatiḥ ।। mahājambīranīrasya prasthadvandvena peṣayet ।
etadaṣṭaśarāvasthaṃ śuddhaṃ khāryāstuṣasya ca ।। karīṣabhāre ca pacedatha māṣadvayaṃ tataḥ । etāvadgandhakātpādaṃ maricādbhāvitādapi ।। madhunāloḍitaṃ lihyāttāmbūlīpatralepitam ।
gate'sya ghaṭikāmātre pratiyāmaṃ ca pathyabhuk ।। no ceduddīpito vahniḥ kṣaṇāddhātūnpacatyataḥ । dinamekaṃ niṣevyainaṃ tyājyānyāmaṇḍalaṃ tyajet ।। tataḥ paraṃ yatheṣṭāśī dvādaśābdaṃ sukhī bhavet ।
ekamekaṃ dinaṃ bhuktvā varṣe varṣe mahārasam ।। varṣādau ca tyajettyājyaṃ dvādaśābdaṃ jarāṃ jayet । eṣa vajraraso nāma kṣayaparvatabhedanaḥ ।। niṣkau dvau tutthabhāgasya rasād ekaṃ susaṃskṛtāt ।
niṣkaṃ viṣasya dvau tīkṣṇātkarṣāṃśaṃ gandhamauktikāt ।। agniparṇīharilatābhṛṅgārdrasurasārasaiḥ । marditaṃ lāṅgalīkandapralipte sampuṭe pacet ।। ardhapādaṃ ca poṭalyāḥ kākinyau dve viṣasya ca ।
lihenmaricacūrṇaṃ ca madhunā poṭalīsamam ।। kṣayagrahaṇyatīsāravahnidaurbalyakāsinām । pāṇḍugulmavatāṃ śreṣṭho mahāvīro hito rasaḥ ।। atisthūlasya pūyāsṛkkaphānudvamatākṣaye ।
na yojayetkṣīrarasānviruddhakramatattvataḥ ।। mātuluṅgasya mūlāni lājacūrṇaṃ sasaindhavam । pippalīmadhunā yuktaṃ khādedvāntipraśāntaye ।। rajanīśaṅkhapūgaṃ ca niṣkaikaṃ vāntināśanam ।
niṣkārdhaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ vātha kākamācīdravaiḥ pibet ।। sugandhāṃ vā pibetkhādet sarvavāntipraśāntaye । alaktakarasaṃ kṣaudrai raktavāntiharaṃ param ।। yuktaṃ gandhakapiṣṭyāyastālakaṃ svarṇamākṣikam ।
yuktyā tadbhasmatāṃ nītaṃ tṛṣṇāchardinivāraṇam ।। rājāvarto rasaḥ śulbaṃ mākṣikaṃ ghṛtapācitam । madhvājyaśarkarāyuktaṃ hanti sarvānmadātyayān ।। rājāvartarasaḥ śulbaṃ sūtagarbhe niyojitam ।
yaṣṭīmadhurasairghṛṣṭaṃ ghṛtamadhye vipācitam ।। madhvājyaśarkarāyuktaṃ hanti sarvānmadātyayān ।। suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ sattvābhraṃ kāntalohakam । kramavṛddhamidaṃ sarvaṃ śāṇeyau nāgavaṅgakau ।।
drāvayitvaikataḥ sarvaṃ retayitvā tataścaret । pṛthakpalamitaṃ gandhaṃ śilālaṃ vinidhāya ca ।। sarvaṃ khalle vinikṣipya mardayed amlavargataḥ । tāpyaṃ nīlāñjanaṃ tālaṃ śilāgandhaṃ ca cūrṇitam ।।
dattvā dattvā puṭettāvadyāvadviṃśativārakam । lohād dviguṇasūtena tato dviguṇagandhataḥ ।। vidhāya kajjalīṃ ślakṣṇāṃ kṣiptvā tāṃ lohapātrake । drāvayed badarāṅgārair mṛdubhiścātha nikṣipet ।।
hemādipañcalohānāṃ bhasma cātha viloḍayet । atha tatkadalīpatre gomayasthe vinikṣipet ।। patreṇānyena saṃchādya kuryādyatnena cippiṭīm । tasyopari kṣipetsadyo gomayaṃ stokameva ca ।।
svataḥ śītaṃ samāhṛtya paṭacūrṇaṃ vidhāya ca । nikṣipedūrdhvadaṇḍāyāṃ pālikāyāṃ tataḥ param ।। pūrvavadbadarāṅgārair mṛdubhir drāvayecchanaiḥ । tulyālakaśilāgandhaṃ palārdhaṃ viṣabhāvitam ।।
pūrvaparpaṭikātulyaṃ tasmādalpaṃ muhurmuhuḥ । jārayetpalikāmadhye yathā dahyenna parpaṭī ।। paliketi vinirdiṣṭā snehakṣepaṇayantrikā । jīrṇe tālādike cūrṇe paṭacūrṇaṃ vidhīyatām ।।
pūtīkarañjaṣaṭkolavyāghrīsaubhāñjanāṅghribhiḥ । etaiḥ pañcapalaiḥ kvāthaṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśāvaśeṣitam ।। tena kvāthena saṃsvedya śoṣayetsaptadhā hi tām । viṣatinduphalodbhūtai rasairnirguṇḍikārasaiḥ ।।
vibhāvya palikāmadhye kṣiptvā badaravahninā । īṣatprasvedanaṃ kṛtvā sthāpayedatiyatnataḥ ।। uktā bhairavanāthena syāt pañcāmṛtaparpaṭī । vyoṣājyasahitā līḍhā guñjābījena saṃmitā ।।
sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇaṃ vinihanti kṣayāmayam । śvāsaṃ kāsaṃ viṣūcīṃ ca pramehamudarāmayam ।। arocakaṃ ca duḥsādhyaṃ prasekaṃ chardihṛdbhavam । sarvajaṃ gudarogaṃ ca śūlakuṣṭhānyaśeṣataḥ ।।
vātajvaraṃ ca viḍbandhaṃ grahaṇīṃ kaphajāngadān । ekadvandvatridoṣotthān rogān anyān mahāgadān ।। agnimāndyaṃ viśeṣeṇa hantīyaṃ parpaṭī dhruvam । evaṃ samūhya dātavyā rogeṣu bhiṣaguttamaiḥ ।।
tattadrogaharair yogais tattadrogānupānataḥ । kṣayādisarvarogaghnī syāt pañcāmṛtaparpaṭī ।। tilasarṣapabilvāmlakāravellakusumbhakam । tyajetpārāvataṃ māṃsaṃ vṛntākaṃ kukkuṭaṃ tathā ।।
gudasya bahirantarvā jāyante carmakīlakāḥ । sarvarogakarāḥ puṃsāmarśāṃsīti hi viśrutāḥ ।। rudhirasrāviṇasteṣāṃ pittajāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। vātajā niḥsahotthānā udāvartaṃ prakurvate ।।
śvayathuṃ śleṣmajāḥ kuryuḥ sarvaṃ kuryustridoṣajāḥ ।। śuddhasūtaṃ palaikaṃ tu dvipalaṃ śuddhagandhakam । mṛtaṃ tāmraṃ mṛtaṃ lohaṃ pratyekaṃ tu palatrayam ।। tryūṣaṇaṃ lāṅgalī dantī pirukaṃ citrakaṃ tathā ।
pratyekaṃ dvipalaṃ yojyaṃ yavakṣāraṃ ca ṭaṅkaṇam ।। ubhau pañcapalau yojyau saindhavaṃ palapañcakam । dvātriṃśatpalagomūtraṃ snuhīkṣīraṃ ca tatsamam ।। mṛdvagninā pacetsthālyāṃ sarvaṃ yāvatsupiṇḍitam ।
māṣadvayaṃ sadā khāded raso hyarśaḥkuṭhārakaḥ । takreṇa dāḍimāmbhobhiḥ pakvakandena vātha tat ।। mṛtasūtārkahemābhratīkṣṇamuṇḍaṃ sagandhakam । maṇḍūraṃ mākṣikaṃ tulyaṃ mardyaṃ kanyādravairdinam ।।
andhamūṣāgataṃ pācyaṃ tridinaṃ tuṣavahninā । cūrṇitaṃ sitayā māṣaṃ khādetpittārśasāṃ jayet ।। śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ palaṃ gandhaṃ gandhārdhaṃ tālatāpyakam । amṛtaṃ rasakaṃ caiva tālakārdhavibhāgikam ।।
eteṣāṃ kajjalīṃ kuryād dṛḍhaṃ saṃmardya vāsaram । tridinaṃ mardayeccātha dattvā nimbujalaṃ khalu ।। vaṭīkṛtya viśoṣyātha kācakupyāṃ nidhāpayet । niṣkatulyārkapatreṇa pidhāyāsyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।।
sārdhāṃgulamitotsedhaṃ mṛtsnayā tāṃ vilepya ca । nato bhāṇḍatṛtīyāṃśe sikatāparipūrite ।। nidhāya sikatāmūrdhni sikatābhiḥ prapūrayet । ruddhvāsyaṃ tadadho vahniṃ jvālayetsārdhavāsaram ।।
svāṃgaśītalitaṃ kācaghaṭādākṛṣya taṃ rasam । paṭacūrṇaṃ vidhāyātha tāmramabhraṃ paladvayam ।। palārdhamamṛtaṃ caiva maricaṃ ca catuṣpalam । ekīkṛtya kṣipetsarvaṃ nārikelakaraṇḍake ।।
sājyo guñjādvimāno harati rasavaraḥ sarvalokāśrayo'yaṃ vātaśleṣmottharogāngudajanitagadaṃ śoṣapāṇḍvāmayaṃ ca । yakṣmāṇaṃ vātaśūlaṃ jvaramapi nikhilaṃ vahnimāndyaṃ ca gulmaṃ tattadrogaghnayogaiḥ sakalagadacayaṃ dīpanaṃ tatkṣaṇena ।। arśoghnaṃ vaṭakaṃ vakṣye putrakaṃ śṛṇu bhadraka । pippalī pippalīmūlavanasūraṇacitrakam ।।
māricaṃ kaṇṭakārī ca raktapuṣpī samāṃśakā । palamekaṃ pṛthak sarvaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ dṛṣadi peṣayet ।। gajājapaśumūtreṣu śubhe bhāṇḍe vinikṣipet । mṛdvagninā pacetsarvaṃ cūrṇaśeṣaṃ yathā bhavet ।।
loṇatrayaṃ ca tatraiva palamekaṃ tu nikṣipet । akṣapramāṇavaṭakānkuryādevaṃ pṛthakpṛthak ।। triṃśaddināni matimānarśoghnaṃ dīpanaṃ param । ghṛtatakrasamāyuktaṃ bhojanaṃ saṃpradāpayet ।।
gandhakaṃ tāratāmraṃ ca kṛtvā caikatra piṣṭikām । tatsamaṃ cābhrakaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ gandhakātpañcamāṃśakam ।। viṣaṃ ca ṣoḍaśāṃśena dvau bhāgau sūtakasya ca । ekīkṛtya prayatnena jambīradravamarditam ।।
bhājane mṛṇmaye sthāpya varākvāthena bhāvayet । daśamūlaśatāvaryoḥ kvāthe pācyaḥ krameṇa hi ।। athottārya prayatnena vaṭikāṃ kārayed budhaḥ । guñjātrayapramāṇena hanti śūlaṃ gudāṅkuram ।।
varanāgaṃ tathā vyomasattvaṃ śulbaṃ ca tīkṣṇakam । sarvamekatra vidrāvya kṣiptvālaṃ cālpamalpakam ।। cālayedaniśaṃ yāvattālakaṃ triguṇaṃ khalu । tatastena vimardyātha piṣṭīṃ kuryādrasena tu ।।
tato bhallātakīvṛkṣamūlāntasthāṃ khanecca tām । māsādākṛṣya tāṃ piṣṭīṃ gavyadugdhe vinikṣipet ।। tato bhallātakītailaṃ hṛtaṃ pātālayantrataḥ । āyase bhājane snigdhe piṣṭikāṃ tāṃ niveśya ca ।।
prasthamātraṃ hi tattailaṃ jārayed atiyatnataḥ । tattailabhāvitairgandhaiḥ puṭitvā bhasmatāṃ vrajet ।। tataḥ kārtikamāsotthakoraṃṭadalajai rasaiḥ । rasaṃ saṃmardya saṃmardya gharme saṃsthāpya mārayet ।।
tadbhasma melayetpūrvabhasmanā samabhāgikam । vanasūraṇanirguṇḍīmahārāṣṭrībhakaṇṭikā ।। vajravallī śikhī caiṣāṃ rasaiḥ piṣṭvā viśoṣayet । trivāraṃ mārkavadrāvairdrāvayitvā viśoṣayet ।
cūrṇīkṛtya prayatnena kṣipetkācakaraṇḍake ।। so'yaṃ mūlakuṭhārako rasavaro dīpyāgnivellottamāsaṃyuktaḥ saghṛtaśca vallatulitaḥ saṃsevito nāśayet । arśāṃsyānananāsikākṣigudajānyatyugrapīḍāni ca plīhānaṃ grahaṇīṃ ca gulmayakṛtau māndyaṃ ca kuṣṭhāmayān ।। rasagrastasamudgīrṇagandhakasya palatrayam ।
mṛtasūtābhratāmrāyaḥ karṣaṃ karṣaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।। palaṃ hiṅgulacūrṇasya mākṣikasya palatrayam । palaṃ kampillakasyāpi viṣasyārdhapalaṃ tathā ।। saptāhaṃ mardayetsarvaṃ dattvā cūrṇodakaṃ muhuḥ ।
tatastadgolakaṃ kṛtvā saptāhaṃ cātape kṣipet ।। guḍacūrṇaṃ śilācūrṇaṃ limpedaṅgulikāghanam । tripalaṃ gandhakaṃ dattvā krauñcyām atha ca golakam ।। golakasyopariṣṭācca kṣipettālapalatrayam ।
saṃrudhyātiprayatnena dadyādgajapuṭaṃ khalu ।। svāṅgaśītalamāhṛtya golakaṃ lepanaiḥ saha । vicūrṇya saptavāraṃ hi viṣatinduphalodbhavaiḥ ।। dravairathātape śuṣkaṃ kṣipedramye karaṇḍake ।
triṃśadaṃśena vaikrāntabhasma tasminvinikṣipet ।। ayaṃ hi nandīśvarasampradiṣṭo raso viśiṣṭaḥ khalu rogahantā । niḥśeṣarogeṣvahatapratāpo mahodayapratyayasāranāmā ।। hanyātsarvagudāmayānkṣayagadaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ ca mandāgnitāṃ śūlādhmānagadaṃ kaphaṃ śvasanatām unmādakāpasmṛtī ।
sarvā vātarujo mahājvaragadān nānāprakārāṃstathā vātaśleṣmabhavaṃ mahāmayacayaṃ duṣṭagrahaṇyāmayam ।। syādrasaṃ dhautamākṣīkaṃ kāntābhraṃ nāgahāṭakam । pṛthvībhaṭena saṃtulyaṃ sarvatulyaṃ ca gandhakam ।। dattvā vidyādhare yantre puṭedāraṇyakotpalaiḥ ।
svāṅgaśītalam uddhṛtya tryūṣaṇena vimiśrayet ।। arśovyādhau kaṭīśūle cakṣuḥśūle ca dāruṇe । sannipāte kṣaye kāse śvāse mandānale jvare ।। karṇaśūle śiraḥśūle dantaśūle prayojayet ।
pīnase plīhni hṛcchūle granthivāte ca dāruṇe ।। ekāṅge vā dhanurvāte kampavāte ca mūrchite । jvarāṃśca viṣamān sarvānhanti rogānanekadhā ।। sevitaḥ pathyayogena rasaḥ kanakasundaraḥ ।
guñjāmātraṃ dadītāsya yathāyuktānupānataḥ ।। ghṛtena saṃyuto vāte madhunā paittike jvare । pippalyā ślaiṣmike deyaḥ pittodbhūte sacandanaḥ ।। takreṇa śleṣmavātotthe vātapitte ghṛtānvitaḥ ।
śleṣmapitte cārdrakeṇa nirguṇḍyā sānnipātike ।। phalatrayeṇa śūleṣu viṣameṣu jvareṣvapi । ārdrakeṇātha vā dadyādvahnimāndye viśeṣataḥ ।। abhiṣyande śiraḥśūle gāyatrībolasaṃyutam ।
pakṣimāṃsasamāyuktaṃ kaphavāte ca mūrchite ।। ekāṅge ca dhanurvāte kṣīrayuktaṃ ca pīnase । pāṇḍuroge kṣaye kāse maricājyaiśca kāmale ।। ajamodāviḍaṅgaiśca nābhiśūle'gnimāndyajit ।
rūkṣajvare'rucau deyaḥ kadalīphalasaṃyutaḥ । bolenārdhakaṭīśūle bhāṣitaṃ nāgabodhinā ।। nāgaṃ pāradagandhakaṃ trilavaṇaṃ vāyarkajaṃ melayed ekaikaṃ ca palaṃ palaṃ trayamataḥ pañca kramānmardayet । sarvaṃ taddivasatrayaṃ tadanu taddattvā puṭaṃ bhāvanāḥ kuryātsatriphalāgnivetasarasaiḥ pañcādhikā viṃśatiḥ ।।
pañcaitat kramaśastato guḍabhavair datto'sya vallo jalair hantyarśāṃsyakhilāni sūraṇaghṛtaistasyānnam asminhitam । arkeśaḥ parivarjyatāmiti muniḥ śrīvāsudevo'vadat kūṣmāṇḍīphalamāṣapāyasam ativyāyāmam arkātapam ।। rasendrahemārkabiḍālagolasurāyasalohamalābhragandhāḥ । tāpyaṃ ca kanyārasamardito'yaṃ pakvaḥ puṭe tīkṣṇamukho'rśasāṃ syāt ।।
śreṣṭhā dantyagniyugmatrikaṭukahalinīpīlukumbhaṃ vipakvaṃ prasthe mūtrasya sasnukpayasi rasapalaṃ dve pale gandhakasya । lohasya trīṇi tāmrātkuḍavamatha rajaḥkṣārayoścāpi pañca kṣiptvā sthālyāṃ pacettu jvalati dahanataścūrṇam arśaḥkuṭhāraḥ ।। vajrakṛṣṇābhrajaṃ sattvaṃ śodhitaṃ kācaṭaṅkaṇam । retayitvā rajaḥkṛtvā bharjayitvā ghṛtena tat ।।
aṣṭāṃśasasyakopetaṃ puṭedvāratrayaṃ tataḥ । trivāraṃ nṛpavartena luṅgasvarasayoginā ।। caturvāraṃ ca varṣābhūvāsāmatsyākṣikārasaiḥ । guggulutriphalākvāthaistriṃśadvārāṇi yatnataḥ ।।
tulyāṃśarasagandhotthakajjalyāṣṭāṃśabhāgayā । puṭetpañcāśataṃ vārānmardayecca puṭe puṭe ।। śodhitaṃ retitaṃ kāntasatvaṃ ca ghṛtamarditam । puṭedaṣṭāṃśadaradaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ lakucāmbunā ।।
daśavāraṃ tathā samyak tāraṃ śuddhaṃ manohvayā । tathā viṃśativārāṇi balinā mīnadṛgrasaiḥ ।। daśavārāṇi tāpyena kṛṣṇagoghṛtayoginā । ubhayaṃ samabhāgaṃ tat puṭennirguṃḍikārasaiḥ ।।
rasagandhotthakajjalyā daśavāraṃ puṭetpunaḥ । tasminnaṣṭāṃśabhāgena kṣipedvaikrāntabhasmakam ।। rājāvartakalāṃśena samabhāgena parpaṭī । tatsarvaṃ parimardyātha bhāvayitvārdrakāmbunā ।।
guḍūcyāḥ svarasenāpi bhūkadambarasena vā । bhṛṅgarājarasenāpi citramūlarasena ca ।। vyoṣagañjākinīkandair bhūyo apyārdradraveṇa ca । paṭacūrṇamataḥ kṛtvā kṣipecchuddhakaraṇḍake ।।
trailokyatilakaḥ so'yaṃ khyātaḥ sarvarasottamaḥ । sarvavyādhiharaḥ śrīmāñchambhunā parikīrtitaḥ ।। udāvartaṃ ca viḍbandhaṃ vyathāṃ ca jaṭharodbhavām । lohalaṃ mandabuddhitvaṃ śūlitvamapi vandhyatām ।।
sūtirogān aśeṣāṃśca śūlaṃ nānāvidhaṃ tathā । pariṇāmākhyaśūlaṃ ca tathā bhindyāt samutkaṭam ।। raktagulmaṃ ca nārīṇāṃ rajaḥśūlaṃ ca duḥsaham । anupānaṃ ca pathyaṃ ca tattadrogānurūpataḥ ।।
vacāhiṅguviḍaṅgāni saindhavaṃ jīranāgaram । maricaṃ pippalī kuṣṭhaṃ pathyā vahnyajamodakam ।। kramottaraguṇaṃ cūrṇaṃ sarveṣāṃ dviguṇaṃ guḍam । karṣaṃ coṣṇajalenānupibedvātārśasāṃ jaye ।।
mṛtaṃ lohaṃ cendrayavaṃ śuṇṭhībhallātacitrakam । bilvamajjāviḍaṅgāni pathyā tulyaṃ vicūrṇayet ।। sarvatulyaṃ guḍaṃ yojyaṃ karṣaṃ bhuktvārśasāṃ jayet । śleṣmārśasāṃ praśāntyarthaṃ deyamānandabhairavam ।
mṛtatāmreṇa santulyaṃ deyaṃ guñjātrayaṃ hi tat ।। kusumbhamṛdupatrāṇi kāñjikenaiva pācayet । śākavadbhakṣayennityamarśorogapraśāntaye ।। devadālyāśca bījāni saindhavena sucūrṇitaḥ ।
āranālena lepo'yaṃ mūlaroganikṛntanaḥ ।। kāñcanīkusumaṃ cūrṇaṃ śaṅkhacūrṇaṃ manaḥśilām । gajapippalikātoyairlepo hyarśaḥkuṭhārakaḥ ।। devadālyāḥ kaṣāyeṇa hyarśoghnaṃ śaucamācaret ।
gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ cāpi śāntimāyāti nānyathā ।। āranālena sampiṣṭā sabījā kaṭutumbikā । saguḍā hanti lepena durnāmāni samūlataḥ ।। pīlutailena saṃliptā vartikā gudamadhyagā ।
ghātayatyarśasāṃ śīghraṃ sakalāṃ vedanāṃ tathā ।। arkakṣīraṃ snuhīkāṃḍaṃ kaṭulāvupatrakam । karaṃjaṃ chāgamūtreṇa lepaḥ srāvyarśasāṃ hitaḥ ।। śigrumūlārkajaiḥ patrairlepanaṃ hitamarśasām ।।
rūkṣaiḥ kodravajīrṇamudgacaṇakaiḥ kruddho'nilo'dho vahan ruddhvā vartma malaṃ viśoṣya kurute viṇmūtrasaṃgaṃ tataḥ । hṛtpṛṣṭhodaravastimastakarujaḥ saśvāsakāsaṃ jvaraṃ gacchannūrdhvamasau hi nūnam aniśaṃ kopādudāvartayet ।। kaṃkuṣṭhahiṃgusiṃdhūtthatrivṛddaṃtīvacābhayāḥ । citrakasya tu mūlaṃ ca kalkīkṛtya paced ghṛtam ।।
caturguṇe gavāṃ kṣīre yuktaṃ snukkṣīramātrayā । udāvartodarān hanti pānena sarvadā ।। atyambupānatilapiṣṭavirūḍharūkṣaśuṣkāmiṣādhyaśanabaddhamalagrahādyaiḥ । kruddho'nilo atisaraṇāya ca kalpate'gniṃ hatvā malaṃ śithilayannapi toyadhātūn ।।
suślakṣṇatīkṣṇacūrṇaṃ tu rasendrasamabhāgikam । kāṃcanārarasairghṛṣṭaṃ sarvātīsāranāśanam ।। piṣṭaḥ samena tīkṣṇena kāñcanārāṃbumarditaḥ । puṭapakvo'tisāraghnaḥ sūto'yaṃ dardurāhvayaḥ ।।
hiṃgulaṃ vatsanābhaṃ ca maricaṃ ṭaṃkaṇaṃ kaṇā । mardayetsamabhāgaṃ ca raso hyānandabhairavaḥ ।। guṃjaikāṃ vārdhaguñjāṃ vā balaṃ jñātvā pradāpayet । madhunā lehayeccānu kuṭajasya phalaṃ tvacam ।।
cūrṇitaṃ karṣamātraṃ tu tridoṣotthātisārajit । dadhyannaṃ dāpayetpathyaṃ gavājyaṃ takrameva vā । pipāsāyāṃ jalaṃ śītaṃ vijayā ca hitā niśi ।। pṛthakpalikagaṃdhāśmasūtasaṃjātakajjalīm ।
pradrāvya nikṣipedvyoma palaikaṃ gatacandrikam ।। kāṣṭhenāloḍya tatsarvaṃ kṣipetkuṭajapatrake । punaḥ saṃcūrṇya yatnena bhāvayet tadanantaram ।। bālatinduphaladrāvaiḥ kṣīrairauduṃbarais tathā ।
aralutvagrasaiścāpi dugdhinīsvarasaistathā ।। puṭapakvasya bālasya dāḍimasya rasaiḥ śubhaiḥ । kṛṣṇakāmbojikāmūlarasaiḥ kuṭajavalkajaiḥ ।। tulyāṃśaviśvagāṃdhārīcūrṇaṃ dvipalikaṃ kṣipet ।
mustāvatsakadīpyāgnimocasāraṃ sajīrakam ।। vatsanābhaṃ ca karṣāṃśaṃ pratyekaṃ tatra nikṣipet । vicūrṇya bhāvayedbhūyaḥ śuṇṭhīkvāthena saptadhā ।। itthaṃ siddho rasaḥ piṣṭaḥ karaṇḍe viniveśayet ।
sudhāsāra iti khyātaḥ sudhārasasamadyutiḥ ।। dīpanaḥ pācano grāhī hṛdyo rucikarastathā । doṣatrayātisāraṃ ca durjayaṃ bheṣajāntaraiḥ ।। āmaṃ caivamāraktaṃ ca jvarātīsāram eva ca ।
sātisārāṃ viṣūcīṃ ca pratibadhnāti tatkṣaṇāt । mānyamānavyatikrāntiriva puṇyaphalodayam ।। piṣṭaviśvābdakalkena vidhāya khalu cakrikām । nikṣipet svedanīyantre paktvārdhaghaṭikāvadhi ।।
ākṛṣya tajjalairevaṃ saṃpramardyāhared rasam । sudhāsārarasaṃ tatra kṣiptvā dhānyakasaṃmitam ।। pūrvoditeṣu rogeṣu pradadīta bhiṣagvaraḥ । gotakreṇātha dadhnā vā pathyaṃ deyaṃ hitaṃ mitam ।।
bālarambhāphalaṃ gurvīphalaṃ bilvaphalaṃ tathā । āmrapeśī ca madhukaṃ vṛntākaṃ ca praśasyate ।। sarvātisāraṃ grahaṇīṃ ca hikkāṃ mandāgnim ānāhamarocakaṃ ca । nihanti sadyo vihitāmapāke dvitriprayogeṇa rasottamo'yam ।।
sāṃbusthālīmukhābaddhe vastre pākyaṃ nidhāya ca । pidhāya pacyate yatra svedanīyantram ucyate ।। dvau bhāgau gaṃdhakasyāṣṭau śaṃkhacūrṇasya yojayet । ekameva rasasyāṃśamarkakṣīreṇa mardayet ।।
citrakasya draveṇaivaṃ śoṣayitvā punaḥ punaḥ । ekīkṛtya rasenātha kṣāraṃ dattvā tadardhakam ।। arkakṣīreṇa kurvīta golakānatha śoṣayet । nirudhya cūrṇalipte'tha bhāṇḍe dadyātpuṭaṃ tataḥ ।।
lokeśvararaso hyeṣa grahaṇīrogakṛntanaḥ । guñjācatuṣṭayaṃ cāsya marīcājyasamanvitam । dadīta dadhibhaktaṃ ca pathyaṃ lokeśvare tathā ।। mṛtapāradabhāgaikaṃ catvāraḥ śuddhagaṃdhakāt ।
yāmaṃ ca mardayetkhalle tena pūrvā varāṭakāḥ ।। ṭaṅkaṇaṃ tu gavāṃ kṣīraiḥ piṣṭvā tena mukhaṃ lipet । varāṭānāṃ prayatnena ruddhvā bhāṇḍe puṭe pacet ।। svāṅgaśītaṃ samuddhṛtya tataścūrṇya varāṭakāḥ ।
lokanātharaso nāmnā kṣaudrairguñjācatuṣṭayam ।। nāgarātiviṣāmustādevadāruvacānvitam । kaṣāyamanupānaṃ syādvātātīsāranāśanaḥ ।। nāgabhasmarasavyomagandhair ardhapalonmitaiḥ ।
kurvīta kajjalīṃ ślakṣṇāṃ prakṣipettadanantaram ।। dvipalonmitarālāyāṃ drutāyāṃ parimiśritām । bhṛṣṭair yakṣākṣasiṃdhūtthavacāvyoṣadvijīrakaiḥ ।। sapathyāvijayādīpyais tulyāṃśair avacūrṇitaiḥ ।
melayetprāktanaṃ kalkaṃ bhāvayettadanantaram ।। mahāniṃbatvacāsāraiḥ kāṃbojīmūlajadravaiḥ । rasair nāgabalāyāśca guḍūcyāśca tridhā tridhā । tataśca guṭikāḥ kāryā badarāsthipramāṇataḥ ।।
hanyādeva hi nāgasundararaso vallonmitaḥ sevitaḥ । nānātīsaraṇāmayaṃ gudaparibhraṃśaṃ tathā biṃbiśim ।। ṣaṇniṣkaṃ tilatailasya niṣkaṃ jambīrajaṃ rasam । lavaṇaṃ pañcaguñjaṃ ca aṃgulyā mardayed dṛḍham ।
āmavātārtasāraghnaṃ lihetpathyaṃ ca pūrvavat ।। malaṃ saṃgṛhya saṃgṛhya kadācid atirecayet । aruciḥ śvayathur māndyaṃ grahaṇīrogalakṣaṇam ।। mṛtasūtābhrakaṃ gandhaṃ yavakṣāraṃ saṭaṅkaṇam ।
vacā jayā samaṃ sarvaṃ jayantī bhṛṃgajadravaiḥ ।। sajaṃbīraistryahaṃ mardyaṃ śoṣayettaṃ ca golakam । mandavahnau śanaiḥ svedyaṃ yāmārdhaṃ lauhapātrake ।। rasasāmye pratiniśā deyā mocarasastathā ।
bhāvayedvijayādrāvaiḥ śoṣyaṃ peṣyaṃca saptadhā । raso vajrakapāṭo'yaṃ niṣkārdhaṃ madhunā lihet ।। dagdhāṃ kapardikāṃ piṣṭvā tryūṣaṇaṃ ṭaṅkaṇaṃ viṣam । gandhakaṃ śuddhasūtaṃ ca tulyaṃ jambīrajair dravaiḥ ।।
mardayedbhakṣayenmāṣaṃ maricājyaṃ lihedanu । nihanti grahaṇīrogaṃ pathyaṃ takraudanaṃ hitam ।। hiṅgulaṃ maricaṃ gandhaṃ pippalī ṭaṅkaṇaṃ viṣam । kanakasya ca bījāni samāṃśaṃ vijayādravaiḥ ।।
mardayedyāmamātraṃ tu caṇamātraṃ vaṭīkṛtam । bhakṣayed grahaṇīṃ hanti rasaḥ kanakasundaraḥ ।। agnimāndyaṃ jvaraṃ tīvramatisāraṃ ca nāśayet । dadhyannaṃ dāpayetpathyaṃ gavyājaṃ takrameva vā ।।
rasābhragandhāḥ kramavṛddhabhāgā jayārasena tridinaṃ vimardyāḥ । gadyāṇakārdhaṃ madhunā sametaṃ dadīta pathyaṃ dadhibhaktakaṃ ca ।। hiṃgulasthitamaheśvarabījaṃ pātayantravidhinā haraṇīyam । gaṃdhaṭaṃkaṇamṛtābhrakatulyaṃ kokilākṣam atha cāyasakhalle ।।
mardanīyam abhidhāraṇayukte dhūmahīnadahanopari saṃsthe । yāvadeṣa jalaśoṣaṇadakṣo jīrakārdrakayutena sa vallaḥ ।। saṃgrahajvaram atisrutigulmān arśasāṃ ca vinihanti samūham । vāsudevakathito rasarājaś caṇḍasaṃgrahagadaikakapāṭaḥ ।।
samāṃśaṃ rasagaṃdhābhradaradaṃ ca viśodhitam । lohakhalle vinikṣipya gavyājyena samanvitam ।। droṇīcullyāṃ nyasetkhallaṃ sāṅgārāyāṃ prayatnataḥ । mardakenāpi lauhena mardayeddivasadvayam ।।
iti siddho raseṃdro'yaṃ laghusiddhābhrako mataḥ । vallatulyo raso jīravāriṇā sahitaḥ prage ।। pīto harati vegena grahaṇīmatidurdharām । atisāraṃ mahāghoraṃ sātisāraṃ jvaraṃ tathā ।।
pācano dīpano hṛdyo gātralāghavakārakaḥ । nāgārjunena kathitaḥ sadyaḥ pratyayakārakaḥ ।। rasaṃ palamitaṃ tulyaṃ śuddhanāgena saṃyutam । drāvayitvāyase pātre sataile nikṣipetkṣitau ।।
tato drute vinikṣipya gaṃdhake tad viloḍya ca । punarāyasapātre tatkṣiptvā pradrāvya nikṣipet ।। tattulyaṃ jārayettālaṃ punaḥ saṃcūrṇya pūrvavat । tattulyāṃ jārayetsamyakkunaṭīṃ pariśodhitām ।।
tattulyaṃ cūrṇite tasminkṣipennāgaṃ nirutthakam । tāvadeva mṛtaṃ tāpyaṃ sarvamanyacca tatsamam ।। tīkṣṇāyaḥ kharparaṃ vyoma hiṃgulaṃ ca śilājatu । pṛthakkarṣāṃśamānena ṣaṭkolaṃ kaṭphalaṃ miśīm ।।
dīpyakaṃ ca caturjātaṃ reṇukośīravellakam । tuṃbaruṃ bhārṅgikāṃ rāsnāṃ kaṅkolaṃ corapuṣkaram ।। riṅgiṇīṃ ciratiktaṃ ca bījānyunmattakasya ca । paladvayaṃ ca lāṃgalyāḥ sarveṣāṃ dvādaśāṃśakam ।।
vatsanābhaṃ sitaṃ bhūri vinikṣipya tataḥ param । triphalānāṃ daśāṅghrīṇāṃ kaṣāyeṇa tataḥ param ।। jayantyārdrakavāsānāṃ mārkavasya rasaistathā । bhāvayitvā ca kartavyā vaṭakāścaṇakopamāḥ ।।
ekaikā vaṭikā sevyā kuryāttīvratarāṃ kṣudhām । viṣūcīmaratiṃ hikkāṃ sevyaṃ svādu ca śītalam ।। sāmāṃ ca grahaṇīṃ sadāṅgatudanaṃ śoṣotkaṭaṃ pāṇḍutām ārtiṃ vātakaphatridoṣajanitāṃ śūlaṃ ca gulmāmayam । hikkādhmānaviṣūcikāṃ ca kasanaṃ śvāsārśasāṃ vidradhiṃ sarvāropyavaṭī kṣaṇādvijayate rogāṃstathānyānapi ।।
rasagaṃdhakayoḥ kṛtvā kajjalīṃ tulyabhāgayoḥ । drāvayitvāyase pātre rasatulyaṃ vinikṣipet ।। carācarabhavaṃ bhasma tatra mākṣikasaṃbhavam । gaṃdhapāṣāṇasahitaṃ pātre lohamaye kṣipet ।।
tatkāṣṭhena viloḍyātha nikṣipetkadalīdale । tata ācchādya saṃcūrṇya nidhāyāyasabhājane ।। akṣamātraṃ kṣipedbhasma tatra mākṣikasambhavam । samyaṅniścandratāṃ nītaṃ vyomabhasma palonmitam ।।
viṣaṃ viṣāṃ ca gandhārīṃ mocasāraṃ sajīrakam । sarvaṃ samāṃśikaṃ kṛtvā rase cārdhāṃśikaṃ kṣipet ।। sarvametanmardayitvā bhāvayedatiyatnataḥ । jayaṃtyā ca mahārāṣṭryā gañjākinyāśvagandhayā ।।
pañcakolakaṣāyaiśca kuryāccūrṇaṃ tataḥ param । itthaṃ siddho rasaḥ so'yaṃ grahaṇīgajakesarī ।। nāmato nandinā proktaḥ karmataśca sudhānidhiḥ । vallena pramitaścāyaṃ rasaḥ śuṇṭhyā ghṛtāktayā ।।
sevito grahaṇīṃ hanti satsaṅga iva vigraham । pathyamatra pradātavyaṃ svalpājyaṃ dadhitakrayuk ।। hitaṃ mitaṃ ca viśadaṃ laghu grāhi rucipradam । pācano dīpano'tyarthamāmaghno rucikārakaḥ ।।
tattadauṣadhayogena sarvātīsāranāśanaḥ । badhnannapi malaṃ śīghraṃ nādhmānaṃ kurute nṛṇām ।। pāradaṃ gandhakaṃ vyoma tīkṣṇaṃ tālaṃ manaḥśilā । sauvīramañjanaṃ śuddhaṃ vimalaṃ ca samāṃśakam ।।
ebhiḥ kajjalikāṃ kṛtvā svalpatailena bharjayet । granthikaṃ jīrakaṃ citraṃ dīpyakaṃ mustakaṃ viṣam ।। bālāmraṃ bālabilvaṃ ca mocasāraṃ samāṃśakam । vicūrṇya pūrvavatkalkaṃ tadardhena vinikṣipet ।।
punarvimardayed yatnādekarūpaṃ bhavedyathā । bhāvayetsaptavārāṇi pañcakolakaṣāyataḥ ।। aralutvagrasenāpi daśavārāṇi bhāvayet । proktena kramayogena raso niṣpadyate hyayam ।।
jagdho viśvaghanāmbunā sa hi rasaḥ śīghraprabhāvābhidho niṣkārdhapramito mahāgrahaṇikāroge'tisārāmaye । ādhmāne grahaṇībhave rucihate vāte ca mandānale mukte cāpi male punaścalamalāśaṅkāsu hikkāsu ca ।। kapardatulyaṃ rasagandhakalkaṃ lohaṃ mṛtaṃ ṭaṅkaṇakaṃ ca tulyam । jayārasenaikadinaṃ vimardya cūrṇena sampiṣya puṭettu bhāṇḍe ।।
dadīta tāṃ poṭalikāṃ ca doṣatrayapradhānagrahaṇīnivṛttyai ।। naṣṭapiṣṭau caturmāṣamekaikaṃ rasagaṃdhakau । abhrakaṃ māṣamānaṃ ca mātuluṃgāmlamarditam ।। śodhitaṃ saptadhā caiva dvimāṣaṃ tryūṣaṇaṃ pṛthak ।
triśūlī bhṛṃgacāṅgerī sātalā tīkṣṇaparṇikā ।। śvetāparājitā kanyā matsyākṣī grīṣmasundarā । kariṇī karṇamoṭī ca rudaṃtī citrakārdrakāt ।। dhustūrakākamācībhyāṃ musalyāśca pṛthagrasaiḥ ।
marditaṃ dvipalaiḥ kuryādvaṭikā māṣasaṃmitā ।। grahaṇyāṃ parṇakhaṇḍena vyoṣayuktā niṣevitā । aruciṃ rājayakṣmāṇaṃ mandāgniṃ sūtikāgadān । śamayedvaṭikā nāmnā vahnijvāleti gīyate ।।
rasagaṃdhakatāmrābhraṃ kṣārāṃstrīnvaruṇo vṛṣam । apāmārgasya ca kṣāraṃ lavaṇaṃ dvidvimāṣakam ।। cāṅgeryā hastiśuṃḍyāśca rasaiḥ piṣṭaṃ pacetpuṭe । bhakṣayitvā tato guñjāṃ grahaṇyāṃ kāṃjikaṃ pibet ।।
paktiśūle ca kāse ca mandāgnāv ārdrakadravam । amlapitte ca dhāroṣṇaṃ kṣīraṃ vajradharo hyayam ।। raseṃdragandhātiviṣābhayābhraṃ kṣāradvayaṃ mocaraso vacā ca । jayā ca jaṃbīrarasena piṣṭaṃ piṇḍīkṛtaṃ syādgrahaṇīkapāṭaḥ ।।
tasyārdhamāṣaṃ madhunā prabhāte śambukabhasmājyamadhūni lihyāt । sakṣīriṇījīrakamāṇimanthatīkṣṇāni cādau dadhibhojanaṃ ca ।। sauvarcalaṃ jīrakayugmadhānyajayāyavānī kaṇanāgaraṃ ca । kapitthasāreṇa samaṃ pragṛhya dadīta cūrṇaṃ niśi tīvrapittaiḥ ।।
gadyāṇamātraṃ madhukhaṇḍayuktaṃ takreṇa yuktaṃ tvarucipraśāntyai । vātapradhāne ca kaphapradhāne rātrau kaṣāyaṃ kuṭajasya dadyāt ।। mustāvatsakapāṭhāgnivyoṣaprativiṣāviṣam । dhātakīmocaniryāsaścūtāsthigrahaṇīharam ।।
vahniśuṃṭhībiḍaṃ bilvaṃ lavaṇaṃ peṣayetsamam । pibeduṣṇāṃbhasā cānu vātotthāṃ grahaṇīṃ jayet ।। dagdhaśaṃbūkasiṃdhūtthaṃ tulyaṃ kṣaudreṇa lehayet । niṣkaikaikaṃ nihantyāśu grahaṇīrogam utkaṭam ।।
kṛśānvajājīdvayamākṣikeṇa kaṭutrayeṇāpi yutaṃ tvanuṣṇam । cāṅgerikājīrakayugmadhānyaṃ dugdhenduśākāya dadīta dadhnā ।। vireko jaṭhare śūlaṃ vamanaṃ ca muhurmuhuḥ । hastapādādisaṃkocaḥ sarvājīrṇasya lakṣaṇam ।।
śuddhasūtaṃ viṣaṃ gandhaṃ samaṃ sarvavicūrṇitam । maricaṃ sarvatulyāṃśaṃ kaṃṭakāryā phaladravaiḥ ।। mardayed bhāvayet sarvam ekaviṃśativārakam । vaṭīṃ guñjātrayīṃ khādetsarvājīrṇapraśāntaye ।।
ajīrṇakaṇṭakaḥ so'yaṃ raso hanti viṣūcikām । vāriṇā tilaparṇyutthamūlaṃ piṣṭvā pibedanu ।। vimardya gandhopalaṭaṃkaṇena saṃbhāvya vārānatha saptajātyāḥ । toyaiḥ phalānāmatha siddhasūto vidhvaṃsanāmā śamano viṣūcyāḥ ।।
amuṣya guñjā nava dāpanīyā hantuṃ viṣūcīṃ sitayā sametāḥ । takraudanaṃ syādiha bhojanāya pathyaṃ ca śākaṃ kila vāstukasya ।। rasagaṃdhaṭaṃkabhasitaṃ samāṃśakaṃ parimardya jātiphalasaptabhāvitam । sitayopayujya navaraktikonmitaṃ mathitānnabhugvijayate viṣūcikām ।।
haṃsapādīrasaiḥ siddhaṃ rasagaṃdhakayoḥ palam । kolaṃ ca viṣacūrṇasya vālukāyaṃtrapācitam ।। śāṇaṃ viṣasyārdhapalaṃ maricasya vimiśrayet । dīpano'gnikumāro'yaṃ grahaṇyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
savātaśleṣmajānrogānkṣaṇād evāpakarṣati । sannipātajvaraśvāsakṣayakāsāṃśca nāśayet ।। ṭaṃkaṇaṃ maricaṃ tutthaṃ pṛthak karṣatrayaṃ bhavet । sundaraṃ dvādaśaṃ niṣkaṃ triṃśanniṣkam ayomalam ।।
cūrṇānyetāni saṃyojya sthāpayecchuddhabhājane । śuddhadeho narastasya pānaṃ yadbhojanottaram ।। adyātpathyaṃ tataḥ svalpaṃ tatastāṃbūlabhāgbhavet । udarāgnirnarasyāsya vaḍavāgnisamo bhavet ।
bahunātra kimuktena rasāyanamayaṃ nṛṇām ।। kāntaṃ padmarase ghṛṣṭaṃ puṭapakvaṃ varārase । mārkavasvarase ghṛṣṭaṃ saptakṛtvas tvayomalam ।। śuddhau sūtabalī carācararajaḥ karṣāṃśataḥ kajjalīm kṛtvā gopayasā vimardya divasaṃ ruddhvā ca mūṣodare ।
siddhaṃ kumbhapuṭe svataśca śiśirā piṣṭā karaṇḍe sthitā syād vaiśvānarapoṭalīti kathitā tīvrāgnidīptipradā ।। ekonaviṃśateścūrṇairmaricānāṃ ghṛtānvitaiḥ । deyeyaṃ vallamānena vayobalam avekṣyatām ।। giled galaviśuddhyarthaṃ dadhibhaktamanuttamam ।
kavalatrayamānena durgandhodgāraśāntaye ।। madhyaṃdine tato bhojyaṃ ghṛtatakropadaṃśayuk । rātrau ca payasā sārdhaṃ yadvā rogānusārataḥ ।। vidāhi dvidalaṃ bhūrilavaṇaṃ tailapācitam ।
bilvaṃ ca kāravellaṃ ca vṛṃtākaṃ kāṃjikaṃ tyajet ।। iyaṃ hi poṭalī proktā siṅghaṇena mahībhṛtā । maṃdāgniprabhavāśeṣarogasaṃghātaghātinī ।। siṃghaṇasya vinirdiṣṭā bhairavānaṃdayoginā ।
lokanāthoktapoṭalyā upacārā iha smṛtāḥ । poṭalyo dīpanāḥ snigdhā maṃdāgnau nitarāṃ hitāḥ ।। pītavarṇā gurusnigdhā pṛṣṭhato granthilāmalā । carācareti sā proktā varāṭī naṃdinā khalu ।।
sārdhaniṣkamitā śreṣṭhā madhyamā niṣkamānikā । pādonaniṣkamānā ca kaniṣṭhātra varāṭikā ।। niṣphalāśca tato nyūnāḥ puṃvarāṭāśca pittalāḥ । dattvā dattvā guṇānbhūyo vikārānkurvate hi te ।।
śulbāyoghanabhasmavellahalinīvyoṣāmbunimbacchadaiḥ saṃyuktaiśca haridrayā samalavaiḥ sārdhaṃ saśubhrāmṛtaiḥ । bhṛṅgāmbhoviṣatindukārdrakarasaiḥ sampiṣya guṃjāmitā saṃśuṣkā vaḍavāmukhīti guṭikā nāmnoditā tārayā ।। kṣipraṃ kṣutparibodhinī khalu matā sarvāmayadhvaṃsinī śleṣmavyādhividhūnanī kasanahṛcchvāsāpahā śūlanut kṣudvaiṣamyaharā ca gulmaśamanī mūlārtimūlaṃkaṣā śophavyādhiharātra kiṃ bahugirā sarvāmayotsādinī ।। dvipalaṃ gandhakaṃ śuddhaṃ drāvayitvā vinikṣipet ।
pāradaṃ palamānena mṛtaśulvāyasaṃ punaḥ ।। tolamānena saṃkṣipya pañcāṅguladale kṣipet । tato vicūrṇya yatnena nikṣipyāyasabhājane ।। cullyāṃ niveśya yatnena jvālayenmṛduvahninā ।
pātramātraṃ hi jaṃbīrarasaṃ samyagvijārayet ।। saṃcūrṇya pañcakolotthaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ sāmlavetasaiḥ । bhāvanāḥ khalu kartavyāḥ pañcāśatpramitāstataḥ ।। bhṛṣṭaṭaṃkaṇacūrṇena tulyena saha melayet ।
tadardhaṃ kṛṣṇalavaṇaṃ sarvatulyaṃ marīcakam ।। saptadhā bhāvayetpaścāccaṇakakṣāravāriṇā । tataḥ saṃśoṣya sampiṣya kūpikājaṭhare kṣipet ।। atyarthaṃ gurumāṃsāni gurubhojyānyanekaśaḥ ।
bhuktvā ca kaṃṭhaparyantaṃ caturvallamitaṃ rasam ।। paṭvamlatakrasahitaṃ pibettadanupānataḥ । kṣipraṃ tajjīryate bhuktaṃ jāyate dīpanaṃ punaḥ ।। rasaḥ kravyādanāmāyaṃ prokto manthānabhairavaiḥ ।
siṃghaṇakṣoṇipālasya bhūrimāṃsapriyasya ca । diṣṭo grāmaṃ samāsādya bhairavānandayoginā ।। kuryāddīpanamuddhataṃ ca pacanaṃ duṣṭāmasaṃśoṣaṇaṃ tundasthaulyanibarhaṇaṃ garaharaṃ mūlārtiśūlāpaham । gulmaplīhavināśanaṃ grahaṇikāvidhvaṃsanaṃ sraṃsanaṃ vātagranthimahodarāpaharaṇaṃ kravyādanāmā rasaḥ ।।
bhāgo mṛtarasasyaiko vatsanābhāṃśakadvayam । rasatulyaṃ śivācūrṇaṃ gandhakaṃ tryūṣaṇaṃ tathā ।। vicūrṇyātiprayatnena bhāvayetsaptavāsaram । tāmbūlapatratoyena svarṇadhustūrajadravaiḥ ।
piṣṭvā caṇamitāḥ kuryācchāyāśuṣkāstu golikāḥ ।। uṣṇāṃbhoyutarājaśekharavaṭī mandāgninirṇāśinī nānākāramahājvarārtiśamanī niḥśeṣamūlāpahā । pāṇḍuvyādhimahodarārtiśamanī śūlāntakṛt pācinī śophaghnī pavanārtināśanapaṭuḥ śleṣmāmayadhvaṃsinī ।। śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ viṣaṃ gaṃdhaṃ dvikṣāraṃ paṭupañcakam ।
daśakaṃ tulyāṃśaṃ bharjitā vijayā navā ।। daśānāṃ tulyabhāgā ca tasyārdhaṃ śigrumūlakam । tatsarvaṃ vijayādrāvaiḥ śigrucitrakabhṛṃgajaiḥ ।। drāvair dinatrayaṃ mardyaṃ ruddhvā bhāṇḍe pacellaghu ।
dīpāgninā tu yāmaikaṃ śuṣkaṃ yāvatsamuddharet ।। saptadhā cārdrakadrāvairbhāvayeccūrṇayedbhiṣak । dīpako'gnikumāro'yaṃ niṣkaikaṃ madhunā lihet । pratikarṣaṃ guḍaṃ śuṃṭhī hyanupānaṃ ca dīpanam ।।
kuṣṭhagaṃdhaviṣavyomatriphalāpāradaiḥ samaiḥ । mṛgāmbumarditair mudgamānāmṛtavaṭī śubhā । ajīrṇaśleṣmavātaghnī dīpanī rucivardhinī ।। tāmraṃ pāradagaṃdhakau trikaṭukaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca sauvarcalaṃ khalle mardya dṛḍhaṃ vidhāya sikatākumbhe'ṣṭayāmaṃ tataḥ ।
svinnaṃ tasya ca raktaśākinibhavaṃ kṣāraṃ samaṃ melayet sarvaṃ bhāvitamātuluṃgajarasairnāmnā raso rākṣasaḥ ।। mandāgnau satataṃ dadīta munaye prātaḥ purā śaṃkaraḥ sakhya asmai cyavanāya maṃdahutabhugvaryāya naṣṭaujase । tenādāya samastalokagurave sūryāya tasmai namo martyānāmapi cāsya dānasamaye guṃjāṣṭakaṃ varjayet ।। rasagaṃdhau sindhukaṇāṭaṅkaṇam abhayāgnihiyāvalīkatakaphalam ।
kramaśa uttaraṃ ca vicūrṇitayā bṛhatīrasasaṃyutabhāvanayā ।। ārdrakahiṃgupunarnavapūticchinnarasaiḥ kramaśastu bhāvanayā । tatra kalāṃśaviśaṃ ca vimiśraṃ tadrasamānaṃ mānavidhayā ।। sarvamajīrṇaṃ kaphamārutapāṇḍuśophahalīmakakāmalāśūlam ।
nāśayate hyudarāgnikaro'yaṃ dīpanajīvananāmarasendraḥ ।। śulbaṃ tālakagandhakau jalanidheḥ pheno agnigarbhāśayaḥ kāntāyo lavaṇāni hemapavayo nīlāṃjanaṃ tutthakam । bhāgo dvādaśako rasasya tu dinaṃ vallyaṃbughṛṣṭaṃ śanaiḥ siddho'yaṃ vaḍavānalo gajapuṭe rogānaśeṣāñjayet ।। kaṇanāgaragandhakapāradakaṃ garalaṃ maricaṃ samabhāgayutam ।
lakucasya rasaiścaṇakapramitā guṭikā janayatyacirādanalam ।। śuddhasūtaṃ viṣaṃ gaṃdham ajamodaṃ phalatrayam । sarjīkṣāraṃ yavakṣāraṃ vahnisaindhavajīrakam ।। sauvarcalaṃ viḍaṅgāni sāmudraṃ tryūṣaṇaṃ samam ।
viṣamuṣṭiḥ sarvatulyā jaṃbīrāmlena marditam ।। maricābhāṃ vaṭīṃ khādedvahnimāṃdyapraśāṃtaye । pathyā śuṇṭhī guḍaṃ cānu palārdhaṃ bhakṣayetsadā ।। agnimāṃdye vaṭī khyātā sarvarogakulāntakā ।।
mṛtaṃ tāmraṃ kaṇātulyaṃ cūrṇaṃ kṣaudravimiśritam । niṣkārdhaṃ bhakṣayennityaṃ naṣṭavahnipradīptaye ।। ārdrakasvarasaḥ kṣaudraṃ palamātraṃ pibedanu । yatheṣṭaṃ ghṛtamāṃsāśī śakto bhavati pāvakaḥ ।।
kaṭau kukṣipradeśe ca śūlaṃ prathamato bhavet । paścādrodho jvalanmūtram aśmarīrogalakṣaṇam ।। rasaṃ dviguṇagaṃdhena mardayitvā prayatnataḥ । vasuḥ punarnavā vāsā śvetā grāhyā prayatnataḥ ।।
taddravairbhāvayedenaṃ pratyekaṃ tu dinatrayam । pakvaṃ mūṣāgataṃ śuṣkaṃ svedayejjalayantrataḥ ।। pāṣāṇabhedī nāmāyaṃ niyuñjītāsya vallayuk । gopālakarkaṭīdugdhaṃ bhūmyāmalakamūlikā ।
kulatthakvāthatoyena piṣṭvā tadanupāyayet ।। rasena sitavarṣābhvā rasaṃ dviguṇagaṃdhakam । ghṛṣṭaṃ pacecca mūṣāyāṃ dvau māṣau tasya bhakṣayet ।। pātālakarkaṭīmūlaṃ kulatthodaiḥ pibedanu ।
gokaṇṭakasadābhadrāmūlakvāthaṃ pibenniśi । ayaṃ pāṣāṇabhinnāmnā rasaḥ pāṣāṇabhedakaḥ ।। gokṣurabījasamutthaṃ cūrṇamavikṣīrasaṃyuktam । rasavaramiśraṃ pibataścūrṇībhūtvāśmarī patati ।।
mṛtatāmramajākṣīraiḥ pācyaṃ tulyaṃ gate drave । tattāmraṃ śuddhasūtaṃ ca gaṃdhakaṃ ca samaṃ samam ।। nirguṇḍyutthadravairmardyaṃ dinaṃ tadgolam andhrayet । yāmaikaṃ vālukāyaṃtre pācyaṃ yojyaṃ dviguñjakam ।।
bījapūrasya mūlaṃ tu sajalaṃ cānupāyayet । rasastrivikramo nāmnā māsaikenāśmarīpraṇut ।। tilāpāmārgakāṇḍaṃ ca kāravellyā yavasya ca । palāśakāṣṭhasaṃyuktaṃ sarvaṃ tulyaṃ dahetpuṭe ।।
tanniṣkaikamajāmūtrairvaṭīṃ cānandabhairavīm । pāyayedaśmarīṃ hanti saptāhānnātra saṃśayaḥ ।। pāṇḍuraṃ phalikāmūlaṃ jalenaivāśmarīharam ।। madhunā ca yavakṣāraṃ līḍhaṃ syād aśmarīharam ।।
haridrāguḍakarṣaikaṃ cāranālena vā pibet ।। vandhyākarkoṭakīkandaṃ bhakṣya kṣaudraṃ sitāyutam । aśmarīṃ hanti no citraṃ karṣamātraṃ śivoditam ।। śoṣastāpo'ṅgakārśyaṃ ca bahumūtratvam eva ca ।
asvāsthyaṃ sarvagātreṣu mūtramehasya lakṣaṇam ।। mārkaṇḍīcūrṇamādāya saguḍaṃ khādayenniśi ।। mṛtasūtasya bhāgaikaṃ catvāraḥ śuddhagandhakāt । piṣṭvā varāṭakaṃ tena rasapādaṃ ca ṭaṃkaṇam ।।
kṣīraiḥ piṣṭvā mukhaṃ ruddhvā varāṭāṃścāndhrayetpuṭet । svāṃgaśītaṃ vicūrṇyātha laghulokeśvaro rasaḥ ।। caturguṃjārasaścāyaṃ maricaikonaviṃśatiḥ । jātimūlapalaikaṃ tu ajākṣīreṇa peṣayet ।
śarkarābhāvitaṃ cānu pītvā kṛcchraharaṃ param ।। bhedā vandhyābalānāṃ hi navadhā parikīrtitāḥ । tatrādivandhyā prathamā pāpakarmavinirmitā ।। raktena ca pṛthagdoṣaiḥ samastaiḥ pañcadhā bhavet ।
bhūtadevābhicāraiśca tisro vandhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। pumānapi bhavedvandhyo doṣairetaiśca śukrataḥ ।। garbhasrāvī smṛtā pūrvaṃ mṛtavatsā dvitīyakā । tṛtīyā strīprasūtiḥ syātkākavandhyā sakṛtprasūḥ ।।
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ tāpyasattvaṃ ca vaikṛtam । ekaikaṃ niṣkamānena saṃśuddhaṃ parimāritam ।। etaccaturguṇaṃ sūtaṃ sūtāddviguṇagandhakam । mardayellakṣmaṇātoyairbandhujīvarasairapi ।।
kācakūpyāṃ tataḥ kṣiptvā tāmrapātraṃ mukhe nyaset । vilimpedabhitaḥ kūpīmaṅgulotsedhayā mṛdā ।। viśoṣya ca puṭaṃ dadyādbhūmau nikṣipya kūpikām । gajākhyapuṭaparyāptiḥ śāṇakarṣamitotpalaiḥ ।।
svāṃgaśītaṃ vicūrṇyātha bhāvayellakṣmaṇādravaiḥ । saptavāraṃ viśoṣyātha karaṇḍāntarvinikṣipet ।। aśvagandhārajoyuktaratāmragokṣīrasaṃyutaḥ । sevito guñjayā tulyaḥ sitayā ca rasottamaḥ ।।
māsatrayaprayogeṇa vandhyā bhavati putriṇī । putriṇyai snānaśuddhāyai jaratkauśikacakṣuṣī ।। gavyājyena ca saṃsādhya tattadānīṃ hi bhojayet । ṛtāvṛtāvidaṃ deyaṃ yāvanmāsatrayaṃ bhavet ।।
rasendraḥ kathitaḥ so'yaṃ campakāraṇyavāsibhiḥ । pūrṇāmṛtākhyayogīndrair nāmato jayasundaraḥ ।। sevite'sminrase strīṇāṃ na bhavet sūtikāgadaḥ । bhavetputraśca dīrghāyuḥ paṇḍito bhāgyamaṇḍitaḥ ।।
vajraṃ marakataṃ padmarāgaṃ puṣpaṃ ca nīlakam । vaidūryaṃ cātha gomedaṃ mauktikaṃ vidrumaṃ tathā ।। pañcaguñjāmitaṃ sarvaṃ ratnaṃ bhāgottaraṃ param । tattantroktavidhānena bhasmīkuryātprayatnataḥ ।।
sarvasmād aṣṭaguṇitaṃ bhasma vaikrāntasambhavam । tattulyaṃ tāpyajaṃ bhasma tadvadvimalabhasma ca ।। sarvatastriguṇāṃ tulyāṃ rasagandhakakajjalīm । sarvamekatra saṃmardya chāgīdugdhena taddvyaham ।।
vidhāya parpaṭīṃ yatnātparicūrṇya prayatnataḥ । vandhyākarkoṭakīparṇakvāthena parimardayet ।। kānanotpalaviṃśatyā puṭetṣoḍaśavārakam । evaṃ raso viniṣpanno ratnabhāgottarābhidhaḥ ।।
mahāvandhyādivandhyānāṃ sarvāsāṃ saṃtatipradaḥ । devīśāstre vinirdiṣṭaḥ puṃsāṃ vandhyatvaroganut ।। so'yaṃ pācanadīpano rucikaro vṛṣyastathā garbhiṇīsarvavyādhivināśano ratikaraḥ pāṇḍupracaṇḍārtinut । dhanyo buddhikaraśca putrajananaḥ saubhāgyakṛdyoṣitāṃ nirdoṣaḥ smaramandirāmayaharo yogādaśeṣārtinut ।।
gandhakaḥ palamātraśca pṛthagakṣau śilālakau । tridinaṃ mardayitvātha vidadhyātkajjalīṃ śubhām ।। viṣāṇākāramūṣāyāṃ kajjalīṃ nikṣipettataḥ । dvipalasya ca tāmrasya tanmukhe cakrikāṃ nyaset ।।
saṃnirudhyātiyatnena saṃdhibandhe viśoṣite । tataḥ karipuṭārdhena pākaṃ samyak prakalpayet ।। svataḥśītaṃ samuddhṛtya cakrikāṃ paricūrṇayet । sthagayetkūpikāmadhye vastreṇa parigālitam ।।
raso'yaṃ cakrikābandhas tattadrogaharauṣadhaiḥ । dātavyaḥ śūlarogeṣu mūle gulme bhagandare ।। grahaṇyāmagnimāṃdye ca vidradhau jaṭharāmaye । nāgodare tathaivopaviṣṭake jalakūrmake ।।
skandenāmandakṛpayā trilokatrāṇahetave ।
